atha brahmāṇḍamahāpurāṇaṃ pūrvabhāgaprārambhaḥ । namonamaḥ kṣaye sṛṣṭau sthitau sattvamayāya vā । namo rajastamaḥsattvatrirūpāya svayaṃbhuve ।। jitaṃ bhagavatā tena hariṇā lokadhāriṇā ।
ajena viśvarūpeṇa nirguṇena guṇātmanā ।। brahmāṇaṃ lokakarttāraṃ sarvajñamaparājitam । prabhuṃbhūtabhaviṣyasya sāmpratasya ca satpatim ।। jñānamabratimaṃ tasya vairāgyaṃ ca jagatpateḥ ।
aiśvaryyaṃ caiva dharmaśca sadbhiḥ sevyaṃ catuṣṭayam ।। imānnarasya vai bhāvānnityaṃ sadasadātmakān । aviṃśakaḥ punastānvai kriyābhāvārthamīśvaraḥ ।। lokakṛllokatattvajño yogamāsthāya yogavit ।
asṛjatsarvabhūtāni sthāvarāṇi carāṇi ca ।। tasahaṃ viśvakarmāṇaṃ satpatiṃ lokasākṣiṇam । purāṇākhyānajijñāsurgacchāmi śaraṇaṃ vibhum ।। purāṇaṃ lokatattvārthamaśilaṃ vedasaṃmitam ।
praśaśaṃsa sa bhagavān vasiṣṭhāya prajāpatiḥ ।। tattvajñānāmṛtaṃ puṇyaṃ vasiṣṭho bhagavānṛṣiḥ । pautramadhyāpayāmāsa śakteḥ putraṃ parāśaram ।। parāśaraśca bhagavān jātūkarṇyamṛṣiṃ purā ।
tamadhyāpitavāndivyaṃ purāṇaṃ vedasaṃmitam ।। adhigamya purāṇaṃ tu jātūkarṇyo viśeṣavit । dvaipāyanāya pradadau paraṃ brahma sanātanam ।। dvaipāyanastataḥ prītaḥśaṣyebhyaḥpradadauvaśī ।
lokatattvavidhānārthaṃ pañcabhyaḥ paramādbhutam ।। vikhyāpanārthaṃ lokeṣu bahvarthaṃ śrutisaṃmatam । jaiminiñca sumantuṃ ca vaiśaṃpāyanamevaca ।। caturthaṃ pailavaṃ teṣāṃ pañcamaṃ lomaharṣaṇam ।
sūtamadbhutavṛttāntaṃ vinītaṃ dhārmikaṃ śrucim ।। adhītya ca purāṇaṃ ca vinīto lomaharṣaṇaḥ । ṛṣiṇā ca tvayā pṛṣṭaḥ kṛtaprajñaḥ sudhārmikaḥ ।। vasiṣṭhaścāpi munibhiḥ praṇāmya śirasā munīn ।
bhaktyā paramayā yuktaḥ kṛtvā cāpi pradakṣiṇam ।। avāptavidyaḥ sartuṣṭaḥ kurukṣetramupāgamat । satre savitate yatra yajamānānṛṣīñśucīn ।। vinayenopasaṃgamya satrriṇo romaharṣaṇam ।
vidhānato yathāśāstraṃ prajñayātijagāma ha ।। ṛṣayaścāpi te sarve tadānīṃ romaharṣaṇam । dṛṣṭvā paramasaṃhṛṣṭāḥ prītāḥ sumanasastathā ।। satkārairarccayāmāsurarghyapādyādibhistataḥ ।
abhivādya munīnsarvān rājājñāmabhigamya ca ।। ṛṣibhistairanujñātaḥ pṛṣṭaḥ sarvamanāmayam । abhigamya munīnsarvāṃstejo brahma sanātanam । sadasyānumate ramye svāstīrṇe samupāviśat ।।
upaviṣṭe tadā tasminmunayaḥ śaṃsitavratāḥ । mudānvitā yathānyāyaṃ vinayasthāḥ samāhitāḥ ।। sarve te ṛṣayaścainaṃ parivārya mahāvratam । paramaprītisaṃyuktā ityūcuḥ sūtanandanam ।।
svāgataṃ te mahābhāga diṣṭyā ca tvāṃnirāmayam । paśyāma dhīmannatrasthāḥ subrataṃ munisattamam ।। aśūnyā me rasādyaiva bhavataḥ puṇyakarmaṇaḥ । bhavāṃstasya muneḥ sūta vyāsasyāpi mahātmanaḥ ।।
anugrāhyaḥ sadā dhīmātr śiṣyaḥ śiṣyaguṇānvitaḥ । kṛtabuddhiśca te tattvamanugrāhyatayā prabho ।। avāpya vipulaṃ jñānaṃ sarvataśchinnasaṃśayaḥ । pṛccatāṃ naḥ sadā prājña sarvamākhyātumarhasi ।।
tadicchāmaḥ kathāṃ divyāṃ paurāṇīṃ śrutisaṃmitām । śrotuṃ dharmārthayuktāṃ tu etavdyāsācchrutaṃ tvayā ।। evasuktastadā sūtastvṛṣibhirvinayānvitaḥ । uvāca paramāprākjño vinītottara muttamam ।।
ṛṣeḥ śuśrūṣaṇaṃ yacca tasmātprajñā ca yā mama । yasmācchuśūṣaṇārthaṃ ca tatsatyamiti niścayaḥ ।। evaṃ gater'the yacchakyaṃ mayā vaktuṃ dvijottamāḥ । jijñāsā yatra yuṣmākaṃ tadājñātumihārhatha ।।
etacchrutvā tu munayo madhuraṃ tasya bhāṣitam । pratyūcuste punaḥ sūtaṃ bāṣpaparyākulekṣaṇam ।। bhavān viśeṣakuśalo vyāsaṃ sākṣāttu dṛṣṭavān । tasmāttvaṃ saṃbhavaṃ kṛtsnaṃ lokasyemaṃ vidarśaya ।।
yasya yasyānvaye ye ye tāṃstānicchāma veditum । teṣāṃ pūrvavisṛṣṭiṃ ca vicitrāṃ tvaṃ prajāpateḥ । satkṛtya paripṛṣṭaḥ sa mahātmā romaharṣaṇaḥ ।। vistareṇānupūrvyā ca kathayāmāsa sattamaḥ ।
yo me dvaipāyanaprītaḥ kathāṃ vai dvijasattamāḥ ।। puṇyāmākhyātavānviprāstāṃ vai vakṣyāmyanukramāt । purāṇaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi yaduktaṃ mātariśvanā ।। pṛṣṭena munibhiḥ pūrvaṃ naimiṣīyairma hātmabhiḥ ।
sargaśca pratisargaśca vaṃśo manvantarāṇi ca ।। vaṃśyānucaritaṃ caiva purāṇaṃ pañcalakṣaṇam । prakriyā prathamaḥ pādaḥ kathāyāṃ syātparigrahaḥ ।। anuṣaṅga utpoddhāta upasaṃhāra eva ca ।
evaṃ pādāstu catvāraḥ samāsātkīṃrtitā mayā ।। vakṣyāmi tānpurastāttu vistareṇa yathākramam । prathamaṃ sarvaśāstrāṇāṃ purāṇaṃ brahmaṇā śrutam ।। anantaraṃ ca vaktrebhyo vedāstasya viniḥsṛtāḥ ।
aṅgāni dharmaśāstraṃ ca vratāni niyamāstathā ।। avyaktaṃ kāraṇaṃ yattannityaṃ sadasadātmakam । mahadādiviśeṣāntaṃ sṛjāmīti viniścayaḥ ।। aṇḍaṃ hiraṇmayaṃ caiva brahmaṇaḥsūtiruttamā ।
aḍasyāvaraṇaṃ vārdhirapāmapi ca tejasā ।। vāyunā tasya vāyośca khena bhūtādinā tataḥ । bhūtādirmahatā caiva avyaktenāvṛto mahān ।। antarvarti ca bhūtānāmaṇḍamevopavarṇitam ।
nadīnāṃ parvatānāṃ ca prādurbhāvo atra paṭhyate ।। manvantarāṇāṃ sarveṣāṃ kalpānāṃ caiva varṇanam । kīrttanaṃ brahmavṛkṣasya brahmajanma prakīrtyate ।। ataḥ paraṃ brahmaṇaśca prajāsargopavarṇanam ।
avasthāścātra kīrtyante brahmaṇo avyaktajanmanaḥ ।। kalpānāṃ saṃbhavaśceva jagataḥ sthāpanaṃ tathā । śayanaṃ ca harerapsu pṛthivyuddharaṇaṃ tathā ।। saviśeṣaḥ purādīnāṃ varṇāśramavibhājanam ।
ṛkṣāṇāṃ grahasaṃsthānāṃ siddhānāṃ ca niveśanam ।। yojanānāṃ yathā cava saṃcaro bahuvistaraḥ । svargasthānavibhāgaśca sartyānāṃ śubhacāriṇām ।। vṛkṣāṇāmauṣadhīnāṃ ca vīrudhāṃ ca prakīrttanam ।
devatānāmṛṣīṇāṃ ca dve sṛtī parikīrtite ।। āmlādīnāṃ tarūṇāṃ ca sarjanaṃ vyañjanaṃ tathā । paśūnāṃ puruṣāṇāṃ ca saṃbhavaḥ parikīrttitaḥ ।। tathā nirvacanaṃ proktaṃ kalpasya ca parigrahaḥ ।
nava sargāḥ punaḥ proktā brahmaṇo buddhipūrvakāḥ ।। trayo ye buddhipūrvāstu tathā yallokakalpanam । brahmaṇo avayavebhyaśca dharmādīnāṃ samudbhavaḥ ।। ye dvādaśa prasūyante prajākalpe punaḥ punaḥ ।
kalpayorantare proktaṃ pratisaṃdhiśca yastayoḥ ।। tamomātrā vṛtatvāttu brahmaṇo adharmasaṃbhavaḥ । sattvodriktācca dehācca puruṣasya ca saṃbhavaḥ ।। tathaiva śatarūpāyāṃ tayoḥ putrāstataḥ param ।
priyavratottānapādau prasūtyākṛtayaḥ śubhāḥ ।। kīrtyante dhūtapāpmānastrailokye ye pratiṣṭhitāḥ । ruceḥ prajāpateścorddhamākūtyāṃ mithunodbhavaḥ ।। prasūtyamapi dakṣasya kanyānāmudbhavaḥ śubhaḥ ।
dākṣāyaṇīṣu vāpyūrdhvaṃśabdādyāsu mahātmanaḥ ।। dharmasya kīrtyate sargaḥ sāttvikastu sukhodayaḥ । tathādharmasya hiṃsāyāṃ tamaso aśubhalakṣaṇaḥ ।। bhṛgvādīnāmṛṣīṇāṃ ca prajāsargopavarṇanam ।
brahmarṣeśca vasiṣṭhasya yatra gotrānukīrttanam ।। agneḥ prajāyāḥ saṃbhūtiḥ svāhāyāṃ yatra kīrtyate । pitṝṇāṃ dviprakārāṇāṃ svadhāyāṃ tadanantaram ।। pitṛvaṃśaprasaṃgena kīrtyate ca maheśvarāt ।
dakṣasya śāpaḥ satyāśca bhṛgvādīnāṃ ca dhīmatām ।। pratiśāpaśca dakṣasya rudrādadbhutakarmaṇaḥ । pratiṣedhaśca vairasya kīrtyate doṣadarśanāt ।। manvantaraprasaṃgena kālākhyānaṃ ca kīrtyate ।
prajāpateḥ karddamasya kanyāyāḥ śubhalakṣaṇam ।। priyavratasya putrāṇāṃ kīrtyate yatra vistaraḥ । teṣāṃ niyogo dvīpeṣu deśeṣu ca pṛthak pṛthak ।। svāyaṃbhuvasya sargasya tataścāpyanukīrttanam ।
varṣāṇāṃ ca nadīnāṃ ca tadbhedānāṃ ca sarvaśaḥ ।। dvīpabhedasahasrāṇā mantarbhāvaśca saptasu । vistarānmaṇḍalaṃ caiva jaṃbūdvīpasamudrayoḥ ।। pramāṇaṃ yojanāgreṇa kīrtyante parvataiḥ saha ।
himavānhemakūṭaśca niṣadho merureva ca । nīlaḥ śvetaśca śṛṅgī ca kīrtyante sapta parvatāḥ ।। teṣāmantaraviṣkaṃbhā ucchrāyāyāmavistarāḥ ।। kīrtyante yojanāgreṇa ye ca tatra nivāsinaḥ ।
bhāratādīni varṣāṇi nadībhiḥ parvataistathā ।। bhūtaiścopaniviṣṭāni gatimadbhirdhuvai stathā । jaṃbūdvīpādayo dvīpāḥ samudraiḥ saptabhirvṛtāḥ ।। tataḥ svarṇamayī bhūmirlokālokaśca kīrtyate ।
sapramāṇā ime lokāḥ saptadvīpā ca medinī ।। rūpādayaḥ prakīrtyante karaṇātprākṛtaiḥ saha । sarvaṃ caitatpradhānasya pariṇāmaikadeśikam ।। paryāyaparimāṇaṃ ca saṃkṣepeṇātra kīrtyate ।
sūryācandramasoścaiva pṛthivyāścāpyaśeṣataḥ ।। pramāṇaṃ yojanāgreṇa sāṃpratairabhimānibhiḥ । mahendrādyāḥ śubhāḥ puṇyā mānasottaramūrdhani ।। ata ūrdhdagatiścoktā sūryasyālātayakravat ।
nāgavīthyakṣavīthyośca lakṣaṇaṃ ca prakīrtyate ।। koṣṭhayorlekhayoścaiva maṇḍalānāṃ ca yojanaiḥ । lokālokasya sandhyāyā ahno viṣuvatastathā ।। lokapālāḥ sthitāścorddhaṃ kīrtyante te caturddiśam ।
pitṝṇāṃ devatānāṃ ca panthānau dakṣiṇottarau ।। gṛhiṇāṃ nyāsināṃ cokto rajaḥsattvasamāśrayaḥ । kīrtyate ca padaṃ viṣṇordharmādyā yatra ca sthitāḥ ।। sūryācandramasoścāro grahāṇāṃ jyotiṣāṃ tathā ।
kīrtyate dhṛtasāmarthyātprajānāṃ ca śubhāśubham ।। brahmaṇā nirmitaḥ sauraḥ sādanārthaṃ ca sa svayam । kīrtyate bhagavānyena prasarppati divaḥ kṣayam ।। sa ratho adhiṣṭhito devair ādityai ṛṣibhistathā ।
gandharvairapsarobhiśca grāmaṇīsarparākṣasaiḥ ।। apāṃ sāramayātsyandātkathyate ca rasastathā । vṛddhikṣayau ca somasya kīrtyete somakāritau ।। sūryādīnāṃ syandanānāṃ dhruvādeva pravarttanam ।
kīrtyate śiśumārasya yasya pucche dhruvaḥ sthitaḥ ।। tārārūpāṇi sarvāṇi nakṣatrāṇi grahaiḥ saha । nivāsā yatra kīrtyante devānāṃ puṇyakarmaṇām ।। sūryaraśmisahasraṃ ca varṣaśītoṣṇaviśravaḥ ।
pravibhāgaścaraśmīnāṃ nāmataḥ karmatīrthataḥ ।। parimāṇaṃ gatiścoktā grahāṇāṃ sūryasaṃśrayāt । veśyārūpātpradhānasya parimāṇo mahādbhavaḥ ।। purūravasa ailasya māhātmyasyānukīrttanam ।
pitṝṇāṃ dviprakārāṇāṃ māhātmyaṃ vā mṛtasya ca ।। tataḥ parvāṇi kīrtyante parvaṇāṃ caiva saṃdhayaḥ । svargalokagatānāñca prāptānāñcāpyadhogatim ।। pitṝṇāṃ dviprakārāṇāṃ śrāddhenānugraho mahān ।
yugasaṃkhyāpramāṇaṃ ca kīrtyate ca kṛtaṃ yugam ।। tretāyuge cāpakarṣādvār ttāyāḥ saṃpravarttanam । varṇānāmāśramāṇāṃ ca saṃsthitirdharmatastathā ।। vajrapravarttanaṃ caiva saṃvādo yatra kīrtyate ।
ṛṣīṇāṃ vasunā sārddhaṃ vasoścādhaḥ punargatiḥ । śabdatvaṃ ca pradhānāttu svāyambhuvamṛte manum ।। praśaṃsā tapasaścoktā yugāvasthāśca kṛtsnaśaḥ । dvāparasya kaleścāpi saṃkṣepeṇa prakīrttanam ।।
manvantaraṃ ca saṃkhyā ca mānuṣeṇa prakīrttitā । manvantarāṇāṃ sarveṣāmetadeva ca lakṣaṇam ।। atītānāgatānāṃ ca varttamānaṃ ca kīrtyate । tathā manvantarāṇāṃ ca pratisaṃdhānalakṣaṇam ।।
atītānā gatānāṃ ca proktaṃ svāyambhuve tataḥ । ṛṣīṇāṃ ca gatiḥ proktā kālajñānagatistathā ।। durgasaṃkhyāpramāṇaṃ ca yugavārtā pravarttanam । tretāyāṃ cakravartīnāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ janma caiva hi ।।
pramateśca tathā janma atho kaliyugasya vai । aṅgulairhāsanaṃ caiva bhūtānāṃ yacca cocyate ।। śāśānāṃ parisaṃkhyānaṃ śiṣyaprādhānyameva ca । vākyaṃ saptavidhaṃ caiva ṛṣigotrānukīrtanam ।।
lakṣaṇaṃ sūtaputrāṇāṃ brahmaṇāsya ca kṛtsnaśaḥ । dedānāṃ vyasanaṃ caiva vedavyāsairmahātmabhiḥ ।। manvantareṣu devānāṃ prajeśānāṃ ca kīrttanam । manvantarakramaścaiva kālajñānaṃ ca kīrtyate ।।
dakṣasya cāpi dauhitrāḥ priyāyā duhituḥ śubhāḥ । brahmādibhistejanitā dakṣeṇaiva ca dhīmatā ।। sāvarṇāścātra kīrtyante manavo merumāśritāḥ । dhruvasyauttānapādasya prajāsargopavarṇanam ।।
cākṣuṣasya manoḥ sargaḥ prajānāṃ vīryavarmanam । prabhuṇā caiva vainyena bhūmidohapravartatā ।। pātrāṇāṃ payasāṃ caiva vatsānāṃ ca viśeṣaṇam । brahmādibhiḥ pūrvameva dugdhā caiyaṃ vasuṃdharā ।।
daśabhyaścaṃ pracetobhyo māriṣāyāṃ prajāpateḥ । dakṣasya kīrtyata janma samasyāṃśena dhīmataḥ ।। bhūtabhavyabhaveśatvaṃ mahendrāṇāṃ ca kīrtyate । manvādikā bhaviṣyanti ākhyānaibarhubhirvṛtāḥ ।।
vaivasvatasya ca manoḥ kīrtyate sargavistaraḥ । brahmādikośa utpattirbhṛgvadīnāṃ ca kīrtyate ।। viniṣkṛṣya prajāsarge cākṣuṣasya manoḥśubhe । dakṣasya kīrtyate sargo dhyānādvaivasvatāntare ।।
nāradaḥ kṛtasaṃvādo dakṣaputrānmahābalān । nāśayāmāsa śāpāya mānaso brahmaṇaḥ sutaḥ ।। tato dakṣo asṛjatkanyā vairiṇā nāma viśrutāḥ । marutpravāhe maruto dityāṃ devyāṃ ca saṃbhavaḥ ।।
kīrtyate marutāṃ cātragaṇāste saptasaptakāḥ । devatvamindravāsena vāyuskandheṣu cāśramaḥ ।। daityānāṃ dānavānāṃ ca yakṣagandharvarakṣasām । sarvabhūtapiśācānāṃ yakṣaṇāṃ pakṣivīrudhām ।।
utpattayaścāpsarasāṃ kīrtyante bahuvistarāt । mārtaṇḍamaṇḍalaṃ kṛtsnaṃ janmairāvatahastinaḥ ।। vainateyasamutpattistathā rājyā bhiṣecanam । bhṛgūṇāṃ vistaraścoktastathā cāṅgirasāmapi ।।
kaśyapasya pulastyasya tathaivātrermahātmanaḥ । parāśarasya ca muneḥ prajānāṃ yatra vistaraḥ ।। tisraḥ kanyāḥ sukīrtyante yāsulokāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ । icchāyā vistaraścokta ādityasya tataḥ param ।।
kiṅkuviccaritaṃ proktaṃ dhruvasyaiva nibarhaṇam । bṛhadbalānāṃ saṃkṣepādikṣvākvādyāḥ prakīrttitāḥ ।। niśyādīnāṃ kṣitīśānāṃ palāṇḍu haraṇādibhiḥ । kīrtyate vistarātsarge yayāterapi bhūpateḥ ।।
yaduvaṃśasamuddeśo haihayasya ca vistaraḥ । krodhādanantaraṃ coktastathā vaṃśasya vistaraḥ ।। jyāmaghasya ca māhātmyaṃ prajāsargaśca kīrtyate । devāvṛdhasyāndhakasya dhṛṣṭeścapi mahātmanaḥ ।।
animitrānvayaścaiva viśormithyābhiśaṃsanam । viśodhamanusaṃprāptirmaṇiratnasya dhīmataḥ ।। satrājitaḥ prajāsarge rājarṣerdevamīḍhuṣaḥ । śūrasya janma cāpyuktaṃ caritaṃ ca māhātmanaḥ ।।
kaṃsasyāpi ca daurātmyamekīvaṃśyātsamudbhavaḥ । vāsudevasya deva kyāṃ viṣṇoramitatejasaḥ ।। anantaramṛṣeḥ sargaḥ prajāsargopavarṇanam । devāsure samutpanne viṣṇunā strīvadhe kṛte ।।
saṃrakṣatā śakravadhaṃ śāpaḥ prāptaḥ purā bhṛgoḥ । bhṛguścotthāpayāmāsa divyāṃ śukrasya mātaram ।। devānāṃ ca ṛṣīṇāṃ ca saṃkramā dvādaśātdṛtāḥ । nārasihaprabhṛtayaḥ kīrtyante pāpanāśanāḥ ।।
śukeṇārādhanaṃ sthāṇorghoreṇa tapasā tathā । varapradāna kṛttena yatra śarvastavaḥ kṛtaḥ ।। anantaraṃ ca nirdiṣṭaṃ devāsuraviceṣṭitam । jayantyā saha śakreṇa yatra śuko mahātmani ।।
asurānmohayāmāsa śakrarūpeṇa buddhimān । bṛhaspatiśca taṃ śukaṃ śaśāpa sa mahādyutiḥ ।। ukta ca viṣṇormāhātmyaṃ viṣṇorjanmani śabdyate । turvasuścātra dauhitro yavīyānyo yadorabhūt ।।
anurdruhyādayaḥ sarve tathā tattanayā nṛpāḥ । anuvaṃśyāmahātmānasteṣāṃ pārthivasattamāḥ ।। kīrtyante yatra kārtsnyena bhūridraviṇatejasaḥ । ātithyasya tu vibrarṣeḥ saptadhā dharmasaṃśrayāt ।।
bārhasvatyaṃ sūribhiśca yatra śāpamupāvṛtam । haravaṃśayaśaḥsparśaḥ śantanorvīryaśabdanam ।। bhaviṣyatāṃ tathā rājñāmupasaṃhāraśabdanam । anāgatānāṃsaṃghānāṃ prabhūṇāṃ copavarṇanam ।।
bhautyasyānte kaliyuge kṣīṇe saṃhāravarṇanam । naimittikāḥ prākṛtikā yathaivātyantikāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। vividhaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ kīrtyate pratisaṃcaraḥ । anādṛṣṭirbhāskarasya ghoraḥ saṃvarttakānalaḥ ।।
sāṃkhye lakṣaṇamuddiṣṭaṃ tato brahma viśeṣataḥ । bhuvādīnāṃ ca lokānāṃ saptānāṃ copavarṇanam ।। aparārddhāparaiścaiva lakṣaṇaṃ parikīrtyate । brahmaṇoyojanāgreṇa parimāṇavinirṇayaḥ ।।
kīrtyante cātra nirayāḥ pāpānāṃ rauravādayaḥ । sarveṣāṃ caiva sattvānāṃ pariṇāmavinirṇayaḥ ।। brahmaṇaḥ pratisaṃsargātsarva saṃsāravarṇanam । gatirūrddhamadhaścoktā dharmādharmasamāśrayā ।।
kalpe kalpe ca bhūtānāṃ mahatāmapi saṃkṣayam । asaṃkhyayā ca duḥkhāni brahmaṇaścāpyanityatā ।। daurātmyaṃ caiva bhogānāṃ saṃhārasya ca kaṣṭatā । durlabhatvaṃ ca mokṣasya vairāgyāddoṣadarśanāt ।।
vyaktāvyaktaṃ parityajya sattvaṃ brahmaṇi saṃsthitam । nānātvadarśanācchuddhastavastatra nivarttate ।। tatastāpatrayād bhīto rūpārthohi nirañjanaḥ । ānandaṃ brahmaṇaḥ prāpya na bibheti kutaścana ।।
kīrtyate ca punaḥ sargo brahmaṇo anyasya pūrvavat । kīrtyate jagataścatra sargapralayavikriyāḥ ।। pravṛttayaśca bhūtānāṃ prasutānāṃ phalāni ca । kīrtyate ṛṣivargasya sargaḥ pāpapraṇāśanaḥ ।।
prādurbhāvo vasiṣṭhasya śakterjanma tathaiva ca । saudāsāsthigrahaścāsya viśvāmitrakṛtena tu ।। parāśarasya cotpattiradṛśyantyāṃ tathā vibhoḥ । saṃjajñe pitṛkanyāyāṃ vyāsaścāpi mahāmuniḥ ।।
śukasya ca tathā janma saha putrasya dhīmaptaḥ । parāśarasya pradvepo viśvāmitra ṛṣiṃ prati ।। vasiṣṭhasaṃbhṛtiścāgnerviśvāmitrajighāṃsayā । devena vidhinā vipra viśvāmitrahitaiṣiṇā ।।
saṃtānahetorvibhunā gīrṇaskandhena dhīmatā । ekaṃ vedaṃ catuṣpādaṃ caturddhā punarīśvaraḥ ।। tathā bibheda bhāgavān vyāsaḥ śārvādanugrahāt । tasya śiṣyapraśiṣyaiśca śākhā vedāyutāḥ kṛtāḥ ।।
prayoge prahvalā naiva yathā dṛṣṭaḥ svayaṃbhuvā । pṛṣṭa vanto viśiṣṭāste munayo dharmakāṅkṣiṇaḥ ।। deśaṃ puṇyamabhīpsato vibhunā taddhitaiṣiṇā । sunābhaṃ divyarūpābhaṃ saptāṅgaṃ śubhaśaṃsanam ।।
ānaupamyamidaṃ cakraṃ varttamānamatandritāḥ । pṛṣṭhato yāta niyatāstataḥ prāpsyatha pāṭitam ।। gacchatastasya cakrasya yatra nemirviśīryate । puṇyaḥ sa deśo mantavyaḥ pratyuvāca tadā prabhuḥ ।।
uktvā caivamṛṣīnsarvānadṛśyatvamupāgamat । gaṅgā garbha yavāhārā naimiṣeyāstathaiva ca ।। īśire caiva satreṇa munayo naimiṣe tadā ।। mṛteśaradvatitathā tasya cotthāpanaṅkṛtam ।
ṛṣayo naimiṣeyāśca dayayā parayā yutāḥ ।। niḥsīmāṃ gāmimāṃ kṛtvā kṛṣaṇaṃ rājānamāharat । prītiṃ caiva kṛtātithyaṃ rājānaṃ vidhivattadā ।। antaḥ sargagataḥ krūraḥ svarbhānurasuro haran ।
drute rājani rājānu madrate munayastataḥ ।। gandharvarakṣitaṃ dṛṣṭvā kalāpagrāmaketanam । sannipātaḥ punastasya tathā yajñe maharṣibhiḥ ।। dṛṣṭvā hiraṇmayaṃ sarvaṃ vivādastasya tairabhūt ।
tadā vai naimiṣeyānāṃ satre dvādaśavārṣike ।। tathā vivadamānaiśca yaduḥ saṃsthāpitaśca taiḥ । janayitvā tvaraṇyaṃ vai yaduputramathāyutam ।। samāpayitvā tatsatraṃ vāyuṃ te paryupāsata ।
iti kṛtyasamuddeśaḥ purāṇāṃśopavarṇitaḥ ।। anenānukrameṇaiva purāṇaṃ saṃprakāśate । sukhamarthaḥ samāsena mahānapyupalakṣyate ।। tasmātsamāsamuddiśya vakṣyāmi tava vistaram ।
pādamādyamidaṃ samyag yo adhīte vijitedriyaḥ ।। tenādhītaṃ purāṇaṃ syātsarvaṃ nāstyatrasaṃśayaḥ । yo vidyāccaturo vedān sāṃgopaniṣadān dvijāḥ ।। itihāsapurāṇābhyāṃ vedaṃ samupabṛṃhayet ।
bibhetyalpaśrutādvedo māmayaṃ prahariṣyati ।। abhyasannimamadhyāyaṃ sākṣātproktaṃ svayaṃbhuvā । nāpadaṃ prāpya muhyeta yatheṣṭāṃ prāpnuyādgatim ।। yasmātpurā hyabhūccaitatpurāṇaṃ tena tatsmṛtam ।
niruktamasya yo veda sarvapāpaiḥ pramucyate ।। ataśca saṃkṣepamimaṃ śṛṇudhvaṃ nārāyaṇaḥ sarvamidaṃ purāṇam । saṃsargakāle api karoti marga saṃhāra kāle ca na vāsti bhūyaḥ ।। pratyavocanpunaḥ sūtamṛṣayaste tapodhanāḥ ।
kutra satraṃ samabhattevaṣāmadbhutakarmaṇām ।। kiyantaṃ caiva tatkālaṃ kathaṃ ca samavarttata । ācacakṣe purāṇaṃ ca kathaṃ tatsaprabhañjanaḥ ।। ācakhyau vistareṇaiva para kautūhalaṃ hi naḥ ।
iti saṃcoditaḥ sūtaḥ pratyuvāca śubhaṃ vacaḥ ।। śṛṇudhvaṃ yatra te dhīrā menire mantramuttamam । yāvantaṃ cābhavatkālaṃ yathā ca samavartata ।। sisṛkṣamāṇo viśvaṃ hi yajate visṛjatpurā ।
satraṃ hi te atipuṇyaṃ ca sahasraparivatsarān ।। tapogṛhapateryatra brahmā caivābhavatsvayam । iḍāyā yatra patnītvaṃ śāmitraṃ yatra buddhimān ।। mṛtyuścake mahātejāstasminsatre mahātmanām ।
vibudhāścoṣire tatra sahasraparivatsarān ।। bhramato dharmacakrasya yatra nemiraśīryata । karmaṇā tena vikhyātaṃ naimiṣaṃ munipūjitam ।। yatra sā gomatī puṇyā siddhacāraṇasevitā ।
rohiṇī sa sutā tatra gomatī sābhavat kṣaṇāt ।। śaktirjyeṣṭhā samabhavadvasiṣṭhasya mahātmanaḥ । rundhatyāḥ sutāyātrādānamuttamatejasaḥ ।। kalmāṣapādo nṛpatiryatra śakraśca śaktinā ।
yatra vairaṃ samabhavadviśvāmitravasiṣṭhayoḥ ।। adṛśyantyāṃ samabhavanmuniryatra parāśaraḥ । parābhavo vasiṣṭhasya yasya jñāne hyavarttayat ।। tatra te menire śailaṃ naimiṣe brahmavādinaḥ ।
naimiṣaṃ jajñire yasmānnaimiṣīyāstataḥ smṛtāḥ ।। tatsatramabhavatteṣāṃ samā dvādaśa dhīmatām । purūravasi vikrānte praśāsati vasuṃdharām ।। aṣṭādaśa samudrasya dvīpānaśran purūravāḥ ।
tutoṣa naiva ratnānāṃ lobhāditi hi naḥ śrutam ।। urvaśī cakame taṃ ca devadūtapracoditā । ājahāra ca tatsatramurvaśyā saha saṃgataḥ ।। tasminnarapatau satre naimiṣīyāḥ pracakrire ।
yaṃ garbhaṃ suṣuve gaṅgā pāvakāddīptatejasam ।। tattulyaṃ parvate nyastaṃ hiraṇyaṃ samapadyata । hiraṇmayaṃ tataścake yajñavāṭaṃ mahātmanām ।। viśvakarmā svayandevo bhāvano lokabhāvanaḥ ।
sa praviśya tataḥ satre teṣāmamitatejasām ।। aiḍaḥ purūravā bheje taṃ deśaṃ mṛgayāṃ caran । taṃ dṛṣṭvā mahādāśvaryaṃ yajñavāṭaṃ hiraṇmayam ।। lobhena hatavijñānastadādātumupākramat ।
naimiṣeyāstatastasya cukrudhurnṛpatiṃ bhṛśam ।। nijaghnuścāpi taṃ kruddhāḥ kuśavajrairmanīṣiṇaḥ । taponiṣṭhāśca rājānaṃ munayo devacoditāḥ ।। kuśavajraurviniṣpiṣṭaḥ sa rājā vyajahāttanum ।
aurvaśeyaistatastasya yuddhaṃ cakre nṛpo bhuvi ।। nahuṣasya mahātmānaṃ pitaraṃ yaṃ pracakṣate । sa teṣvavabhṛtheṣveva dharmmaśīlo mahīpatiḥ ।। āyurāyabhavāyāgryamasmin satre narottamaḥ ।
śāntayitvā tu rājānaṃ tadā brahmavidastathā ।। satramārebhire karttuṃ pṛthvīvatsā tmamūrtayaḥ । babhūva satre teṣāṃ tu brahmacaryaṃ mahātmanām ।। viśvaṃ sisṛkṣamāṇānāṃ purā visvasṛjāmiva ।
vaikhānasaiḥ priyasakhairvāla khilyairmarīcibhiḥ ।। ajaiśca munibhirjātaṃ sūryavaiśvānaraprabhaḥ । vitṛdevāpsaraḥsiddhairgandharvoragacāraṇaiḥ ।। bhārataiḥ śuśubhe rājā devairindrasamo yathā ।
stotraśastrairgṛhairdevānpitṝnpitryaiśca karmabhiḥ ।। ānarcuḥsma yathājāti gandharvādīn yathāvidhi । ārādhane sa sasmāra tataḥ karmāntareṣu ca ।। jaguḥ sāmāni gandharvā nanṛtuścāpsarogaṇāḥ ।
vyājahrurmunayo vācaṃ citrākṣarapadāṃ śubhām ।। mantrādi tatra vidvāṃso jajapuśca parasparam । vitaṇḍāvacanaiścaiva nijaghnuḥ prativādinaḥ ।। ṛṣayaścaiva vidvāṃsaḥ śabdārthanyāyakovidāḥ ।
na tatra hāritaṃ kiñcidviviśurbrahmarākṣasāḥ ।। naiva yajñaharā daityā naiva vājamukhāstriṇaḥ । prāyaścittaṃ daridraṃ ca na tatra samajāyata ।। śaktiprajñākriyāyegairvidhirāśīṣvanuṣṭitaḥ ।
evaṃ ca vavṛdhe satraṃ dvādaśābdaṃ manīṣiṇām ।। ṛṣīṇāṃ naimiṣīyāṇāṃ tadabhūdiva vajriṇaḥ । vṛddhādyā ṛtvijo vīrā jyotiṣṭomān pṛthakpṛthak ।। cakrire pṛṣṭhagamanāḥ sarvānayutadakṣiṇān ।
samāptayajño yatrāste vāsudevaṃ mahādhipam ।। papracchuramitātmānaṃ bhavadbhiryadahaṃ dvijaḥ । pracoditaḥ svavaṃśārthaṃ sa ca tānabravītprabhuḥ ।। śiṣyaḥsvayaṃbhuvo devaḥ sarvaṃ pratyakṣadṛgvaśī ।
aṇimādibhiraṣṭābhiḥ sūkṣmairaṅgaiḥ samanvitaḥ ।। tiryagvātādibhirvarṣaiḥ sarvāṃ llokānbibharti yaḥ । saptaskandhā bhṛtāḥ śākhāḥ sarvatoyājarājarān ।। viṣayair maruto yasya saṃsthitāḥ saptasaptakāḥ ।
vyūhatrayāṇāṃ sūtānāṃ kurvan satraṃ mahābalaḥ ।। tejasaśvāpyupāyānāṃ dadhātīha śarīriṇaḥ । prāṇādyā vṛttayaḥ pañca dhāraṇānāṃ svavṛttibhiḥ ।। pūryamāmaḥ śarīrāṇāṃ dhāraṇaṃ yasya kurvate ।
ākāśayonirdviguṇaḥ śābdasparśasamanvitaḥ ।। vācoraṇiḥ samākhyātā śabdaśāstravicakṣaṇaiḥ । bhāratyārḥ ślakṣṇayā sarvānmunīnprahlādayanniva ।। purāṇajñāḥ sumanasaḥ purāṇāśrayayuktayā ।
purāma niyatā viprāḥ kathāmakathayadvibhuḥ ।। etatsarvaṃ yathāvṛttamākhyānaṃ dvijasattamāḥ । ṛṣīṇāṃ ca paraṃ caitallokatattvamanuttamam ।। brahmaṇā yatpurā proktaṃ purāṇaṃ jñānamuttamam ।
devatānāmṛṣīṇāṃ ca sarvapāpapramocanam ।। vistareṇānupūrvyā ca tasya vakṣyāmyanukramam ।। śṛṇu teṣāṃ kathāṃ divyāṃ sarvapāpapramocanīm । kathyamānāṃ mayā citrāṃ bahvarthāṃ śrutisaṃmatām ।।
ya imāṃ dhārayennityaṃ śṛṇuyādvāpyabhīkṣṇaśaḥ । svavaṃśaṃ dhāraṇaṃ kṛtvā svargaloke mahīyate ।। viśvatārā yā ca pañca yathāvṛttaṃ yathāśrutam । kīrtyamānaṃ nibodhārthaṃ pūrveṣāṃ kīrttivarddhanam ।।
dhanyaṃ yaśasyamāyuṣyaṃ svargyaṃ śatrughnameva ca । kīrttanaṃ sthirakīrtīnāṃ sarveṣāṃ puṇyakarmaṇām ।। yasmātkalpāyate kalpaḥ samagraṃ śucaye śuciḥ । tasmai hiraṇyagarbhāya puruṣāyeśvarāya ca ।।
ajāya prathamāyaiva variṣṭhāya prajāsṛje । brahmaṇe lokatantrāya namaskṛtya svayaṃbhuve ।। mahadādyaṃ viśeṣāntaṃ savairūpyaṃ salakṣaṇam । pañcapramāṇaṃ ṣadśrāntaḥ puruṣādhiṣṭhitaṃ ca yat ।।
āsaṃyamātpravakṣyāmi bhūtasargamanuttamam । avyaktaṃ kāraṇaṃ yattannityaṃ sadasadātmakam ।। pradhānaṃ prakṛtiṃ caiva yamāhustattvacintakāḥ । gandharūparasairhīnaṃ śabdasparśavivarjitam ।।
jagadyonimmahābhūtaṃ paraṃ brahmasanātanam । vigrahaṃ sarvabhūtānāmavyaktamabhavatkila ।। anādyantamajaṃ sūkṣmaṃ triguṇaṃ prabhavāpyayam । asāṃpratikamajñeyaṃ brahma yatsadasatparam ।।
tasyātmanā sarvamidaṃ vyāptamāsīttamomayam । guṇasāmye tadā tasminnavibhātaṃ tamomayam ।। sargakāle pradhānasya kṣatrajñādhiṣṭhitasya vai । guṇabhāvādbhāsamāne mahātattva babhūva ha ।।
sūkṣmaḥ sa tu mahānagre avyaktena samāvṛtaḥ । sattvodreko mahānagre sattvamātraprakāśakaḥ ।। sattvānmahānsa vijñeya ekastatkāraṇaḥ samṛtaḥ । niṅgamātraṃ samutpannaṃ kṣetrajñādhiṣṭitaṃ mahat ।।
saṃkalpo adhyavasāyaśca tasya vṛttidvayaṃ smṛtam । mahāsṛṣṭiṃ ca kurute vītamānaḥ sisṛkṣayā ।। dharmādīni ca bhūtāni lokatattvārthahetavaḥ । mano mahātmani brahma durbuddhikhyātirīśvarāt ।।
prajñāsaṃdhiśca sarvasvaṃ saṃkhyāyatanaraśmibhiḥ । manute sarvabhūtānāṃ tasmācceṣṭaphalo vibhuḥ ।। bhoktā trātā vibhaktātmā varttanaṃ mana ucyate । tattvānāṃ saṃgrahe yasmānmahāṃśca parimāṇataḥ ।।
śeṣebhyo guṇātattvebhyo mahāniva tanuḥ smṛtaḥ । vibhaktimānaṃ manute vibhāgaṃ manyate api vā ।। puruṣo bhogasaṃbandhāttena cāsau sati smṛtaḥ । bṛhattvādvṛṃhaṇatvācca bhāvānāmakhilāśrayāt ।।
yasmādvṛṃhayata bhāvān brahmā tena nirucyate । āpūrayati yasmācca sarvān dehānanugrahaiḥ ।। budhyate puruṣaścātra sarvān bhāvānpṛthak pṛthak । tasmiṃstu kāryakaraṇaṃ saṃsiddhaṃ brahmaṇaḥ purā ।।
prākṛtaṃ devi vartaṃ māṃ kṣetrajño brahmasaṃmitaḥ । sa vai śarīrī prathamaḥ purā puruṣa ucyate ।। ādikarttā sa bhūtānāṃ brahmāgre samavarttinām ।। hiraṇyagabhaḥ so aṇḍe asminprādurbhūtaścaturmukhaḥ ।
sarge ca pratisarge ca kṣetrajño brahma saṃsitaḥ ।। karaṇaiḥ saha pṛcchante pratyāhārestyajanti ca । bhajante ca punardehāṃste samāhārasaṃdhisu ।। hiraṇmayastu yo merustasyoddharturmahātmanaḥ ।
gartodakaṃ sabudāstu hareyuścāpi pañcatāḥ ।। yasminnaṇḍa ime lokāḥ sapta vai saṃpratiṣṭhitāḥ । pṛthivī saptabhirdvīpaiḥ samudraiḥ saha saptabhiḥ ।। parvataiḥ sumahadbhiśca nadībhiśca sahasraśaḥ ।
antaḥsthasya tvime lokā antarviśvamidaṃ jagat ।। candrādityau sanakṣatau saṃgrahaḥ saha vāyunā । lokālokaṃ ca yat kiñcidaṇḍe tasminpratiṣṭitam ।। āpo daśaguṇe naiva tejasā bāhyato vṛtāḥ ।
tejo daśaguṇenaiva bāhyato vāyunā vṛtam ।। vāyurdaśaguṇenaiva bāhyato nabhasā vṛtaḥ । ākāśamāvṛtaṃ sarvaṃ bahirbhūtādinā tathā ।। bhūtādirmahatā caiva pradhānenāvṛto mahān ।
ebhirāvaraṇairaṇḍaṃ saptabhiḥ prākṛtairvṛtam ।। icchayā vṛtya cānyonyamaraṇe prakṛtayaḥ sthitaḥ । prasargakāle sthitvā ca grasaṃtasca parasparam ।। evaṃ parasparaiścaiva dhārayanti parasparam ।
ādhārādheyabhāvena vikārāste vikāriṣu ।। avyaktaṃ kṣetramityuktaṃ brahma kṣetrajñamucyate । ityevaṃ prākṛtaḥ sargaḥ kṣetrajñādhiṣṭhitastu saḥ ।। abuddhipūrvaḥ prathamaḥ prādurbhūtastaḍidyathā ।
etaddhiraṇyagarbhasya canma yo vetti tattvataḥ । āyuṣmānkīrtimāndhanyaḥ prajñāvāṃśca na saṃśayaḥ ।। ātmanyavasthite vyakte vikāre pratisaṃhate । sādharmyeṇāvatiṣṭhete pradhānapuruṣau tadā ।।
tamaḥsattva guṇāvetau samatvena vyavasthitau । anudriktāvanucarau tena proktau parasparam ।। guṇasāmye layo jñeya ādhikye sṛṣṭirucyate । sattvavṛddhau sthitirabhūd dhruvaṃ padma śikhāsthitam ।।
yadā tamasi sattve ca rajopyanugataṃ sthitam । rajaḥ pravartakaṃ tacca bījeṣviva yathā jalam ।। guṇā vaiṣamyamāsādya prasaṃgena pratiṣṭhitāḥ । guṇebhyaḥ kṣobhyamāṇebhyastrayo jñeyā hi sādare ।।
śāśvatāḥ paramā guhyāḥ sarvātmānaḥ śarīriṇaḥ । sattvaṃ viṣṇū rajo brahmā tamo rudraḥ prajāpatiḥ ।। rajaḥprakāśakoviṣṇurbrahmasraṣṭṛtvamāpnuyāt । jāyate ca yataścatrā lokasṛṣṭirmahojasaḥ ।।
tamaḥprakāśako viṣṇuḥ kālatvena vyavasthitaḥ । sattvaprakāśako viṣṇuḥ sthititvena vyavasthitaḥ ।। eta eva trayo lokā eta eva trayo guṇāḥ । eta eva trayo vedā eta eva trajo agnayaḥ ।।
parasparānvayā hyete parasparamanuvratāḥ । paraspareṇa vartante prerayanti parasparam ।। anyonyaṃ mithunaṃ hyete anyonyamupajīvinaḥ । kṣaṇaṃ viyogo na hyeṣāṃ na tyajanti parasparam ।।
pradhānaguṇavaiṣamyātsargakāle pravarttate । adṛṣṭādhiṣṭhitātpūrve tasmātsadasadātmakāt ।। brahmā buddhitvamithunaṃ yugapatsaṃbabhūva ha । tasmāttamovyaktamayaṃ kṣetrajño brahmasaṃjñakaḥ ।।
saṃsiddhakāryakaraṇo brahmagre samavarttata । tejasāpratimo dhīmānavyaktaḥ saṃprakāśakaḥ ।। sa vai śarīraprathamo dhāraṇatvavyavasthitaḥ । jñānenāpratimeneha vairāgyeṇa ca saptatiḥ ।।
avyaktatvāya tenāsya manasā yadyadicchati । vaśīkṛtatvāttraiguṇyātsāpekṣatvācca bhāvataḥ ।। caturmukhastu brahmatve kālatve cāntakṛdbhavaḥ । sahasramūrdhā puruṣastisro avasthāḥsvayaṃbhuvaḥ ।।
sarvaṃ rajaśca brahmatve kālatve carajastamaḥ । sāttvikaḥ puruṣatve ca guṇavṛtaṃ svayaṃbhuvaḥ ।। brahmatve sṛjate lokān kālatve saṃkṣayatyapi । puruṣatve udāsīnastisro avasthāḥ svayaṃbhuvaḥ ।।
brahmā kamala patrākṣaḥ kālo jātyañjanaprabhaḥ । puruṣaḥ puṇḍarīkākṣo rūpeṇa paramātmanaḥ ।। ekadhā sa dvidhā caiva tridhā ca bahudhā punaḥ । yogīśvaraḥ śarīrāṇi karoti vikarotica ।।
nānākṛtikriyārūpamāśrayantisvalīlayā । tridhā yadvartate loke tasmātrriguṇa ucyate ।। caturddhā pravibhaktatvāccaturvyūhaḥ prakīrttitaḥ । yadā śete tadārdhāte yadbhuṅkte viṣayānprabhuḥ ।।
yatsvasthāḥ satataṃ bhāvastasmādātmā nirūcyate । ṛṣiḥ sarvagataścātra śarīre so abhyayātprabhuḥ ।। svāmī sarvasya yatsarvaṃviṣṇuḥ sarvapraveśanāt । bhagavānagrasadbhāvānnāgo nāgasvasaṃśrayāt ।।
paramaḥ saṃprahṛṣṭatvāddevatādomiti smṛtiḥ । sarvajñaḥ sarvavijñānātsarvaḥsarvaṃyatastataḥ ।। narāṇāṃ svāpanaṃ brahmā tasmānnārāyaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ । tridhā vibhajya cātmānaṃ sakalaḥ saṃpravarttate ।।
sṛjate grasate caiva pālyate ca tribhiḥ svayam । so agre hiraṇyagarbhaḥ san prādurbhūtaḥ svayaṃ prabhuḥ ।। ādyo hi svavaśaścaiva ajātatvādajaḥ smṛtaḥ । tasmāddhiraṇyagarbhaśca purāṇeṣu nirucyate ।।
svayaṃbhuvo nivṛttasya kālo varṇāgratastu yaḥ । na śakyaḥ parisaṃkhyātuṃ manuvarṣaśatairapi ।। kalpasaṃkhyānivṛttastu parārdho brahmaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ । tāvattve so asya kālo anyastasyānte pratibuddhyate ।।
koṭivarṣasahasrāṇi gṛhabhūtāni yāni ca । samatītāni kalpānāṃ tāvaccheṣātparetu ye ।। yatsvayaṃ varttate kalpo vārāhastannibodhata । prathamaṃ sāṃpratasteṣāṃ kalpo vai varttate ca yaḥ ।।
pūrṇe yugasahasre tu paripālyaṃ nareśvaraiḥ ।। āpo agre sarvagā āsannenasimanpṛthivītale । śāntavātaiḥ pralīne asminna prājñāyata kiñcana ।। ekārṇave tadā tasminnaṣṭe sthāvarajaṅgame ।
vibhurbhavati sa brahmā sahasrākṣaḥ sahasrapāt ।। sahasraśīrṣā puruṣo rukmavarṇo hyatīndriyaḥ । brahma nārāyaṇākhyastu suṣvāpa salile tadā ।। sattvodrekānniṣiddhastu śūnyaṃ lokamavaikṣata ।
imaṃ codāharantyatrar ślokaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ prati ।। āpo nārā iti proktā āpo vai narasūnavaḥ । ayana tasya tāḥproktāstena nārāyaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। tulya yugasahasrasya vasankālamupāsyataḥ ।
svarṇapatreprakurute brahmatvādarśakāraṇāt ।। brahma tu salile tasminnavāg bhūtvā tadā caran । niśāyāmiva khadyotaḥ prāpṛṭkāle tatastataḥ ।। tatastu salile tasmin vijñāyāntargate mahat ।
anumānādasaṃmūḍho bhūmeraddharaṇaṃ prati ।। oṅkārāṣṛtanuṃ tvanyāṃ kalpādiṣu yathā purā । tato mahātmā manasā divyarūpama cintayat ।। salile avaplutāṃ bhūmiṃ dṛṣṭvā sa samacintayat ।
kiṃ tu rūpamahaṃ kṛtvā salilāduddhare mahīm ।। jalakrīḍāsamucitaṃ vārāhaṃ rūpamasmarat । udṛśyaṃ sarvabhūtānāṃ vāṅmayaṃ brahmasaṃjñitam ।। daśayojanavistīrṇamāyataṃśatayojanam ।
nīlameghapratīkāśaṃ meghastanitaniḥsvanam ।। mahāparvatavarṣmāṇaṃ śvetatīkṣṇogradaṃṣṭriṇām । vidyudagnipratikāśamādityasamatejasam ।। pīnavṛttāyataskandhaṃ viṣṇuvikramagāmi ca ।
pīnonnatakaṭīdeśaṃ vṛṣalakṣaṇapūjitam ।। āsthāya rūpamatulaṃ vārāhamamitaṃ hariḥ । pṛthivyuddharaṇārthāya praviveśa rasātalam ।। dīkṣāsamāptīṣṭidaṃṣṭraḥkratudanto juhūsukhaḥ ।
agnijihvo darbharomā brahmaśīrṣo mahātapāḥ ।। vedaskandho havirgandhirhavyakavyādivegavān । prāgvaṃśakāyo dyutimān nānādīkṣābhiranvitaḥ ।। dakṣiṇā tdṛdayo yogī śraddhāsattvamayo vibhuḥ ।
upākarmaruciścaiva pravargyāvartabhūṣaṇaḥ ।। nānāchandogatipatho guhyopaniṣadāsanaḥ । māyāpatnīsahāyo vai giriśṛṅgamivocchrayaḥ ।। ahorātrekṣaṇādharo vedāṅgaśrutibhūṣaṇaḥ ।
ājyagandhaḥ sruvastuṇḍaḥ sāmaghoṣasvano mahān ।। satyadharmamayaḥ śrīmān karmavikramasatkṛtaḥ । prāyaścittanakho ghoraḥ paśujānurmahāmakhaḥ ।। udgātātro homaliṅgaḥ phalabījamahoṣadhīḥ ।
vādyantarātmasatrasya nāsmikāso maśoṇitaḥ ।। bhaktā yajñavarāhāntāścāpaḥ saṃprāviśatpunaḥ । agnisaṃchāditāṃ bhūmiṃ samāmicchanprajāpatim ।। upagamyā juhāvaitā madyaścādyasamanyasat ।
māmudrāśca samudreṣu nādeyāśca nadīṣu ca । pṛthak tāstu samīkṛtya pṛthivyāṃ so acinodgirīn ।। prāksarge dahyamānāstu tadā saṃvartakāgninā । denāgninā vilīnāste parvatā bhuvi sarvaśaḥ ।।
satyādekārṇave tasmin vāyunā yattu saṃhitāḥ । niṣiktā yatrayatrāsaṃstatratatrācalo abhavat ।। tatasteṣu prakīrṇeṣu lokodadhigirīṃstathā । viśvakarmā vibhajate kalpādiṣu punaḥ punaḥ ।।
sasamudrāmimāṃ pṛthvīṃ saptadvīpāṃ saparvatām । bhūrādyāṃścaturo lokānpunaḥpunarakalpayat ।। lākānprakalpayitvā ca prajāsarga sasarja ha । brahmā svayaṃbhūrbhagavām sisṛkṣurvividhāḥ prajāḥ ।।
sasarja sṛṣṭaṃ tadrūpaṃ kalpādiṣu yathā purā । tasyābhidhyāyataḥ sargaṃ tadā vai buddhipūrvakam ।। pradhānasamakāle ca prādurbhūtastamo mayaḥ । tamo moho mahāmohastāmisro hyandhasaṃjñitaḥ ।।
avidyā pañcaparvaiṣā prādurbhūtā mahātmanaḥ । pañcadhāvasthitaḥ sargo dhyāyata sābhimāninaḥ ।। sarvatastamasā caiva bījakuṃbhalatāvṛtāḥ । bahirantaścāprakāśastathāniḥsaṃjña eva ca ।।
yasmātteṣāṃ kṛtā buddhir duḥkhāni karaṇāni ca । tasmācca saṃvṛtātmāno nagā mukhyāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ।। mukhyasarge tadodbhūtaṃ dṛṣṭvā brahmātmasaṃbhavaḥ । apratī tamanāḥ sotha tadotpattimamanyata ।।
tasyābhidhyāyataścānyastiryaksroto abhyavartata । yasmāttiryagvivartteta tiryakasrotastataḥ smṛtaḥ ।। tamobahutvātte sarve hyajñānabahulāḥ smṛtāḥ । utpādyagrāhimaścaiva te ajñāne jñānamāninaḥ ।।
ahaṅkṛtā ahaṃmānā aṣṭāviṃśaddvidhātmikāḥ । ekādaśandriyavidhā navadhātmādayastathā ।। aṣṭau tu tārakādyāśca teṣāṃ śaktivadhāḥ smṛtāḥ । antaḥ prakāśāste sarve āvṛtāśca bahiḥ punaḥ ।।
tiryak srotasa ucyante vaśyātmānastrisaṃjñakāḥ ।। tiryak srotastu sṛṣṭvā vai dvitīyaṃ viśvamīśvaraḥ । abhiprāyamathodbhūtaṃ dṛṣṭvā sargaṃ tathāvidham ।। tasyābhidhyāyato yontyaḥ sāttvikaḥ samajāyata ।
ūrddhasrotastṛtīyastu tadvai corddhaṃ vyavasthitam ।। yasmādūrddhaṃ nyavartanta tadūrddhasrotasaṃjñakam । tāḥ sukhaṃ prītibahulā bahirantaśca vāvṛtāḥ ।। prakāśā bahirantaśca ūrddhasrotaḥprajāḥ smṛtāḥ ।
navadhātādayaste vai tuṣṭātmāno budhāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। ūrddhasrota stutīyo yaḥ smṛtaḥ sarvaḥ sadaivikaḥ । ūrddhasrotaḥsu sṛṣṭeṣu deveṣu sa tadā prabhuḥ ।। prītimānabhavadbrahmā tato anyaṃ nābhimanyata ।
sargamanyaṃ simṛkṣustaṃ sādhakaṃ punarīśvaraḥ ।। tasyābhidhyāyataḥ sargaṃ satyābhidhyāyinastadā । prādurbabhau bhautasargaḥ sorvāk srotastu sādhakaḥ ।। yasmāttervākpravartante tatorvākūsrotasastu te ।
te ca prakāśabahulāstamaspṛṣṭarajodhikāḥ ।। tasmātte duḥkhabahulā bhūyobhūyaśca kārimaḥ । prakāśā bahirantaśca manuṣyāḥ sādhakāśca te ।। lakṣaṇairnārakādyaistairaṣṭadhā ca vyavasthitāḥ ।
siddhātmāno manuṣyāste gandharvaiḥ saha dharmiṇaḥ ।। pañcamo anugrahaḥ sargaścaturddhā sa vyavasthitaḥ । viparyayeṇa śaktyā ca siddha mukhyāstathaiva ca ।। nivṛttā vartamānāśca prajāyante punaḥpunaḥ ।
bhūtādikānāṃ sattvānāṃ ṣaṣṭhaḥ sargaḥ sa ucyate ।। svādanāścāpyaśīlāśca jñeyā bhūtādikāśca te । prathamo mahataḥ sargo vijñeyo brahmaṇastu saḥ ।। tanmātrāṇāṃ dvitīyastu bhūta sargaḥ sa ucyate ।
vaikārikastṛtīyastu caidriyaḥ sarga ucyate ।। ityeta prākṛtāḥ sargā utpannā buddhipūrvakāḥ । mukhyasargaśca turthastu mukhyā vai sthāvarāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। tiryaksrotaḥsasargastu tairyagyonyastu pañcamaḥ ।
tathorddhasrotasāṃ sargaḥ ṣaṣṭho devata ucyate ।। tatrorddhasrotasāṃ sargaḥ saptamaḥ sa tu mānuṣaḥ । aṣṭamonugrahaḥ sargaḥ sāttvikastāmasaśca saḥ ।। pañcaite vaikṛtāḥ sargāḥ prākṛtādyāstrayaḥ smṛtāḥ ।
prākṛto vaikṛtaścaiva kaumāro navamaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। prakṛtā buddhipūrvāstu trayaḥ sargāstu vaikṛtāḥ । duddhiburvāḥ pravarteyustadvargā brāhmaṇāstu vai ।। vistarācca yathā sarve kīrtyamānaṃ nibodhata ।
caturddhā ca sthitasso api sarvabhūteṣu kṛtsnaśaḥ ।। viparyayoṇa śattyā ca buddhyā siddhyā tathaiva ca । sthāvareṣu viparyāsastiryagyoniṣu śaktitaḥ ।। siddhātmāno manuṣyāstu puṣṭirdeveṣu kṛtsnaśaḥ ।
atho sasarja vai brahmā mānasānātmanaḥ samān ।। vaivartyena tu jñānena nivṛttāste mahau jasaḥ । saṃbuddhya caiva nāmātho apavṛttāstrayastu te ।। asṛṣṭvaiva prajāsargaṃpratisargaṃ tatastataḥ ।
brahmā teṣu vyarakteṣu tato anyānsā dhakānsṛjan ।। sthānābhimānino devāḥ punarbrahmānuśāsanam । abhūtasṛṣṭyavasthā ce sthāninastānnibodha me ।। āpo agniḥ pṛthivī vāyurantarikṣo divaṃ tathā ।
svargo diśaḥ samudrāśca nadyaścaiva vanaspatīn ।। auṣadhīnāṃ tathātmāno hyātmano vṛkṣavīrudhām । latāḥ kāṣṭhāḥ kalāścaiva muhūrtāḥ saṃdhirātryahāḥ ।। arddhamāsāśca māsāśca ayanābdayugāni ca ।
sthāne srotaḥsvabhīmānāḥ sthānākhyāścaiva te smṛtāḥ ।। sthānātmanaḥ sa sṛṣṭvā tu tato anyānsa tadāsṛjat । devāṃścaiva pitṝṃścaiva yaurimā varddhitāḥ prajāḥ ।। bhṛgvaṅgirā marīciśca pulastyaḥ pulahaḥ kratuḥ ।
dakṣo atriśca vasiṣṭhaśca sāsṛjannava mānasān ।। nava brahmāṇa ityete purāṇe niścayaṃ gatāḥ । brahmā yathātmakānāṃ tu sarveṣāṃ brahmayoginām ।। tato asṛjatpunarbrahmā rudraṃ roṣatmasaṃbhavam ।
saṃkalpaṃ caiva dharma ca sarveṣāmeva parvatau ।। so asṛjadvyavasāyaṃ tu brahmā bhūtaṃ sukhātmakam । saṃkalpāccaiva saṃkalpo jajñe so avyaktayoninaḥ ।। prāṇāddakṣo asṛjadvācaṃ cakṣurbhyāṃ ca marīcinam ।
bhṛguśca hṛdayājjajñe ṛṣiḥ salilayoninaḥ ।। śirasaścāṅgirāścaiva śrotrādatristathaiva ca । pulastyaśca tathodānādvyānāttu pulahastathā ।। samānato vasiṣṭhaśca hyapānānnirmame kratum ।
ityete brahmaṇaḥ śreṣṭhāḥ putrā vai dvādaśa smṛtāḥ ।। dharmādayaḥ prathamajā vijñeyā brahmamaḥ smṛtāḥ । bhṛgvādayastu ye sṛṣṭā na ca te brahmavādinaḥ ।। gṛhamedhipurāṇāste vijñeyā brahmaṇaḥ sutāḥ ।
dvādaśaite prasūyante saha rūdreṇa ca dvijāḥ ।। kratuḥ sanatkumāraśca dvāvetāvūrddharetasau । pūrvotpattau purā hyetau sarveṣāmapi pūrvajau ।। vyatītau saptame kalpe purāṇau lokasādhakau ।
virajete atra vai loke tejasākṣipya cātmanaḥ ।। tāpubhau yogadharmāṇāvāropyātmānamātmanā । prajādharmaṃ ca kāmaṃ ca vartayete mahaujasau ।। yathotpannastathaiveha kumāra iti cocyate ।
tataḥ sanatkumāreti nāma tasya pratiṣṭhitam ।। teṣāṃ dvādaśa te vaṃśā divyā devagāṇānvitāḥ । kriyāvantaḥ prajāvanto maharṣibhiralaṅkṛtāḥ ।। prāṇajāṃstu sa dṛṣṭvā vai brahmā dvādaśa sāttvikān ।
tato asurānpitṝndevānmanuṣyāṃścāsṛjatprabhuḥ ।। mukhāddevānajanayat pitṝṃścaivātha vakṣasaḥ । prajananānmanuṣyānvai jaghanānnirmame asurān ।। naktaṃ sṛjanpunarbrahmā jyotsnāyā mānuṣātmanaḥ ।
sudhāyāśca pitṝṃścaiva devadevaḥ sasarjaha ।। mukhyāmukhyān mṛjandevānasurāṃśca tataḥ punaḥ । sanasaśca manuṣyāṃśca pitṛvanmahataḥ pitṝn ।। vidyuto aśanimeghāṃśca lohitendradhanūṃṣi ca ।
ṛco yajūṃṣi sāmāni nirmame yajñasiddhaye ।। uccāvacāni bhūtāni mahasastasya jajñire । brahmaṇastu prajāsargaṃ devārṣipitṛmānavam ।। punaḥ sṛjati bhūtāni carāṇi sthāvarāṇi ca ।
yakṣānpiśācān gandharvānsarvaśo apsarasastathā ।। narakinnararakṣāṃsi vayaḥ paśumṛgoragān । avyayaṃ vā vyayañcaiva dvayaṃ sthāvarajaṅgamam ।। teṣāṃ te yānti karmāṇi prāk sṛṣṭāni svayaṃbhuvā ।
tānyeva pratipadyante sṛjyamānāḥ punaḥ punaḥ ।। hiṃsrāhiṃsre mṛdukrūre dharmādharmauṃ kṛtākṛte । teṣāmeva pṛthak sūtamavibhaktaṃ trayaṃ viduḥ ।। etadevaṃ ca naivaṃ ca na cobhe nānubhe tathā ।
karma svaviṣayaṃ prāhuḥ sattvasthāḥ samadarśinaḥ ।। nāmātmapañcabhūtānāṃ kṛtānāṃ ca prapañcatām । divaśabdena pañcaite nirmame samaheśvaraḥ ।। ārṣāṇi caiva nāmāni yāśca deveṣu sṛṣṭayaḥ ।
śarvaryāṃ na prasūyante punastebhyodadhatprabhuḥ ।। ityevaṃ kāraṇādbhūto lokasargaḥ svayaṃbhuvaḥ । mahadādyā viśeṣāntā vikārāḥ prākṛtāḥ svayam ।। candrasūryaprabho loko grahanakṣatramaṇḍitaḥ ।
nadībhiśca samudraiśca parvataiśca sahasraśaḥ ।। puraiśca vividhai ramyaiḥ sphītairjanapadaistathā । asmin brahmavane avyakto brahmā carati sarvavit ।। avyaktabījaprabhavastasyaivānugrahe sthitaḥ ।
buddhiskandhamayaścaiva indriyāntarakoṭaraḥ ।। mahābhūtaprakāśaśca viśeṣaiḥ patravāṃstu saḥ । dharmādharmasupuṣpastu sukhaduḥkhaphalodayaḥ ।। ājīvaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ brahmavṛkṣaḥ sanātanaḥ ।
etadbrahmavanaṃ caiva brahmavṛkṣasya tasya tat ।। avyaktaṃ kāraṇaṃ yatra nityaṃ sadasadātmakam । pradhānaṃ prakṛtiṃmāyāṃ caivāhustattvacintakāḥ ।। ityeṣo anugrahaḥmargo brahmanaimittikaḥ smṛtaḥ ।
abuddhipūrvakāḥ sargā brahmaṇaḥ prākṛtāstrayaḥ ।। sukhyādayastu ṣaṭ sargā vaikṛtā buddhipūrvakāḥ । vaikalpātsaṃpravartante brahmaṇastebhimanyavaḥ ।। ityete prākṛtāścaiva vaikṛtāśca nava smṛtāḥ ।
sargāḥ parasparotpannāḥ kāraṇaṃ tu budhaiḥ smṛtam ।। mūrddhānaṃ vai yasya vedā vadanti viyannābhiścandrasūryauṃ ca netre । diśaḥ śrotre viddhi pādau kṣitiṃ ca so acintyātmā sarvabhūtapraṇetā ।। vaktrādyasya brāhmaṇāḥ saṃprasūtā vakṣasaścaiva kṣatriyāḥ pūrvabhāge ।
vaiśyā ūrubhyāṃ yasya padbhyāṃ ca śūdrāḥsarvevarṇā gātrataḥ saṃprasūtāḥ ।। nārāyaṇātparovyaktādaṇḍamavyaktasaṃjñitam । aṇḍajastu svayaṃ brahmā lokāstena kṛtāḥ svayam ।। tatra kalpān daśasthitvā satyaṃ gacchanti te punaḥ ।
te lokā brahmalokaṃ vai aparāvartinīṃ gatim ।। ādhipatyaṃ vinā te vai aiśvaryeṇa tu tatsamāḥ । bhavanti brahmaṇā tulyā rūpeṇa viṣayeṇa ca ।। tatra te hyavatiṣṭhante prītiyuktāḥ svasaṃyutāḥ ।
avaśyaṃbhāvinārthena prākṛtaṃ tanute svayam ।। nānātvanābhisaṃbadhyāstadā tatkālabhāvitāḥ । svapato abuddhipūrva hi bodho bhavati vai yathā ।। tatkālabhāvite teṣāṃ tathā jñānaṃ pravarttate ।
pratyāhāraistu bhedānāṃ teṣāṃ hi na tu śuṣmiṇām ।। taiśva sārdhaṃ pravartante kāryāṇi kāraṇāni ca । nānātvadarśināṃ teṣāṃ brahmalokanivāsinām ।। vinivṛttavikārāṇāṃ svena dharmeṇa tiṣṭhatām ।
tulyalakṣaṇa siddhāstu śubhātmāno nirañjanāḥ ।। prākṛte karaṇopetāḥ svātmanyeva vyavasthitāḥ । prasthāpayitvā cātmānaṃ prakṛtistveṣa tattavataḥ ।। puruṣānyabahutvena pratītā na pravartate ।
pravartate punaḥ sargasteṣāṃ sākāraṇātmanām ।। saṃyogaḥ prakṛtirjñeyā yaktānāṃ tattvadarśinām । tatropavargiṇī teṣāmapunarbhāragāminām ।। abhāvataḥ punaḥ satyaṃ śāntānāmarciṣāmiva ।
tatarateṣu gateṣūrddhaṃ trailokyāttu mudātmasu ।। te sārddhaṃ cairmaharllokastadānāsāditastu vai । tacchiṣyā ye ha tiṣṭhanti kalpadāha upasthite ।। gandharvādyāḥ piśācāścamānuṣā brahmaṇādayaḥ ।
paśavaḥ pakṣiṇaścaiva sthāvarāḥ sasarīsṛpāḥ ।। tiṣṭhatsuteṣu tatkālaṃ pṛthivītalavasiṣu । sahasraṃyattu raśmīnāṃ sūryasyeha vinaśyati ।। te sapta raśmayo bhūtvā ekaiko jāyate raviḥ ।
krameṇa śatamānāste trīṃllokānpradahantyuta ।। jaṅgamānsthāvarāṃścaiva nadīḥ sarvāśca parvatān । śuṣke pūrvamanāvṛṣṭyā caistaiśacaiva pratāpitāḥ ।। tadā te vivaśāḥ sarve nirdagdhāḥ sūryaraśmibhiḥ ।
jaṅgamāḥ sthāvarāścaiva dharmādharmādikāstu vai ।। dagdhadehāstadā te tu dhūtapāpā yugātyaye । khyātātapā vinirmuktāḥ śubhayā cātibandhayā ।। tataste hyupapadyante tulyarūpairjanairjanāḥ ।
uṣitvā rajanīṃ te ca brahmaṇo avyaktajanmanaḥ ।। punaḥ sarge bhavantīha mānasyo brahmaṇaḥ prajāḥ । tatasteṣu prapanneṣu janaistrailokyavāsiṣu ।। nirdagdheṣu ca lokeṣu tadā sūryaistu saptabhiḥ ।
vṛṣṭyā kṣitau plāvitāyāṃ vijaneṣvarṇaveṣu vā ।। samudrāścaiva meghāśca āpaścaivātha pārthivāḥ । śaramāṇā vrajantyeva salilākhyāstathācalāḥ ।। āgatāgatikaṃ caiva yadā tu salilaṃ bahu ।
saṃchādyemāṃ sthitāṃ bhūmimarṇavākhyaṃ tadābhavata ।। ābhāti yasmāccābhāsādbhāśabdaḥ kāntidīptiṣu । sa sarvaḥ samanuprāptā māsāṃ bhābhyo vibhāvyate ।। tadantastanute yasmātsarvāṃ pṛthvīṃ samatataḥ ।
dhātustanoti vistāraṃ tatopatanavaḥ smṛtāḥ ।। śāra ityeva śīrṇe tu nānārtho dhātu rucyate । ekārṇave bhavantyāpo na śīrṇāstena tā narāḥ ।। tasmin yugasahasrānte saṃsthite brahmaṇo ahani ।
tāvatkālaṃ rajanyāṃ ca vartantyāṃ salilātmanaḥ ।। tataste salile tasmin naṣṭāgnau pṛthivītale । praśāntavāte andhakāre nirāloke samantataḥ ।। yenaivādhiṣṭhitaṃ hīdaṃ brahmaṇaḥ puruṣaḥ prabhuḥ ।
vibhāgamasya lokasya prakartuṃ punaraicchata ।। śāra ityeva śīrṇe tu nānārtho dhātu rucyate । ekarṇave tatastasminnaṣṭe sthāvara jaṅgame । tadā bhavati sa brahmā sahasrākṣaḥ sahasrapāt ।।
sahasraśīrṣā puruṣo rukmavarṇo hyatīndriyaḥ । brahmā nārāyaṇā khyastu suṣvāpa salile tadā ।। sattvodrekātprabuddhastu sa śūnyaṃ lokamaikṣata । anenādyena pādena purāṇaṃ parikīrtitam ।।
ityevaṃ prathamaṃ pādaṃ prakṛtyarthaṃ prakīrtitam । śrutvā tu saṃhṛṣṭamanāḥ kāpeyaḥ saṃśayāyati ।। ārādhya vacasā sūtaṃ tasyārtha tvaparāṃ kathām । atha prabṛti kalpajñaḥ pratisaṃdhiḥ pracakṣate ।।
samatītasya kalpasya vartamānasya cānayoḥ । kalpayorantaraṃ yatra pratisaṃdhiśca yastayoḥ । etadveditumicchāmi yathāvatkuśalo hyasi ।। kāpeyenaivamuktastu sūtaḥ pravadatāṃ varaḥ ।
trailokyasyodbhavaṃ kṛtsnamākhyātumupacakrame ।। atra vai varṇayiṣyāmi yāthātathyena suvratāḥ । kalpaṃ bhūtaṃ bhaviṣyaṃ ca pratisaṃdhiśca yastayoḥ ।। manvantarāṇi kalpeṣu yāni yāni ca suvratāḥ ।
yaścāyaṃ vartate kalpo vārāhaḥ sāṃprataḥ śubhaḥ ।। asmātkalpāttu yaḥ pūrvaḥ kalpo atītaḥ sanātanaḥ । tasya cāsya ca kalpasya madhyāvasthāṃ nibodhata ।। pratyāgate pūrvakalpe pratisaṃdhiṃ vinānaghāḥ ।
anyaḥ pravarttate kalpo janalokādayaḥ punaḥ ।। vyucchinnapratisaṃdhistu kalpātkalpaḥ parasparam । vyucchidyante prajāḥ sarvāḥ kalpānte sarvaśastadā ।। tasmātkalpāttu kalpasya pratisaṃdhirna vidyate ।
manvantare yugākhyānāmavicchinnāstu saṃdhayaḥ ।। parasparāt pravartante manvantarayugaiḥ saha । uktā ye prakriyārthena pūrvakalpāḥ samāsataḥ ।। teṣāṃ parārddhakalpānāṃ pūrve yasmāttu yaḥ paraḥ ।
āsītkalpe vyatīte vai pararddhātparamastu yaḥ ।। kalpāstvanye bhaviṣyā ye hyaparārddhaguṇīkṛtāḥ । prathamaḥ sāṃpratasteṣāṃ kalpoṃ yo vartate dvijāḥ ।। asminpūrve parārddhe tu dvitīyaḥ para ucyate ।
eṣa saṃsthitakālastu pratyāhārastataḥ smṛtaḥ ।। asmātkalpāttataḥ pūrvaṃ kalpo atītaḥ purātanaḥ । caturyugasahasrati saha manvantaraiḥ purā ।। kṣīṇe kalpe tatastasmin dāhakāla upasthite ।
tasminkāle tadā devā āsanvaimānikāstu ye ।। nakṣatragrahatārāśca candrasūryādayastu te । aṣṭāviṃśatirevaitāḥ koṭyastu sukṛtātma nām ।। manvantare yathaikasmin caturddaśasu vai tathā ।
trīṇi koṭiśatānyāsan koṭyo dvinavatistathā ।। athādhikāsapta tiśca sahasrāṇāṃ purā smṛtā । ekaikasmiṃstu kalpe vai devā vaimānikāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। atha manvantareṣvāsaṃścaturdaśasu khe divi ।
devāśca pitaraścaiva ṛṣayo amṛtapāstathā ।। teṣāmanucarāścaiva patnyaḥ putrāstathaiva ca । varṇāśramātiriktāśca tasminkāle tu khe surāḥ ।। taistaiḥ sāyujyagaiḥ sārddha prāpte vastumaye tadā ।
tulyaniṣṭhābhavansarve prāpte hyābhūtasaṃplave ।। tataste avaśyabhāvitvādū buddhyāḥ paryā yamātmanaḥ । trailokyavāsino devā iha tānābhimāninaḥ ।। sthitikāle tadā pūrṇe āsanne paścimottare ।
kalpāvasānikā devāsta sminaprāpte hyupaplave ।। tadotsukā viṣādeṃna tyaktasthānāni bhāgaśaḥ । maharlokāya saṃvignāstataste dadhire manaḥ ।। te yuktā nupapadyante mahatīṃ ca śarīrike ।
viśuddhibahulāḥ sarve mānasīṃ siddhimāsthitāḥ ।। taiḥ kalpavāsibhiḥ sārddhaṃ mahānāsāditastadā । brāhmaṇaiḥ kṣatriyairvaiśyaistadbhavaiścāparairjanaiḥ ।। gatvā tu te mahārlokaṃ devasaṃghāścaturddaśa ।
stataste janalokāya sodvegā dadhire manaḥ ।। etena kramayogena yayuste kalpavāsinaḥ । evaṃ devayugānāṃ tu sahasrāṇi parasparam ।। viśuddhibahulāḥ sarve mānasīṃ siddhimāsthitāḥ ।
taiḥ kalpavāsibhiḥ sārddhaṃ jana āsāditastu vai ।। tatra kalpāndaśa sthitvā satyaṃ gacchanti vai punaḥ । gatvā te brahmalokaṃ vai aparāvarttinīṃ gatim ।। ādhipatyaṃ vimāne vai aiśvaryeṇa tu tatsamāḥ ।
bhavanti brahmaṇā tulyā rūpeṇa viṣayeṇa ca ।। tatra te hyavatiṣṭhanta prītiyuktāśca saṃyamān । ānandaṃ brahmaṇaḥ prāpya mucyante brahmaṇā saha ।। avaśyabhāvinārthena prākṛtenaiva te svayam ।
mānārcanābhiḥ saṃbaddhāstadā tatkālabhāvitāḥ ।। svapato buddhipūrvaṃ tu bodho bhavati vai yathā । tathātu bhāvite sevāṃ tathānandaḥ pravartate ।। pratyāhāraistu bhodānāṃ yeṣāṃ bhinnāni śuṣmiṇām ।
taiḥ sārddha varddhate teṣāṃ kāryāṇi karaṇāni ca ।। nānā tvadarśināṃ teṣāṃ brahmalokanivāsinām । vinivṛttādhikāraṇāṃ svena dharmeṇa tiṣṭhatām ।। te tulyalakṣaṇāḥ siddhāḥ śuddhātmāno nirañjanāḥ ।
prākṛte karaṇopetāḥ svātmanyeva vyavasthitāḥ ।। prakhyāpayitvā cātmānaṃ prakṛtistveṣa tattvataḥ । puruṣānyabahutvena pratītā tatpravartate ।। pravartite punaḥ sarge teṣāṃ sākāraṇātmanām ।
saṃyoge prakṛtirjñaiyā muktānāṃ tattvadarśinām ।। tatropavargiṇāṃ teṣāṃ na punarmārgagāminām । abhāvaḥ punarutpannaḥ śāntānāmarciṣāmiva ।। tatasteṣu gateṣūrdhvaṃ trailokyeṣu mahātmasu ।
etaiḥ sārdhaṃ maharlokastadānāsāditastu vai ।। tacchiṣyā vai bhaviṣyanti kalpadāha upasthite । gandharvādyāḥ piśācāśca mānuṣā brāhmaṇādayaḥ ।। paśavaḥ pakṣiṇascaiva sthāvarāśca sarīsṛpāḥ ।
tiṣṭhatsu teṣu tatkālaṃ pṛthivītalavāsiṣu ।। sahasraṃ yattu raśmīnāṃ svayameva vibhāvyate । tatsaptaraśmayo bhūtvā ekaiko jāyate raviḥ ।। krameṇottiṣṭamānāste trīṃllokānpradahantyuta ।
jaṅgamāḥ sthāvarāścaivanadyaḥ sarve ca parvatāḥ ।। śuṣkāḥ pūrvamanāvṛṣṭyā sūryyaiste ca pradhūpitāḥ । tadā tu vivaśāḥ sarve nirdagdhāḥ sūryaraśmi bhiḥ ।। jaṅgamāḥ sthāvarāścaiva dharmādharmātmakāstu vai ।
dagdhadehāstadā te tu dhūtapāpāyugāntare ।। khyātātapā vinirmuktāḥ śubhaya cātibandhayā । tataste hyupapadyante tulyarūpairjanairjanāḥ ।। uṣitvā rajanīṃ tatra brahmaṇo avyaktajanmanaḥ ।
punaḥ sarge bhavantīha mānasā brahmaṇaḥ sutāḥ ।। tatasteṣūpapanneṣu janaistrailokyavāsiṣu । nirdagdheṣu ca lokeṣu tadā sūryaistu saptabhiḥ ।। vṛṣṭyā kṣitau plāvitāyāṃ vijaneṣvarṇaveṣu ca ।
sāmudrāścaiva meghāśca āpaḥ sarvāśca pārthivāḥ ।। śaramāṇā vrajantyeva salilākhyāstathā nugāḥ । āgatāgatikaṃ caiva yadā tatsalilaṃ bahu ।। saṃchādyemāṃ sthitāṃ bhamimarṇavākhyaṃ tadābhavat ।
ābhāti yasmāt svābhāso bhāśabdo vyāptidīptiṣu ।। sarvataḥ samanuprāptyā tāsāṃ cāmbho vibhāvyate । tadantastanute yasmātsarvāṃ pṛthvīṃ samanta tataḥ ।। dhātustanoti vistāre nacaitāstanavaḥ smṛtāḥ ।
śara ityeṣa śīrṇe tu nānārtho dhāturucyate ।। ekārṇave bhavatyāpo na śīghrāstena te narāḥ । tasmin yugasahasrānte saṃsthite brahmaṇo ahani ।। tāvatkāle rajanyāṃ ca vartantyāṃ salilātmanā ।
tatastu salile tāsminnaṣṭāgnau pṛthavītale ।। praśāntavāte andhakāre nirāloke samantataḥ । etenādhiṣṭhitaṃ hīdaṃ brahmā sa puruṣaḥ prabhuḥ ।। vibhāgamasya lokasya prakartuṃ punaraicchata ।
ekārṇave tadā tasminnaṣṭe sthāvarajaṅgame ।। tadā bhavati sa brahmā sahasrākṣaḥ sahasrapāt । sahasraśīrṣā puruṣo rukmavarṇo jitendriyaḥ । imaṃ codāharantyatrar ślokaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ prati ।।
āpo nārāstattanava ityarthā nanuśuśruma । āpūryamāṇāstatrāste tena nārāyaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। sahasraśīrṣā sumanāḥ sahasrapāt sahasracakṣurvadanaḥ sahasrakṛt । sahasrabāhuḥ prathamaḥ prajāpatistrayīmayo ayaṃ puruṣo nirucyate ।।
ādityavarṇo bhuvanasya goptā eko hyamūrtaḥ prathamastvaso virāṭ । hiraṇya garbhaḥ puruṣo mahātmā saṃpadyate vai manasaḥ parastāt ।। kalpādau rajasodrikto brahmā bhūstvāsṛjatprabhuḥ । kalpānte tamasodriktaḥ kālo bhūtvāgrasatpunaḥ ।।
sa vai nārāyaṇo bhūtvā sattvodrikto jalāśaye । tridhā vibhajya cātmānaṃ trailokye saṃpravarttate ।। sṛjati grasate caiva vīkṣyate ca tribhiḥ svayam । ekārṇave tadā tasminnaṣṭe sthāvarajaṅgame ।।
caturyugasahasrānte sarvataḥ sa jalāvṛte । brahmāṃ nārāyaṇākhyastu sa cakāśe bhave svayam ।। caturvidhāḥ prajāḥ sarvā brahmaśaktyā tamovṛtāḥ । paśyanti taṃ maharloke kālaṃ suptaṃ maharṣayaḥ ।।
bhṛgvādayo yathoddiṣṭāstasmin kāle maharṣayaḥ । satyādayastathā tvaṣṭau kalpe līne maharṣayaḥ । tadā vivartyamānaistairmahatparigataṃ parām ।। gatyarthādṛṣaterdhātornāmaniṣpattirucyate ।
yasmādṛṣatisattvena mahattasmānmaharṣayaḥ ।। maharlokasthitairdṛṣṭaḥ kālaḥ suptastadā ca taiḥ । sattvādyāḥ sapta ye tvāsankalpe atīte maharṣayaḥ ।। evaṃ brahmā tāsu tāsu rajanīṣu sahasraśaḥ ।
dṛṣṭavantastadānītāḥ kālaṃ suptaṃ maharṣayaḥ ।। kalpasyādau subahulā yasmātsaṃsthāścaturddaśa । kalpayā māsa vai brahmā tasmātkalpo nirucyate ।। sa sraṣṭā sarvabhūtānāṃ kalpādiṣu punaḥ punaḥ ।
vyaktāvyako mahādevastasya sarvamidaṃ jagat ।। ityeṣa pratisaṃbandhaḥ kīrtitaḥ kalpayordvayoḥ । sāṃprataṃ hi tayormadhye prāgavasthā babhūva ha ।। kīrtitastu samāsena pūrvakalpe yathātatham ।
sāṃprataṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi kalpametaṃ nibodhata ।। tulyaṃ yugasahasraṃ vai naiśaṃ kālamupāsya saḥ । śarvaryaṃte prakurute brahmā tūtsargakāraṇāt ।। brahmā tu salile tasmin vāyurbhūtvā tadācarat ।
andhakārārṇave tasminnaṣṭe sthāvarajaṃgame ।। jalena samanuplāvya sarvataḥ pṛthivītale । pravibhāgena bhūteṣu satyamātre sthiteṣu vā ।। niśayāmiva khadyotaḥ prāvṛṭ kāle tatastadā ।
tadā kāmena tarasāmanyāmānaḥsvayaṃ dhiyā ।। sopyupāyaṃ pratiṣṭhāyāṃ mārgamāṇastadā bhuvam । tatastu salile tasmin jñātvā tvantargato mahīm ।। andhamanyatamaṃ buddhā bhūmeruddharaṇakṣamaḥ ।
cakāra taṃ tu devo atha pūrvakalpādiṣu smṛtaḥ ।। satyaṃ rūpaṃ varāhasya kṛtvābho anupraviśya ca । adbhiḥ saṃchāditāmicchan pṛthivīṃ sa prajāpatiḥ ।। uddhṛtyorvīmatha nyastā sāpatyāṃtāmatinyasat ।
sāmudrāśca samudreṣu nādeyāśca nadīṣu ca ।। pṛthaktāstu samīkṛtya pṛthivyāṃ so acinodgirīn । prāksarge dahyamāne tu purā saṃvarta kāgninā ।। tenāgninā vilīnāste parvatā bhuvi sarvaśaḥ ।
śailyādekārṇave tasminvāyunā ye tu saṃhitāḥ ।। niṣiktā yatra yatrāsaṃstatratatrācalo abhavat । skandhācalatvādacalāḥ parvabhiḥ parvatāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। girayo hi nigīrṇatvādayanāttu śiloccayāḥ ।
tata stāvāsamuddhṛtya kṣitimaṃtarjalātprabhuḥ ।। saptasapta tu varṣāṇi tasyā dvīpeṣu saptasu । viṣamāṇi samīkṛtya śilābhirabhito girīn ।। dvīpeṣu teṣu varṣāṇi catvāriṃśattathaiva tu ।
tāvaṃtaḥ parvatāścaiva varṣāṃte samavasthitāḥ ।। svargādau kāṃtiviṣṭāste svabhāvenaiva nānyathā । saptadvīpā samudrāśca anyonyasyānumaṃḍalam ।। sanniviṣṭāḥ svabhāvena samāvṛtya parasparam ।
bhūrādyāścaturo lokāścaṃdrādityau grahaiḥ saha ।। pūrvavannirmame brahmā sthāvarāṇīha sarvaśaḥ । kalpasya cāsya brahmā cāsṛjadyaḥ sthāninaḥ surān ।। āpogniṃ pṛthivīṃ vāyumaṃtarikṣaṃ divaṃ tathā ।
svargaṃ diśaḥ samudrāṃśca nadīḥ sarvāṃstu parvatān ।। oṣadhīnāmātmanaśca ātmano vṛkṣavīrudhām । lavakāṣṭhāḥ kalāścaiva muhurttānsaṃdhirātryahān ।। arddhamāsāṃśca māsāṃśca ayanābdān yugāni ca ।
sthānābhimāninaścaiva sthānānica pṛthakpṛthak ।। sthānātmanastu sṛṣṭvā ca yugāvasthā vinirmame । kṛtaṃ tretā dvāparaṃ ca tiṣyaṃ caiva tathā yugam ।। kalpasyādau kṛtayuge prathamaṃ so asṛjatprajāḥ ।
prāguktāśca mayā tubhyaṃ pūrvve kalpe prajāstu tāḥ ।। tasminsaṃvarta māne tu kalpe dagdhāstadagninā । aprāptāyāstapolokaṃ pṛthivyāṃ yāḥ samāsata ।। āvartante punaḥ sarge vīkṣārthaṃ tā bhavanti hi ।
vīkṣyārthaṃ tāḥ sthitāstatra punaḥ sargasya kāraṇāt ।। tatastāḥ sṛjyamānāstu santānārthaṃ bhavanti hi । dharmmārtha kāmamokṣāṇāmiha tāḥ sādhitāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। devāśca pitaraścaiva kramaśo mānavāstathā ।
tataste tapasā yuktāḥ sthānānyāpūrayanpurā ।। brāhmaṇo manavaste vai siddhātmāno bhavanti hi । āsaṃgadveṣayuktena karmaṇā te divaṃ gatāḥ ।। āvartamānāste dehe saṃbhavanti yuge yuge ।
svakarmmaphalaśeṣeṇa khyātāścaiva tadātmakāḥ ।। saṃbhavanti jane lokāḥ kalpāgamanibandhanāḥ । apsu yaḥ kāraṇaṃ teṣāṃ bodhayankarmmaṇā tu saḥ ।। karmmabhistaistu jāyante janalokācchubhāśubhaiḥ ।
gṛhṇanti te śarīrāṇi nānārūpāṇi yoniṣu ।। devādyāḥ sthāvarāṃtāstu āpadyante parasparam । teṣāṃ medhyāni karmmāṇi prāyaśaḥ pratipedire ।। tasmādyannāṃmarūpāṇi tānyeva pratipedire ।
punaḥ punaste kalpeṣu jāyante nāmarūpeṇaḥ ।। tataḥ sargo hyupasṛṣṭiṃ sisṛkṣorbrahmaṇastu vai । tāḥ prajā dhyāyatastasya satyābhidhyāyinastadā ।। mithunānāṃ sahasraṃ tu mukhātsamabhavatkila ।
janāste hyupapadyante sattvodriktāḥ sutejasaḥ ।। cakṣuṣo anyatsahasraṃ tu mithunānāṃ sasarjja ha । te sarve rajasodriktāḥ śuṣmiṇaścāpyamarṣiṇaḥ ।। sahasramanyadasṛjad bāhūnāmasatāṃ punaḥ ।
rajastamobhyāsuddhiktā gṛhaśīlāstataḥ smṛtāḥ ।। āyuṣoṃ'te prasūyaṃte mithunānyeva vāsakṛt । kūṭakākūṭakāścaiva utpadyaṃte mumūrṣuṇām ।। kutaḥ kulamathotpādya tāḥ śarīrāṇi tatyajuḥ ।
tataḥ prabhṛti kalpe asminmaithunānāṃ ca saṃbhavaḥ ।। dhyānena manasā tāsāṃ prajānāṃ jāyate kṛte । śabdādiviṣayaḥ śuddhaḥ pratyekaṃ pañcalakṣaṇam ।। ityevaṃ mānasairbhāvaiḥ preṣṭhaṃ tiṣṭhaṃti cāprajāḥ ।
tathānvayāstu saṃbhūtā yairidaṃ pūritaṃ jagat ।। saritsaraḥsamudrāṃśca sevaṃte parvatānapi । tadā tā hyalpasaṃtoṣāyuddhe tasmiṃścaraṃti vai ।। pṛthvī rasavatī nāma āhāraṃ vyāharaṃti ca ।
tāḥ prajāḥ kāmacāriṇyo mānasīṃ siddhimicchataḥ ।। tulyamāyuḥ sukhaṃ rūpaṃ tāsāmāsītkṛte yuge । dharmādharmauṃ tadā na staḥ kalpādau prathame yuge ।। svenasvenādhi kāreṇa jajñire tu yugeyuge ।
catvāri tu sahasrāṇi varṣāṇāṃ divyasaṃkhyayā ।। ādau kṛtayugaṃ prāhuḥ saṃdhyāṃśau ca catuḥśatau । tataḥ sahasraśastāstu prajāsu prathitāsviha ।। na tāsāṃ pratighāto asti na dvaṃdvaṃ nāpi ca kramaḥ ।
parvatodadhivāsinyo hyaniketāśrayāstu tāḥ ।। viśokāḥ sattvabahulā ekāṃtasukhinaḥ prajāḥ । tāśśaśvat kāmacariṇyo nityaṃ muditamānasāḥ ।। paśavaḥ pakṣiṇaścaiva na tadāsansarīsṛpāḥ ।
nodvijā notkaṭāścaiva dharmasya prakriyā tu sā ।। samūla phalapuṣpāṇi varttanāya tvaśeṣataḥ । sarvaikāntasukhaḥ kālo nātyarthaṃ hyuṣṇaśītalaḥ ।। mano abhilaṣitaḥ kāma stāsāṃ sarvatra sarvadā ।
uttiṣṭhaṃti pṛthivyāṃ vai teṣāṃ dhyānai rasātalāt ।। balavarṇakarī teṣāṃ jarārogapraṇāśinī । asaṃskāryaiḥ śarīraistu prajāstāḥ sthirayauvanāḥ ।। tāsāṃ vinā tu saṃkalpājjāyaṃte sithunātprajāḥ ।
samaṃ janma ca rūpaṃ ca prīyaṃte caiva tāḥ samāḥ ।। tadā satyamalobhaśca saṃtuṣṭiśca ca sukhaṃ damaḥ । nirviśeṣāśca tāḥ sarvā rūpāyuḥśilpaceṣṭitaiḥ ।। abuddhipūrvikā pṛttiḥ prajānāṃ bhavati svayam ।
apravṛttiḥ kṛtadvāre karmaṇaḥ śubhapāpayoḥ ।। varṇāśramavyavasthāśca na tadāsanna tatkarāḥ । anicchādveṣayuktāstā varttayanti parasparam ।। tulyarūpāyuṣaḥ sarvā adhamottamavarjitāḥ ।
sukhaprāyā viśokāśca utpadyaṃte kṛte yuge ।। lābhālābhau na vā syātāṃ mitrāmitrau priyāpriyau । manasā viṣayastāsāṃ nirīhāṇāṃ pravartate ।। nāti hiṃsati vānyonyaṃ nānugṛṅṇaṃti vai tadā ।।
jñānaṃ paraṃ kṛtayuge tretāyāṃ yajña ucyate । pavṛttaṃ dvāpare yuddhaṃ steyameva kalau yuge ।। sattvaṃ kṛtaṃ rajastretā dvāparaṃ tu rajastamaḥ । kalistamastu vijñeyaṃ guṇavṛttaṃ gumeṣu tat ।।
kālaḥ kṛtayuge tveṣa tasya sandhyāṃ nibodhata । catvāri tu sahasrāṇi varṣāṇāṃ tatkṛtaṃ yugam ।। sādhyāṃśau tasya divyāni śatānyaṣṭau tu saṃkhyayā । catvāryaiva sahasrāṇi varṣāṇāṃ monuṣāṇi tu ।।
tadā tāsu bhavaṃtyāśu notkrośācca viparyayāḥ । tataḥ kṛtyuge tasmin sasaṃdhyāṃśe gate tadā ।। pādāvaśiṣṭo bhavati yugadharmastu sarvaśaḥ । sandhyāyāstu vyatītāyāḥ sāṃdhyaḥ kālo yugasya saḥ ।।
pādamiśrāvaśiṣṭena saṃdhyādharme punaḥ punaḥ । evaṃ kṛtayuge tasminniśśeṣeṃtardadhe tadā ।। tasyāṃ ca sandhau naṣṭāyāṃ mānasī cābhavatprajā । siddhiranyayuge tasmiṃstretākhye anaṃtare kṛtāt ।।
sargādau yā mayāṣṭau tu mānasyo vai prakīrtitāḥ । aṣṭau tāḥ kramayogena siddhayo yāṃti saṃkṣayam ।। kalpādau mānasī hyekā siddhirbhavati sā kṛte । manvaṃtareṣu sarveṣu caturyugavibhāgaśaḥ ।।
varṇāśramācārakṛtaḥ karmasiddhyudbhavaḥ kṛtaḥ । saṃdhyā kṛtasya pādena saṃkṣepeṇa vaśāttataḥ ।। kṛtasaṃdhyāṃśakā hyete trīnādāya parasparam । hīyaṃte yugadharmāste tapaḥśrutabalāyuṣaḥ ।।
kṛte kṛtāśe atīte tu vabhūva tadanantaram । tretāyugasamutpattiḥ sāṃśā ca ṛṣisattamāḥ ।। tasmin kṣīṇe kṛtāṃśe vai tāsu śiṣṭāsu saptasu । kalpādau saṃpravṛttāyāstretāyāḥ prasukhe tadā ।।
praṇaśyati tadā siddhiḥ kālayogena nānyathā । tasyāṃ siddhau pranaṣṭāyāmanyā siddhirajāyata ।। apāṃśau tau pratigatau tadā meghātmānā tu vai । meghebhyaḥ stanayitṛbhyaḥ pravṛttaṃ pṛṣṭisarjanam ।।
sakṛdeva tayā vṛṣṭyā saṃsiddhe pṛṣivītale । prajā āsaṃstatastāsāṃ vṛkṣaśca gṛha saṃjñitāḥ ।। sarvaḥ pratyupabhogastu tāsāṃ tebhyo vyajāyata । varttayaṃtesma tebhyastāstretāyugamukhe prajāḥ ।।
tataḥ kālena mahatā tāsāmeva viparyayāt । saṃgalolātmako bhāvastadā hyākasmiko abhavat ।। yattadbhavati nārīṇāṃ jīvitāṃte tadārtavam । tadā tadvai na bhavati punaryugabalena tu ।।
tāsāṃ punaḥ pravṛttaṃ tanmāsimāsi tadārtavam । tatastenaiva yogena varttate maithunaṃ tadā ।। teṣāṃ tatkā labhāvitvānmāsimāsyupagacchatām । akāle cārtavotpattyā garbhotpattistadābhavat ।।
viparyayeṇa teṣāṃ tu tena tatkāla bhāvitā । praṇaśyaṃti tataḥ sarve vṛkṣāste gṛhasaṃjñitāḥ ।। tatasteṣu pranaṣṭeṣu vibhrāṃtā vyākulendriyāḥ । abhidhyāyaṃti tāḥ siddhiṃ satyābhidhyāyinastadā ।।
prādurbabhūvusteṣāṃ tu vṛkṣāste gṛhasaṃjñitāḥ । vastrāṇi ca prasūyaṃte phalānyābharaṇāni ca ।। tathaiva jāyate teṣāṃ gandharvāṇāṃ rasānvitam । ānvīkṣikaṃ mahāvīryaṃ puṭake puṭake madhu ।।
tena tā varttayanti smamukhe tretāyugasya vai । tdṛṣṭapuṣṭāstayā siddhyā prajāstā vigatajvarāḥ ।। tataḥ kālāṃtarepyevaṃ punarlobhāvṛtāḥ prajāḥ । vṛkṣāṃstāḥ paryagṛhṇaṃta madhu vā mākṣikaṃ balāt ।।
tāsāṃ tenāpacāreṇa punarlobhakṛtena vai । pranaṣṭā prabhuṇā sārddhaṃ kalpavṛkṣāḥ kvacitkvacit ।। tasyāmevālpaśiṣṭāyāṃ siddhyāṃ kālavaśāttadā । varttaṃte cānayā tāsāṃ dvaṃdvānyatyutthitāni tu ।।
śītavātātapāstīvrāstatastā duḥkhitā bhṛśam । dvaṃdvaistaiḥ pīḍyamānāstu cukruśurāvṛṇāni vā ।। kṛtvā dvandvapratīyātaṃ niketāni vicetasaḥ । pūrva nikāmacārāste hyaniketā yathābhavan ।।
yathāyogaṃ yathāprīti niketeṣvavasanpurā । madhudhunvatsu niṣṭheṣu parvateṣu nadīṣu ca ।। saṃśrayaṃti ca durgāṇi dhanvapāvartamaudakam । yathājoṣaṃ yathākāmaṃ sameṣu viṣameṣu ca ।।
ārabdhāstānniketānvai kartuṃ śītoṣṇavāraṇāt । tatastānnirmayāmāsuḥ kheṭāni ca purāṇi ca ।। grāmāṃścaiva yathābhāgaṃ tathaiva nagarāṇi ca । teṣāmāyāmaviṣkaṃbhāḥ sanniveśāṃtarāṇi ca ।।
cakrustadā yathājñānaṃ mītvāmītvātmanogulaiḥ । mānārthāni pramāṇāni tadā prabhṛti cakrire ।। yayāṃgulapradeśāṃstrīnhastaḥ kiṣkuṃ dhanūṃṣi ca । daśa tvaṃgulaparvāṇi prādeśa iti saṃjñitaḥ ।।
aṃguṣṭhasya pradeśinyā vyāsaprādeśa ucyate । tālaḥ smṛto madhyamayā gokarṇaścāpyanāmayā ।। kaniṣṭhayā vitastistu dvādaśāṃgula ucyate । ratniraṃgulaparvāṇi saṃkhyayā tvekaviśatiḥ ।।
catvāri viṃśatiścaiva hastaḥ syādaṃgulāni tu । kiṣkuḥ smṛto dviratnistu dvicatvāriṃśadaṃgulaḥ ।। caturhasto dhanurddaṃḍo nālikā yugameva ca । dhanuḥsahastre dve tatra gavyūtistauḥ kṛtā tadā ।।
aṣṭau dhanuḥsahasrāṇi yojanaṃ tairvibhāvitam । etena yojaneneha sanniveśāstataḥ kṛtāḥ ।। caturṇāmatha durgāṇāṃ svayamutthāni trīṇi ca । caturtha kṛtimaṃ duga tasya vakṣyāmi nirṇayam ।।
sotsedharaṃdhraprākāraṃ sarvataḥ khātakāvṛtam । rucakaḥ pratikadvāraṃ kumārīpurameva ca ।। dvihastaḥ srotasāṃ śreṣṭhaṃ kumārīpuramañcatān । hastasroto daśaśreṣṭho navahastoṣṭa eva ca ।।
kheṭānāṃ ca purāṇāṃ ca grāmāṇāṃ caiva sarvaśaḥ । trividhānāṃ ca durgāṇāṃ parvatodakadhanvinām ।। kṛtrimāṇāṃ ca durgāṇāṃ viṣkambhāyāmameva ca । yojanādarddhaviṣkambhamaṣṭabhāgādhikāyatam ।।
paramārddhārddhamāyāmaṃ prāgudakplavanaṃ puram । chinnakarṇavikarṇaṃ ca vyajanākṛtisaṃsthitam ।। vṛttaṃ vajraṃ ca dīrgha ca nagaraṃ na praśasyate । caturasrayutaṃ divyaṃ praśastaṃ taiḥ puraṃ kṛtam ।।
caturviṃśatparaṃ hrasvaṃ vāstu vāṣṭaśataṃ param । atra madhyaṃ praśaṃsaṃti hrasvaṃ kāṣṭhavivarjjitam ।। atha kiṣkuśatānyaṣṭau prāhurmukhyaṃ niveśanam । nagarādarddhaviṣakaṃbhaḥ kheṭaṃ pānaṃ tadūrddhataḥ ।।
nagarādyojanaṃ kheṭaṃ kheṭādgāmorddhayojanam । dvikrośaḥ paramā sīmā kṣetrasīmā caturddhanuḥ ।। viṃśaddhanūṃṣi vistīrṇo diśāṃ mārgastu taiḥ kṛtaḥ । viṃśaddhanurgrāmamārgaḥ sīmāmārgo daśaiva tu ।।
dhanūṃṣi daśa vistīrṇaḥ śrīmān rājapathaḥ kṛtaḥ । nṛvājirathanāgānāmasaṃbādhastu saṃcaraḥ ।। dhanūṃṣi cāpi catvāri śākhārathyāśca tairmitāḥ । trikā rathyoparathyāḥ syurdvikā ścāpyuparatyakāḥ ।।
jaṃghāpathaścatuṣpādastripadaṃ ca gṛhāṃtaram । dhṛtimārgastūrddhaṣaṣṭhaṃ kramaśaḥ padikaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। avaskāraparīvāraḥ pādamātraṃ samaṃtataḥ । kṛteṣu teṣu sthāneṣu punargehagṛhāṇi vai ।।
yathā te pūrvamāsaṃśca vṛkṣāstu gṛha saṃsthitāḥ । tathā kartuṃ samārabdhāściṃtayitvā punaḥ punaḥ ।। vṛkṣasyārvāggatāḥ śākhā itaścaivāparā gatāḥ । ata ūrddha gatāścānyā evaṃ tiryaggatāḥ parā ।।
buddhyānviṣya yathānyāyaṃ vṛkṣaśākhā gatā yathā । yathā kṛtāstu taiḥ śākhāsta smācchālāstu tāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। evaṃ prasiddhāḥ śākhābhyaḥ śāloścaiva gṛhāṇi ca । tasmāttāśca smṛtāḥ śālāḥ śālātvaṃ tāsu tatsmṛtam ।।
prasīdaṃti yatasteṣu tataḥ prāsādasaṃjñitaḥ । tasmād gṛhāṇi śālāśca prāsādāścaiva saṃjñitā ।। kṛtvā dvaṃdvābhighātāstāntvārtopāyamaciṃtayān । naṣṭeṣu madhunā sārddhaṃ kalpavṛkṣeṣu vai tadā ।।
viṣādavyākulāstā vai prajāḥ sṛṣṭāstu darśitāḥ । tataḥ prādurbabhau tāsāṃ siddhistretāyuge tadā ।। sarvārthasādhakā hyanyā vṛṣṭistāsāṃ nikāmataḥ । tāsāṃ vṛṣṭyudakānīha yāni miṣṭagatāni ca ।।
evaṃ nayaḥ pravṛttastu dvitīye vṛṣṭisarjane । ye parastādapāṃ stokāḥ saṃpātāḥ puthivītale ।। apāṃ bhūmestu saṃyogādoṣadhyastāstadābhavan । puṣpamūlaphalinyastu oṣadhyastā hi jajñire ।।
aphālakṛṣṭāścānuptā grābhyāramyāścaturddaśa । ṛtupuṣpaphalāścaiva vṛkṣā gulmāśca jajñire ।। prādurbhūtāstu tretāyāṃ māyāyāmauṣadhasya vā । tadauṣadhena vartaṃte prajāstretā mukhe tadā ।।
tataḥ punarabhūttāsāṃ rāgo lobhastu sarvadā । avaśyabhāvinārthena tretāyugavaśena ca ।। tataste paryagṛhṇaṃstu nadīkṣetrāṇi parvatān । vṛkṣagulmauṣadhīścaiva prasahya tu yathābalam ।।
siddhātmānastu ye pūrvaṃ vyākhyātā vaḥ kṛte mayā । brahmaṇo mānasāste vai utpannā ye janādiha ।। śāṃtā ye śuṣmiṇaścaiva karmiṇo duḥkhitāstathā । tata āvarttamānāste tretāyāṃ jajñire punaḥ ।।
brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyāḥśūdrā drohajanāstathā । bhāvitāḥ pūrvajātīṣu khyātyā te śubhapāpayoḥ ।। tataste prabalā ye tu satyaśīlā ahiṃsakāḥ । vītalobhā jitātmāno nivasaṃti smṛteṣu vai ।।
parigrahaṃ na kurvaṃti vadaṃtastu upasthitāḥ । teṣāṃ karmāṇi kurvaṃti tebhyaścaivābalāśca ye ।। paricaryāsu varttante tebhyaścānye alpatejasaḥ । evaṃ vipratipanneṣu prapanneṣu parasparam ।।
tena doṣeṇa vai śāṃtā oṣadhyo nitarāṃ tadā । pranaṣṭā gṛhyamāṇā vai muṣṭibhyāṃ sikatā yathā ।। athāsya tu yugabalādgāmyāraṇyāścaturddaśa । phalairgṛhṇaṃti puṣpaiśca tathā mūlaiśca tāḥ punaḥ ।।
tatastāsu pranaṣṭāsu vibhrāṃtāstāḥ prajāstadā । kṣudhāviṣṭāstadā sarvā jagmustā vai svayambhuvam ।। vṛttyarthamabhilipsaṃtyo hyādau tretāyugasya tāḥ । brahmā svayaṃbhūrbhagavān jñātvā tāsāṃ manīṣitam ।।
puṣṭipratyakṣadṛṣṭena darśanena vicārya saḥ । grastāḥ pṛthivyā tvoṣadhyo jñātvā pratyarūhatpunaḥ ।। kṛtvā vatsaṃ sameruṃ tu dudoha pṛthivīmimām । dugdheyaṃ gaustadā tena bījāni vasudhātale ।।
jajñire tāni bījāni grāmāraṇyāstu tāḥ prabhuḥ । oṣadhyaḥ phalapākātāḥ kṣaṇasaptavaśāstu tāḥ ।। vrīhayaśca yavāścaiva godhūmāścaṇakāstilāḥ । priyaṃgava udārāste koraduṣṭāḥ savāmakāḥ ।।
māṣā mudgā masūrāstu nīvārāḥ sakulatthakāḥ । harikāścarakāścaiva gamaḥ saptadaśa smṛtāḥ ।। ityetā oṣadhīnāṃ tu grāmyāṇāṃ jātayaḥ smṛtāḥ । śyāmākāścaiva nīvārā jartilāḥ sagavedhukāḥ ।।
kuruviṃdo veṇuyavāstā mātīrkāṭakāḥ smṛtāḥ । grāmāraṇyāḥ smṛtā hyetā oṣadhyastu caturdaśa ।। utpannāḥ prathamasyaitā ādau tretāyugasya ha । aphālakṛṣṭāstāḥ sarvā grāmyāraṇyaścaturddaśa ।।
vṛkṣagulmalatāvallyo vīrudhastṛṇajātayaḥ । mūlaiḥ phalaiśca rohaiścagṛhṇanpuṣṭāśca yatphalam ।। pṛthvī dugdhā tu bījāni yāni pūrvaṃ svayaṃbhuvā । ṛtupuṣpaphalāstā vai oṣadhyo jajñire tviha ।।
yadā prasṛṣṭā oṣadhyo na prathaṃtīha yāḥ punaḥ । tatastāsāṃ ca pṛttyarthai vārtopāyaṃ cakāra ha ।। tāsāṃ svayaṃbhūrbhagavān hastasiddhiṃ svakarmajām । tataḥ prabhṛti cauṣadhyaḥ kṛṣṭapacyāstu jajñire ।।
saṃsiddhakāyo vārtāyāṃ tatastāsāṃ prajāpatiḥ । maryādāṃ sthāpayāmāsa yayārakṣatparasparam ।। ye vai parigrahītārastāsāmāsanbalīyasaḥ । itareṣāṃ kṛtatrāṇān sthāpayāmāsa kṣatriyān ।।
upatiṣṭhaṃti tāvaṃto yāvanto nirmitāstathā । satyaṃ būta yathābhūtaṃ dhruvaṃ vo brahmaṇāstu tāḥ ।। ye cānye hyabalāsteṣāṃ saṃrakṣākarmmaṇi sthitāḥ । krītāni nāśayaṃti sma pṛthivyāṃ te vyavasthitāḥ ।।
vaiśyānityeva tānāhuḥ kīnāśānvṛttisādhakān । sevaṃtaśca dravaṃtaśca paricaryāsu ye ratāḥ ।। nistejaso alpavīryāśca śūdrāṃstānabravīcca saḥ । teṣāṃ karmāṇi dharmāṃśca brahmā tu vyadadhātprabhuḥ ।।
saṃsthityāṃ tu kṛtāyāṃ hi yāturvarṇyasya tena vai । punaḥ prajāstu tā mohāddharmmaṃ taṃ nānvapālayan ।। varṇadharmaiśca jīvaṃtyo vyaruddhyaṃta parasparam । brahmā buddhā tu tatsarvaṃ yāthātathyena sa prabhuḥ ।।
kṣatriyāṇāṃ balaṃ daṃḍaṃ yuddhamājīvyamādiśat । yājanādhyāpane brahmā tathā dānapratigraham ।। brāhmaṇānāṃ vibhusteṣāṃ karmāṇyetā nyathādiśat । pāśupālyaṃ ca vāṇijyaṃ kṛṣiṃ caiva viśāṃ dadau ।।
śilpājīvabhṛtāṃ caiva śūdrāṇāṃ vyadadhātpunaḥ । sāmānyāni ca karmāṇi brahmakṣatraviśāṃ punaḥ ।। yajanādhyāpane dānaṃ sāmānyānītareṣu ca । karmājīvaṃ tu vai dattvā teṣāmiha parasparam ।।
teṣāṃ lokāṃtare mūrdhni sthānāni vidadhe punaḥ । prājāpatyaṃ dvijātīnāṃ smṛtaṃ sthānaṃ kriyāvatām ।। sthānamaidraṃ kṣatriyāṇāṃ saṃgrāmeṣvapalāyinām । vaiśyānāṃ mārutaṃ sthānaṃ svasvakarmopajīvinām ।।
gāṃdharvaṃ śūdrajātīnāṃ paricarye ca tiṣṭhatām । sthānānyetāni varṇānāṃ yogyācāravatāṃ satām ।। saṃsthityāṃ sukṛtāyāṃ vai cāturvarṇyasya tasya tat । varṇāstu daṃḍabhayataḥ svesve varṇye vyavasthitāḥ ।
tataḥ sthiteṣu varṇeṣu sthāpayāmāsa hyāśramān ।। gṛhastho brahmacārī ca vānaprastho yatistathā । āśramāścaturo hyetānpūrvavatsthāpayanprabhuḥ ।। varṇakarmāṇi ye kecitteṣāmiha caturbhavaḥ ।
kṛtakarmma kṛtāvāsā āśramādupabhuñjate ।। brahmā tānsthāpayāmāsa āśramān bhrāmatāmataḥ । nirddideśa tatasteṣāṃ brahmā dharmānprabhā ṣate ।। prasthānāni tu teṣāṃ ca yamānsaniyamāṃstathā ।
caturvarṇātmakaḥ pūrvaṃ gṛhasthasyāśramaḥ sthitaḥ ।। trayāṇā māśramāṇāṃ ca vṛttiyonīti caiva hi । yathākramaṃ ca vakṣyāmi vrataiśca niyamaistathā ।। dārāgnayaścātithaya iṣṭāḥ śrāddhakriyāḥ prajāḥ ।
ityeṣa vai gṛhasthasya samāsāddharmasaṃgrahaḥ ।। ḍhaṃḍī ca mekhalī caiva adhaḥśāyī tathājinī । guruśuśrūṣaṇaṃ bhaikṣyaṃvidyārthī brahmacāriṇaḥ ।। cīrapatrājināni syurvanamūlaphalauṣadhaiḥ ।
ubhe saṃdhye vagāhaśca homaścāraṇyavāsinām ।। vipannamusale bhaikṣyamāsteyaṃ śaucameva ca । apramādo avyavāyaśca dayā bhūteṣu ca kṣamā ।। śravaṇaṃ guruśuśrūṣā satyaṃ ca daśamaṃ smṛtam ।
daśalakṣaṇako hyeṣa dharmaḥ proktaḥ svayaṃbhūvā ।। bhikṣorvratāni paṃcātra bhaikṣyavedavratāni ca । teṣāṃ sthānānyaśuṣmiṃ ca saṃsthitānā macaṣṭa saḥ ।। aṣṭāśītisahasrāṇi ṛṣīṇāmūrdhvaretasām ।
smṛtaṃ teṣāṃ tu yat sthānaṃ tadeva guruvāsinām ।। saptarṣīṇā tu yatsthānaṃ smṛtaṃ tadvai vanaukasām । prājāpatyaṃ gṛhasthānāṃ nyāsināṃ brahmaṇaḥkṣayam ।। yogināmakṛtaṃ sthānaṃ tānājitbā na vidyate ।
sthānānyāśramiṇastāni brahmasthānasthitāni tu ।। catvāra eva paṃthāno devayānāni nirmitāḥ । paṃthānaḥ pitṛyānāstu samṛtāścatvāra eva te ।। brahmaṇāṃ lokatantreṇa ādye manvantare purā ।
paṃthāno devayānā ye teṣāṃ dvāraṃ raṃviḥ smṛtaḥ । tathaiva pitṛyānānāṃ candramā dvāramucyate ।। evaṃ varṇāśramāṇāṃ ca pravibhāge kṛte tadā । yadā prajā nā varddhaṃta varṇadharmasamāsikāḥ ।।
tato anyāṃ mānasīṃ svāṃ vai tretāmadhye asṛjatprajāḥ । ātmanastu śarīrebhyastulyāścaivātmanā tu tāḥ ।। tasmistretāyuge tvādye madhyaṃ prāpte krameṇa tu । tato anyāṃ mānasīṃ so atha prajāḥ sraṣṭuṃ pracakrame ।।
tataḥ sattvarajodriktāḥ prajāḥ sahyasṛjatprabhuḥ । dharmārthakāmamokṣāṇāṃ vārttānāṃ sādhakāśca yāḥ ।। devāśca pitaraścaiva ṛṣayo manavastathā । yugānurūpā dharmeṇa yairimā varddhitāḥ prajāḥ ।।
upasthite tadā tasmin sṛṣṭivarge svayaṃbhuvaḥ । abhidhyāya prajā brahmā nānāvīryāḥ svamānasīḥ ।। pūrvoktā yā mayā tubhyaṃ janānīkaṃ samāśritāḥ । kalpe atīte purāṇyāsīddevādyāstu prajā iha ।।
dhyāyatastasya tānīha saṃbhūtyarthamupastitāḥ । manvaṃtarakrameṇeha kaniṣṭhāḥ prathamena tāḥ ।। khyātāstu vaṃśyairetaistu pūrvaṃ yairiha bhāvitāḥ । kuśalākuśalaiḥ kaṃdairakṣīṇaistaistadā yutāḥ ।।
tatkarmaphaladoṣeṇa hyupabādhāḥ prajajñire । devāsurapitṝṃścaiva yakṣairgandharvamānuṣaiḥ ।। rākṣasaistu piśācaistaiḥ paśupakṣisarīsṛpaiḥ । vṛkṣanārakakīṭādyaistaistaiḥ sarvairupasthitāḥ ।
āhārārthaṃ prajānāṃ vai vidātmāno vinirmame ।। tatobhidhyāyatastasya mānasyo jajñire prajāḥ । taccharīrasamutpannaiḥ kāryaistaiḥ kāraṇaiḥ saha ।। kṣetrajñāḥ samavarttanta kṣetrasyaitasya dhīmataḥ ।
tato devāsurapitṝnmanuṣyāṃśca catuṣṛyam ।। sisṛkṣurayutātāni sa cātmānamayūyujat । yuktātmanastatastasya tamomātrāsamudbhavaḥ ।। tadābhidhyāyataḥ sargaṃ prayatno abhūtprajāpateḥ ।
tato asya jagha nātpūrvamasurā jajñira sutāḥ ।। asuḥ prāṇaḥ smṛto vijñaistajjanmānastato asurāḥ । sṛṣṭā yayā surāstanvā tāṃ tanuṃ sa vyapohata ।। sāpaviddhā tanustena sadyo rātrirajāyata ।
sā tamobahulā yasmāttato rātristriyāmikā ।। āvṛtāstamasā rātrau prajā stasmātsvayaṃ punaḥ । sṛṣṭvāsurāṃstataḥ so atha tanumanyāmapadyata ।। avyaktāṃ sattvabahulāṃ tatastāṃ so abhyayuñjata ।
tatastāṃ yuñja mānasya priyamāsītprabhoḥ kila ।। tato mukhātsamutpannā dīvyatastasya devatāḥ । yato asya dīvyato jātāstena devāḥ prakīrttitāḥ ।। dhāturdivyeti yaḥ proktaḥ krīḍāyāṃ sa vibhāvyate ।
tasmāttanvāstu divyāyā jajñire tena devatāḥ ।। devān sṛṣṭvā tataḥ so atha tanuṃ divyāmapohata । utsṛṣṭā sā tanustena ahaḥ samabhavattadā ।। tasmādahaḥkarmayuktā devatāḥ samupāsate ।
devānsṛṣṭvā tataḥ so atha tanumanyāmapadyata ।। sattvamātrātmikāmeva tato anyāmabhyayuṅkta vai । piteva manyamānastānputrānpradhyāya sa prabhuḥ ।। pitaro hyabhavaṃstasyā sadhye rātryahayoḥ pṛthak ।
tasmātte pitaro devāḥ pitṛtvaṃ teṣu tatsmṛtam ।। yayāsṛṣṭāstu pitarastāṃ tanuṃ sa vyapohata । sāpaviddhā tanustena sadyaḥ saṃdhyā vyajāyata ।। tasmādahardevatānāṃ rātriryā sā'surī smṛtā ।
tayormadhye tu vai paitrī yā tanuḥ sā garīyasī ।। tasmāddevāsurāścaiva ṛṣayo mānavāstathā । yuktāstanumupāsaṃte uṣāvyuṣṭyoryadantaram ।। tasmādrātryahayoḥ saṃdhimupāsaṃte tathā dvijāḥ ।
tato anyasyāṃ punarbrahmā svatanvāmupapadyata ।। rajomātrātmikā yā tu manasā so asṛjatprabhuḥ । manasā tu sutāstasya prajanājjajñire prajāḥ ।। mananācca manuṣayāste prajanātprathitāḥ prajāḥ ।
sṛṣṭvā punaḥ prajāḥ so atha svāṃ tanuṃ sa vyapohata ।। sāpaviddhā tanustena jyotsnā sadyastvajāyata । tasmādbhavanti saṃhṛṣṭā jyotsnāyā udbhave prajāḥ ।। ityetāstanavastena hyapaviddhā mahātmanā ।
sadyo rātryahanī caivasaṃdhyā jyotsnā ca jajñire ।। jyotsnā saṃdhyāhanī caiva sattvamātrātmakaṃ trayam । tamomātrātmikā rātriḥ sā vai tasmānniyāmikā ।। tasmāddevā divyatanvā tuṣṭyā sṛṣṭā sukhāttu vai ।
yasmātteṣāṃ divā janma balinastena te divā ।। tanvā yadasurānratryā jaghanādasṛjatprabhuḥ । prāṇebhyo rātrijanmāno hyajeyā niśi tena te ।। etānyeva bhaviṣyāṇāṃ devānāmasuraiḥ saha ।
pitṝṇāṃ mānuṣāṇāṃ ca atītānā gateṣu vai ।। manvantareṣu sarveṣu nimittāni bhavanti hi । jyotsnā rātryahanī saṃdhyā catvāryetāni tāni vā ।। bhānti yasmāttato bhāti bhāśabdo vyāptidīptiṣu ।
aṃbhāṃsyetāni sṛṣṭvā tu devadānavamānuṣān ।। pitṝṃścaiva tathā cānyānvividhānvya sṛjatprajāḥ । tāmutsṛjya tato cyotsnāṃ tato anyāṃ prāpya sa prabhuḥ ।। mūrttiṃ rajastamodriktāṃ tatastāṃ so abhyayuñjata ।
tato anyāḥ soṃ'dhakāre ca kṣudhāviṣṭāḥ prajāḥ sṛjan ।। tāḥ sṛṣṭāstu kṣudhāviṣṭā ambhāṃsyādātumudyatāḥ । ambhāṃsyetāni rakṣāma uktavantastu teṣu ye ।। rākṣasāste smṛtāstasmātkṣudhātmāno niśācarāḥ ।
ye abruvan kṣiṇumo ambhāṃsi teṣāṃ tdṛṣṭāḥ parasparam ।। tena te karmaṇā yakṣā guhyakāḥ krūrakarmiṇaḥ । rakṣeti pālane cāpi dhātureṣa vibhāvyate ।। ya eṣa kṣītidhāturvai kṣapaṇe sa nirucyate ।
rakṣaṇādrakṣa ityuktaṃ kṣapaṇādyakṣa ucyata ।। tāndṛṣṭvā tvapriyeṇāsya keśāḥ śīrṇāśca dhīmataḥ । te śīrṇā vyutthitā hyūrddhamāro hantaḥ punaḥ punaḥ ।। hīnā ye śiraso bālāḥ pannāścaivāpasarpiṇaḥ ।
bālātmanā smṛtā vyālā hīnatvādahayaḥ smṛtāḥ ।। pannatvātpannagāścāpi vyapasarpācca sarppatā । teṣāṃ layaḥ pṛthivyāṃ yaḥ sūryācandramasau ghanāḥ ।। tasya krodhodbhavo yo asāvagnigarbhaḥ sudāruṇaḥ ।
sa tānsarppān sahotpannānāviveśa viṣātmakaḥ ।। sarppānsṛṣṭvā tataḥ krodhāt krodhātmāno vinirmitāḥ । varṇena kapiśenogrāste bhūtāḥ piśitāśanāḥ ।। bhūtatvātte ramṛtā bhūtāḥ piśācā piśitāśanāt ।
gāyato gāṃ tatastasya gandharvā jajñire sutāḥ ।। dhayeti dhātuḥ kavibhiḥ pānārthe paripaṭhyate । pibato jajñire vācaṃ gandharvāstena te smṛtāḥ ।। aṣṭāsvetāsu sṛṣṭāsu devayoniṣu sa prabhuḥ ।
chandataścaiva chandāsi vayāṃsi vayasāsṛjat ।। pakṣiṇastu sa sṛṣṭvā vai tataḥ paśugaṇānsṛjan । mukhatojāḥ sṛjanso atha vakṣasaścāpyavīḥ sṛjan ।। gāvaścaivodarādbrahmā pāśvībhyāṃ ca vinirmame ।
pādato aśvānsamātaṅgān rāsabhān gavayānmṛgān ।। uṣṭrāṃścaiva varāhāṃśca śuno anyāṃścaiva jātayaḥ । oṣadhyaḥ phala mūlinyo romabhyastasya jajñire ।। evaṃ pañcauṣadhīḥ sṛṣṭvā vyayuñjatso adhvareṣu vai ।
asya tvādau tu kalpasya tretāyugamukhepurā ।। gaurajaḥ puruṣo athāviraśvāśvataragardabhāḥ । ete grāmyāḥ samṛtāḥ sapta āraṇyāḥ sapta cāpare ।। śvāpado dvīpino hastī vānaraḥ pakṣipañcamaḥ ।
audakāḥ paśavaḥ ṣaṣṭhāḥ saptamāstu sarīsṛpāḥ ।। mahiṣā gavayoṣṭrāśca dvikhurāḥ śarabho dviṣaḥ । markaṭaḥ saptamo hyeṣāṃ cāraṇyāḥ paśavastu te ।। gāyatrīṃ ca ṛcaṃ caiva trivṛtsatomarathantare ।
agniṣṭomaṃ ca yajñānāṃ nirmame prathamānmukhāt ।। yajūṃṣi traiṣṭubhaṃ chandaḥ stomaṃ pañcadaśaṃ tathā । bṛhatsāma tathoktaṃ ca dakṣiṇātso asṛjanmukhāt ।। sāmāni jagatīṃ caiva stomaṃ saptadaśaṃ tathā ।
vairūpyamatirātraṃ ca paścimātso asṛjanmakhāt ।। ekaviṃśamatharvāṇamāptoryāmaṃ tathaiva ca । anuṣṭubhaṃ savairājaṃ caturthādasṛjanmukhāt ।। vidyuto aśanimeghāṃśva rohitedradhanūṃṣi ca ।
sṛṣṭvāsau bhagavāndevaḥ parjanyamitiviśrutam ।। ṛco yajūṃṣi sāmāni nirmame yajñasiddhaye । uccāvacāni bhūtāni gātrebhyastasya jajñire ।। brahmaṇāstu prajāsargaṃ sṛjato hi prajāpateḥ ।
sṛṣṭvā catuṣṭayaṃ pūrvaṃ devarṣipitṛmānavān ।। tato asṛjata bhūtāni carāṇi sthāvarāṇi ca । sṛṣṭvā yakṣapiśācāṃśca gandharvapsarasastadā ।। narakinnararakṣāṃsi vayaḥpaśumṛgoragān ।
avyayaṃ ca vyayaṃ caiva dvayaṃ sthāvarajaṅgamam ।। teṣāṃ ye yāni karmāṇi prāk sṛṣṭāni prapedire । tānyeva pratipadyante sṛjyamānāḥ punaḥpunaḥ ।। hiṃsrāhiṃsre sṛjan krūre dharmādharmāvṛtānṛte ।
tadbhāvitāḥ prapadyante tasmāttattasya rocate ।। mahābhūteṣu nānātvamindriyārteṣu mūrtiṣu । viniyogaṃ ca bhūtānāṃ dhātaiva vyadadhātsvayam ।। kecitpuruṣakāraṃ tu prāhuḥ karma ca mānavāḥ ।
daivamityapare viprāḥ svabhāvaṃ bhūtacintakāḥ ।। pauruṣaṃ karma daivaṃ ca phalavṛttisvabhāvataḥ । na caiva tu pṛthagbhāvamadhikena tato viduḥ ।। etadevaṃ ca naivaṃ ca na cobhe nānubhe na ca ।
svakarmaviṣayaṃ brūyuḥ sattvasthāḥ samadarśinaḥ ।। nānārūpaṃ ca bhūtānāṃ kṛtānāṃ ca prapañcanam । vedaśabdebhya evādau nirmame sa maheśvaraḥ ।। ārṣāṇi caiva nāmāni yāśca deveṣu dṛṣṭayaḥ ।
śarvaryante prasūtānāṃ punastebhyo dadhātyajaḥ ।। rudraṃ dharmaṃ manaścaiva ruciṃ caivākṛtiṃ tathā । pañca kartṝn hi sa tadā manasā vyasṛjatprabhuḥ ।। ete mahābhujāḥ sarve prajānāṃ sthitihetavaḥ ।
auṣadhīḥ pratisaṃdhatte rudraḥ kṣīṇaḥ punaḥ punaḥ ।। prāptauṣadhiphalairdevaḥ samyagiṣṭaḥ phalārthibhiḥ । tribhireva kapālaistu tryaṃbakairoṣadhīkṣaye ।। ijyate munibhiryasmāttasmātttryaṃbaka ucyate ।
gāyatrīṃ caiva triṣṭup ca jagatī caiva tāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। aṃbikānāṃ mayā proktā yonayaḥ svanaspateḥ । tābhirekatvabhūtā bhistrividhābhiḥ svavīryataḥ ।। trisādhanaḥ puroḍāśastrikapālastataḥ smṛtaḥ ।
tryaṃbakaḥ sa puroḍāśasteneha tryaṃbakaḥsmṛtaḥ ।। dhatte dharmaḥ prajāḥ sarvā mano jñānakaraṃ smṛtam । ākṛtiḥ suruce rūpaṃ ruciḥ śraddhākaraḥ smṛtaḥ ।। evamete prajāpālāḥ prajānāṃ sthitihetavaḥ ।
athāsya sṛjataḥ sargaṃ prajānāṃ parivṛddhaye ।। na vyavarddhata tāḥ sṛṣṭāḥ prajāḥ kenāpi hetunā । tataḥ sa vidadhe buddhimarthaniścayagā minīm ।। athātmani samadrākṣīttamomātrāṃ tu cāriṇīm ।
rajaḥ sattvaṃ parityajya vartamānāṃ svakarmataḥ ।। tataḥ sa tena dukhenaśucaṃ cakre jagatpatiḥ । tamaśca vyanudatpaścād rajasātu samāvṛṇot ।। tattamaḥ pratinuttaṃ vai mithunaṃ saṃprasūyata ।
adharmācaraṇā ttasya hiṃsā śoko vyajāyata ।। tatastasminsamudbhūte mithune varaṇātmake । tataḥ sa bhagavānāsīt prītaścaitaṃ hi śiśriye ।। evaṃ prītātmanastasya svadehārddhādviniḥsṛtā ।
nārī paramakalyāṇī sarvabhūtamanoharā ।। sā hi kāmātmanā sṛṣṭā prakṛteḥ sā surūpiṇī । śatarūpeti sā proktā sā proktaiva punaḥ punaḥ ।। tataḥ prajāḥ samudbhūtā yathā proktā mayā purā ।
prakriyāyāṃ yathā tubhyaṃ tretāmadhye mahātmanaḥ ।। yadā prajāstu tāḥ sṛṣṭā na vyavaddhata dhīmataḥ । tato anyānmānasānputrānātmanaḥ sadṛśo asṛjata ।। bhṛgvaṅgiromarīcīṃśca pulastyaṃ pulahaṃ kratum ।
dakṣamatriṃ vasiṣṭhaṃ ca nirmame mānasānsutān ।। nava brahmāṇa ityete purāṇe niścayaṃ gatāḥ । brahmā yatātmakānāṃ tu sarveṣāmātmayoninām ।। tato asṛjatpunarbrahmā dharmaṃ bhūtasukhāvaham ।
prajāpatiṃ ruciṃ caiva pūrveṣāmeva pūrvajau ।। buddhitaḥ sasṛje dharmaṃ sarvabhūtasukhāvaham । manasastu rucirnāma jajñe jo avyaktajanmanaḥ ।। bhṛgustu tdṛdayājjajñe ṛṣiḥ sālalayoninaḥ ।
prāṇāddakṣaṃ sṛjanbrahmā cakṣurbhyāṃ tu marīcinam ।। abhimānātmakaṃ rudraṃ nirmame nīlalohitam । śirasoṃgirasaṃ caiva śrotrādatriṃ tathaiva ca ।। pulastyaṃ ca tathodānādvyānācca pulahaṃ punaḥ ।
samānajo vasiṣṭhaśca hyapānānnirmame kratum ।। ityete brahmaṇaḥ putrāḥ prajādau dvādaśa smṛtāḥ । dharmasteṣāṃ prathamajo devatānāṃ smṛtastu vai ।। bhṛgvādayastu ye sṛṣṭāste vai brahmarṣayaḥ smṛtāḥ ।
gṛhamedhipurāṇāste dharmastaiḥ prāk pravarttitaḥ ।। dvādaśaite prasūyante prajāḥ kalpe punaḥ punaḥ । teṣāṃ dvādaśa te vaṃśā divyā devaguṇānvitāḥ ।। kriyāvantaḥ prajāvanto maharṣibhiralaṅkṛtāḥ ।
yadā tairiha sṛṣṭaistu dharmmādyaiśca maharṣibhiḥ ।। sṛjyamānāḥ prajāścaiva na vyavarddhanta dhīmataḥ । tamomātrāvṛtaḥ so abhūcchokapratihataśca vai ।। yathā'vṛtaḥ sa vai brahmā tamomātrā tu sā punaḥ ।
putrāṇāṃ ca tamomātrā aparā niḥsṛtābhavat ।। pratisrotātmako adharmo hiṃsā caivāśubhātmikā । tataḥ pratihate tasya pratīte varaṇātmake ।। svāṃ tanuṃ sa tadā brahmā samapohata bhāsvarām ।
dvidhā kṛtvā svakaṃ dehamarddhena puruṣo abhavat ।। ardhena nārī sā tasya śatarūpā vyajāyata । prakṛtirbhūtadhātrī sā kāmādvai sṛjataḥ prabhoḥ ।। sā divaṃ pṛthivīṃ caiva mahimnā vyāpya susthitā ।
brahmāṇaḥ sā tanuḥ pūrvā divamāvṛtya tiṣṭataḥ ।। yā tvarddhā sṛjyate nārī śatarūpā vyajāyata । sā devī niyutaṃ taptvā tapaḥ parama duścaram ।। bharttāraṃ dīptayaśasaṃ puruṣaṃ pratyapadyata ।
sa vai svāyaṃbhuvaḥ pūrvaṃ puruṣo manurucyate ।। tasyaikasaptatiyugaṃ manvantaramihocyate । labdhvā tu puruṣaḥ patnīṃ śatarūpāmayonijām ।। tayā sa ramate sārddhaṃ tasmātsā ratirucyate ।
prathamaḥ saṃprayogaḥ sa kalpādau samavarttata ।। virājamasṛjadbrahmā so abhavatpuruṣo virāṭ । samrāṭ saśatarūpastu vairājastu manuḥ smṛtaḥ ।। sa vairājaḥ prajāsargaṃ sasarja puruṣo manuḥ ।
vairājātpuruṣādvīrau śatarūpā vyajāyata ।। priyavratottānapādau putrau putravatāṃ varau । kanye dve sumahābhāge yābhyāṃ jātā imāḥ prajāḥ ।। devī nāmnā tathākūliḥ prasūtiścaiva te śubhe ।
svāyaṃbhuvaḥ prasūtiṃ tu dakṣāya vyasṛjatprabhuḥ ।। ruceḥ prajāpateścaiva ākūtiṃ pratya pādayat । ākūtyāṃ mithunaṃ jajñe mānasasya ruceḥ śubham ।। yajñaśca dakṣiṇā caiva yamalau tau babhūvatuḥ ।
yajñasya dakṣiṇāyāṃ ca putrā dvādaśa jajñire ।। yāmā iti samākhyātā devāḥ svāyaṃbhuvetare । yamasya putrā yajñasya tasmādyāmāstu te smṛtāḥ ।। ajitāścaiva śukrāśca dvau gaṇau brahmaṇaḥ smṛtau ।
yāmāḥ pūrvaṃ parikrāntā yeṣāṃ saṃjñā divaukasaḥ ।। svāyaṃbhūva sutāyāṃ tu prasūtyāṃ lokamātaraḥ । tasyāṃ kanyāścaturviṃśaddakṣastvajanayatprabhuḥ ।। sarvāstāśca mahābhāgāḥ sarvāḥ kamalalocanāḥ ।
yogapatnyaśca tāḥ sarvāḥ sarvāstā yogamātaraḥ ।। sarvāśca brahmavādinyaḥ sarvā viśvasya mātaraḥ । śraddhā lakṣmīrdhṛtistuṣṭiḥ puṣṭirmedhā tathā kriyā ।। buddhirlajjā vasuḥ śāntiḥ siddhiḥ kīrttistrayodaśa ।
patnyarthaṃ pratijagrāha dharmo dākṣāyaṇīḥ prabhuḥ ।। dvārāṇyetāni caivāsya vihitāni svayaṃbhuvā । yānyāḥ śiṣṭā yavīyasya ekādaśa sulocanāḥ ।। satī khyātiśca saṃbhūtiḥ smṛtiḥ prītiḥ kṣamā tathā ।
sannatiścānasūyā ca ūrjā svāhā svadhā tathā ।। tāstadā pratyagṛhṇanta punaranye mahārṣayaḥ । rudro bhṛgurmarīciśca aṅgirāḥ pulahaḥ kratuḥ ।। pulastyo atrirvasiṣṭhaśca pitaro agristathaiva ca ।
satīṃ bhavāya prāyacchatkhyātiṃ ca bhṛgave tathā ।। marīcaye tu saṃbhūtiṃ smṛtimaṅgirase dadau । prītiṃ caiva pulastyāya kṣamāṃ vai pulahāya ca ।। kratave saṃtatiṃ nāma anasūyāṃ tathātraye ।
ūrjāṃ dadau vasiṣṭhāya svāhāṃ caivāgnaye dadau ।। svadhāṃ caiva pitṛbhyastu tāsvapatyāni me śṛṇu । etāḥ sarvā mahābhāgāḥ prajāstvanusṛtāḥ sthitāḥ ।। manvantareṣu sarveṣu yāvadābhūtasaṃplavam ।
śraddhā kāmaṃ prajajñe atha darpo lakṣmī sutaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। dhṛtyāstu niyamaḥ putrastuṣṭyāḥ saṃtoṣa ucyate । puṣṭyā lābhaḥ sutaścāpi medhāputraḥ śrutastathā ।। kriyāyāstanayau proktau damaśca śama eva ca ।
