buddherbodhaḥ sutaścāpi apramādaśca tāvubhau ।। lajjāyā vinayaḥ putro vyavasāyo vasoḥ sutaḥ । kṣemaḥ śānteḥ sutaścāpi sukhaṃ siddhervyajāyata ।। yaśaḥ kīrteḥ sutaścāpi ityete dharmasūnavaḥ ।
kāmasya tu suto harṣo devyāṃ siddhyāṃ vyajāyata ।। ityeṣa vai sukhodarkaḥ sargo dharmasya sāttvikaḥ । jajñe hiṃsā tvadharmādvai nikṛtiṃ cānṛtaṃ ca te ।। nikṛtyanṛtayorjajña bhayaṃ naraka eva ca ।
māyā ca vedanā cāpi mithunadvayametayoḥ ।। mayājjajñe atha vai māyā mṛtyuṃ bhūtāpahāriṇam । vedanāyāṃ tataścāpi jejña duḥkhaṃ tu rauravāt ।। mṛtyorvyādhirjarāśokakrodhāsūyā vijajñire ।
duḥkhottarāḥ smṛtā hyete sarve cādharmalakṣaṇāḥ ।। teṣāṃ bhāryāsti putro vā sarve hyanidhanāḥ smṛtāḥ । ityeṣa tāmasaḥ sargo jajñe dharmaniyā makaḥ ।। prajāḥ sṛceti vyādiṣṭo brahmaṇā nīlalohitaḥ ।
so abhidhyāya satīṃ bhāryāṃ nirmame cātmasaṃbhavān ।। nādhikānna ca hīnāstānmānasānātmanā samān । sahasraṃ ca sahasrāṇāmasṛjatkṛttivāsasaḥ ।। tulyānevātmanā sarvān rūpatejobala śrutaiḥ ।
piṅgalānsaniṣaṅgāṃśca kapardī nīlalohitān ।। viśikhānhīnakeśāṃśca dṛṣṭighnāstānkapālinaḥ । mahārūpānvirūpāṃśca viśvarūpāśca rūpiṇaḥ ।। rathino varmiṇaścaiva dhanvino atha varūthinaḥ ।
sahasraśatabāhūṃśca divyabhaumāntarikṣagān ।। sthūla śīrṣānaṣṭadaṃṣṭrān dvijihvāṃstu trilocanān । annādānpiśitādāṃśca ājyapānsomapostathā ।। atimeḍhrograkāyāṃśca śitikaṇṭhogramanyukān ।
saniṣaṅgatanutrāṃśca dhanvino hyasicarmiṇaḥ ।। āsīnān dhāvataścāpi jṛṃbhataścāpyadhiṣṭhitān । adhīyānāśca japato yuñjato dhyāyatastathā ।। jvalato varṣataścaiva dyotamānānpradhūpitān ।
buddhānbuddhatamāṃścaiva brahmasvān brahmadarśinaḥ ।। nīlagrīvānsahasrākṣān sarvāṃścaiva kṣamācarān । adṛśyānsarvabhūtānāṃ mahāyogānmahaujasaḥ ।। rudato dravataścaiva evaṃ yuktānsahasraśaḥ ।
ayātayāmān sṛjataṃ rudrametānsurottamān ।। dṛṣṭvā brahmābravīdenaṃ māsrākṣīrīdṛśīḥ prajāḥ । na sraṣṭavyātmana stalyā prajā naivādhikā tathā ।। anyāḥ sṛjasva bhadraṃ te prajāstvaṃ mṛtyusaṃyutāḥ ।
nārabhante hi karmāṇi prajā vigatamṛtyavaḥ ।। evasukto abravīdenaṃ nāhaṃ mṛtyujarānvitāḥ । prajāḥ srakṣyāmi bhadraṃ te sthito ahaṃ tvaṃ sṛja prabho ।। ete ye vai mayā sṛṣṭā virūpā nīlalohitāḥ ।
sahasraṃ hi sahasrāṇāmātmano mama niḥsṛtāḥ ।। ete devā bhaviṣyanti rudrā nāma mahābalāḥ । pṛthivyāmantarikṣe ca rudrāṇyastāḥ pariśrutāḥ ।। śatarudre samāmnātā bhaviṣyantīha yajñiyāḥ ।
yajñabhājo bhaviṣyanti sarve devagaṇaiḥ saha ।। manvantareṣu ye devā bhaviṣyantīha chandajāḥ । taiḥ sārddhamijyamānāste sthāsyantīhāyugakṣayāt ।। evamuktastato brahmā mahādevena sa prabhuḥ ।
pratyuvāca tathā bhīmaṃ tdṛṣyamāṇaḥ prajāpatiḥ ।। evaṃ bhavatu bhadraṃ te yathā te vyātdṛtaṃ prabho । brahmaṇā samanu jñāte tataḥ sarvamabhūtkila ।। tataḥ prabhṛti devaḥ sa na prāsūyata vai prajāḥ ।
ūrdhvaretāḥ sthitaḥ sthāṇuryāvadābhūtasaṃplavam ।। yasmātproktaṃ sthito asmīti tasmātsthāṇurbudhaiḥ smṛtaḥ । jñānaṃ tapaśca satyaṃ ca hyaiśvaryaṃ dharma eva ca ।। vairāgyamātmasaṃbodhaḥ kṛtsnānyetāni śaṅkare ।
sarvāndevānṛṣīṃścaiva sametānasuraiḥ saha ।। atyeti tejasā devo mahādevastataḥ smṛtaḥ । atyeti devā naiśvaryādvalena ca mahāsurān ।। jñānena ca munīnsarvānyogādbhūtāni sarvaśaḥ ।
evameva mahādevaḥ sarvadevanamaskṛtaḥ । prajāmanu dyāmāṃ sṛṣṭvā sargādupararāma ha ।। asminkalpe tvayā noktaḥ prādurbhāvo mahātmanaḥ । mahādevasya rudrasya sādhakairṛṣibhiḥ saha ।।
utpattirādisargasya mayā proktā samāsataḥ । vistareṇa pravakṣyāmi nāmāni tanubhiḥ saha ।। patnīṣu janayāmāsa mahādevaḥ sutānbahūna । kalpeṣvanyeṣvatīteṣu hyasminkalpe tu tāñśṛṇu ।।
kalpādāvātmanastulyaṃ sutamadhyāyata prabhuḥ । prādurā sīttatoṅke asya kumāro nīlalohitaḥ ।। ruroda susvaraṃ ghoraṃ nirdahanniva tejasā । dṛṣṭvā rudantaṃ sahasā kumāraṃ nīlalohitam ।।
kiṃ rodiṣi kumāreti brahmā taṃ pratyabhāṣata । so abravīddehi me nāma prathamaṃ tvaṃ pitāmaha ।। rudrastvaṃ deva nāmāsi sa ityukto arudatpunaḥ । kiṃ rodiṣi kumāreti brahmā taṃ pratyabhāṣata ।।
nāma dehi dvitīyaṃ me ityuvāca svayaṃbhuvam । bhavastvaṃ devanāmnāsi ityuktaḥ so arudatpunaḥ ।। kiṃ rodiṣīti taṃ brahmā rudantaṃ pratyuvāca ha । tṛtīyaṃ dehi me nāma ityuktaḥ so abravītpunaḥ ।।
śarvastvaṃ deva nāmnāsi ityuktaḥ so arudatpunaḥ । kiṃ rodiṣīti taṃ brahmā rudantaṃ pratyuvāca ha ।। caturtha dehi me nāma ityuktaḥ so abravītpunaḥ । īśāno devanāmnāsi ityuktaḥ so arudatpunaḥ ।।
kiṃ rodiṣīti taṃ brahmā rudantaṃ punarabravīt । pañcamaṃ nāma dehīti pratyuvāca svayaṃbhuvam ।। paśūnāṃ tvaṃ patirdeva ityuktaḥ so arudatpunaḥ । kiṃ rodiṣīti taṃ brahmā rudantaṃ punarabravīt ।।
ṣaṣṭhaṃ vai dehi me nāma ityuktaḥ pratyuvāca tam । bhīmastvaṃ deva nāmnāsi ityuktaḥ so arudatpunaḥ ।। kiṃ rodiṣīti taṃ brahmā rudantaṃ punarabravīt । saptamaṃ dehi me nāma ityuktaḥ pratyuvāca ha ।।
ugrastvaṃ deva nāmnāsi ityuktaḥ so arudatpunaḥ । taṃ rudantaṃ kumāraṃ tu mārodīriti so abravīt ।। so abravīdaṣṭamaṃ nāma dehi me tvaṃ vibho punaḥ । tvaṃ mahādevanāmāsi ityukto virarāma ha ।।
labdhvā nāmāni caitāni brahmāṇaṃ nīlalohitaḥ । provāca nāmnāmeteṣāṃ sthānāni pradiśeti ha ।। tato visṛṣṭāstanava eṣāṃ nāmnā svayaṃbhuvā । sūryo jalaṃ mahī vāyurva hnirākāśameva ca ।।
dīkṣitā brāhmaṇaścandra ityevaṃ te aṣṭadhā tanuḥ । teṣu pūjyaśca vandyaśca namaskāryaśca yatnataḥ ।। provāca taṃ punarbrahmā kumāraṃ nīlalohitam । yaduktaṃ te mayā pūrvaṃ nāma rudreti vai vibho ।।
tasyādityatanurnāmnaḥ prathamā prathamasya te । ityukte tasya yattejaścakṣustvāsītprakāśakam ।। viveśa tattadādityaṃ tasmādrudro hyasau smṛtaḥ । udyatamastaṃ yantaṃ ca varjayeddarśaneravim ।।
śaśvacca jāyate yasmācchaśvatsaṃtiṣṭhate tu yat । tasmātmūryaṃ na vīkṣeta āyuṣkāmaḥ śuciḥ sadā ।। atītānāgataṃ rudraṃ viprā hyāpyāyayanti yat । ubhe saṃdhye hyupāsīnā gṛṇantaḥ sāmaṛgyajuḥ ।।
udyansa tiṣṭhate ṛkṣu madhyāhne ca yajuḥṣvatha । sāmasvathāparāhṇe tu rudraḥ saṃviśati kramāt ।। tasmādbhavennābhyudito bāhyastamita eva ca । na rudramprati meheta sarvāvasthaṃ kathaṃ cana ।।
evaṃ yuktān dvijān devo rudrastānna hinasti vai । tato apravītpunarbrahmā taṃ devaṃ nīlalohitam ।। dvitīyaṃ nāmadheyaṃ te mayā proktaṃ bhaveti yat । etasyāpo dvitīyā te tanurnāmnā bhavatviti ।।
ityukte tvatha tasyāsīccharīrasthaṃ rasātmakam । viveśa tattadā yastu tasmādāpo bhavaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। yasmādbhavanti bhūtāni tābhyastā bhāvayanti ca । bhavanādrāvanāccaiva bhūtānāmucyate bhavaḥ ।।
tasmānmūtraṃ purīṣaṃ ca nāpsu kurvīta karhicit । na niṣṭhīvennāvagāhennaiva gacchecca maithunam ।। na caitāḥ paricakṣīta vahantyo vā sthitā api । maidhyāmedhyāstvapāmetāstanavo munibhiḥ smṛtāḥ ।।
vivarṇarasagandhāśca varjyā alpāśca sarvaśaḥ । apāṃ yoniḥ samudrastu tasmāttaṃ kāmayanti tāḥ ।। madhyāścaivāmṛtā hyāpo bhavanti prāpya sāgaram । tasmādapo na rundhīta samudraṃ kāmayanti tāḥ ।।
na hinasti bhavo devo ya evaṃ hyapsu vartate । tato abravītpunarbrahmā kumāraṃ nīlalohitam ।। śarveti yattṛtīyaṃ te nāma proktaṃ mayā vibho । tasya bhūmistṛtīyasya tanurnāmnā bhavattviyam ।।
ityukte yatsthiraṃ tasya śarīre hyasthisaṃjñitam । viveśa tattadā bhūmiṃ yasmātsā śarva ucyate ।। tasmātkṛṣṭena kurvīta purīṣaṃ mūtrameva ca । na cchāyāyāṃ tathā mārge svacchāyāyāṃ na mehayet ।।
śiraḥ prāvṛtya kurvīta antardhāya tṛṇairmahīm । evaṃ yo vartate bhūmau śarvastaṃ na hinasti vai ।। tato abravītpunarbrahmā kumāraṃ nīlalohitam । īśāneti caturtha te nāma proktaṃ mayeha yat ।।
caturthasya caturthī tu vāyurnāmnā tanustava । ityukte yaccharīrasthaṃ pañcadhā prāṇasaṃjñitam ।। viveśa tasya tadvāyumīśānastana mārutaḥ । tasmānnainaṃ parivadetpravāntaṃ vāyumīśvaram ।।
yajñairvyavaharantyenaṃ ye vai paricaranti ca । evaṃ yuktaṃ maheśāno naiva devo hinasti tam ।। tato abravītpunarbrahmā taṃ devaṃ dhalamīśvaram । nāma yadvai paśupatirityuktaṃ pañcamaṃ mayā ।।
pañcamī pañcama syaiṣā tanurnāmnāgnirastu te । ityukte yaccharīrasthaṃ tejastasyoṣṇasaṃjñitam ।। viveśa tattadā hyagniṃ tasmātpaśupatistu saḥ । yasmādagniḥ paśuścāsīdyasmātpāti paśūṃśca saḥ ।।
tasmātpaśupatestasya tanuragnirnirucyate । tasmādamedyaṃ na dahenna ca pādau pratāpayet ।। adhastānnopadadhyācca na cainamatilaṅghayet । nainaṃ paśupatirdeva evaṃ yuktaṃ hinasti vai ।।
tato abravītpunarbrahmā taṃ devaṃ śvetapiṅgalam । ṣaṣṭaṃ nāma mayā proktaṃ tava bhīmeti yatprabho ।। ākāśaṃ tasya nāmnastu tanuḥ ṣaṣṭhī bhavatviti । ityukte suṣiraṃ tasya śarīrasthamabhūcca yat ।।
viveśa tattadākāśaṃ tasmādbhīmasya sā tanuḥ । yadākāśe smṛto devastasmānnā saṃvṛtaḥ kvacit ।। kuryānmūtraṃ purīṣaṃ vā na bhuñjīta pibenna vā । maithunaṃ vāpi na careducchiṣṭāni ca notkṣipet ।।
na hinasti ca taṃ devo yo bhīme hyevamācaret । tato abravītpunarbrahmā taṃ devaṃ sabalaṃ prabhum ।। saptamaṃ yanmayā proktaṃ nāmogreti tava prabho । tasya nāmnastanustubhyaṃ dvijo bhavati dīkṣitaḥ ।।
evamukte tu yattasya caitanyaṃ vai śarīragam । viveśa dīkṣitaṃ tadvai brāhmaṇaṃ somayājinam ।। tāvatkālaṃ smṛto vipra ugro devastu dīkṣitaḥ । tasmānnemaṃ parivadennāślīlaṃ cāsya kīrttayet ।।
te harantyasya pāpmānaṃ ye vai parivadanti tam । evaṃ yuktān dvijānugro devastānna hinasti vai ।। tatobravītpunarbrahmā taṃ devaṃ bhāskaradyutim । aṣṭamaṃ nāma yat proktaṃ mahādeveti te mayā ।।
tasya nāmno aṣṭamasyāstu tanustubhyaṃ tu candramāḥ । ityukte yanmana stasya saṃkalpakamabhūtprabhoḥ ।। viveśa taccandramasaṃ mahādevastataḥ śaśī । tasmādvibhāvyate hyeṣa mahādevastu candramāḥ ।।
amāvāsyāṃ na vai chindyādvṛkṣagulmauṣadhīrdvijaḥ । mahādevaḥ smṛtaḥ somastasyātmā hyauṣadhīgaṇaḥ ।। evaṃ yo varttate caiha sadā parvaṇi parvaṇi । na hanti taṃ mahādevo ya evaṃ veda taṃ prabhum ।।
gopāyati divādityaḥ prajā naktaṃ tu candramāḥ । ekarātrau sameyātāṃ sūryā candramasāvubhau ।। amāvāsyāniśāyāṃ tu tasyāṃ yuktaḥ sādā bhavet । rudrāviṣṭaṃ sarvamidaṃ tanubhirnnāmabhiśca ha ।।
ekākī caścaratyeṣa sūryo asau rudra ucyate । sūryasya yatprakāśena vīkṣante cakṣuṣā prajāḥ ।। muktātmā saṃsthito rudraḥ pibatyaṃbho gabhastibhiḥ । adyate pīyate caiva hyannapānādikāmyayā ।।
tanuraṃbūdbhavā sā vai deheṣvevopacīyate । yayā dhatte prajāḥ sarvāḥ sthirībhūtena tejasā ।। pārthivī sā tanustasya sādhvī dhārayate prajāḥ । yā ca sthitā śarīreṣu bhūtānāṃ prāṇavṛttibhiḥ ।।
vātātmikā tu caiśānī sā prāṇaḥ prāṇināmiha । pītāśitāni pacati bhūtānāṃ jaṭhareṣviha ।। tanuḥ pāśupatī tasya pācakaḥ so agnirucyate । yānīha śuṣirāṇi syurdeheṣvantargatāni vai ।।
vāyoḥ saṃcaraṇārthāni bhīmā sā procyate tanuḥ । vaitānyādīkṣitānāṃ tu yā sthitirbrahmavādinām ।। tanurugrātmikā sā tu tenogro dīkṣitaḥ smṛtaḥ । yattu saṃkalpakaṃ tasya prajāsviha samāsthitam ।।
sā tanurmānasī tasya candramāḥ prāṇiṣu sthitaḥ । navonavo yo bhavati jāyamānaḥ punaḥpunaḥ ।। pīyate asau yathākālaṃ vibudhaiḥ pitṛbhiḥ saha । mahādevo amṛtātmā sa candramā ammayaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।
tasya yā prathamā nāmnā tanū raudrī prakīrttitā । patnī suvarccalā tasyāḥ putraścāsya śanaiścaraḥ ।। bhavasya yā dvitīyā tu āpo nāmnā tanuḥ smṛtā । tasyā dhātrī smṛtā patnī putraśca uśanā smṛtaḥ ।।
śarvasya yā tṛtīyasya nāmno bhūmistanuḥ smṛtā । tasyāḥ patnī vikeśī tu putro asyāṅgārakaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। īśānasya caturthasya nāmnā vātastanustu yā । tasyāḥ patnī śivā nāma putraścāsyā manojavaḥ ।।
avijñātagatiścaiva dvau putrau cānilasya tu । nāmnā paśupateryā tu tanuragnirdvijaiḥ smṛtā ।। tasyāḥ patnī smṛtā svāhā skandastasyāḥ sutaḥ smṛtaḥ । nāmnā ṣaṣṭhasya yā bhīmā tanurākāśamucyate ।।
diśaḥ patnyaḥ smṛtāstasya svargaścāpi sutaḥ smṛtaḥ । agrā tanuḥ saptamī yā dīkṣito brāhmaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। dīkṣā patnī smṛtā tasyāḥ saṃtānaḥ putra ucyate । nāmnāṣṭamasya mahastanuryā candramāḥ smṛtaḥ ।।
tasya vai rohiṇī patnī putrastasya budhaḥ smṛtaḥ । ityetāstanavastasya nāmabhiḥ saha kīrtitāḥ ।। tāsu vandyo namasyaśca pratināmatanūṣu vai । sūryepsūrvyāṃ tathā vāyāvagnau vyomnyatha dīkṣite ।।
bhaktaistathā candramasi bhattayā vandyastu nāmabhiḥ । evaṃ yo vetti taṃ devaṃ tanubhirnāmabhiśca ha ।। prajāvāneti sāyujyamīśvarasya bhavasya saḥ । ityetadvo mayā proktaṃ guhyaṃ bhīmāsya yadyaśaḥ ।।
śanno astu dvipade viprāḥ śanno astu ca catuṣpade । etatproktamidānīṃ ca tanūnāṃ nāmabhi saha । mahādevasya devasya bhṛgostu śṛṇuta prajāḥ ।। bhṛgoḥ khyātirvijajñe vai īśvarau sukhaduḥkhayoḥ ।
śubhāśubhapradātārau sarvaprāṇabhṛtāmiha ।। devau dhātṛvidhātārau manvantaravicāriṇau । tayārjyeṣṭhā tu bhaginī devī śrīrlokabhāvinī ।। sā tu nārāyaṇaṃ devaṃ pati māsadya śobhanā ।
nārāyaṇātmajau tasyāṃ balonmādauvyajāyatām ।। balasya tejaḥ putrastu unmādasya tu saṃśayaḥ । tasyānye mānasāḥ putrā āsan vyomavicāriṇaḥ ।। ye vahanti vimānāni devānāṃ puṇyakarmaṇām ।
merukalpe smṛte bhārye vidhāturdhātureva ca ।। āyatirniyatiścaiva tayoḥ putrau dṛḍhavratau । prāṇaścaiva mṛkaṇḍaśca brahmakośau sanātanau ।। manasvinyāṃ mṛkaṇḍasya mārkaṇḍeyo babhūva ha ।
suto vedaśirāstasya dhūmrapatnyāmajāyata ।। pīvaryāṃ vedaśirasaḥ putrā vaśakarāḥ smṛtāḥ । mārkaṇḍeyāḥ samākhyātā ṛṣayo vedapāragāḥ ।। prāṇasya puṇḍarīkāyāṃ dyutimānātmajo abhavat ।
unnataścadyutimataḥ svanavātaśca tāvubhau ।। tayoḥ putrāśca pautrāśca bhārgavāṇāṃ parasparāt । svāyaṃbhuventare atītā marīceḥ śṛṇuta prajāḥ ।। patnī marīceḥ saṃbhūtirvijajñe hyātmasaṃbhaṃvam ।
prajāpateḥ pūrṇamāsaṃ kanyāścemā nibodhata ।। kṛṣirvṛṣṭistviṣā caiva tathā copacitiḥ śubhā । pūrṇamāsaḥ sarasvatyāṃ putrau dvāvudapādayat ।। virajaṃ caiva dharmiṣṭhaṃ parvaśaṃ caiva tāvubhau ।
virajasyātmajo vidvān sudhāmā nāma viśrutaḥ ।। sudhāmā sa tu vairājaḥ prācīṃ diśamupā śritaḥ । lokapālaḥ sa dharmātmā gaurīputraḥ pratāpavān ।। parvaśaḥ parvagaṇanāṃ praviṣṭaḥ sa mahāyaśāḥ ।
parvaśaḥ parvaśāyāṃ tu janayā māsa vai sutau ।। yajurdhāma ca dhīmantaṃ staṃbhakāśyapameva ca । tayorgotrakarau putrau jātau saṃnyāsaniścitau ।। smṛtastvaṃ girasaḥ patnī jajñe sā hyātmasaṃbhavān ।
putro kanyāścatasraśca puṇyāstā lokaviśrutāḥ ।। sinīvālī kuhūścaiva rākā cānumatistathā । tathaiva bharatāgniṃ ca kīrtimantaṃ ca tāvubhau ।। agneḥ putraṃ ca parjanyaṃ sadvatī suṣuve tathā ।
hiraṇyaromā parjanyo mārīcyāmudapadyata ।। ābhūtasaṃplavasthāyī lokapālaḥ sa vai smṛtaḥ । yajñe kīrttimataścāpi dhenukā vītakalmaṣau ।। cariṣṇuṃ dhṛtimantaṃ ca ubhāvaṅgirasāṃ varau ।
tayoḥ putrāśca pautrāśca atītā vai sahasraśaḥ ।। anasūyā vijajñe vai pañcātreyānakalmaṣān । kanyāṃ caiva śrutiṃ nāma mātā śaṅkhapadasya sā ।। kardasasya tu patnī sā paulahasya prajāpateḥ ।
satyanetraśca havyaśca āpo mūrttiḥ śanaiścaraḥ ।। somaśca pañcamasteṣāmāsītsvāyaṃbhuventare । yāmadevaissahātītāḥ pañcātreyāḥ prakīrttitāḥ ।। teṣāṃ putrāśca pautrāśca ātreyāṇāṃ mahātmanām ।
svāyaṃbhuve antare atītāḥ śataśo atha sahasraśaḥ ।। prītyāṃ pulastyabhāryāyāṃ dānā gnistatsuto abhavat । pūrvajanmani so agastyaḥ smṛtaḥ svāyaṃbhuve antare ।। madhyamo devabāhuśca atrināmā ca te trayaḥ ।
svamā yavīyasī teṣāṃ sadvatī nāma viśrutā ।। parjanyajananī śubhrā patnī cāgneḥ smṛtā śubhā । paulastyasya ca brahmarṣeḥ prītiputrasya dhīmataḥ ।। dānācca suṣuve patnī sujaṅghī caṃ bahūnsutān ।
paulastyā iti vikhyātāḥ smṛtāḥ svāyaṃbhuve antare ।। kṣamā tu suṣuve putrānpulastyasya prajāpateḥ । tretāgnivarcasaḥ sarve yeṣāṃ kīrttiḥ pratiṣṭhitā ।। kardamaścorvarīvāṃśca sahiṣṇuśceti te trayaḥ ।
ṛṣiḥ kanakapīṭhaśca śubhā kanyā ca pīvarī ।। kardamasya śrutiḥ patnī ātreyyajanayatsvayam । putraṃ śaṅkhapadaṃ nāma kanyāṃ kāmyāṃ tathaiva ca ।। sa vai śaṅkhapadaḥ śrīmāṃllokapālaḥ prajāpatiḥ ।
dakṣiṇasyāṃ diśi rataḥ kāmyā dattā priyavrate ।। kāmyā priyavratāllebhe svāyaṃbhuvasamānsutān । daśa kanyādvayaṃ caiva yaiḥ kṣatraṃ sampravarttitam ।। putraṃ kanakapīṭhasya sahiṣṇuṃ nāma viśrutam ।
yaśodharā vijajñe vai kāmadevaṃ sumadhyāmā ।। kratoḥ kratusamānpu trān vijajñe saṃnatiḥ śubhān । teṣāṃ na bhāryā putro vā sarve te urddharetasaḥ ।। tāni ṣaṣṭisahasrāṇi vālakhilyā iti śrutāḥ ।
aruṇasyāgrato yānti parivārya divākaram ।। ābhūtasaṃplavātsarvepataṅgasahacāriṇaḥ । svasārau tadyavīyasyau puṇyā satyavatī cate ।। parvaśasya snuve te vai pūrṇamāsa sutasya tu ।
ūrjāyāṃ tu vasiṣṭhasya vāsiṣṭhāḥ sapta jajñire ।। jyāyasī ca sutā teṣāṃ puṇḍarīkā sumadhyamā । jananī sā dyutimataḥ prāṇasya mahiṣī priyāḥ ।। tasyāstu ye yavīyāṃso vāsiṣṭhāḥ sapta viśrutāḥ ।
rakṣo garttorddhabā huśca savanaḥ pavanaśca yaḥ ।। sutapāḥ saṃkurityete sarve saptarṣayaḥ samṛtāḥ । ratno varāṅgyajanayanmārkaṇḍeyī yaśasvinī ।। pratīcyāṃ diśi rājānaṃ ketumantaṃ prajāpatim ।
gotrāṇi nāmabhisteṣāṃ vāsiṣṭhānāṃ mahātmanām ।। svāyaṃbhuve antaretītānyagnestu śṛṇuta prajāḥ । ityeṣa ṛṣisargastu sānubandhaḥ prakīrttitaḥ ।। vistareṇānupūrvyācca agnervakṣyāmyataḥ param ।
yo asāvagne rabhimānī smṛtaḥ svāyaṃbhuve antare । brahmaṇo mānasaḥ putrastasmātsvāhā vyajāyata ।। pāvakaṃ pavamānaṃ ca śuciragniśca yaḥ smṛtaḥ । nirmathyaḥ pavamānastu vaidyutaḥ pāvakaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।
śuciḥ saurastu vijñeyaḥ svāhāputrāstu te trayaḥ । nirmathyaḥ pavamānastu śuciḥ saurastu yaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। abyonirvaidyutaścaiva teṣāṃ sthānāni tāni vai । pavamānātmajaścaiva kavyavāhana ucyate ।।
pāvakiḥ saharakṣastu havyavāhaḥ śuceḥ sutaḥ । devānāṃ havyavāho agniḥ pitṝṇāṃ kavyavāhanaḥ ।। saha rakṣo asurāṇāṃ tu trayāṇāṃ tu trayo agnayaḥ । eteṣāṃ putrapautrāstu catvāriṃśanna vaiva tu ।।
vakṣyāmi nāmabhisteṣāṃ pravibhāgaṃ pṛthakpṛthak । viśrupto laukiko agnistu prathamo brahmaṇaḥ sutaḥ ।। brahmo dattāgnisa tputro bharato nāma viśrutaḥ । vaiśvānaraḥ sutastasya vahan havyaṃ samāḥ śatam ।।
saṃbhṛto atharvaṇā pūrvamedhitiḥ puṣkarodadhau । sotharvā laukiko agnistu darpahātharvaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। atharvā tu bhṛgurjajñe hyagnirātharvaṇaḥ smṛtaḥ । tasmātsa laukiko agnistu dadhyaṅṅātharvaṇo mataḥ ।।
ātharvaḥ pavamānastu nirmathyaḥ kavibhiḥ smṛtaḥ । sa jñeyo gārhapatyo agnistasya putradvayaṃ smṛtam ।। śaṃsyastvāha vanīyo agneḥ smṛto yo havyavāhanaḥ । dvitīyastu sutaḥ proktaḥ śuko agniryaḥ praṇīyate ।।
tathā savyāpasavyau ca śaṃsyasyāgneḥ sutāvubhau । śaṃsyastu ṣoḍaśa nadīścakame havyavāhanaḥ ।। yo sāvāhavanīyo agnirabhimānī dvijaiḥ smṛtaḥ । kāverīṃ kṛṣṇaveṇāṃ ca narmadāṃ yamunāṃ tathā ।।
godāvarīṃ vitastāṃ ca candrabhāgāmirāvatīm । vipāśāṃ kauśikīñcaiva śatadrūṃ sarayūṃ tathā ।। sītāṃ sarasvatīṃ caiva hrādinīṃ pāvanīntathā । tāsu ṣoḍaśadhāmānaṃ pravibhajya pṛthakpṛthak ।।
ātmānaṃ vyadadhāttāsu dhiṣṇīṣvatha babhūva saḥ । kṛttikācāriṇī dhiṣṇī jajñire tāśca dhiṣṇayaḥ ।। dhiṣṇīṣu jajñire yasmād dhiṣṇayastena kīrttitāḥ । ityete vai nadīputrā dhiṣṇīṣvevaṃ vijajñire ।।
teṣāṃ viharaṇīyā ye upastheyāśca ye agnayaḥ । tāñśṛṇudhvaṃ samāsena kīrtyamānānyathātatham ।। vibhuḥ pravāhaṇo gnīdhrastatrasthā dhiṣṇayo apare । vidhīyante yathāsthānaṃ sūtyāhe savane kramāt ।।
anuddeśya nivāsyānāmagnīnāṃ śṛṇuta kramam । samrāḍagni kṛśānuryo dvitīyoṃ'taravedikaḥ ।। samrāḍagnamukhānaṣṭau upatiṣṭhanti tān dvijān । pariṣatpavamānastu dvitīya so anudiśyate ।।
pratalkānyo nabhonāma catvaresau vibhāvyate । havyastato hyasaṃmṛṣṭaḥ śāmitre agnau vibhāvyate ।। ṛtudhāmā ca sujyotirauduṃbaryaḥ prakīrtyate । viśvavyacāḥ samudro agnirbrahmasthāne sa kīrtyate ।।
brahmajyotirvasurdhāmā brahmasthāne sa ucyate । acaukapādupastho yaḥ sa vai śālāsukhīyakaḥ ।। anuheśyo hyahirbudhnyo so agrirgṛhapatiḥ smṛtaḥ । śaṃsyasyaite sutāḥ sarve upastheyā dvijaiḥ smṛtāḥ ।।
tato viharaṇīyāṃśca vakṣyāmyaṣṭau ca tatsutān । vibhuḥ pravāhaṇo agnīdhrasteṣāṃ dhiṣṇyastathā pare ।। vidhīyante yathāsthānaṃ sautye ahni savane kramāt । hotrīyastu smṛte hyagnirvahniryo havyavāhanaḥ ।।
praśānto agniḥ pracetāstu dvitīyaścātra nāmakaḥ । tato agnirvaiśvadevastu brāhmaṇācchaṃsirucyate ।। uśigagniḥ kaviryastu poto agniḥ sa vibhāvyate । āvāriragnirvābhārirvaiṣṭhīyaḥ sa vibhāvyate ।।
avasphūrjo vivasvāṃstu āsthāṃścaiva sa ucyate । aṣṭamaḥ sudhyuragniryomārjālīyaḥ sa ucyante ।। dhiṣṇyāvāharaṇā hyete sautyehnījyanta vai dvijaiḥ । apāṃ yoniḥ smṛto asau sa hyapsunāmā vibhāvyate ।।
tato yaḥ pāvako nāmnā abjo yo garbha ucyate । agniḥ so avabhṛthe jñeyo varuṇena sahejyate ।। tdṛcchayastatsuto hyagnirjaṭhare yo nṛṇāṃ pacan । mṛtyumāñ jāṭharasyāgnervidvānāgniḥ sutaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।
parasparotthitaḥ so agnirbhūtānīha vinirdahet । putrastvagnermanyumato ghoraḥ saṃvartakaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। pibannavaḥ sa vasati samudre vaḍavāmukhaḥ । samudravāsinaḥ putraḥ sāharakṣo vibhāvyate ।।
saharakṣasutaḥ kṣāmo gṛhāṇāṃ dahate nṛṇām । kravyādagniḥ sutastasya puruṣānatti yo mṛtān ।। ityete pāvakasyāgneḥ putrā eva prakīrttitāḥ । tataḥ śucistu vai sauro gandharvairāyurāhutaḥ ।।
mathito yastvaraṇyāṃ ca so agniragniṃ samindhati । āyurnāmnā tu bhagavānasau yastu praṇīyate ।। āyuṣo mahiṣaḥ putraḥ sahaso nāma tatsutaḥ । pākayajñeṣvabhīmānī sognistu sahasaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।
putraśca sahasasyāgneradbhutaḥ sa mahāyaśāḥ । vividhiścādbhutasyāpi putro agnestumāhānsmṛtaḥ ।। prāyaścitteṣvabhīmānī hutaṃ bhuṅkte haviḥ sadā । vividhestu suto hyarkka stasya cāgneḥ sutā ime ।।
anīkavān vājasṛk ca rakṣohā caṣṭikṛttathā । surabhirvasurannādo praviṣṭo yaḥ sa rukamarāṭ ।। śuceragneḥ prajā hyeṣā vahnayaśca caturddaśa । ityete cāgnayaḥ proktāḥ praṇīyantedhvareṣu vai ।।
ādisarge vyatītā vai yāmaiḥ saha surottamaiḥ । svāyaṃbhuve antare pūrvamagnayastebhimāninaḥ ।। ete viharaṇīyeṣu cetanācetaneṣu vai । sthānābhimānino loke prāgāsanhavyavāhanāḥ ।।
kāmyanai mittikā yajñeṣvete karmasvavasthitāḥ । pūrvamanvataṃre atītāḥ śukairyāgaiśca taiḥ saha ।। devairmahātmabhiḥ puṇyaiḥ prathamasyāntare manoḥ । ityetāni majoktāni sthānāni sthāninaśca ha ।।
taireva tu prasaṃkhyātamatītānāgateṣviha । sanvantareṣu sarveṣu lakṣaṇaṃ jātavedasām ।। sarve tapasvino hyete sarve brahmabhṛtastathā । prajānāṃ patayaḥ sarve jyotiṣmantaśca te smṛtāḥ ।।
svārociṣādiṣu jñeyāḥ sāvarṇyaṃ teṣu saptasu । manvantareṣu sarveṣu nāmarūpaprayojanaiḥ ।। varttante varttamānaiśca yāmaidevaiḥ sahāgnayaḥ । anāgataiḥ suraiḥ sārddhaṃ vartsyante anāgatāgnayaḥ ।।
ityeṣa nicayo agnīnāmanukrānto yathākramam । vistareṇānupurvyā ca pitṝṇāṃ vakṣyate punaḥ ।। brahmaṇaḥ sṛjataḥ putrān pūrvaṃ svāyaṃbhuveṃ'tare । gātrebhyo jajñire tasya manuṣyāsuradevatāḥ ।।
pitṛvanmanyamānāstaṃ jajñire pitaro api ca । teṣāṃ nisargaḥ prāguktaḥ samāsācchruyatāṃ punaḥ ।। devāsuramanuṣyāṃśca sṛṣṭvā brahmābhyamanyata । pitṛvanmanyamānā vai jajñire asyopapakṣataḥ ।।
madhvādayaḥ ṣaḍṛtavaḥ pitṝṃstānparicakṣate । ṛtavaḥ pitaro devā ityeṣā vaidikī śrutiḥ ।। manvantareṣu sarveṣu hyatītānāgateṣu vai । ete svāyaṃbhuve pūrvamutpannāścāntare śubhe ।।
agniṣvāttā smṛtā nāmnā tathā barhiṣadaśca vai । ayajvānastathā teṣāmāsanye gṛhamedhinaḥ ।। agniṣvāttā smṛtāste vai pitaro nāhitāgnayaḥ । yajvānasteṣu ye tvāsanpitaraḥ somapīthinaḥ ।।
smṛtā barhiṣadaste vai pitara stvagnihotriṇaḥ । ṛtavaḥ pitaro devāḥ śāstre asminniścayaṃ gatāḥ ।। madhumādhavau rasau jñeyau śuciśukrau ca śuṣmiṇau । nabhāścaiva nabhasyaśca jīvāvetāpudātdṛtau ।।
iṣaścaiva tathorjaśca svadhāvantāvṛdātdṛtau । sahaścaiva sahasyaśca ghorāvetāpudātdṛtau ।। tapāścaiva tapasyaśca manyumantau tu śaiśirau । kālāvasthāsu ṣaṭsvete māsākhyā vai vyavasthitāḥ ।।
ime ca ṛtavaḥ proktāścetanācetaneṣu vai । ṛtavo brahmaṇaḥ putrā vijñeyāste abhimāninaḥ ।। māsārddhamāsasthāneṣu sthāninau ṛtavo matāḥ । sthānānāṃ vyatirekeṇa jñeyāḥ sthānāgimāninaḥ ।।
ahorātrāṇi māsāśca ṛtavaścāyanāni ca । saṃvatsarāśca sthānāni kāmākhyā hyabhimāninām ।। eteṣu sthānino ye tu kālāvasthā vyavasthitāḥ । tatsatattvāstadātmānastānvakṣyāmi nibodhata ।।
pārvaṇyasti thayaḥ saṃdhyāḥ pakṣā māsārddhasaṃmitāḥ । nimeṣāśca kalāḥ kaṣṭhā muhurttā divasāḥ kṣayāḥ ।। dvāvarddhamāsau māsastu dvau māsāvṛ turucyate । ṛtutrayaṃ cāpyayanaṃ dve ayane dakṣiṇottare ।।
saṃvatsaraḥ sametaśca sthānānyetāni sthāninām । ṛtavastu nimeḥ putrā vijñeyāste tathaiva ṣaṭ ।। ṛtuputrāḥ smṛtāḥ pañca prajāḥ svārtavalakṣaṇāḥ । yasmāccaivārttavebhyastu jāyante sthāṇu jaṅgamāḥ ।।
ārtavāḥ pitarastasmādṛtavaśca pitāmahāḥ । sametāstu prasūyante prajāścaiva prajāpateḥ ।। tasmātsmṛtaḥ prajānāṃ vai vatsaraḥ prapitāmahaḥ । sthāneṣu sthānino hyete sthānātmānaḥ prakīrttitāḥ ।।
tadākhyāstatsasattvāśca tadātmānaśca te smṛtāḥ । prajāpatiḥ smṛto yastu sa tu saṃvatsaro mataḥ ।। saṃvatsarasuto hyagni ṛta ityucyate budhaiḥ । ṛtāttu ṛtavo yasmājjajñire ṛtavastataḥ ।।
māsāḥ ṣaḍartavo jñeyāsteṣāṃ pañcartavāḥ smṛtāḥ । dvipadāṃ catuṣpadāṃ caiva pakṣiṇāṃ sarvatāmapi ।। sthāvarāṇāṃ ca pañcānāṃ puṣpaṃ kālārttavaṃ smṛtam । ṛtutvamārtavatvaṃ ca pitṛtvaṃ ca prakīrttitam ।।
ityete pitaro jñeyā ṛtavaścārtavāśca ye । sarvabhūtāni tebhyo yadṛtukālādvijajñire ।। tasmādete hi pitara ārtavā iti naḥ śrutam । manvantareṣviha tvete sthitāḥ kālabhimāninaḥ ।।
kāryakāraṇayuktāstu e śvaryādvyāpya saṃsthitāḥ । sthānābhimānino hyete tiṣṭhantīha prasaṃgamāt ।। agniṣvāttā barhiṣadaḥ pitaro vividhāḥ punaḥ । jajñe svadhāpitṛbhyastu dve kanye lokaviśrute ।।
menā ca dhāraṇī caiva yābhyāṃ dhatamidaṃ jagat । te ubhe brahmavādinyau yoginyau caiva te ubhe ।। pitaraste nije kanye dharmārthaṃ pradaduḥ śubhe । agniṣvāttāstu ye proktāsteṣāṃ menā tu mānasī ।।
dhāraṇī mānasī caiva kanyā barhiṣadāṃ smṛtā । merostāṃ dhāraṇīṃ nāma patnyarthaṃ vā sṛjan ghubhām ।। pitaraste barhiṣadaḥ smṛtā ye somapāyinaḥ । agniṣvāttāstu tāṃ menā patnī himavate daduḥ ।।
upahūtā smṛtā ye vai taddauhitrānnibodhata । menā himavataḥ patnī mainākaṃ sā vyajāyata ।। gaṅgāṃ saridvarāṃ caiva patnī yā lavaṇodadheḥ । mainākasyā tmajaḥ kraucaḥ kraiñcadvīpo yataḥ smṛtaḥ ।।
merostu dhāraṇī patnī divyauṣadhisamanvitam । mandaraṃ suṣuve putraṃ tisraḥ kanyāśca viśrutāḥ ।। velāṃ ca niyatiṃ caiva tṛtīyāṃ cāyatiṃ viduḥ । dhātuścaivāyatiḥ patnī vidhāturniyatiḥ smṛtā ।।
svāyaṃ bhuveṃ'tare pūrvaṃ yayorvai kīrttitāḥ prajāḥ । suṣuve sāgarādvelā kanyāmekāmaninditām ।। savarṇāṃ nāma sāmudrīṃ patnīṃ prācīnabarhiṣaḥ । savarṇāyāṃ sutā jātā daśa prācīnabarhiṣaḥ ।।
sarve pracetaso nāma dhanurvedasya pāragāḥ । teṣāṃ svāyaṃbhuvo dakṣaḥ putratvaṃ jagmi vānprabhuḥ ।। trayaṃbakasyābhiśāpena cākṣuṣasyātare manoḥ । etacchutvā tataḥ sūtamapṛcchacchāṃśapāyaniḥ ।।
utpannaḥ sa kathaṃ dakṣo hyabhiśāpādbhavasya tu । cākṣuṣasyāntare pūrvaṃ tannaḥ prabrūhi pṛcchatām ।। ityuktaḥ kathayāmāsa sūto dakṣāśrayāṃ kathām । śāṃśapāyanimāmantrya tryaṃbakācchāpakāraṇam ।।
dakṣasyāsansutā hyaṣṭau kanyā yāḥ kīrttitā mayā । svebhyo gṛhebhya ānāyya tāḥ pitābhyarcayadgṛhe ।। tatastvabhyarcitāḥ sarvā nyavasaṃstāḥ piturgṛhe । tāsāṃ jyeṣṭhā satī nāma patnī yā tryaṃbakasya vai ।।
nājuhāvātmajāṃ tāṃ vai dakṣo rudramabhidviṣan । akarotsaṃnatiṃ dakṣe na kadācinmaheśvaraḥ ।। jāmātā śvaśure tasminsvabhāvāttejasi sthitaḥ । tato jñātvā satī sarvāḥ nyavasaṃstāḥ piturgṛhe ।।
jagāma sāpyanāhūtā satī tatsva piturgṛham । tābhyo hīnāṃ pitā cakre satyāḥ pūjāmasaṃmatām ।। tato abravītsā pitaraṃ devī krodhādamarṣitā । yavīyasībhyo pyadhamāṃ pūjāṃ kṛtvā mama prabho ।।
asatkṛtya pitarmāṃ tvaṃ kṛtavānasi garhitam । ahaṃ jyeṣṭhā variṣṭhā ca tvaṃ māṃ satkartumarha si ।। evamukto abravīdenāṃ dakṣaḥ saṃraktalocanaḥ । tvattaḥ śreṣṭhāvariṣṭhāśca pūjyā bālāḥ sutā mama ।।
tāsāṃ caiva tu bhartāra ste me bahumātāḥ sati । brahmiṣṭhāḥ sutapaskāśca mahāyogāḥ sudhārmikāḥ ।। guṇaiścaivādhikāḥ ślāghyāḥ sarve te tryaṃbakātsati । vasiṣṭho atriḥ pulastyaśca hyaṅgirā pulahaḥ kratuḥ ।।
bhṛgurmarīciśca tathā śraiṣṭhā jāmātaro mama । yasmānmāṃ sparddhate śarvaḥ sadā caivāvamanyate ।। tena tvāṃ na vibhūṣomi pratikūlo hi me bhavaḥ । ityuktavāṃstadā dakṣaḥ saṃpramūḍhena cetasā ।।
śāpārthamātmanaścaiva ye coktāḥ paramarṣayaḥ । tathoktā pitaraṃ sā vai kruddhā devīdama bravīt ।। vāṅmanaḥ karmabhiryasmādaduṣṭāṃ māṃ vigarhase । tasmāttyajāmyahamimaṃ dehaṃ tāta tavātmajam ।।
tatastenāvamānena satī duḥkhādamarṣitā । abravīdvacanaṃ devī namaskṛtya svayaṃbhuve ।। yatrāhamupapadye ca punardehena bhāsvatā । tatrāpyahamasaṃbhūtā saṃbhūtā dhārmikādapi ।।
gaccheyaṃ dharmapatnītvaṃ tryaṃbakasyaiva dhīmataḥ । tatraivātha samāsīnā yuktātmānaṃ samādadhe ।। dhārayāmāsa cāgneyīṃ dhāraṇāṃ manasātmanaḥ । tata ātmasamuttho asyā vāyunā samudīritaḥ ।
sarvāgebhyo viniḥsṛtya vahnistāṃ bhasmasātkarot ।। tadupaśrutya nidhanaṃ satyā devo atha śūlabhṛt । saṃvādaṃ ca tayorbuddhā yāthātathyena śaṅkaraḥ । dakṣasya ca ṛṣīṇāṃ ca cukopa bhagavānprabhuḥ ।।
sarveṣāmeva lokānāṃ bhūrlokastvādirucyate । taṃ sadā dhārayiṣyāmi nideśātparameṣṭhinaḥ ।। asyāṃ kṣitau dhṛtā lokāḥ sarve tiṣṭhanti bhāsvarāḥ । tānahaṃ dhārayā mīha satataṃ ca tadājñayā ।।
cāturvarṇyaṃ hi devānāṃ te cāpyekatra bhuñjate । nāhaṃ taiḥ saha bhokṣaye vai tato dāsyanti te pṛthak ।। yasmādavamatā dakṣa matkṛte anāgasā satī । praśastāścetarāḥ sarvāḥ svasutā bhartṛbhiḥ saha ।।
tasmā dvaivasvate prāpte punarete maharṣayaḥ । utpatsyante dvitīye vai mama yajña hyayonicāḥ ।। hute vai brahmaṇā śukre cākṣuṣasyātare manoḥ । abhivyāhṛtya sarvāṃstān dakṣaṃ caivāśapatpunaḥ ।।
bhavitā mānuṣo rājā cākṣuṣasya tvamanvaye । prācīnabarhiṣaḥ pautraḥ putraścaiva prace tasām ।। dakṣa eveha nāmnā tu māriṣāyāṃ janiṣyasi । kanyāyāṃ śākhināṃ tvaṃ vai prāpte vaivasvateṃ'tare ।।
vighnaṃ tatrā pyahaṃ tubhyamācariṣyāmi durmate । dharmmayukte ca te kārye ekasmiṃstu durāsade ।। tadupaśrutya dakṣastu rudraṃ so abhya śapatpunaḥ । yasmāttvaṃ matkṛte aniṣṭamṛṣīṇāṃ kṛtavānasi ।
tasmātsārddhaṃ surairyajñe na tvāṃ yakṣyanti vai dvijāḥ ।। hutvā'hutiṃ tava krūra hyapaḥ sprakṣyanti karmasu । ihaiva vatsyasi tathā divaṃ hitvā yugakṣayāt ।। tato devaiḥsa taiḥ sārddhaṃ nejyate pṛthasijyate ।
tato abhivyāhṛto dakṣo rudreṇāmitatejasā ।। svāyaṃbhuvīṃ tanuṃ tyaktvā utpanno mānuṣeṣviha ।। jñātvā gṛhapatirdakṣo yajñānā mīśvaraṃ prabhum । samasteneha yajñena so ayajaddaivataiḥ saha ।।
atha devī satī yā tu prāpte vaivasvateṃ'tare । menāyāṃ tāmumāṃ devīṃ janayāmāsa śailarāṭ ।। yā tu devī satī pūrvamāsītpaścādumābhavat । sadā patnī bhavasyaiṣā na tayā mucyate bhavaḥ ।।
marīcaṃ kaśyapaṃ devī yathāditiranuvratā । yathā nārāyaṇaṃ śrīśca maghavataṃ śacī yathā ।। viṣṇuṃ kīrtī ruṣā mūryaṃ vasiṣṭhaṃ cāpyarundhatī । naitāstu vijahatyetān bhartṝn devyaḥ kadācana ।।
āvartamānāḥ kalpeṣu jāyante taiḥ punaḥ saha । evaṃ prācetaso dakṣo jajñe vai cākṣuṣeṃ'tare ।। daśabhyastu pracetobhyo māriṣāyāṃ punarnṛpaḥ । jajñe tadābhiśāpena dvitīya iti naḥ śrutam ।।
bhṛgavādayaśca ye sapta jajñire ca maharṣayaḥ । ādye tretāyuge pūrvaṃ manorvaivasvatasya ca ।। devasya mahato yajñe vāruṇīṃ bibhratastanum । ityeṣo anuśayo hyāsīttayorjātyantarānugaḥ ।।
prajāpateśca dakṣasya tryabakasya ca dhīmataḥ । tasmānnānuśayaḥ kāryo vaireṣviha kadācana ।। jātyantaragatasyāpi bhavitasya śubhāśubhaiḥ । khyātiṃ na muñcate jantustanna kāryaṃ vipaścitā ।।
ityeṣā samanukrāntā kathā pāpapramocanī । yā dakṣamadhikṛtyeha tvayā pūrvaṃ pracauditā ।। pitṛvaṃśaprasaṃgena kathā hyeṣā prakīrttitā । pitṝṇāmānupūrvyeṇa devānvakṣyāmyataḥ param ।।
tretāyugamukhe pūrvamāsansvāyaṃbhuveṃ'tare । devāyāmā iti khyātāḥ pūrvaṃ ye yajñasūnavaḥ ।। prathitā brahmaṇaḥ putrā ajatvādajitāstu te । putrāḥ svāyaṃbhuvasyaite śaktā nāma tu mānasāḥ ।।
teṣāṃ yato gaṇā hyete devānāṃ tu trayaḥ smṛtāḥ । chandajāstu trayastriṃśatsarge svāyaṃbhuvasya ha ।। yaduryayātirdevau dvau vīvadhasrāsato matiḥ । vibhāsaśca kratuścaiva prayātirviśruto dyutiḥ ।।
vāyavyaḥ saṃyamaścaiva yāmā dvādaśa kīrttitāḥ । asamaścogradṛṣṭiśca sunayo atha śuciśravāḥ ।। kevalo viśvarūpaśca sudakṣo madhupastathā । turīya idrayukcaiva yukto grāvajitastu vai ।।
canimā viśvadevā ca javiṣṭho mitavānapi । jaro vibhurvibhāvaśca sa ṛcīko atha durdihaḥ ।। śrutirgṛṇāno atha bṛhacchukrā dvādaśa kīrttitāḥ । āsansvāyaṃbhuvasyaite cāntare somapāyinaḥ ।।
dīptimanto gaṇā hyete vīryavanto mahābalāḥ । teṣāmindrastaddā hyāsītprathame viśvabhukta prabhuḥ ।। asurā ye tadā teṣāmāsan dāyādabāndhavāḥ । suparṇayakṣagandharvāḥ piśācoragarākṣasāḥ ।।
aṣṭau tāḥ pitṛbhiḥ sārddhamāsanyā devayonayaḥ । svāyaṃbhuventare atītāḥ prajāstāsāṃ mahasraśaḥ ।। prabhāvarūpasaṃpannā āyuṣā ca balena ca । vistarādiha nocyante māprasaṃgo bhavediha ।।
svāyaṃbhuvo visargastu vijñeyaḥ sāṃpratena ha । atīto vartamānena dṛṣṭo vaivasvate na saḥ ।। prajābhirdevātābhiśca ṛṣibhiḥ pitṛbhiḥ saha । teṣāṃ sarparṣayaḥ pūrvamāsanye tānnibodhata ।।
bhṛgvaṃ girā marīciśca pulastyaḥ pulahaḥ kratuḥ । atriścaiva vasiṣṭhasca sapta svāyaṃbhuve atare ।। āgnīdhraścāgnibāhuśca modhā medhātithir vasuḥ । jyotiṣmān dyutimānhavyaḥ savanaḥ sattra eva ca ।।
manoḥ svāyaṃbhuvasyaite daśa putrā mahaujasaḥ । vāyuvegā mahāsattvā rājānaḥ prathameṃ'tare ।। sāsuraṃ tatsugandharvaṃ sayakṣoragarākṣasam । sapiśācamanuṣyañca sasuparṇāpsarogaṇam ।।
naśakyamānu pūrvyeṇa vaktuṃ varṣaśatairapi । bahutvānnāmadheyānāṃ saṃkhyā teṣāṃ kutaḥ kule ।। yā vai prajā yugākhyāstu āsansvāyaṃbhuveṃ'tare । kālena mahatātītā ayanābdayugakramaiḥ ।।
ka eṣa bhagavān kālaḥ sarvabhūtāpahārakaḥ । kasya yoniḥ kimādiśca kiṃ satattvaḥ kimātmakaḥ ।। kimasya cakṣuḥ kā mūrtiḥ ke vā avayavāḥ smṛtāḥ । kiṃ nāmadheyaṃ ko asyātmā eptattvaṃ brūhi tattvataḥ ।।
śrūyatā kālasadbhāvaḥ śrutvā caivāvadhāryatām । sūryayonirnimeṣādiḥ saṃkhyācakṣuḥ sa ucyate ।। mūrtirasya tvaho rātro nimeṣāvayavaśca saḥ । saṃvatsaraḥ satattvaśca nāma cāsya kalātmakaḥ ।।
sāmpratānāgatātītakālātmā sa prajāpatiḥ । pañcadhā pravibhaktāṃ tu kālāvasthāṃ nibodhata ।। divasārddhamāsamāsaiśca ṛtubhistvayanaistathā । saṃvatsarastu prathamo dvitīyaḥ parivatsaraḥ ।।
iḍravatsarastṛtīyaśca caturthaścānuvatsaraḥ । pañcamo vatsarasteṣāṃ kālaḥsa yugasajñitaḥ ।। teṣāṃ tattvaṃ pravakṣyāmi kīrtyamānaṃ nibodhata । kraturagnistu yaḥ proktaḥ sa tu saṃvatsaro mataḥ ।।
āditeyastvasau sūryaḥ kālāgniḥ parivatsaraḥ । śuklakṛṣṇagatiścāpi apāṃ sāramayaḥ khagaḥ ।। sa iḍāvatsaraḥ somaḥ purāṇe niścayaṃ gataḥ । yaścāyaṃ pavate lokāṃstanubhiḥ saptasaptabhiḥ ।।
anuvātā ca lokasya sa vāyuranuvatsaraḥ । ahaṅkārādudagrudraḥ saṃbhūto brahmaṇāstu yaḥ ।। sa rudro vatsara steṣāṃ vijñeyo nīlalohitaḥ । satattvaṃ tasya vakṣyami kīrtyamānaṃ nibodhata ।।
aṅgapratyaṅgasaṃyogātkālātmā pratitāmahaḥ । ṛksāmayajuṣāṃ yoniḥ pañcānāṃ patirīśvaraḥ ।। so agniryamaśca kālaśca saṃbhūtiḥ sa prajāpatiḥ । proktaḥ saṃvatsaraśceti sūrya conirmanīṣibhiḥ ।।
yasmātkālavibhāgānāṃ māsartvayanayorapi । grahanakṣatraśītoṣṇavarṣāyuḥ karmaṇāṃ tathā ।। yoniḥ sa pravibhāgānāṃ divasānāṃ ca bhāskaraḥ । vaikārikaḥ prasannātmā brahmaputraḥ prajāpatiḥ ।।
eko naiko atha divaso māso athartuḥ pitāmahaḥ । ādityaḥ savitā bhānurjīvano brahmasatkṛtaḥ ।। prabhavaścāvyayaścaiva bhūtānāṃ tena bhāskaraḥ । tārābhimānī vijñeyo dvitīyaḥ parivatsaraḥ ।।
somaḥ sarvauṃṣadhipatiryasmātsa prapitāmahaḥ । ājīvaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ yogakṣemakṛdīśvaraḥ ।। āvekṣamāṇaḥ satataṃ bibharti jagadaṃśubhiḥ । tithīnāṃ parvasaṃdhīnāṃ pūrṇimādarśayorapi ।।
yonirniśākaro yaśca amṛtātmā prajāpatiḥ । tasmātsa pitṛmānsomaḥ smṛta iṅvatsarātmakaḥ ।। prāṇāpānasamānādyairvyānodānātmakairapi । karmabhiḥ prāṇināṃ loke sarvaceṣṭāpravartakaḥ ।।
pañcānāṃ cendriyamanorbuddhismṛtibalātmanām । samānakālakaraṇakriyāḥ saṃpādayannapi ।। sarvātmā sarvalokeśa āvahapravahādibhiḥ । varttate copakārairyastanubhiḥ saptasaptabhiḥ ।।
vidhātā sarvabhūtānāṅkṣemī nityaṃ prabhañjanaḥ । yoniragnerapāṃ bhūme raveścandramasaścayaḥ ।। vāyuḥ prajāpatirbhūto lokātmā prapitāmahaḥ । ahorātrakarastasmātsa vāyuranuvatsaraḥ ।।
ete prajānāṃ patayaścatvāra upapakṣajāḥ । pitaraḥ sarvalokānāṃ lokātmānaḥ prakīrttitāḥ ।। dhyāyato brahmāṇo vaktrādudansamabhavadbhavaḥ । ṛṣirviprā mahādevo bhūtātmā prapitāmahaḥ ।।
īśvaraḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ praṇavo yo athapaṭhyate । ātmāveśena bhūtānāmaṅgapratyaṅgasaṃbhavaḥ ।। unmādako anugrahakṛdrudro vatsara ucyate । sūryyaśca candramāścāgnirvāyū rudrastathaiva ca ।।
yugābhimānī kālātmā nityaṃ saṃkṣayakṛdvibhuḥ । rudraḥ praviṣṭo bhagavāñjagatyasminsvatejasā ।। āśrayānmayi saṃyogāttanubhirnāmamistathā । tatastasya tu vīryeṇa lokānugrahakārakam ।।
devatvaṃ ca pitṛtvaṃ ca kālatvaṃ cāsya yatparam । tasmādvai sarvathā rudrastadvidvadbhirabhījyate ।। yataḥ patiḥ sa bhagavān prajeśānāṃ prajāpatiḥ । bhāvanaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ sarvātmā nīlalohitaḥ ।।
auṣadhīḥ pratisaṃdhatte rudraḥ kṣīṇāḥ punaḥpunaḥ । prajāpatimukhairdevaiḥ samyagiṣṭaphalārthibhiḥ ।। tribhireva kapālaiśca trayaṃbakairauṣadhikṣaye । ijyate bhagavān yasmāttasmārtryaṃbaka ucyate ।।
gāyatrī caiva triṣṭupca jagatī caiva yāḥ smṛtāḥ । tryaṃbakā nāmataḥ premṇā yonayastā vanaspateḥ ।। tābhirekatvabhūtābhistrividhābhiḥ svavīryataḥ । trisādhanaḥ puroḍāśastrikapālaḥ sa vai smṛtaḥ ।।
tryaṃbakaḥ sa puroḍāśastenaiṣa tryaṃbakaḥ smṛtaḥ । ityetatpañcavarṣaṃ hi yugaṃ proktaṃ manīṣibhiḥ ।। yaścaiṣa pañcadhātmā vai proktaḥ saṃvatsaro dvijaiḥ । saikaḥ ṣaṭko vijajñe atha madhvādiṛtusaṃjñakaḥ ।।
ṛtuputrārttavāḥ pañca iti sargaḥ samāsataḥ । ityeṣa bahumāno vai prāṇinā jīvitāni ca । nadīvega ivāsaktaḥ kālo dhāvati saṃharan ।। eteṣāṃ yadapatyaṃ vai tadaśakyaṃ pramāṇataḥ ।
bahutvātparisaṃkhyātuṃ putra pautramanantakam ।। imaṃ vaṃśaṃ prajeśānāṃ mahataḥ puṇyakarmaṇām । kīrttayanpuṇyakīrttīnāṃ mahatīṃ siddhimāpnuyāt ।। athāntareṣu sarveṣu atītānāgateṣviha ।
tulyābhimāninaḥ sarve jāyante nāmarūpataḥ ।। devāścāṣṭavidhā ye ca tasminmamvantare adhipāḥ । ṛṣayo manavaścaiva sarve tulyaprayojanāḥ ।। maharṣisargaḥ saṃkrānto vaṃśaṃ svāyaṃbhuvasya tu ।
vistareṇānupūrvyā ca kīrtya mānaṃ nibodhata ।। manoḥ svāyaṃbhūvasyāsan daśa pautrāstu tatsamāḥ । yairiyaṃ pṛthivī sarvā saptadvīpā sapattanā ।। sasamudrā karavatī prativarṣaṃ niveśitā ।
svāyaṃbhuveṃ'tare pūrvamādye tretāyuge tathā ।। priyavratasya putraistaiḥ pautraiḥ svāyaṃbhuvasya tu । prajā sattvatapoyuktaistairiyaṃ viniveśitā ।। priyavratātprajopetān vīrānkāmyānvyajāyata ।
kanyā sā tu mahābhāga kardamasya prajā pateḥ ।। kanye dve daśa putrāśca samrāṭ kukṣiśca te śubhe । tayorvai bhrātaraḥ śūrāḥ prajāpatisamā daśa ।। āgnīdhraścāgnibā huśca medhā medhātithirvasuḥ ।
jyotiṣmān dyutimānhavyaḥ savanaḥ sabhra eva ca ।। priyavrato abhyaṣiñcattānsaptasaptasu pārthivān । dvīpeṣu teṣu dharmeṇa dvīpāntāśca nibodhata ।। jaṃbūdvīpeśvaraṃ cakre āgnīdhraṃ sumahābalam ।
plakṣadvīpeśvaraścāpi tena medhātithiḥ kṛtaḥ ।। śālmale tu vapuṣmantaṃ rājānaṃ so abhiṣiktavān । jyotiṣmantaṃ kuśadvīpe rājānaṃ kṛtavānprabhuḥ ।। dyutimantaṃ ca rājānaṃ kraiñcadvīpe abhyaṣecayat ।
śākadvīpeśvaraṃ cāpi havyaṃ cakre priyavrataḥ ।। puṣkarādhipatiṃ caiva savanaṃ kṛtavānprabhuḥ । puṣkare savanasyātha mahāvītaḥ suto abhavat ।। dhātakiścāpi dvāvetau putrau putravatā varau ।
mahāvītaṃ smṛtaṃ varṣaṃ tasya nāmnā mahātmanaḥ ।। nāmnā ca dhātakeścāpi dhātakīkhaṇḍa ucyate । havyo vyajanayatputrāñ śākadvīpeśvarāñ prabhuḥ ।। jaladaṃ ca kumāraṃ ca sukumāraṃ maṇīvakam ।
kusumottaramodākau saptamaṃ ca mahādrugam ।। jaladaṃ jaladasyātha prathamaṃ varṣamucyate । kumārasya tu kaumāraṃ dvitīyaṃ parikīrtitam ।। sukumāraṃ tṛtīyaṃ tu sukumārasya tatssatam ।
maṇīvasya caturthaṃ tu maṇīvakamihocyate ।। kusumottaravarṣaṃ yatpañcamaṃ kusumottaram । modakasyāpi modākaṃ ṣaṣṭhaṃ varṣaṃ prakīrttitam ।। mahādrumasya nāmnā ca saptamaṃ tanmahādrumam ।
teṣāṃ tu nāmabhistāni sapta varṣāṇi tatra vai ।। kraiñcadvīpeśvarasyāpi putro dyutimatastu vai । kuśalo manonugaschoṣṇaḥ pāvanaścāndhakārakaḥ ।। muniśca dundubhiścaiva sutā dyutimatastu vai ।
teṣāṃ svanāmabhirdeśāḥ kraiñcadvīpāśrayāḥ śubhāḥ ।। kuśalasya tu deśo abhūta kauśalo nāma viśrutaḥ । deśo manonugasyāpi mānonuge ite smṛtaḥ ।। uṣṇasyoṣṇaḥ smṛto deśaḥ pāvanasyāpi pāvanaḥ ।
andhakārasya deśastu āndhakāraḥ prakīrttitaḥ ।। muneśca maunideśo vai dundubherdundubhiḥ smṛtaḥ । ete janapadāḥ sapta kraiñcadvīpe tu bhāsvarāḥ ।। jyotiṣmataḥ kuśadvīpe saptaivāsanmahaujasaḥ ।
udbhijjo veṇumāṃścaiva vairatho lavaṇo dhṛtiḥ ।। ṣaṣṭhaḥ prabhākaraścā pi saptamaḥ kapilaḥ smṛtaḥ । udbhijjaṃ prathamaṃ varṣaṃ dvitīyaṃ veṇumaṇḍalam ।। tṛtīyaṃ vai rathākāraṃ caturthaṃ lavaṇaṃ smṛtam ।
pañcamaṃ dhṛtimadvarṣaṃ ṣaṣṭhaṃ varṣaṃ prabhākaram ।। saptamaṃ kapilaṃ nāma kapilasya prakīrttitam । teṣāṃ deśāḥ kaśadvīpe tatsanāmāna eva ca ।। āśramācārayuktābhiḥ prajābhiḥ samalaṅkṛtāḥ ।
śālmalasyeśvarāḥ sapta sutāste ca vapuṣmataḥ ।। śvetaśca haritaścaiva jīmūto rohitastathā । vaidyuto mānasaścāpi suprabhaḥ saptamastathā ।। śvetastu deśaḥ śvetasya haritasya suhāritaḥ ।
jīmūtasyāpi jīmūto rohitasyāpi rohitaḥ ।। vaidyuto vaidyutasyāpi mānasasya tu mānasaḥ । suprabhaḥ suprabhasyāpi saptaite deśapālakāḥ ।। plakṣa dvīpaṃ pravakṣyāmi jaṃbūdvīpādanantaram ।
sapta medhātithe putrāḥ plakṣadvīpeśvarā nṛpāḥ ।। jyeṣṭhaḥ śāntabhayo nāma dvitīyaḥ śiśiraḥ smṛtaḥ । sukhodayastṛtīyastu caturtho nanda ucyate ।। śivastu pecamasteṣāṃ kṣemakaḥ ṣaṣṭha ucyate ।
dhruvastu saptamo jñeyaḥ putrā medhātitheḥ smṛtāḥ ।। saptānāṃ nāmabhisteṣāṃ tāni varṣāṇi sapta vai । tasmācchāntabhayaṃ caiva śiśiraṃ ca sukhodayam ।। ānandaṃ ca śivaṃ caiva kṣemakaṃ ca dhruvaṃ tathā ।
tāni teṣāṃ samānāni sapta varṣāṇi bhāgaśaḥ ।। niveśitāni taistāni pūrvaṃ svāyaṃbhūventare । medhā tithestu putraistaiḥ plakṣadvīpeśvarairnṛbaiḥ ।। varṇāśramācārayuktāḥ plakṣadvīpe prajāḥ kṛtāḥ ।
plakṣadvīpādiṣu tveṣu śākadvīpāntikeṣu vai ।। jñeyaḥ pañcasu dharmo vai varṇāśramavibhājakaḥ । sukhamāyuśca rūpaṃ ca balaṃ dharmaśca nityaśaḥ ।। pañcasveteṣu dvīpeṣu sarvasādhā raṇaṃ smṛtam ।
prakṣadvīpaḥ pariṣkrānto jaṃbūdvīpaṃ nibodhata ।। āgnīdhraṃ jyeṣṭhadāyādaṃ kāmyāputraṃ mahābalam । priyavrato abhya ṣiñcattaṃ jaṃbūdvīpeśvaraṃ nṛpam ।। tasya putrā babhūvurhi prajāpatisamā nava ।
jyeṣṭho nābhiriti khyātastasya kiṃpuruṣo anujaḥ ।। harivarṣastṛtīyastu caturtho abhūdilāvṛtaḥ । ramyastu pañcamaḥ putro hiraṇvān ṣaṣṭha ucyate ।। kurustu saptamasteṣāṃ bhadrāśvaścāṣṭamaḥ smṛtaḥ ।
navamaḥ ketumālaśca teṣāṃ deśānnibodhata ।। nābhestu dakṣiṇaṃ varṣaṃ himākhyaṃ tu pitā dadau । hemakūṭaṃ tu yadvarṣaṃ dadau kipuruṣāya tat ।। naiṣadhaṃ yatsmṛtaṃ varṣaṃ harivarṣāya taṃ dadau ।
madhyamaṃ yatsumerostu dadau sa tadilāvṛtam ।। nīlaṃ tu yatsmṛtaṃ varṣaṃ ramyāyaitaptitā dadau । śvetaṃ yaduttaraṃ tasmātpitrā dattaṃ hiraṇvate ।। yaduttare śṛṅgavato varṣaṃ tatkurave dadau ।
sālyavantaṃ tathā varṣaṃ bhadrāśvāya nyavedayat ।। gandhamādanavarṣaṃ tu ketumāle nyavedayat । ityetāni mayoktāni nava varṣāṇi bhāgaśaḥ ।। āgnī dhrasteṣu varṣeṣu putrāṃstānabhyaṣecayat ।
yathākramaṃ sa dharmātmā tatastu tapasi sthitaḥ ।। ityetauḥ saptabhiḥ kṛtsnā saptadvīpā nive śitāḥ । priyavratasya putraistaiḥ pautaiḥ svāyaṃbhuvasya ca ।। evaṃ varṣeṣu sarveṣu sanniveśāḥ punaḥ punaḥ ।
kriyante pralaye vṛtte sapta saptasu pārthivaiḥ ।। evaṃ svabhāvaḥ kalpānāṃ dvīpānāṃ ca niveśane । yāni kiṃpuruṣādyāni varṇāṇyaṣṭau śrutāni tu ।। teṣāṃ svabhāvataḥ siddhiḥ sukhaprāyamayatnataḥ ।
viparyayo na teṣvasti jarāmṛtyubhayaṃ na ca ।। dharmādharmauṃ na teṣvāstā nottamādhamamadhyamāḥ । na teṣvasti yugāvasthā kṣetreṣvaṣṭāsu sarvaśaḥ ।। nābhernisargaṃ vakṣyāmi himāhve asminnibodhata ।
nābhistvaja nayatputraṃ merudevyāṃ mahādyutim ।। ṛṣabhaṃ pārthivaśreṣṭhaṃ sarvakṣatrasya pūrvajam । ṛṣabhādbharato jajñe vīraḥ putraśatāgrajaḥ ।। sobhiṣicyarṣabhaḥ putraṃ mahāpravrajyayā sthitaḥ ।
himāhvaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ varṣaṃ bharatāya nyavedayat ।। tasmāttu bhārataṃ varṣaṃ tasya nāmnā vidurbudhāḥ । bharatasyātmajo vidvānsumatirnāma dhārmikaḥ ।। babhūva tasmin rājye taṃbharatastvabhyaṣecayat ।
putrasaṃkrāmitaśrīstu vanaṃ rājā viveśa saḥ ।। tejasastatsutaścāpi prajāpatiramitrajit । tejasasyātmajo vidvānindradyumna iti smṛtaḥ ।। parameṣṭhī sutaścāpi nidhane tasya cāpyabhūt ।
pratīhāraḥ kulaṃ tasya nāmnā jajñe tadanvayaḥ ।। pratiharteti vikhyāto jajñe tasyāpi dhīmataḥ । unnetā pratihartustu bhūmā tasya sutaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। udgīthastasya putro abhūtaprastāviścāpi tatsutaḥ ।
prastāvestu vibhuḥ putraḥ pṛthustasya suto abhavat ।। pṛthoścāpi suto nakto naktasyāpi gayaḥ sutaḥ । gayasyāpi naraḥ putro narasyāpi suto virāṭ ।। virāṭsuto mahāvīryo dhīmāṃstasya suto abhavat ।
dhīmataśca mahānputro mahataścāpi bhauvanaḥ ।। bhauvanasya satastvaṣṭā virajāstasya cātmajaḥ । rajā virajasaḥ putraḥ śatajidrajasastathā ।। tasya putraśataṃ tvāsīdrājānaḥ sarva eva tu ।
viśvajyotiṣpradhānāste yairimā varddhitāḥ prajāḥ ।। tairidaṃ bhārataṃ varṣaṃ saptadvīpamihāṅkitam । teṣāṃ vaṃśaprasūtaistu bhukteyaṃ bhāratī purā ।। kṛtatretādiyuktāstu yugākhyā hyekasaptatiḥ ।
ye atītāstairyugaiḥ sārdhaṃ rājānaste tadanvayāḥ ।। svāyaṃbhuveṃ'tare pūrvaṃ śataśo atha sahasraśaḥ । evaṃ svāyaṃ bhuvaḥ sargo yenedaṃ pūritaṃ jagat ।। ṛṣibhirdaivataiścāpi pirtṛgandhavarākṣasaiḥ ।
yakṣabhūtapiśācaiśca manuṣyamṛgapakṣibhiḥ । teṣāṃ sṛṣṭiriyaṃ proktā yugaiḥ saha vivarttate ।। evaṃ prajāsanniveśaṃ śrutvā vai śāṃśapāyaniḥ । papraccha niyataṃ sūtaṃ pṛthivyuda dhivistaram ।।
kati dvīpā samudrā vā pavatā vā kati smṛtāḥ । kiyanti caiva varṣāṇi teṣu nadyaśca kāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। mahā bhūtapramāṇaṃ ca lokālokaṃ tathaiva ca । paryāyaṃ parimāṇaṃ ca gatiṃ candrārkayostathā ।
etatprabūhi naḥ sarvaṃ vistareṇa yathārthataḥ ।। hanta vo ahaṃ pravakṣyāmi pṛthivyāyāmavistaram ।। saṃkhyāṃ caiva samudrāṇāṃ dvīpānāṃ caiva vistaram । dvīpabhedasahasrāṇi saptasvantargatāni ca ।।
na śakyante krameṇeha vaktuṃ yaiḥ satataṃ jagat । sapta dvīpānpravakṣyāmi candrādityagrahaiḥ saha ।। teṣāṃ manuṣyā starkkeṇa pramāṇāni pracakṣate । acintyāḥ khalu ye bhāvā na tāṃstarkeṇa sādhayet ।।
prakṛtibhyaḥ paraṃ yacca tadacintyaṃ pracakṣate । navavarṣaṃ pravakṣyāmi jaṃbūdvīpaṃ yathātatham ।। vistarānmaṇḍalāccaiva yojanaistannibodhata । śatamekaṃ sahasrāṇāṃ yojanāgrātsamantataḥ ।।
nānājanapadākīrṇaḥ puraiśca vividhaiśśubhaiḥ । siddhacāraṇasaṃkīṇaḥ parvatairupaśobhitaḥ ।। sarvadhātunibaddhaiśca śilājāla samudbhavaiḥ । parvataprabhavābhiśca nadībhiḥ sarvatastataḥ ।।
jaṃbūdvīpaḥ pṛthuḥ śrīmān sarvataḥ pṛthumaṇḍalaḥ । navabhiścāvṛtaḥ sarvo bhuvanairbhūtabhāvanaiḥ ।। lavaṇena samudreṇa sarvataḥ parivāritaḥ । jaṃbūdvīpasya vistārāt samena tu samantataḥ ।।
prāgāyatāḥ sūparvāṇaḥ ṣaḍime varṣaparvatāḥ । avagāḍhā hyubhayataḥ masudrau pūrvapaścimau ।। himaprāyaśca himavān hemakūṭaśca hemavān । sarvarttuṣu sukhaścāpi niṣadhaḥ parvato mahān ।।
caturvarṇaśca sauvarṇo meruścārutamaḥ smṛtaḥ । dvātriṃśacca sahasrāṇi vistīrṇaḥ sa ca mūrddhani ।। vṛttākṛtipramāṇaśca caturasraḥ samucchritaḥ । nānāvarṇāstu pārśveṣu prajāpatiguṇānvitaḥ ।।
nābhibandhanasaṃbhūto brahmaṇo avyaktajanmanaḥ । pūrvatarḥ śvetavarṇaśca brāhmaṇastasya tena tat ।। pārśvamuttaratastasya raktavarmaḥ svabhāvataḥ । tenāsya kṣattrabhāvastu merornānārthakāraṇāt ।।
pītaśca dakṣiṇenāsau tena vaiśyatvamiṣyate । bhṛṅgapatranibhaścāpi paścimena samācitaḥ ।। tenāsya śūdrabhāvaḥ syāditi varṇāḥ prakīrttitāḥ । vṛttaḥ svabhāvataḥ prokto varṇataḥ parimāṇataḥ ।।
nīlaśca vaiduryamayaḥ śvetaḥ ghuklo hiraṇmayaḥ । mayurabarhavarṇastu śātakaiṃbhaśca śṛṅgavān ।। ete parvatarājānaḥ siddhacāraṇasevitāḥ । teṣāmantaraviṣkaṃbho navasāhasra ucyate ।।
madhye tvilāvṛtaṃ nāma mahāmeroḥ samantamaḥ । navaivaṃ tu sahasrāṇi vistīrṇaṃ sarvatastu tat ।। madhye tasya mahāmerurvidhūma iva pāvakaḥ । vedyarddhaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ meroruttarārddhaṃ tathottaram ।।
varṣāṇi yāni ṣaṭ caiva teṣāṃ ye varṣaparvatāḥ । dve dve sahasre vistīrṇā yojanānāṃ samucchrayāt ।। jaṃbūdvīpasya vistārātteṣāmāyāma ucyate । yojanānāṃ sahasrāṇi śataṃ dvāvāyatau girī ।।
nīlaśca niṣadhaścaiva tābhyāṃ hīnāstu ye pare । śvetaśca hemakūṭaśca himavāñchṛṅgavāṃstathā ।। navatī dve aśītī dve sahasrāṇyāyatāstu teḥ । teṣāṃ madhye janapadāstāni varṇāṇi sapta vai ।।
prapātaviṣamaistaistu parvatairāvṛtāni tu । saṃtatāni nadībhedairagamyāni parasparam ।। vasaṃti teṣu sattvāni nānājātīni sarvaśaḥ । idaṃ haimavataṃ varṣaṃ bhārataṃ nāma viśrutam ।।
hemakūṭaṃ paraṃ hyasmā nnānnā kiṃṣurupaṃ smṛtam । naiṣadhaṃ hemakūṭāttu harivarṣaṃ taducyate ।। harivarṣātparaṃ cāpi merośva tadilāvṛtam । ilāvṛtātpiraṃ nīlaṃ samyakaṃ nāma viśrutam ।।
ramyakātparatarḥ śvetaṃ viśrutaṃ taddhiraṇmayam । hiraṇmayātparaṃ caiva śṛṅgavattaḥ kuru smṛtam ।। dhanuḥsaṃsthe tu vijñeye dve varṣe dakṣiṇottare । dīrghāṇi tatra catvāri madhyamaṃ tadilāvṛtam ।।
arvāk ca niṣadhasyātha vedyarddhaṃ dakṣiṇaṃ smṛtam । paraṃ nīlavato yacca vedyarddhaṃ tu taduttaram ।। vedyarddhe dakṣiṇe trīṇi trīṇi varṣāṇi cottare । tayormadhye tu vijñeyo merurmadhya ilāvṛtam ।।
dakṣiṇena tu nīlasya niṣadhasyottarema tu । udagāyeto mahāśailo mālyavānnāma nāmataḥ ।। yojanānāṃ sahasraṃ tu ānīla niṣadhāyataḥ । āyāmataścatustriṃśatsahasrāṇi prakīrtitaḥ ।।
tasya pratīcyāṃ vijñeyaḥ parvato gandhamādanaḥ । āyāmato atha vistārānmālyavā nitiviśrutaḥ ।। parimaṇḍalayormerurmadhye kanakaparvataḥ । caturvaṇaḥ sa sauvarṇaḥ caturasraḥ samucchritaḥ ।।
sumeruḥ śuśubheśubhro rājava tsamadhiṣṭhitaḥ । taruṇādityavarṇābho vidhūma iva pāvakaḥ ।। yojanānāṃ sahasrāṇi caturaśītarucchritaḥ । praviṣṭaḥ ṣoḍaśādhastādvistṛtaḥ ṣoḍaśaiva tu ।।
śarāvasaṃsthitatvāttu dvātriṃśanmūrdhnivistṛtaḥ । vistārātriguṇastasya pariṇāhaḥ samantataḥ ।। maṇḍalena pramāṇena tryasre mānaṃ tadiṣyate । catvāriṃśatsahasrāṇi yojanānāṃ samantataḥ ।।
aṣṭābhiradhikāni syustryasre mānaṃ prakīrttitam । caturasreṇa mānena pariṇāhaḥ samantataḥ ।। catuḥ ṣaṣṭisahasrāṇi yojanānāṃ vidhīyate । sa parvato mahādivyo divyauṣadhisamanvitaḥ ।।
bhuvanairāvṛtaḥ sarvo jātarūpamayaiḥ śubhaiḥ । tatra devagaṇāḥ sarve gandharvoragarākṣasāḥ ।। śailarāje pradṛśyante śubhāścāpsarasāṃ gaṇāḥ । sa tu meruḥ parivṛto bhuvanairbhūtabhāvanaiḥ ।।
catvāro yasya deśā vai catuḥpārśveṣvadhiṣṭhitāḥ । bhadrāśvā bharatāśvaiva ketumālāśca paścimāḥ ।। uttarāḥ kuravaścaiva kṛtapuṇyapratiśrayāḥ । gandhamādanaparśve tu paraiṣāparagaṇḍikā ।।
sarvartturamaṇīyā ca nityaṃ pramuditā śivā । dvātriṃśattu sahasrāṇi yojanaiḥ pūrvapaścimāt ।। āyāmataścatustriṃśatsahasrāṇi pramāṇataḥ । tatra te śubhakarmāṇaḥ ketumālāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ ।।
tatra kālā narāḥ sarve mahāsattvā mahābalāḥ । striyaścotpala patrābhāḥ sarvāstāḥ priyadarśanāḥ ।। tatra divyo mahāvṛkṣaḥ panasaḥ paḍrasāśrayaḥ । īśvaro brahmaṇaḥ putraḥ kāmacārī manojavaḥ ।।
tasya pītvā phalarasaṃ jīvanti ca samāyutam । pārśve mālyavataścāpi pūrve apūrvā tu gaṇḍikā ।। āyāmādatha vistārādyathaiṣāparagaṇḍikā । bhadrāśvāstatra vijñeyā nityaṃ muditamānasāḥ ।।
bhadraśālavanaṃ cātra kālāmrastu mahādrumaḥ । tatra te puruṣāḥ svetā mahotsāhā balānvitāḥ ।। striyaḥ kumudavarṇābhāḥ sundaryaḥ priyadarśanāḥ । candraprabhāścandravarṇāḥ pūrṇacandra nibhānanāḥ ।।
candraśītalagātryastāḥ striya utpalagandhikāḥ । daśavarṣasahasrāṇi teṣāmāyuranāmayam ।। kālāmrasya rasaṃ pītvā sarve ca sthirayauvanāḥ । dakṣiṇena tu śvetasya nīlasyaivottareṇa ca ।।
varṣaṃ ramaṇakaṃ nāma jāyante tatra mānavāḥ । ratipradhānā vimalā jarādaurgandhyavarjitāḥ ।। śuklābhijanasaṃpannāḥ sarve ca priyadarśanāḥ । tatrāpi sumahānvṛkṣo nyagrodho rohito mahān ।।
tasyāpi te phalarasaṃ pibanto varttayanti vai । daśavarṣasahasrāṇi śatāni daśa pañca ca ।। jīvanti te mahābhāgāḥ sadā tdṛṣṭā narottamāḥ । dakṣiṇe vai śṛṅgavataḥ śvetasyāpyuttareṇa ca ।।
varṣaṃ hairaṇvataṃ nāma yatra hairaṇvatī nadī । mahābalāḥ sutejaskā jāyante tatra mānavāḥ ।। yakṣā vīrā mahāsattvā dhaninaḥ priyadarśanāḥ । ekādaśasahasrāṇi varṣāṇāṃ te mahaujasaḥ ।।
āyuḥ pramāṇaṃ jīvanti śatāni daśa pañca ca । yasminvarṣe mahāvṛkṣo lakucaḥ ṣaḍrasāśrayaḥ ।। tasya pītvā phalarasaṃ te jīvanti nirāmayāḥ । trīṇi śṛṅgavataḥ śṛṅgāṇyucchritāni mahānti ca ।।
ekaṃ maṇimayaṃ teṣāmekaṃ caiva hiraṇmayam । sarvaratnamayaṃ caikaṃ bhavanairupaśobhitam ।। uttare vai śṛṅgāvataḥ samudrasya ca dakṣiṇe । kuravastatra tadvarṣaṃ puṇyaṃ siddhaniṣevitam ।।
tatra vṛkṣā madhu phalā nityapuṣpaphalopagāḥ । vastrāṇi ca prasūyante phaleṣvābharaṇāni ca ।। sarvakāmapradāstatra kecidvakṣā manoramāḥ । gandhavarṇaraso petaṃ prakṣaranti madhūttamam ।।
apare kṣīriṇo nāma vṛkṣāstatra manoramāḥ । ye kṣaranti sadā kṣīraṃ ṣaḍrasaṃ hyamṛtopamam ।। sarvā maṇimayī bhūmiḥ sūkṣmakāñcanavālukā । sarvartusukhasaṃpannā nniṣpaṅkā nīrajā śubhā ।।
devalokacyutāstatra jāyante mānavāḥ śubhāḥ । śuklābhijanasaṃpannāḥ sarve ca sthirayauvanāḥ ।। mithunāni prasūyante striyaścāpsarasaḥ samāḥ । teṣāṃ te kṣīriṇāṃ kṣīraṃ pibanti hyamṛto pamam ।।
mithunaṃ jāyate sadyaḥ samaṃ caiva vivarddhate । samaṃ śīlaṃ ca rūpaṃ ca priyatā caiva tatsamā ।। anyonyamanuraktāśca cakravākasadharmiṇaḥ । anāmayā hyaśokāśca nityaṃ sukhaniṣeviṇaḥ ।।
trayodaśasahasrāṇi śatāni daśa pañca ca । jīvanti te mahāvīryā na cānyastrīniṣeviṇaḥ ।। evameva nisargo vai varṣāṇāṃ bhārate śubhe । dṛṣṭaḥ paramatattvajñairbhūyaḥ kiṃ varṇayāmi vaḥ ।।
yadidaṃ bhārataṃ varṣaṃ yasminsvāyaṃbhuvādayaḥ । caturdaśaite manavaḥ prajāsarge abhavanpunaḥ ।। etadveditumicchāmastanno nigada sattmaḥ । etacchrutavacasteṣāmabravīdromaharṣaṇaḥ ।।
atra vo varṇayiṣyāmi varṣe asmin bhārate prajāḥ । idaṃ tu madhyamaṃ citraṃ śubhāśubhaphalodayam ।। uttaraṃ yatmamudrasya himavaddakṣiṇaṃ ca yat । varṣaṃ tadbhārataṃ nāma yatreyaṃ bhāratī prajā ।।
bharaṇācca prajānāṃ vai manurbharata ucyate । niruktavacanāccaivaṃ varṣaṃ tadbhārataṃ smṛtam ।। itaḥ svargaśca mokṣaśca madhyaścāntaśca gamyate । na khalvanyatra martyānāṃ bhūmau karma vidhīyate ।।
bhāratasyāsya varṣasya nava bhedānnibodhata । samudrātaritā jñeyāste tvagamyāḥ parasparam ।। indradvīpaḥ kaśerūmāṃstāmravarṇo gabhastimān । nāgadvīpastathā saumyo gāndharvastvatha vāruṇaḥ ।।
ayaṃ tu navamasteṣāṃ dvīpaḥ sāgarasaṃvṛtaḥ । yojanānāṃ sahasre tu dvīpo ayaṃ dakṣiṇottarāt ।। āyato hyākumāryyā vai cāgaṅgāprabhavācca vai । tiryaguttaravistīrmaḥ sahasrāṇi navaiva tu ।।
dvīpo hyupaniviṣṭo ayaṃ mlecchairanteṣu sarvaśaḥ । pūrve kirātā hyasyānte paścime yavanāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyā madhye śūdrāśca bhāgaśaḥ । ijyāyudhavaṇijyābhirvarttayanto vyavasthitāḥ ।।
teṣāṃ saṃvyavahāro atra varttate vai parasparam । dharmārthakāmasaṃyukto varṇānāṃ tu svakarmasu ।। saṃkalpaḥ pañcamānāṃ ca hyāśramāṇāṃ yathāvidhi । iha svargāpavargārthaṃ pravṛttiryeṣu mānuṣī ।।
yastvayaṃ navamo dvīpastiryagāyāma ucyate । kṛtsnaṃ jayati yo hyenaṃ samrāḍityabhidhīyate ।। ayaṃ lokastu vai samrāḍantarikṣaṃ virāṭ smṛtam । svarāḍasau smṛto laukaḥ punarvakṣyāmi vistarāt ।।
saptaivāsminsuparvāṇo viśrutāḥ kula parvatāḥ । mahendro malayaḥ sahyaḥ śuktimānṛkṣaparvataḥ ।। vindhyaśca pāriyātraśca saptaite kulaparvatāḥ । teṣāṃ sahasraścānye parva tāstu samīpagāḥ ।।
avijñātāḥ sāravanto vipulāścitrasānavaḥ । saṃdaraḥ parvataśreṣṭho vaihāro durdurastathā ।। kolāhalaḥ sasuraso maināko vaidyutastathā । vātandhamo nāgagiristathā pāṇḍuraparvataḥ ।।
tuṅgaprasthaḥ kṛṣṇagirirgodhano girireva ca । puṣpagiryujjayantau ca śailo raivatakastathā ।। śrīparvataścitrakūṭaḥ kūṭaśailo giristathā । anye tebhyo aparijñātā hrasvāḥ svalapopajī vinaḥ ।।
tairvimiśrā janapadā āryā mlecchāśca bhāgaśaḥ । pīyante yairimā nadyo gaṅgā siṃdhu sarasvatī ।। śatadruścandra bhāgā ca yamunā sarayūstathā । irāvatī vitastā ca vipāśā devikā kuhūḥ ।।
gomatī dhūtapāpā ca budbudā ca dṛṣadvatī । kauśakī tridivā caiva niṣṭhīvī geḍakī tathā ।। cakṣurlohita ityetā himavatpādanissṛtāḥ । vedasmṛtirvedavatī vṛtraghnī siṃdhu reva ca ।।
varṇāśā nandanā caiva sadānīrā mahānadī । pāśā carmaṇvatīnūpā vidiśā vetravatyapi ।। kṣiprā hyavanti ca tathā pāriyātrāśrayāḥ smṛtāḥ । śoṇo mahānadaścaiva narmmadā surasā kriyā ।।
mandākinī daśārṇā ca citrakūṭā tathaiva ca । tamasā pippalā śyenā karamodā piśācikā ।। citropalā viśālā ca bañjulā vāstuvāhinī । sanerujā śuktimatī maṅkutī tridivā kratuḥ ।।
ṛkṣavatsaṃprasūtāstā nadyo maṇijalāḥ śivāḥ । tāpī payoṣṇī nirvindhyā sṛpā ca niṣadhā nadī ।। veṇī vaitaraṇī caiva kṣiprā vālā kumudvatī । toyā caiva mahāgaurī durgā vānnaśilā tathā ।।
vindhyapādaprasūtāstā nadyaḥ puṇyajalāḥ śubhāḥ । godāvarī bhīmarathī kṛṣṇaveṇātha bañjulā ।। tuṅgabhadrā suprayogā bāhyā kāveryathāpi ca । dakṣiṇapravahā nadyaḥ sahya pādādviniḥsmṛtāḥ ।।
kṛtamālā tāmraparṇī puṣpajātyutpalāvatī । nadyo abhijātā malayātsarvāḥ śītajalāḥ śubhāḥ ।। trisāmā ṛṣikulyā ca bañjulā tridivābalā । lāṅgūlinī vaṃśadharā mahendratanayāḥ smṛtāḥ ।।
ṛṣikulyā kumārī ca mandagā mandagāminī । kṛpā palāśinī caiva śuktimatprabhavāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। tāstu nadyaḥ sarasvatyaḥ sarvā gaṅgāḥ samudragāḥ । viśvasya mātaraḥ sarvā jagatpāpaharāḥ smṛtāḥ ।।
tāsāṃ nadyupanadyo anyāḥ śataśo atha sahasraśaḥ । tāsvime kurupāñcālāḥ śālvā mādreyajāṅgalāḥ ।। śūrasenā bhadrakārā bodhāḥ sahapaṭaccarāḥ । matsyāḥ kuśalyāḥ sauśalyāḥ kuntalāḥ kāśikośalāḥ ।।
godhā bhadrāḥ kariṅgāśca māgadhāścotkalaiḥ saha । madhyadeśyā janapadāḥ prāyaśasttra kīrttitāḥ ।। sahyasya cauttarānteṣu yatra godāvarī nadī । pṛthivyāmapi kṛtsnāyāṃ sa pradeśo manoramaḥ ।।
tatra govardhanaṃ nāma puraṃ rāmeṇa nirmitam । rāmapriyātha svargīyā vṛkṣa divyāsta thauṣadhīḥ ।। bharadvājena muninā tatpriyārthe avaropitāḥ । ataḥ purvaroddeśastena jajñe manoramaḥ ।।
bāhlīkā vāṭadhānāśca ābhīrā kālatoyakāḥ । aparāntāśca muhmāśca pāñcalāścarmamaṇḍalāḥ ।। gāndhārā yavanāścaiva siṃdhusauvīramaṇḍalāḥ । cīnāścaiva tuṣārāśca pallavā girigahvarāḥ ।।
śākā bhadrāḥ kulindāśca pāradā vindhyacūlikāḥ । abhīṣāhā ulūtāśca kekayā daśāmālikāḥ ।। brāhmaṇāḥ kṣatriyāścaiva vaiśyaśūdrakulāni tu । kāṃvojā daradāścaiva barbarā aṅgalauhikāḥ ।।
atrayaḥ sabharadvājāḥ prasthalāśca daśerakāḥ । lamakāstālaśālāśca bhūṣikā ījikaiḥ saha ।। ete deśā udīcyā vai prācyāndeśānnibodhata । aṅgavaṅgā ścolabhadrāḥ kirātānāṃ ca jātayaḥ ।
tomarā haṃsabhaṅgāśca kāśmīrāstaṅgaṇāstathā ।। jhillikāścāhukāścaiva hūṇadarvāstathaiva ca ।। andhravākā mudgarakā antargiribahirgirāḥ । tataḥ plavaṅgavo jñeyā maladā malavartikāḥ ।।
samantarāḥ prāvṛṣeyā bhārgavā gopapārthivāḥ । prāgjyotiṣāśca puṇḍrāśca videhāstāmraliptakāḥ ।। mallā magadhagonardāḥ prācyāṃ janapadāḥ smṛtāḥ । athāpare janapadā dakṣiṇāpathavāsinaḥ ।।
paṇḍyāśca keralāścaiva colāḥ kulyāstathaiva ca । setukā mūṣikāścaiva kṣapaṇā vanavāsikāḥ ।। māharāṣṭrā mahiṣikāḥ kaliṅgaścaiva sarvaśaḥ । ābhīrāśca sahaiṣīkā āṭavyā sāravāstathā ।।
pulindā vindhyamaulīyā vaidarbhā daṇḍakaiḥ saha । paurikā maulikāścaiva śmakā bhogavarddhināḥ ।। koṅkaṇāḥ kantalāścāndhrāḥ kulindāṅgāramāriṣāḥ । dākṣiṇāścaiva ye deśā aparāṃstānnibodhata ।।
sūryyārakāḥ kalivanā durgālāḥ kuntarauḥ sahaḥ । pauleyāśca kirātāśca rūpakāstāpakaiḥ saha ।। tathā karītayaścaiva sarve caiva karandharāḥ । nāsikāścaiva ye cānye ye caivāntaranarmadāḥ ।।
sahakacchāḥ samāheyāḥ saha sārasvatairapi । kacchipāśca surāṣṭrāśca ānartāścarbudaiḥ saha ।। ityete aparāntāśca śṛṇudhvaṃ vindhyavāsinaḥ । maladāśca karūthāśca mekalāścaitkalaiḥ saha ।।
uttamānāṃ daśārṇāśca bhojāḥ kiṣkindhakaiḥ saha । tośalāḥ kośalāścaiva traipurā vaidiśāstathā ।। tuhuṇḍā barbarāścaiva ṣaṭpurā naiṣadhaiḥ saha । anūpāstuṇḍikerāśca vītihotrā hyavantayaḥ ।।
ete janapadāḥ sarve vindhyapṛṣṭhanivāsinaḥ । ato deśānpravakṣyāmi parvatāśrayiṇaśca ye ।। nihīrā haṃsamārgāśca kupathāstaṅgaṇāḥ śakāḥ । apaprāva raṇāścaiva ūrṇā darvāḥ sahūhukāḥ ।।
trigarttā maṇḍalāścaiva kirātāstāmaraiḥ saha । catvāri bhārate varṣe yugāni ṛṣayo abruvan ।। kṛtaṃ tretāyugaṃ caiva dvāparaṃ tiṣyameva ca । teṣāṃ nisargaṃ vakṣyāmi upariṣṭādaśeṣataḥ ।।
yacca kiṃpuruṣaṃ varṣaṃ harivarṣaṃ tathaiva ca । ācakṣva no yathātattvaṃ kīrttitaṃ bhārataṃ tvayā ।। śuśrūṣā yatra vo viprāstacchṛṇudhvamatandritāḥ । plakṣakhaṇḍaḥ kiṃpuruṣe sumahānnandanopamaḥ ।।
daśavarṣasahasrāṇi sthitiḥ kiṃpuruṣe smṛtā । suvarṇavarṇāḥ puruṣāḥ striyaścāpsaraso pamāḥ ।। anāmayā aśokāśca nityaṃ muditamānasāḥ । jāyante mānavāstatra nistaptakanakaprabhāḥ ।।
varṣe kiṃpuruṣe puṇye vṛkṣo madhuvahaḥ śubhaḥ । tasya kiṃpuruṣāḥ sarve apiban hi rasamuttamam ।। tataḥ paraṃ kiṃpuruṣo harivarṣaḥ pracakṣate । mahārajatasaṃkāśā jāyante tatra mānavāḥ ।।
devalokacyutāḥ sarve devānūkāśca sarveśaḥ । harivarṣe narāḥ sarve pibantīkṣurasaṃ śupham ।। ekādaśa sahasrāṇi varṣāṇāṃ tu nirāmayāḥ । harivarṣe tu jīvanti sarve muditamānasāḥ ।।
na jarā bādhate tatra na mriyante ca te acirāt । madhyamaṃ yanmayā proktaṃ nāmnā varṣamilāvṛtam ।। na tatra sūryastapati na tu jīryanti mānavāḥ । candrasūryai sanakṣatrau na prakāśāvilā vṛte ।।
padmaprabhāḥ padbavarṇāstathā padbanibhekṣaṇāḥ । padmapatrasugandhāśca jāyante tatra mānavāḥ ।। jaṃbūphalarasāhārā aniṣyandāḥ sugandhinaḥ । manasvino bhuktabhogāḥ satkarmaphalabhoginaḥ ।।
devalokacyatāścaiva mahārajatavāsasaḥ । trayodaśasahasrāṇi varṣāṇāṃ te narottamāḥ ।। āyuḥ pramāṇaṃ jīvanti ye tu varṣa ilāvṛte । meroḥ pratidiśaṃ yacca navasāhasravistṛtam ।।
yojanānāṃ sahasrāṇi ṣaṭtriṃśattasya vistaraḥ । yaturasraṃ samantācca śarāvākārasaṃsthitam ।। meroḥ paścimabhāge tu navasāhasrasammite । catustriṃśatsahasrāṇi gandhamādanaparvataḥ ।।
udagdakṣiṇataścaiva ānīlaniṣadhāyataḥ । catvāriṃśatsahasrāṇi parivṛddho mahītalāt ।। sahasramavagāḍhaśca tāvadeva ca vistṛtaḥ । pūrveṇa mālyavāñchailastatpramāṇaḥ prakīrttitaḥ ।।
dakṣiṇena tu nīlaśca niṣadhaścottareṇa tu । teṣāṃ madhye mahāmeruḥ svaiḥ pramāṇaiḥ pratiṣṭhitaḥ ।। sarveṣāmeva śailānāmavagāḍho yathā bhavet । vistarastatpramāṇaḥ syādāyāmo niyutaṃ smṛtaḥ ।।
vṛttabhāvāssamudrasya mahīmaṇḍalabhāvataḥ । āyāmāḥ parihīyante caturasrasamāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। ilāvṛtaṃ catuṣkoṇaṃ bhindantī madhyabhāgataḥ । prabhinnāñjanasaṃkāśā jambūrasavatī nadī ।।
merostu dakṣiṇe pārśve niṣadhasyottareṇa ca । sudarśano nāma mahāñjambūvṛkṣaḥ sanātanaḥ ।। nityapuṣpaphalopetaḥ siddhacāraṇasevitaḥ । tasya nāmnā samā khyāto jambūdvīpo vanaspateḥ ।।
yojanānāṃ sahasraṃ ca śataṃ cānyanmahātmanaḥ । utsedho vṛkṣarājasya divaṃ spṛśati sarvataḥ ।। aratnīnāṃ śatānyaṣṭāvekaṣaṣṭyadhikāni tu । phalapramāṇaṃ saṃkhyātamṛṣibhistattvadarśibhiḥ ।।
patamānāni tānyurvyāṃ kurvanti vipulaṃ svanam । tasyā jambvāḥ phalaraso nadī bhūtvā prasarppati ।। meruṃ pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā jambūmūlaṃ viśatyadhaḥ । taṃ pibanti sadā tdṛṣṭā jaṃbūrasamilāvṛte ।।
jaṃbūphalarase pīte na jarā bādhate tu tān । na kṣudhā na śramaścāpi na mṛtyurna ca tandri tam ।। tatra jāṃbūnadaṃ nāma kanakaṃ devabhūṣamam । indragopakasaṃkāśaṃ jāyate bhāsvaraṃ tu tat ।।
sarveṣāṃ varṣavṛkṣāṇāṃ śubhaḥ phalarasaḥ stutaḥ । skannaṃ bhavati tacchubhraṃ kanakaṃ devabhūṣaṇam ।। teṣāṃ mūtraṃ purīṣaṃ ca dikṣu sarvāsu sarvaśaḥ । īśvarānugrahādbhūmirmṛtāśca grasate tu tān ।।
rakṣaḥpiśācayakṣāśca sarve haimavataḥ smṛtāḥ । hemakūṭe tu gandharvā vijñeyāḥ sāpsarogaṇāḥ ।। sarve nāgastu niṣadhe śeṣavāsukitakṣakāḥ । mahāmerau trayastriṃśatkrīḍante yajñiyāḥ surāḥ ।।
nīle tu vaidūryamaye siddhā brahmarṣayo amalāḥ । daityānāṃ dānavānāṃ car śvetaḥ parvata ucyate ।। śṛṅgavānparvataśreṣṭhaḥ pitṝṇāṃ pratisaṃcaraḥ । navasveteṣu varṣeṣu yathābhāgaṃ sthiteṣu vai ।।
bhūtānyupaniviṣṭāni gatimanti dhruvāṇi ca । teṣāṃ vivṛddhirbahudhā dṛśyate divyamānuṣī । na saṃkhyā parisaṃkhyātuṃ śraddheyā tu bubhūṣatām ।। madhye himavataḥ pṛṣṭhe kailāso nāma parvataḥ ।
tasminnivasati śrīmānkuberaḥ saha rākṣasaiḥ ।। apsaronucaro rājā modate hyalakādhipaḥ । kailāsapādātsaṃbhūtaṃ puṇyaṃ śītajalaṃ śubham ।। madaṃ nāmnā kumudvatttsarastūdadhisannibham ।
tasmāddivyātprabhavati nadī mandākinī śubhā ।। divyaṃ ca nandanavanaṃ tasyāstīre mahadvanam । prāguttarema kailāsāddivyaṃ sarvauṃṣadhi girim ।। ratnadhātumayaṃ citraṃ sabalaṃ parvataṃ prati ।
candraprabho nāma giriḥ suśubhro ratnasannibhaḥ ।। tasya pāde mahāddivyaṃ svacchodaṃ nāma tatsaraḥ । tasmāddivyātprabhavati svacchodā nāma nimnagā ।। tasyāstīre mahaddivyaṃ vanaṃ caitrarathaṃ śubham ।
tasmin girau nivasati maṇibhadraḥ sahānugaḥ ।। yakṣasenāpatiḥ krūro guhyakaiḥ parivāritaḥ । puṇyā mandākinī caiva nadī svacchodakā ca yā ।। mahīmaṇḍalamadhyena praviṣṭe te mahodadhim ।
kailāsāddakṣiṇe prācyāṃ śivasattvauṣadhiṃ girim ।। manaḥ śilāmayaṃ divyaṃ citrāṅgaṃ parvataṃ prati । lohito hemaśṛṅgaśca giriḥ sūryaprabho mahān ।। tasya pāde mahaddivyaṃ lohitaṃ nāma tatsaraḥ ।
tasmātpuṇyaḥ prabhavati lauhityaḥ sa nado mahān ।। devāraṇyaṃ viśokaṃ ca tasya tīre mahadvanam । tasmingirau nivasati yakṣo maṇidharo vaśī ।। saumyaiḥ mudhārmikaiścaiva guhyake parivāritaḥ ।
kailāsāddakṣiṇe pārśve krūrasattvauṣadhirgiriḥ ।। vṛtrakāyātkilotpannamañjanaṃ trikakuṃ prati । sarvadhātumayastatra sumahānvaidyuto giriḥ ।। tasya pāde kalaḥ puṇyaṃ mānasaṃ siddhasevitam ।
tasmātprabhavete puṇyā sarayūrlokaviśrutā ।। tasyāstīre vana divyaṃ vaibhrājaṃ nāma viśrutam । kuberā nucarastatra prahetitanayo vaśī ।। brahmapito nivasati rākṣaso anantavikramaḥ ।
atarikṣacarairghorairyātudhānaśatairvṛtaḥ ।। apareṇa tu kailāsātpuṇyasattvauṣadhirgiriḥ । aruṇaḥ parvataśreṣṭho rukmadhātumayaḥ śubhaḥ ।। bhavasya dayitaḥ śrīmānparvato meghasannibhaḥ ।
śātakaiṃbhamayaiḥ śubhraiḥ śilājālaiḥ samāvṛtaḥ ।। śātasaṃkhyaistāpanīyaiḥ śṛṅgairdivamivollikhan । muñjavāstu mahādivyo durgaḥ śailo himācitaḥ ।। tasmingirau nivasati girīśo dhūmralocanaḥ ।
tasyā pādātprabhavati śailodaṃ nāma tatsaraḥ ।। tasmātprabhavate puṇyā śilodā nāma nimragā । sā cakṣuḥ sītayormadhye praviṣṭā lavaṇodadhim ।। tasyāstīre vanaṃ divyaṃ viśrutaṃ surabhīti vai ।
savyottareṇa kailāsācchivaḥ sattvauṣadhirgiriḥ ।। gauraṃ nāma giriśreṣṭhaṃ haritālamayaṃ prati । hiraṇyaśṛṅgaḥ sumahān divyo maṇimayo giriḥ ।। tasyā pāde mahāddivyaṃ śubhaṃ kāñcanavālukam ।
ramyaṃ bindusaro nāma yatra rājā bhagīrathaḥ ।। gaṅganimittaṃ rājarṣiruvāsa bahulāḥ samāḥ । divaṃ yāsyanti te burve gaṅgatoyapariplutāḥ ।। madīya iti niścitya samāhitamanāḥ śive ।
tatra tripayagā devī prathamaṃ tu pratiṣṭhitā । somapādātprasūtā sā saptadhā pratipadyate ।। yūpā maṇimayāstatra vitatāśca hiraṇmayāḥ । tatreṣṭvā tu gataḥ siddhiṃ śakraḥ sarvaiḥ suraiḥ saha ।।
divi cchāyāpatho yastu anunakṣatramaṇḍalaḥ । dṛśyate bhāsvaro rātrau devī tripathagā tu sā ।। antarikṣaṃ divañcaiva bhāvayantī surāpagā । bhavottamāṅge patitā saṃrūddhā yaugamāyayā ।।
tasyā ye bindavaḥ kecit kruddhāyāḥ patitā bhuvi । kṛtaṃ tu tairbidusarastato bindusaraḥ smṛtam ।। tato nirūddhā sā devī bhavena smayatā kila । cintayāmāsa manasā śaṅkarakṣepamaṃ prati ।।
bhittvā viśāmi pātālaṃ srotasāgṛhya śaṅkaram । jñātvā tamyā abhiprāyaṃ krūraṃ devyāścikīrṣitam ।। tirobhāvayituṃ buddhirāsīdaṅgeṣu tāṃ nadīm । tasyāvalepaṃ jñātvā tu nadyāḥkruddhastuśaṅkaraḥ ।।
nyarupācca śirasyenāṃ vegena patatīṃ bhuvi । etasminneva kāle tu dṛṣṭvā rājānamagrataḥ ।। dhamanīsaṃtataṃ kṣīṇaṃ kṣudhayā vyākulendriyam । anena toṣitaścāhaṃ nadyarthaṃ pūrvameva tu ।।
buddhāsya varadānaṃ ca kopaṃ niyatavāṃstu saḥ । brahmaṇo vacanaṃ śrutvā dhāraya svarṇadīmiti ।। tato visarjayāmāsa saṃruddhāṃ svena tejasā । nadīṃ bhagīrathasyārthe tapasogreṇa toṣitaḥ ।।
tato visṛjyamānāyāḥ srota statsaptadhā gatam । tisraḥ ptācīmimukhaṃ pratīcīṃ tisra eva tu ।। nadyāḥ srotastu gaṅgāyāḥ pratyapadyata saptadhā । nalinī hlādinī caiva pāvanī caiva prācyagāḥ ।।
sītā cakṣuśca sindhuśca pratīcīndiśamāsthitāḥ । saptamī tvanvagāttāsāṃ dakṣiṇena bhagīratham ।। tasmādbhāgīrathī yā sā praviṣṭā lavaṇodadhim । saptaitā bhāvayantīdaṃ himāhvaṃ varṣameva tu ।।
prasūtāḥ sapta nadyastāḥ śubhā bindu sarodbhavāḥ । nānādeśānplāvayantyo malecchaprāyāstu sarvaśaḥ ।। upagacchanti tāḥ sarvā yato varṣati vāsavaḥ । śilīndhrānkunta lāṃścīnānbarbarānyavanādhrakān ।।
puṣkarāśca kulindāṃśca acoṃladvicarāśca ye । kṛtvā tridhā siṃhavantaṃ sītāgātpaścimoda dhim ।। atha cīnamarūṃścaiva tālāṃśca masamūlikān । bhadrāstuṣārāṃllāmyākānbāhlavānpāraṭānkhaśān ।।
etāñjanapadāṃ ścakṣuḥ prāvayantī gatodadhim । daradāṃśca sakāśmīrān gāndharān raurasān kuhān ।। śivaśailānindrapadānvasatīśca visarjamān । saindhavānrandhrakarakāñchamaṭhābhīrarohakān ।।
śunāsukhāṃścorddhamarūnsindhuretānniṣevate । gandharvakinnarānyakṣānrakṣovidyādharoragān ।। kalāpagrāmakāṃścaiva pāradāṃstadgaṇān khaśān । kirātāṃścapulindāṃśca kurūn sabharatānapi ।।
pañcālānkāśimatsyāṃ śca magadhāṅgāṃstathaiva ca । suhmottarāṃśca vaṅgāṃśca tāmraliptāṃstathaiva ca ।। etāñjanapadānmānyāngaṅgā bhāvayate śubhān । tataḥ pratihatā vindhyātpraviṣṭā lavaṇodadhim ।।
tataśca hlādinī puṇya prācīmabhimukhā yayau । prāvayantyupabhāgāṃśca naiṣadhāṃśca trigarta kān ।। dhīvarānṛṣikāṃścaiva tathā nīlamukhānapi । kekarānauṣṭakarṇāṃśca kirātānapi caiva hi ।।
kālodarānvivarṇāśca kumārānsvarṇabhūmikān । āmaṇḍalaṃ samudrasya tirobhūtāṃśca pūrvataḥ ।। tatastu pāvanī cāpi prācīmeva diśaṃ yayau । supathānpāvayaṃ tīha tvindradyumnasaropi ca ।।
tathā kharapathāṃścaiva vetraśaṅkupathānapi । madhyatojānakimatho kuthaprāvaraṇānyayau ।। indradvīpa samudraṃ tu praviṣṭāṃ lavaṇodadhim । tatastu nalinī prāyāt prācīmāśāṃ javena tu ।।
tomarānbhāvayantīha haṃsamārgānsahaihayān । pūrvandeśāṃśca sevantī bhittvā sā bahudhāgirīn ।। karṇaprāvaraṇānprāpya saṃgatyā śvamukhānapi । sikatāparvatamaruṃ gatvā vidyādharānyayau ।।
nagamaṇḍalamadhyena praviṣṭā lavaṇodadhim । tāsāṃ nadyupanadyaśca śataśo atha sahasraśaḥ ।। upagacchanti tāḥ sarvā yato varṣati vāsavaḥ । vakvaukasāyāstīre tu vanaṃ surabhi viśrutam ।।
hiraṇyaśṛṅge vasati vidvānkauberako vaśī । yajñopetaśca sumahānamitaujāḥ suvikramaḥ ।। tatratyaistaiḥ parivṛtau vidvadbhirbrahmarākṣasaiḥ । kuberānucarā hyete catvārastu samāḥ smṛtāḥ ।।
evameva tu vijñeyā ṛddhiḥ parvatavāsinām । paraspareṇa dviguṇā dharmataḥ kāmator'thataḥ ।। hemakūṭasya pṛṣṭhe tu varcovannāmataḥ saraḥ । manasvinīprabhavati tasmājjyotiṣmatī ca yā ।।
avagāḍhe hyubhayataḥ samudrau pūrvapaścimau । saro viṣṇupadaṃ nāma niṣadhe parvatottame ।। tasmāddvayaṃ prabhavati gāndharvī nākulī ca taiḥ । meroḥ pārśvātprabhavati hradaścandraprabho mahān ।।
tatra jaṃbūnadī puṇyā yasyā jāṃbūnadaṃ smṛtam । payodaṃ tu saro nīle suśubhraṃ puṇḍarīkavat ।। puṇḍarīkā payodā ya tasmānnadyau vinirgate । śvetātpravarttate puṇyaṃ sarayūrmānasāddhruvam ।।
jyotsnā ca mṛgākāmā ca tasmāddve saṃbabhūvatuḥ । saraḥ kuruṣu vikhyātaṃ padmamīnadvijākulam ।। rudrakāntamiti khyātaṃ nirmitaṃ tadbhavena tu । anye cāpyatra vikhyātāḥ padmāmīnadvijākulāḥ ।।
nāmnā hradā jayā nāma dvādaśodadhisannibhāḥ । tebhyaḥ śāntā ya mādhvī ca dve nadyau saṃbabhūvatuḥ ।। yāni kiṃpuruṣādyāni teṣu devo na varṣati । udbhidānyudakānyatra pravahanti saridvarāḥ ।।
ṛṣabho dundubhiścaiva dhūmnaśca sumahāgiriḥ । pūrvāyatā mahāparvā nimagnā lavaṇābhasi ।। candraḥ kākastathā droṇaḥ sumahāntaḥ śiloccayāḥ । udagyātā udīcyāntā avagāḍhā mahodadhim ।।
somakaśca varāhaśca nāradaśca mahīdharaḥ । pratīcyāmāyatāste vai praviṣṭā lavaṇodadhima ।। cakro balāhakaścaiva maināko yaśca parvataḥ । āyatāste mahāśailāḥ samudraṃ dakṣiṇaṃ prati ।।
cakramainākayormadhya vidiśaṃ dakṣiṇāṃ prati । tatra saṃvarttako nāma so agniḥ pibati tajjalam ।। nāmnā samudravāsastu aurvaḥsa vaḍavāmukhaḥ । dvādaśaite praviṣṭā hi parvatā lavaṇodadhim ।।
mahendrabhayavitrastāḥ pakṣacche dabhayātpurā । yadetaddṛśyate candre śvete kṛṣṇaśaśākṛti ।। bhāratasya tu varṣasya bhedāste nava kīrttitāḥ । ihoditasya dṛśyante yathānye anyatra codite ।।
uttarottarameteṣāṃ varṣamuddiśyate guṇaiḥ । ārogyāyuḥ pramāṇānāṃ dharmataḥ kāmator'thataḥ ।। samanvitāni bhūtāni puṇyairetaistu bhāgaśaḥ । vasaṃti nānājātīni teṣu varṣeṣu tāni vai ।
ityeṣā dhārayantīdaṃ pṛthvī viśvaṃ jagatsthitam ।। plakṣadvīpaṃ pravakṣyāmi yathāvadiha saṃgrahāt । śṛṇutemaṃ yathātattvaṃ bruvato me dvijottamāḥ ।। jaṃbūdvīpasya vistārāddviguṇāstasya vistaraḥ ।
vistarāddviguṇaścāsya pariṇāhaḥ samantataḥ ।। tenāvṛtaḥ samudro vai dvīpena lavaṇodakaḥ । tatra puṇyā janapadāścirānna mriyate janaḥ ।। kṛta eva ca durbhikṣaṃ jarāvyādhibhayaṃ kutaḥ ।
tatrāpi parvatāḥ puṇyāḥ saptaiva maṇibhūṣaṇāḥ ।। ratnākarāstathā nadyastāsāṃ nāmāni ca buve । blakṣadvīpādiṣu tveṣu sapta sapta tu pañcasu ।। ṛjvāyatāḥ pratidiśaṃ niviṣṭā varṣaparvatāḥ ।
plakṣadvīpe tu vakṣyāmi saptadvīpān mahā balān ।। gomedako atra prathamaḥ parvato meghasannibhaḥ । khyāyate yasya nāmnā tu varṣaṃ gomedasaṃjñitam ।। dvitīyaḥ parvataścandraḥ sarvauṃṣa dhisamanvitaḥ ।
aśvibhyāmamṛtasyārthamoṣadhyo yatra saṃbhṛtāḥ ।। tṛtīyo nārado nāma durgaśailo mahoccayaḥ । tatrācale samutpannau pūrvaṃ nāradaparvatau ।। caturthastatra vai śailo duduṃbhirnnāma nāmataḥ ।
chandamṛtyuḥ purā tasmindundubhiḥ sāditaḥ suraiḥ ।। rajjudolorukāmaṃ yaḥ śālmaliścāsurāntakṛt । pañcamaḥ somako nāma devairyatrāmṛtaṃ purā ।। saṃbhṛtaṃ cāhṛtaṃ caiva māturarthe garutmatā ।
ṣaṣṭastu sumanā nāma saptamarṣabha ucyate ।। hiraṇyakṣo varāheṇa tasmiñchaile niṣūditaḥ । vaibhrājaḥ saptamastatra bhrājiṣṇuḥ sphāṭiko mahān ।। arcirbhirbhrājate yasmādvaibhrājastena saṃsmṛtaḥ ।
teṣāṃ varṣāṇi vakṣyāmi nāmatastu yathākramam ।। gomedaṃ prathamaṃ varṣaṃ nāmnāśāntabhayaṃ smṛtam । candrasya śiśiraṃ nāma nāradasya sukhodayam ।। ānandaṃ dundubhervarṣaṃ somakasyaśivaṃ smṛtam ।
kṣemakaṃ vṛṣabhasyāpi vaibhrājasya dhruvaṃ tathā ।। eteṣu devagandharvāḥ siddhāśca saha cāraṇaiḥ । viharanti ramante ca dṛśyamānāśca taiḥ saha ।। teṣāṃ nadyastu saptaiva prativarṣaṃ samudragāḥ ।
nāmatastāḥ pravakṣyāmi saptagaṅgāstapodhanāḥ ।। anutaptāsukhī caiva vipāśā tridivā kramuḥ । amṛtā sukṛtā caiva saptaitāḥ saritāṃ varāḥ ।। abhigacchanti tā nadyastābhyaścānyāḥ sahasraśaḥ ।
bahūdakā hyoghavatyo yato varṣati vāsavaḥ ।। tāḥ pibanti sadā hṛṣṭā nadījanapadāstu te । śubhāḥ śāntabhayāścaiva pramudaṃ śaiśirāḥ śivāḥ ।। ānandāśca sukhāścaiva kṣemakāśca dhruvaiḥ saha ।
varṇāśramācārayutā prajāsteṣvavadhiṣṭhitāḥ ।। sarve tvarogāḥ subalāḥ prajāścāmayava rjitāḥ । avasarpiṇī na teṣvasti tathaivotsarpiṇī na ca ।। na tatrāsti yugāvasthā caturyugakṛtā kvacit ।
tretāyugasamaḥ kālaḥ sarvadā tatra varttate ।। plakṣadvīpādiṣu jñeyaḥ pañcasveteṣu sarvaśaḥ । deśasyānuvidhānena kālasyānuvidhāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। pañcavarṣasahasrāṇi teṣu jīvanti mānavāḥ ।
surūpāśca suveṣāśca hyarogā balinastathā ।। sukhamāyurbalaṃ rupamārogyaṃ dharma eva ca । plakṣadvīpādiṣu jñeyaḥ śākadvīpāntikeṣu vai ।। prakṣadvīpaḥ pṛthuḥ śrīmānsarvato dhanadhānyavān ।
divyauṣadhiphalopetaḥ sarvauṃṣadhivanaspatiḥ ।। āvṛtaḥ paśubhiḥ sarvairgrāmyāraṇyaiḥ sahasraśaḥ । jaṃbūvṛkṣema saṃkhyātastasya madhye dvijottamāḥ ।। plakṣo nāma mahāvṛkṣastasya nāmnā sa ucyate ।
sa tatra pūjyate sthāne madhye janapadasya ha ।। sa cāpīkṣurasodena prakṣadvīpaḥ samāvṛtaḥ । plakṣadvīpasamenaiva vaipulyadvistareṇa tu ।। ityevaṃ saṃniveśo vaḥ plakṣadvīpasya kīrtitaḥ ।
ānupūrvyātsamāsena śālmalaṃ tu nibodhata ।। tatastṛtīyaṃ vakṣyāmi śālmalaṃ dvīpasuttamam । śālmalena samudrastu dvīpenekṣurasodakaḥ ।। plakṣadvīpasya vistārāddviguṇena samāvṛtaḥ ।
tatrāpi parvatāḥ sapta vijñeyā ratnayonayaḥ ।। ratnākarāstathā nadyasteṣāṃ varṣeṣu saptasu । prathamaḥ sūryasaṃkāśaḥ kumudo nāma parvataḥ ।। sarvadhātumayaiḥ śṛṅgaiḥ śilājālasamākulaiḥ ।
dvitīyaḥ parvataścātra hyuttamo nāma viśrutaḥ ।। haritālamayaiḥ śṛṅgairdivamāvṛtya tiṣṭhati । tṛtiyaḥ parvatastatra balāhaka iti śrutaḥ ।। jātyañjanamayaiḥ śṛṅgairdivamāvṛtya tiṣṭhati ।
caturthaḥ parvato droṇo yatra sā vai sahoṣadhiḥ ।। viśalyakaraṇī caiva mṛtasañjīvinī tathā । kaṅkastu pañcamastatra parvataḥ sumahodayaḥ ।। nityapuṣpaphalopeto vṛkṣavīrutsamāvṛtaḥ ।
ṣaṣṭhastu parvatastatra mahiṣo meghasannibhaḥ ।। yasminso agnirnivasati mahiṣo nāma vārijaḥ । saptamaḥ parvatastatra kakudmānnāma bhāṣyate ।। tatra ratnānyanekāni svayaṃ rakṣati vāsavaḥ ।
prajāpatimupādāya prajābhyo vidhivatsvayam ।। ityete parvatāḥ sapta śālmale maṇibhūṣaṇāḥ । teṣāṃ varṣāṇi vakṣyāmi sarpaiva tu śubhāni vai ।। kumudasya smṛtaṃ śvetamuttamasya ca lohitam ।
balāhakasya jīmūtaṃ droṇasya haritaṃ smṛtam ।। kaṅkasya vaidyutaṃ nāma mahiṣasya ca mānasam । kakudaḥ supradaṃ nāma saptaitāni tu saptadhā ।। varṣāṇi parvatāścaiva nadīsteṣu nibodhata ।
jyotiḥ śāntistathā tuṣṭā candrā śukrā vimocanī ।। nivṛttiḥ saptamī tāsāṃ prativarṣaṃ tu tāḥ smṛtāḥ । tāsāṃ samīpagāścānyāḥ śataśo atha sahasraśaḥ ।। na saṃkhyāṃ parisaṃkhyātuṃ śaknuyātko api mānavaḥ ।
ityeṣa saṃniveśo vaḥ śālmalasya prakīrttitaḥ ।। plakṣavṛkṣeṇa saṃkhyātastasya madhye mahā drumaḥ । śālmalirvipulaskandhastasya nāmnā sa ucyate ।। śālmalastu samudreṇa surodena samāvṛtaḥ ।
vistarācchālmalasvaiva same na tu samantataḥ ।। uttareṣu tu dharmajñādvīpeṣu śṛṇuta prajāḥ । yathāśrutaṃ yathānyāyaṃ bruvato me nibodhata ।। kuśadvīpaṃ pravakṣyāmi caturthaṃ tu samāsataḥ ।
surodakaḥ parivṛtaḥ kuśadvīpena sarvataḥ ।। śālmalasya tu vistārāddviguṇena samantataḥ । saptaiva ca girīṃstatra varṇyamānānnibodhata ।। kuśadvīpe tu vijñeyaḥ parvato vidrumaśca yaḥ ।
dvīpasya prathamastasya dvitīyo hemaparvataḥ ।। tṛtīyo dyutimānnāma jīmūtasadṛśo giriḥ । caturthaḥ puṣpavānnāma pañcamastu kuśeśayaḥ ।। ṣaṣṭho harigirirnāma saptamo mandaraḥ smṛtaḥ ।
mandā iti hyapā nāma mandaro dāraṇādayam ।। teṣāmantaraviṣakaṃbho dviguṇaḥ pravibhāgataḥ । udbhidaṃ prathamaṃ varṣaṃ dvitīyaṃ veṇumaṇḍalam ।। tṛtīyaṃ vai rathākāraṃ caturthaṃ lavaṇaṃ samṛtam ।
pañcamaṃ dhṛtimadvarṣaṃ ṣaṣṭhaṃ varṣaṃ prabhākaram ।। saptamaṃ kapilaṃ nāma sarve te varṣa bhāvakāḥ । eteṣu devagandharvāḥ prajāstu jagadīśvarāḥ ।। viharanti ramante ca hṛṣyamāṇāstu sarvaśaḥ ।
na teṣu dasyavaḥ saṃti mleccha jātaya eva ca ।। gauraprāyo janaḥ sarvaḥ kramācca mriyate tathā । tatrāpi nadyaḥ saptaiva dhūtapāpāśivā tathā ।। pavitrā saṃtatiścaiva vidyuddaṃbhā mahī tathā ।
anyāstābhyo aparijñātāḥ śataśo atha sahasraśaḥ ।। abhigacchanti tāḥ sarvā yato varṣati vāsavaḥ । ghṛtodena kuśadvīpo bāhyataḥ parivāritaḥ ।। vijñeyaḥ sa tu vistārātkuśadvīpasamena tu ।
ityeṣa sanniveśo vaḥ kuśadvīpasya kīrttitaḥ ।। kraiñcadvīpasya vistāraṃ vakṣyāmyahamataḥ param । kuśadvīpasya vistārāddviguṇaḥ sa tu vai smṛtaḥ ।। ghṛtodakasamudro vai kraiñca dvīpena saṃyutaḥ ।
tasmindvīpe nagaśreṣṭhaḥ kraiñcastu prathamo giriḥ ।। kraiñcātparo vāmanako vāmanādandhakārakaḥ । andhakārātparaścāpi divāvṛnnāma parvataḥ ।। divāvṛtaḥ paraścāpi dvivido girisattamaḥ ।
dvividātparataścāpi puṇḍarīko mahāgiriḥ ।। puṇḍarīkātparaścāpi procyate dundubhisvanaḥ । ete ratnamayāḥ sapta kraiñcadvīpasya parvatāḥ ।। bahupuṣpaphalopetanānāvṛkṣalatāvṛtāḥ ।
paraspareṇa dviguṇā vistṛtā harṣavarddhanāḥ ।। varṣāṇi tatra vakṣyāmi nāmatastānnibodhata । kraiñcasya kuśalo deśo vāmanasya manonugaḥ ।। manonugātparaścoṣṇastṛtīyaṃ varṣamucyate ।
uṣṇātparaḥ pīvarakaḥ pīvarādandhakārakaḥ ।। andhakārātparaścāpi munideśaḥ smṛto budhaiḥ । munideśātparaścaiva procyate dundubhisvanaḥ ।। siddhacāraṇasaṃkīrṇo gauraprayo janaḥ smataḥ ।
tatrāpi nadyaḥ saptaiva prativarṣa smṛtāḥ śubhāḥ ।। gaurī kumudvatī caiva saṃdhyā rātrirmanojavā । khyātiśca puṇḍarīkā ca gaṅgāḥ saptavidhāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। tāsāṃ sahasraśaścānyā nadyo yāstu samīpagāḥ ।
abhigacchanti tāḥ sarvā vipulāḥ subahūdakāḥ ।। kraiñcadvīpaḥ samudreṇa dadhimaṇḍaudakena tu । āvṛtaḥ sarvataḥ śrīmānkraiñcadvīpasamena tu ।। plakṣadvīpādayo hyete samāsena prakīrttitāḥ ।
teṣāṃ nisargodvīpānāmānupūrvyeṇa sarvaśaḥ ।। na śakyo vistarādvaktuṃ divyavarṣaśatairapi । nisargo yaḥ prajānāṃ tu saṃhāro yaśca tāsu vai ।। śākadvīpaṃ pravakṣyāmi yathāvadiha niścayāt ।
śṛṇudhvaṃ tu yathātathyaṃ bruvato me yathārthavat ।। kraiñcadvīpasya vistārāddviguṇāstasya vistaraḥ । parivārya samudraṃ sa dadhimaṇḍodakaṃ sthitaḥ ।। tatra puṇyā janapadāścirāttu mriyate janaḥ ।
kuta eva ca durbhikṣaṃ jarāvyādhibhayaṃ kutaḥ ।। tatrāpi parvatāḥ śabhrāḥ saptaiva maṇibhūṣaṇāḥ । ratnākarāstathā nadyasteṣāṃ nāmāni me śṛṇu ।। devarṣigandharvayutaḥ prathamo merurucyate ।
prāgāyataḥ sa sauvarṇo hyudayo nāma parvataḥ ।। vṛṣṭyarthaṃ jaladāstatra prabhaṃvati ca yānti ca । tasyāpareṇa sumahāñjaladhāro mahāgiriḥ ।। yato nityamupādatte vāsavaḥ paramaṃ jalam ।
tato varṣaṃ prabhavati varṣākāle prajāsviha ।। tasyottare raivatako yatra nityaṃ pratiṣṭhitam । revatī divi nakṣatraṃ pitāmahakṛto vidhiḥ ।। tasyāpareṇa sumahān śyāmo nāma mahāgiriḥ ।
tasmācchyāmatvamāpannāḥ prajāḥ pūrvamimāḥ kila ।। tasyāpareṇa sumahānnājato astagiriḥ smṛtaḥ । tasyāpare cāṃbikeyo durgaśailo mahāgiriḥ ।। aṃbikeyātparo ramyaḥ sarvauṃṣadhisamanvitaḥ ।
kesarī kesarayuto yato vāyuḥ prajāpatiḥ ।। udayātprathamaṃ varṣaṃ mahāttajjaladaṃ smṛtam । dvitīyaṃ jaladhārasya sukumāramiti smṛtam ।। raivatasya tu kaumāraṃ śyāmasya ca maṇīvakam ।
astasyāpi śubhaṃ varṣaṃ vijñeyaṃ kusumottaram ।। ambikeyasya modākaṃ kesarasya mahādrumam । dvīpasya parimāṇaṃ tu hrasvadīrghatvameva ca ।। kraiñcadvīpena vikhyātaṃ tasya keturmahādrumaḥ ।
śāko nāma mahotsedhastasya pūjyā mahānugāḥ ।। tatra puṇyā janapadāścāturvarṇyasamanvitāḥ । nadyaścāpi mahāpuṇyā gaṅgāḥ saptavidhāstathā ।। sukumārī kumārī ca nalinī veṇukā ca yā ।
ikṣuśca veṇukā caiva gabhastiḥ saptamī tathā ।। nadyaścānyāḥ puṇyajalāḥ śītatoyavahāḥ śubhāḥ । sahasraśaḥ samākhyātā yato varṣati vāsavaḥ ।। na tāsāṃ nāmadheyāni parimāṇaṃ tathaiva ca ।
śakyaṃ vai parisaṃkhyātuṃ puṇyāstāḥ sariduttamāḥ ।। tāḥ pibanti sadā hṛṣṭā nadīrjanapadāstu te । śāṃśapāyanavistīrṇo dvīpo asau cakrasaṃsthitaḥ ।। nadījalaiḥ praticchannaḥ parvataiścābhrasannibhaiḥ ।
sarvadhātuvicitraiśca maṇividrumabhūṣitaiḥ ।। nagaraiścaiva vividhaiḥ sphītairjanapadairapi । vṛkṣaiḥ puṣpaphalopetaiḥ samantāddhanadhānyavān ।। kṣīrodena samudreṇa sarvataḥ parivāritaḥ ।
śākadvīpasya vistārātsamena tu samaṃntataḥ ।। tasmiñjanapadāḥ puṇyāḥ parvatāḥ saritaḥ śubhāḥ । varṇāśramasamākīrṇā deśāste sapta vai smṛtāḥ ।। na saṃkaraśca teṣvasti varṇāśramakṛtaḥ kvacit ।
dharmasya cāvyabhīcārādekāntasukhitāḥ prajāḥ ।। na teṣu lobho māyā vā hīrṣāsūyākṛtaḥ kutaḥ । viparyayo na teṣvasti kālātsvābhāvikaṃ param ।। karāvāptirna teṣvasti na daṇḍo na ca daṇḍyakāḥ ।
svadharmeṇaiva dharma jñāste rakṣanti parasparam ।। etāvadeva śakyaṃ vai tasmindvīpe prabhāṣitum । etāvadeva śrotavyaṃ śākadvīpanivāsinām ।। puṣkaraṃ saptamaṃ dvīpaṃ pravakṣyāmi nibodhata ।
puṣkareṇa tu dvīpena vṛtaḥ kṣīrodako bahiḥ ।। śākadvīpasya vistārāddviguṇena saṃmatataḥ । puṣkare parvataḥ śrīmāneka eva mahāśilaḥ ।। citrairmaṇimayaiḥ śṛṅgaiḥ śilājālaiḥ samucchritaḥ ।
dvīpasya tasya pūrvarddhe citrasānuḥ sthito mahān ।। sa maṇḍalasahasrāṇi vistīrṇaḥ pañcaviṃśatiḥ । urddhaṃ caiva catustriṃśatsahasrāṇi mahītalāt ।। dvīpardhasya parikṣiptaḥ parvato mānasottaraḥ ।
sthito velāsamīpe tu navacandra ivoditaḥ ।। yojanānāṃ sahasrāṇi ūrdhvaṃ pañcāśaducchritaḥ । tāvadeva ca vistīrṇaḥ sarvataḥ parimaṇḍalaḥ ।। sa eva dvīpapaścārddhe mānasaḥ pṛthivīdharaḥ ।
eka eva mahāsāraḥ sanniveśo dvidhā kṛtaḥ ।। svādūdakenodadhinā sarvataḥ parivāritaḥ । puṣkaradvīpavistārādvistīrṇo asau samantataḥ ।। tasmindvīpe smṛtau dvau tu puṇyau janapadau śubhau ।
abhito mānasasyātha parvatasya tu maṇḍale ।। mahāvītaṃ tu yadvarṣa bāhyato mānasasya tat । tsyaivābhyantareṇāpi dhātakīkhaṇḍamucyate ।। daśavarṣasahasrāṇi tatra jīvati mānavāḥ ।
arogāḥ sukhabāhulyā mānasīṃ siddhimāsthitāḥ ।। masasāyuśca rūpaṃ ca tasminvarṣadvaye smṛtam । adhamottamā na teṣvasti tulyāste rūpaśīlataḥ ।। na tatra dasyurdamako nerṣyāsūyā bhayaṃ tathā ।
nigraho na ca daṇḍo asti na lobho na parigrahaḥ ।। satyānṛtaṃ na tatrāsti dharmādharmauṃ tathaiva ca । varṇāśramau vā vārtā vā pāśupālyaṃ vaṇikpathaḥ ।। trayī vidyā daṇḍanītiḥ śuśrūṣā śilpameva ca ।
varṣadvaye sarvametatpuṣkarasya na vidyate ।। na tatra varṣaṃ nadyo vā śītoṣṇaṃ vāpi vidyate । udbhidānyudakānyatra giriprasravaṇāni ca ।। uttarāṇāṃ kurūṇāṃ ca tulyakālo janastathā ।
