sarvarttususukhastatra jarākramavivarjitaḥ ।। ityeṣa dhātakīkhaṇḍe mahā vīte tathaiva ca । ānupūrvyādvidhiḥ kṛtsnaḥ puṣkarasya prakīrttitaḥ ।। svādūdakenodadhinā puṣkaraḥ parivāritaḥ ।
vistārānmaṇḍalāccaiva puṣkarasya samena tu ।। evaṃ dvīpāḥ samudraistu sapta saptabhirāvṛtāḥ । dvīpasyānantaro yastu sāmudrastatsamastu saḥ ।। evaṃ dvīpasamudrāṇāṃ vṛddhirjñeyā parasparāt ।
apāṃ caiva samudrekātsāmudra iti saṃjñitaḥ ।। viśantirnivasaṃtyasminprajā yasmāccaturvidhāḥ । tasmādvarṣamiti proktaṃ prajānāṃ sukhadaṃ yataḥ ।। ṛṣa ityeṣa ramaṇe vṛṣaśaktiprabandhane ।
ratiprabadhanātmiddhaṃ varṣaṃ tatteṣu tena vai ।। śuklapakṣe candravṛddhyā samudraḥ pūryate sadā । prakṣīyamāṇe bahule kṣīyate astamite khage ।। āpūryamāṇo hyudadhiḥ svata evābhipūryate ।
tathopakṣīyamāṇe api svātmanyevāvakṛṣyate ।। ukhāsthamagnisaṃyogādudriktaṃ dṛśyate yathā । mahodadhigataṃ toyaṃ svata udricyate tathā ।। anyūnānatiriktāṃśca varndvatyāpo hrasaṃti ca ।
udayāstamaye tvindau pakṣayoḥ śuklakṛṣṇayoḥ ।। kṣayavṛddhatvamudadheḥ somavṛddhikṣayātpunaḥ । daśottarāṇi pañcaiva hyaṅgulāni śatāni ca ।। apāṃ vṛddhiḥ kṣayo dṛṣṭaḥ sāmudrīṇāṃ tu parvasu ।
dvirāpkatvātsmṛtā dvīpāḥ sarvataścodakāvṛtāḥ ।। udakasyāyanaṃ yasmāttasmādudadhirucyate । aparvāṇastu girayaḥ parvabhiḥ parvatāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। plakṣadvīpe tu gomedaḥ parvatastena caucyate ।
śālmaliḥ śālmale dvīpe pūjyate sumahāvrataiḥ ।। kuśadvīpe kuśastaṃbastasyanāmnā sa ucyate । kraiñcadvīpe giriḥ kaiñco madhye janapadasya ha ।। śākadvīpe drumaḥ śākastasya nāmnā sa ucyate ।
nyagrodhaḥ puṣkaradvīpe tatratyaiḥ sa namaskṛtaḥ ।। mahādevaḥ pūjyate tu brahmā tribhuvaneśvaraḥ । tasminni vasati brahmā sādhyaiḥ sārddhaṃ prajāpatiḥ ।। upāsaṃte tatra devāstrayastriṃśanmaharṣibhiḥ ।
sa tatra pūjyate caiva deverdevotamotamaḥ ।। jaṃbūdvīpātpravarttante ratnāni vividhāni ca । dvīpeṣu teṣu sarveṣu prajānāṃ kramatastu vai ।। sarvaśo brahmavaryeṇa satyena ca damena ca ।
ārogyayuḥpramāṇābhyāṃ pramāṇaṃ dviguṇaṃ tataḥ ।। etasminpuṣkaradvīpe yaduktaṃ varṣakadvayam । gopāyati prajāstatra svayaṃbhūrjaḍa paṇḍitāḥ ।। īśvaro daṇḍasudyamya brahmā tribhuvaneśvaraḥ ।
sa viṣṇoḥ sacivo devaḥ sa pitā sa pitāmahaḥ ।। bhojanaṃ cāprayatnena tatra svayamupasthitam । ṣaḍrasaṃ sumahāvīryaṃ bhuñjate tu prajāḥ sadā ।। pareṇa puṣkarasyārddhe āvṛtyāvasthito mahān ।
svādūdakaḥ samudrastu samantātpariveṣṭya tam ।। pareṇa tasya mahatī dṛśyate lokasaṃsthitiḥ । kāñcanī dviguṇā bhūmiḥ sarvāhyekaśilopamā ।। tasyāpareṇa śailaśca paryāsātpasmiṇḍalaḥ ।
prakāśaścāprakāśaśca lokālokaḥ sa ucyate ।। ālokastasya cārvaktu nirālokastataḥ param । yojanānāṃ sahasrāṇi daśa tasyocchrayaḥ samṛtaḥ ।। tāvāṃśca vistarastasya pṛthivyāṃ kāmagaśca saḥ ।
āloko lokavṛttistho nirāloko hyalaukikaḥ ।। lokārddhe saṃmitā lokā nirālokāstu bāhyataḥ । lokavistāramātraṃ tu hyalokaḥ sarvato bahiḥ ।। paricchinnaḥ samantācca udakenāvṛtastu saḥ ।
ālokātparataścāpi hyaṇḍamā vṛtya tiṣṭhati ।। aṇḍasyāntastvime lokāḥ saptadvīpā ca medinī । bhūrloko atha bhuvarllokaḥ svarloko atha mahastathā ।। janastapastathā satyametāvāṃllokasaṃgrahaḥ ।
etāvāneva vijñeyo lokāntaścaiva yaḥ paraḥ ।। kuṃbhasthāyī bhavedyādṛvapratīcyāṃ diśi candramāḥ । āditaḥ śuklapakṣasya vapuścāṇḍasya tadvidham ।। aṇḍānāmīdṛśānāṃ tu koṭyo jñeyāḥ sahasraśaḥ ।
tiryagūrdhvamadho vāpi kāraṇasyāvyayātmanaḥ ।। dharaṇaiḥ prākṛtaistattadāvṛtaṃ prati saptabhiḥ । daśādhikyena cānyonyaṃ dhārayanti parasparam ।। parasparāvṛtāḥ sarve utpannāśca parasparam ।
aṇḍasyāsya samantāttu sanniviṣṭo ghanodadhiḥ ।। samantāttu vanodena dhāryamāṇaḥ sa tiṣṭati । bāhyato ghanato yasya tiryagūrddhvaṃ tu maṇḍalam ।। dhāryamāṇaṃ samantāttu tiṣṭhate yattu tejasā ।
ayoguḍanibho vāhnaḥ samantā nmaṇḍalākṛtiḥ ।। samantāddhanavātena dhāryamāṇaḥ sa tiṣṭhati । ghanavātaṃ tathākāśo dadhānaḥ khalu tiṣṭhati ।। bhūtādiśca tathā kāśaṃ bhūtādiścāpyasau mahān ।
mahāśca so apyanantena hyavyaktena tu dhāryate ।। anantamaparivyaktaṃ daśadhā sūkṣmameva ca । anantama kṛtātmānamanādinidhanaṃ ca yat ।। anityaṃ parato aghoramanālaṃbamanāmayam ।
naikayojanasāhasraṃ viprakṛṣṭamanāvṛtam ।। tama eva nirālokamamaryyādamadaiśikam । devānāmapyaviditaṃ vyavahāravivarjitam ।। tamasoṃte ca viśyātamākāśānte hyabhāsvaram ।
maryādāyāmanantasya devasyāyatanaṃ mahat ।। tridaśānāmagamyaṃ tatasthānaṃ divyamiti śrutiḥ । mahato devadevasya maryādā yā vyavasthitāḥ ।। candrādityāvadhastāttu ye lokāḥ prathitā budhaiḥ ।
te lokā ityabhihitā jagatasca na saṃśayaḥ ।। rasātalatalāḥ saptasaptaivorddhvatalāśca ye । saptaskandhastathā vāyoḥ sabrahmasadanā dvijāḥ ।। āpātālāddivaṃ yāvadatra pañcavidhā gatiḥ ।
pramāṇametajjagata eṣa saṃsārasāgaraḥ ।। anādyantāṃ vrajantyeva naikajātisamudbhavāḥ । vicitrā jagataḥ sā vai prakṛtirbrahmaṇaḥ sthitā ।। yaccaiha daivikaṃ vātha nisargaṃ bahuvistaraḥ ।
atīndriyermahābhāgaiḥ siddhairapi na lakṣitaḥ ।। pṛthivyaṃbvagnivāyūnāṃ nabhasastamasastathā । mānasasya tu dehasya anantasya dvijottamāḥ ।। kṣayo vā pariṇāmo vā anto vāpi na vidyate ।
ananta eṣa sarvatra evaṃ jñāneṣu paṭhyate ।। tasya coktaṃ mayā pūrva tasminnāmānukīrtane । yaḥ padmanābhanāmnā tu tatkārtsnyena ca kīrttitaḥ ।। sa eva sarvatra gataḥ sarvasthāneṣu pūjyate ।
bhūmau rasātale caiva ākāśe pavane anale ।। arṇaveṣu ca sarveṣu divi caiva na saṃśayaḥ । tathā tamasi vijñeya eṣa eva mahādyutiḥ ।। anekadhā vibhaktāṅgo mahāyogī janārdanaḥ ।
sarvalokeṣu lokeśa ijyate bahudhā prabhuḥ ।। evaṃ parasparotpanna dhāryante ca parasparam । ādhārādheyabhāvena vikārāste avikāriṇaḥ ।। pṛthvyādayo vikārāste paricchinnāḥ parasparam ।
parasparadhikāścaiva praviṣṭāste parasparam ।। yasmātsṛṣaṭāstu te anyonyaṃ tasmātsthairyamupāgatāḥ । prāgāsannaviśeṣāstu viśeṣo anyaviśeṣaṇāt ।। pṛthivyādyāstu vādyantāparicchinnāstrayastu te ।
guṇopacayasāreṇa paricchedo viśeṣataḥ ।। śeṣāṇāṃ tu paricchedaḥ saukṣmyānneha vibhāvyate । bhūtebhyaḥ paratastebhyo vyālokā sā dharā smṛtā ।। bhūtānyāloka ākāśe paricchinnāni sarvaśaḥ ।
pātre mahati pātrāṇi yathaivāntargatāni tu ।। bhavantyanyonyahīnāni parasparasamāśrayāt । tathā hyāloka ākāśe bhedāstvantargatā matāḥ ।। kṛttnānyetāni catvāri hyanyonyasyādhikāni tu ।
yāvadetāni bhūtāni tāvadutpattirucyate ।। tantunāmiva saṃtāro bhūteṣvantargato mataḥ । pratyā khyāya tu bhūtāni kāryotparttina vidyate ।। tasmātparimitā bhedāḥ smṛtāḥ kāryyātmakāstu te ।
kāraṇātmakāstathaika syurbhedā ye mahadādayaḥ ।। ityeṣa saṃniveśo vai mayā prokto vibhāgaśaḥ । saptadvīpasamudrāḍyo yāthātathyana vai dvijāḥ ।। vistarānmaṇḍalāścaiva prasaṃkhyānena caiva hi ।
vaiśvarūpradhānasya pariṇāmaikadeśikaḥ ।। adhiṣṭhitaṃ bhagavatā yasya sarvamidaṃ jagat । evaṃbhūtagaṇāḥ sapta sanniviṣṭāḥ parasparam ।। etāvānsaṃniveśastu mayā śakyaḥ prabhāṣitum ।
etāvadeva śrotavyaṃ saṃniveśe tu pārtheve ।। sapta prakṛtayastvetā dhārayanti parasparam । tāstvahaṃ parimāṇena naṃ saṃkhyātumihotsahe ।। asaṃkhyātāḥ prakṛtayastiryyagūrddhvamadhastathā ।
tārakāsaṃniveśaśca yāvaddivyānumaṇḍalam ।। paryyā yasanniveśastu bhūmestadanu maṇḍalaḥ । ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi kṛthivyā vai vicakṣaṇāḥ ।। adhaḥpramāṇamūrddhva ca vakṣyamāṇaṃ nibodhata ।
pṛthivī vāyurākāśamāpo jyotiśca pañcamam ।। anantā dhātavo hyetaṃ vyāpakāstu prakīrttitāḥ । jananī sarvabhūtānāṃ sarvasattvadharā dharā ।। nānājanapadākīrṇā nānādhiṣṭhānapattanā ।
nānānadanadīśailā naikajātisamākulā ।। anantā gīyate devī pṛthivī bahuvistarā । nadīnadasasudrasthāstanthā kṣudrāśrayasthitāḥ ।। parvatākāśasaṃsthāśca antarbhūmigātāśca yāḥ ।
āpo anantā hi vijñeyāstathāgniḥ sarvalokagaḥ ।। anantaḥ paṭhyate caiva vyāpakaḥ sarvasaṃbhavaḥ । tathākāśamanālekhyaṃ ramyaṃ nānāśrayaṃ smṛtam ।। anantaṃ paṭhyate caiva vāyuścākāśasambhavaḥ ।
āpaḥ pṛthivyāmudake pṛthivyupari saṃsthitāḥ ।। ākāśaścāparamatha punarbhūmiḥ punarjalam । evaṃ matamanantasya bhautikasya na vidyate ।। parasparaiḥ sopacitā bhūmiścaiva nibodhata ।
bhūmirjalamathā kāśamiti yā yā paraṃparā ।। sthitireṣā tu vikhyātā saptame asminnasātale । daśayojanasāhasramekaṃ bhaumaṃ rasātalam ।। sādhubhiḥ parisaṃkhyātamekaikenaiva vistaram ।
prathamaṃ tatvalaṃ nāma sutalaṃ tu tataḥ param ।। tatastalātalaṃ vidyādatalaṃ bahuvistaram । tator'vākca talaṃ nāma parataśca rasātalam ।। eteṣāmapyadhobhāge pātālaṃ saptamaṃ smṛtam ।
kṛṣṇabhaumaśca prathamo bhūmibhāgaḥ prakīrttitaḥ ।। pāṇḍubhūmirdvitīyastu tṛtīyo nīlamṛttikaḥ । pītabhaumaścaturthastu pañcamaḥ śarkarāmayaḥ ।। ṣaṣṭhaḥ śilāmayo jñeyaḥ sauvarṇaḥ saptamaḥ smṛtaḥ ।
prathame asmiṃstale khyātamasuredrasya mandiram ।। namucerindraśatrośca mahānādasya cālayam । puraṃ ca śaṅkukarṇasya kabandhasya ca mandiram ।। niṣkulādasya ca puraṃ prahṛṣṭajanasaṃkulam ।
rākṣasasya ca bhīmasya śūladantasya cālayam ।। lohitākṣakaliṅgānāṃ nagaraṃ śvāpadasya ca । dhanañjayasya ca puraṃ nāgendrasya mahātmanaḥ ।। kāliyasya ca nāgasya nagaraṃ kauśikasya ca ।
evaṃ purasahasrāṇi nāgadānavarakṣasām ।। tale jñeyāni prathame kṛṣṇabhaume na saṃśayaḥ । dvitīye sutale viprā daityendrasya ca rakṣasaḥ ।। mahājaṃbhasya tu tathā nagaraṃ prathamasya tu ।
iyagrīvasya kṛṣṇasya nikumbhasya ca mandiram ।। śaṅkhakhyasya ca daityasya nagaraṃ gomukhasya ca । rākṣasasya ca nīlasya meghasya kathanasya ca ।। ālayaṃ kukupādasya mahoṣṇīṣasya cālayam ।
kaṃbalasya ca nāgasya puramaśvatarasya ca ।। kadrūputrasya ca puraṃ takṣakasya mahātmanaḥ । evaṃ purasahasrāṇi nāgadānavarakṣasām ।। dvitīye asmin tale viprāḥ pāṇḍubhaume na saṃśayaḥ ।
tṛtīye tu tale khyātaṃ prahlādasya mahātmanaḥ ।। anudrādasya ca puraṃ puramagnimukhasya ca । tārakāśyasya ca puraṃ puraṃ triśirasastathā ।। śiśumārasya ca puraṃ tripurasya tathā puram ।
purañjanasya daityasya hṛṣṭapuṣṭajanākulam ।। cyavanasya tu vijñeyaṃ rākṣasasya ca mandiram । rākṣaseṃdrasya ca puraṃ kumbhilasya kharasya ca ।। virādhasya ca krūrasya puramulkāsukhasya ca ।
hemakasya ca nāgasya tathā pāṇḍurakasya ca ।। maṇināgasya ca puraṃ kapilasya ca mandiram । nedakasyoragapatorviśālākṣasya mandiram ।। evaṃ purasahasrāṇi nāgadānavarakṣasām ।
tṛtīye asmiṃstale viprā nīlabhaume na saṃśayaḥ ।। caturthe daityasiṃhasya kālanemermahātmanaḥ । gajakarṇasya ca puraṃ nagaraṃ kuñjarasya ca ।। rākṣaseṃdrasya ca puraṃ sumālerbahuvistaram ।
muñjasya lokanāthasya vṛkavaktrasya cālayam ।। bahuyojanavistīrṇaṃ bahupakṣisamākulam । nagalaṃ vainateyasya caturthe asminnasātale ।। pañcame śarkarābhaume bahuyojanavistaram ।
virojanasya nagaraṃ daityasiṃhasya dhīmataḥ ।। vaidyutasyāgniji hvasya hiraṇyākṣasya cālayam । puraṃ ca vidyujjihvasya rākṣasendrasya dhīmataḥ ।। sahāmeghasya ca puraṃ rākṣaseṃdrasya mālinaḥ ।
kirmīrasya ca nāgasya svastikasya jayasya ca ।। evaṃ purasahasrāṇi nāgadānavarakṣasām । pañcame asmiṃstale jñeyaṃ śarkarānicaye sadā ।। ṣaṣṭhe tale daityapateḥ kesare nagarottamam ।
suparvaṇaḥ pulomnaśca nagaraṃ mahiṣasya ca ।। rākṣaseṃdrasya ca puraṃ suroṣasya mahātmanaḥ । tatrāste suramāputraḥ śataśīrṣo mudā yutaḥ ।। mahendrasya sakhā śrīmānvāsukināma nāgarāṭ ।
evaṃ purasahasrāṇi nāgadānavarakṣasām ।। ṣaṣṭhe tale asminvikhyāte śilābhaume rasātale । saptame tu tale jñeyaṃ pātāle sarvapaścime ।। puraṃ baleḥ pramuditaṃ naranā rīgaṇākulam ।
asurāśīviṣaiḥ pūrṇaṃ sukhitairdevaśatrubhiḥ ।। mucukundasya detyasya tatraiva nagaraṃ mahāt । anekairditiputrāṇāṃ samudīrṇairmahāpuraiḥ ।। tathaiva nāganagarairdyutimadbhiḥ sahasraśaḥ ।
daityānāṃ dānavānāṃ ca samudīrṇairmahāpuraiḥ ।। udīrṇai rākṣasāvāsairanekaiśca samākulam । pātālānte ca viprendrā vistīṇa bahuyojane ।। āste raktāravindākṣo mahātmā hyajarāmaraḥ ।
dhautaśaṅkhodaravapurnīla vāsā mahābalaḥ ।। viśālabhogo dyutimāṃścitramālyadharo balī । rukmaśṛṅgāvadātena dīptāsyena virājatā ।। prabhurmukha sahasreṇa śobhate caikakuṇḍalī ।
sa jihvāmālayā dīpto lolajjvālānalārciṣā ।। jvālāmālāparikṣiptaḥ kailāsa iva lakṣya te । sa tu netrasahasreṇa dviguṇena virājatā ।। bālasūryābhitāmreṇa śarīrasnigdhapāṇḍunā ।
tasya kundenduvarṇasya netramālā virājate ।। taruṇādityamāleva śvetaparvatamūrddhani । vikarālocchritatanurlakṣyate śayanāsane ।। vistīrṇa iva medinyāṃ sahasraśikharo giriḥ ।
mahānāgairmahābhogairmahāvijñairmahātmabhiḥ ।। upāsyate mahātejā mahānāgapatiḥ svayam । sa rājā sarvanāgānāṃ śeṣo ananto mahādyutiḥ ।। sā vaiṣṇavī vyavahṛtirmaryādā yā vyavasthitā ।
saptaivamete kathitā vyavahāryā rasātalāḥ ।। devāsurama hānāgarākṣasādhyuṣitāḥ sadā । ataḥ paramanālokamagamyaṃ siddhasādhubhiḥ ।। devānāmapyaviditaṃ vyavahāravivakṣayā ।
pṛthvyaṃbuva ṅnivāyūnāṃ nabhasaśca dvijottamāḥ ।। mahattvamṛṣibhiścaivaṃ varṇyate nātra saṃśayaḥ । ata ūrddhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi sūryācandramasorgatim ।। sūryā candramasāvetau bhramato yāvadeva tu ।
prakāśaistu prabhābhistau maṇḍalābhyāṃ samucchritau ।। saptānāṃ tu samudrāṇāṃ dvīpānāṃ satu vistaraḥ । vistarārddhe pṛthivyāstu bhavedanyatra bāhyataḥ ।। paryāsaparimāṇaṃ tu candrādityau prakāśataḥ ।
paryāstātpārimāṇyena bhūmestulyaṃ divaṃ smṛtam ।। avati trīnimāṃllokān yasmātsūryaḥ paribhraman । avidhātuḥ prakāśākhyo hyavanātsa raviḥ smṛtaḥ ।। ataḥ paraṃ pravakṣyāmi pramāṇaṃ candrasūryayoḥ ।
mahittattvānmahīśabdo ahyasminvarṣe nipādyate ।। asya bhāratavarṣasya viṣkaṃbhāttulyavistṛtam । maṇḍalaṃ bhāskarasyātha yojanāni nibodhata ।। navayojanasāhasro vistāro bhāskarasya tu ।
vistārātrriguṇaścāsya pariṇāhastu maṇḍale ।। viṣkaṃbhamaṇḍalāccaiva bhāskarāddviguṇaḥ śaśī । atha pṛthivyā vakṣyāmi pramāṇaṃ yojanaiḥ saha ।। saptadvīpasamudrāyā vistāro maṇḍalaṃ ca yat ।
ityetadiha saṃkhyātaṃ purāṇe parimāṇataḥ ।। tadvakṣyāmi samākhyāya sāṃpratairabhimānibhiḥ । abhimāninovyatītā ye tulyāste sāṃprataistviha ।। devā ye vai vyatītāstu rūpairnāmabhireva ca ।
tasmāttu sāṃpratairdevairvakṣyāmi vasudhātalam ।। divāstu sanniveśaṃ vai sāṃprataireva kṛtsnaśaḥ । śatārddhakoṭivistārā pṛthivī kṛtsnaśaḥ smṛtā ।। tasyā ūrddhvapramāṇena meroryāvattu saṃsthitiḥ ।
pṛthivyā hyarddhavistāro yojanāgrātprakīrttitaḥ ।। merormadhyātpratidiśaṃ koṭirekā tu sā smṛtā । tathā śātasahasrāṇāmekona navatiḥ punaḥ ।। pañcāśattu sahasrāṇi pṛthivyarddhasya maṇḍalam ।
gaṇitaṃ yojanāgrāttu koṭyastvekādaśa smṛtāḥ ।। tathā śatasahasrāṇi saptatriṃśādhikāni tu । ityetadiha saṃśyātaṃ pṛthivyantasya maṇḍalam ।। tārakāsaṃniveśāsya divi yāva cca maṇḍalam ।
paryāsasanniveśaśca bhūmeryāvattu maṇḍalam ।। paryāsaparimāṇena bhūmestulyaṃ divaḥ smṛtam । saptānāmapi dvīpānāmeta tsthānaṃ prakīrtitam ।। paryāyaparimāṇena maṇḍalānugatena ca ।
uparyupari lokānāṃ chatravatparimaṇḍalam ।। saṃsthitirvihitā sarvā yeṣu tiṣṭhanti jantavaḥ । etadaṇḍakapālasya pramāṇaṃ parikīrttitam ।। aṇḍasyāntastvime lokāḥ saptadvīpā ca medinī ।
bhūrlokaśca bhuvarllokastṛtīyassṛriti ssvataḥ ।। maharlloko janaścaiva tapaḥ satyaṃ ca saptamam । ete sapta kṛtā lokāśchatrākārā vyavasthitāḥ ।। svakairāvaraṇaiḥ sūkṣmairdhāryamāṇāḥ pṛthakpṛthak ।
daśabhāgādhikābhiśca tābhiḥ prakṛtibhirbahiḥ ।। pūryamāṇā viśeṣaiśca samutpannaiḥ parasparāt । asyāṇḍasya samantācca sanniviṣṭo ghanodadhiḥ ।। pṛthivyā maṇḍalaṃ kṛtsnaṃ ghanatoyena dhāryate ।
ghanodadhiḥ pareṇātha dhāryyate ghanatejasā ।। bāhyato ghanatejasca tiryyagūrddhvaṃ tu maṇḍalam । saṃmatāddhanavātena dhāryamāṇaṃ pratiṣṭhitam ।। ghanavātaṃ tathākāśamākāśaṃ ca mahātmanā ।
bhūtādinā vṛtaṃ sarvaṃ bhūtādirmahatā vṛtaḥ ।। vṛto mahānanantena pradhānenāvya yātmanā । purāṇi lokapālānāṃ pravakṣyāmi yathākramam ।। jyotirguṇapracārasya pramāṇaparisiddhaye ।
meroḥ prācyāṃ diśi tathā mānasasyaiva mūrddhani ।। vasvaukasārā māhendrī purī hemapariṣkṛtā । dakṣiṇena punarmerormānasasyaiva mūrddhani ।। vaivasvato niva sati yamaḥ saṃyamane pure ।
pratīcyāṃ tu punarmerormānasasyaiva mūrddhani ।। sukhā nāma purī ramyā varuṇasyāpi dhīmataḥ । varuṇo yādasāṃ nāthassukhākhye vasate pure ।। diśyuttarasyāṃ merostu mānasasyaiva mūrddhani ।
tulyā mahendrapuryyāstu somasyāpi vibhāvarī ।। mānasottaravṛṣṭe tu lokapālāścaturdiśam । sthitā dharmavyavasthārtha lokamaṃrakṣaṇāya ca ।। lokapālopariṣṭāttu sarvato dakṣiṇāyane ।
kāṣṭhāgatasya sūryasya gatiyā tāṃ nibodhata ।। dakṣiṇo apakrame sūryyaḥ kṣipteṣuriva sarpati । jyotiṣāṃ cakramādāya satataṃ parigacchati ।। madhyagaścāmarāvatyāṃ yadā bhavati bhāskaraḥ ।
vaivasvate saṃyamate udayastatra dṛśyate ।। sukhāyāmarddharātraṃ syādvibhāyāmastameti ca । vaivasvate saṃyamane madhyagaḥ syādraviryadā । sukhāyāmatha vāruṇyāmuttiṣṭhansa tu dṛśyate ।।
vibhāyā marddharātraṃ syānmāhendyāmastameti ca । yadā dakṣiṇapurveṣāmaparāhṇo vidhīyate ।। dakṣiṇāparadeśyānāṃ pūrvahṇaḥ parikī rttitaḥ । teṣāmapararātraśca ye janā uttarāḥ pare ।।
deśā uttarapūrvā ye pūvarātrastu tānprati । evamevottareṣvar ke bhuvaneṣu virājate ।। sukhāyāsatha vāruṇyāṃ madhyāhne cāryamā yadā । vibhāyāṃ somapuryāṃ vā uttiṣṭhati vibhāvasuḥ ।।
rātryarddha cāmarāvatyāmastameti yamasya ca । somapuryā vibhāyāṃ tu madhyāhne syāddivākaraḥ ।। mahedrasyāmarāvatyāṃ sūrya uttiṣṭhate tadā । arddharātraṃ saṃyamane vāruṇyāmastameti ca ।।
sa śīghrameva paryeti bhāskaro alātaca travat । bhramanvai bhramamārṇāni ṛkṣāṇi carate raviḥ ।। evaṃ caturṣu pārśveṣu dakṣiṇāṃ tena sarpati । udayāstamane cāsāvṛtti ṣṭhati punaḥ punaḥ ।।
pūvāhṇe cāparāhṇe ca dvau dvau devālayau tu saḥ । tapatyarkaśca madhyāhne taireva ca svaraśmibhiḥ ।। udito varddhamānābhirāmadhyāhnaṃ tapanraviḥ । ataḥ paraṃ hrasaṃtībhirgobhirastaṃ nigacchati ।।
udayāstamayābhyāṃ ca smṛte pūrvāpare diśau । yāvatpurastāttapati tāpatpṛṣṭhe atha pārśvayoḥ ।। yatrodyandṛśyate sūryasteṣāṃ sa udayaḥ samṛtaḥ । praṇāśaṃ gacchate yatra teṣāmastaḥ sa ucyate ।।
sarveṣāmuttare meruloṅkālokaśca dakṣiṇe । vidūrabhāvādarkasya bhūmilekhāvṛtasya ca ।। līyante raśmayo yasmāttena rātrau na dṛśyate । grahanakṣatrasomānāṃ darśanaṃ bhāskarasya ca ।।
ucdhrayasya pramāṇena jñeyamastamathodayam । śuklacchāyo agnirā paśca kṛṣṇacchāyā ca medinī ।। vidūrabhāvādarkasya hyudyate api viraśimatā । raktabhāvo viraśmatvādraktatvācjāpyanuṣṇatā ।।
lekhāyāmāsthitaḥ sūryo yatra yatra ca dṛśyate । ūrddhva śātasahasra tu yojanānāṃ sa dṛśyate ।। prabhā hi saurī pādena hyastaṃ gacchati bhāskare । agnimāviśate rādrau tasmāddūrātprakāśate ।।
udite hi punaḥ sūrye hyauṣṇyamāgneyamāviśet । saṃyukto vahninā sūryastapate tu tato divā ।। prākāśyaṃ ca tathauṣṇyaṃ ca saurāgneye ca tejasī । parasparānupraveśāddīpyete tu divāniśam ।।
uttare caiva bhūmyarddhe tathā tasmiṃśca dakṣiṇe । uttiṣṭhati tathā sūrye rātrirāviśatatvapaḥ ।। tasmācchītā bhaktyāṃpo divārātripraveśanāt । astaṃ yāti punaḥ sūrye dinamāviśate tvaṣaḥ ।।
tasmāduṣṇā bhavatyāpo naktamahnaḥ praveśanāt । etena kramayogena bhūmyarddhe dakṣiṇottare ।। udayāstamaner'kasya ahorātraṃ viśatyapaḥ । denaṃ sūryaprakāśākhyaṃ tāmasī rātrirūcyate ।।
tasmādvyavasthitā rātriḥ sūryāpekṣamahaḥ smṛtam । evaṃ puṣkaramadhyena yadā sarpati bhāskaraḥ ।। aṃśāṃśakaṃ tu medinyāṃ muhūrttenaiva gacchati । yojanāgrānmuhūrttasya iha saṃkhyāṃ nibodhata ।।
pūrṇe śatasahasrāṇāmekatriṃśādhikaṃ smṛtam । pañcāśattu tathānyāni sahasrāṇyadhikāni ca ।। mauhūrtti kī gatirhyeṣā sūryasya tu vidhīyate । etena gatiyogena yadā kāṣṭhāṃ tu dakṣiṇām ।।
paryāgacchetpataṅgo asau madhye kāṣṭhāntameva hi । madhyena puṣkarasyātha bhramate dakṣiṇāyane ।। mānasottaraśaile tu antare viṣuvaṃ ca tat । sarpate dakṣiṇāyāṃ tu kāṣṭhāyāṃ vai nibodhata ।।
navakoṭyaḥ prasaṃkhyātā yojanaiḥ parimaṇḍalam । tathā śatasahasrāṇi catvāriṃśacca pañca ca ।। ahorātrātpataṅgasya gatireṣā vidhīyate । dakṣiṇādvinivṛtto asau viṣuvastho yadā raviḥ ।।
kṣīrodasya samudrasyottarataścādritaścaran । maṇḍalaṃ viṣuvattasya yojanaistannibodhata ।। tisraḥ koṭyastu saṃkhyātā viṣuvasyāpi maṇḍalam । tathā śatasahasrāṇāmaśītyekādhikā punaḥ ।।
śravaṇe cottaraṣāḍhe citrabhānuryadā bhavet । śākadvīpasya ṣaṣṭhasya uttarāto diśaścaran ।। utarāyāḥ pramāṇaṃ ca kāṣṭhāyā maṇḍalasya ca । yojanāgrātprasaṃkhyātā koṭirekā tu sa dvijāḥ ।।
aśītirniyutānīha yojanānāṃ tathaiva ca । aṣṭapañcāśataṃ cava yojanānyadhikāni tu ।। nāgavīthyuttarāvīthī hyaja vīthī ca dakṣiṇā । mūlaṃ caiva tathāṣāḍhe tvajavīthyudayāstrayaḥ ।।
aśvinī kṛttikā yāmyaṃ nāgavīthyudayāstrayaḥ । kāṣṭhayorantaraṃ yacca tadvakṣyeyajanaiḥ punaḥ ।। etacchatasahasrāṇāmaṣṭābhiścottaraṃ śatam । trayaḥ śatādhikāścanye trayastriṃśacca yojanaiḥ ।।
kāṣṭhayorantaraṃ hyetadyojanāgrātprakīrtitam । kāṣṭhayorlekhayoścaiva hyantaraṃ dakṣiṇottare ।। tenvavakṣye prasaṃkhyāya cojanaistannibodhata । ekaikamantaraṃ tasya viyutānyekasaptatiḥ ।।
sahasrāṇyatiriktāśca tato anyā pañcasaptatiḥ । lekhayoḥ kāṣṭhayoścaiva bāhyābhyantarayoḥ smṛtam ।। abhyantaraṃ tu paryeti maṇḍalānyuttarāyaṇe । bāhyato dakṣiṇe caiva satataṃ tu yathākramam ।।
maṇḍalānāṃ śataṃ pūrmaṃ tryaśītyadhikamuttaram । carate dakṣiṇe cāpi tāvadeva vibhāvasuḥ ।। pramāṇaṃ maṇḍalasyātha yojanāgraṃ nibodhata । yojanānāṃ sahasrāṇi saptādaśa samāsataḥ ।।
śate dve punarapyanye yojanāmāṃ prakīrttite । ekaviṃśatibhiścaiva yojanairadhikairhi te ।। etatpramāṇamākhyātaṃ yojanairmaṇḍalasya ca । viṣkaṃbho maṇḍalasyātha tiryak sa tu vidhīyate ।।
pratyahaṃ carate tāni sūryā vai maṇḍalakramāt । kulālacakraparyanto yathā śīghraṃ nivarttate ।। dakṣiṇaprakrame sūryastathā śīghraṃ pravarttate । tasmātprakṛṣṭāṃ bhūmiṃ tu kālenālpena gacchati ।।
sūryo dvādaśabhiḥ śairghyānmuhūrtairdakṣiṇāyane । trayodaśārddhamṛkṣāṇāmahnā tu carate raviḥ ।। muhūrtai stāvadṛkṣāṇi naktamaṣṭādaśaiścaran । kulālacakramadhye tu yathā mandaṃ prasarpati ।।
tathodagayane sūryaḥ sarpate mandavikramaḥ । tasmā ddīrghena kālena bhūmiṃ svalpāni gacchati ।। aṣṭādaśa muhūrta tu uttarāyaṇapaścimam । aho bhavati taccāpi carate mandavikramaḥ ।।
trayodaśārddhaṃ mādyena tvṛkṣāṇāṃ carate raviḥ । muhūrtaistāvadṛkṣāṇi naktaṃ dvādaśabhiścaran ।। tato mandataraṃ nābhyāṃ cakraṃ bhramati vai yathā । mṛtpiṇḍa iva madhyastho dhruvo bhramati vai tathā ।।
triṃśanmuhūrtānevāhurahorātraṃ dhruvo bhraman । ubhayoḥ kāṣṭhayormadhye bhramate maṇḍalāni tu ।। kulālacakranābhiśca yathā tatraiva varttate । dhruvastathā hi vijñeyastatraiva parīvarttate ।।
ubhayoḥ kāṣṭhayormadhye bhramate maṇḍalāni saḥ । divānaktaṃ ca sūryasya mandā śīghrā ca vai gātiḥ ।। uttaraprakrame cāpi divā mandā gatistathā । tathaiva ca punarnaktaṃ śīghrā sūryasya vai gātiḥ ।।
dakṣiṇaprakrameṇaiva divā śīghraṃ vidhīyate । gatiḥ sūryasya naktaṃ ca mandā caiva gatistathā ।। evaṃ gativiśeṣeṇa vibhajan rātryahāni tu । tajāpi saṃcaranmārgaṃ samena viṣameṇa ca ।।
lokālokasthitā hyete lokapālāścaturdiśam । agastyaścarate teṣāmupariṣṭājjavena tu ।। bhuñjannasāpahorā tramevaṃ gativiśeṣaṇam । dakṣiṇe nāgavīthyāstu lokālokasya cottare ।।
lokasantānako hyeṣa vaiśvānarapathādvahiḥ । pṛṣṭe yāvatprabhā saurī purastātsaṃprakāśate ।। pārśvataḥ pṛṣṭhataścaiva lokālokasya varttate । yojanānāṃ sahasrāṇi daśakaṃ tucchrito giriḥ ।।
prakāśaścāprakāśaśca sarvataḥ parimaṇḍalaḥ । nakṣatracandrasūryaśca grahaistārāgaṇaiḥ saha ।। abhyantaraṃ prakāśante lokālokasya vai gireḥ । etāvāneva lokastu nirālokastataḥ param ।।
lokenālokavāneṣa nirālokastvalokataḥ । lokālokaṃ tu saṃdhatte yasmātsuryaparigraham ।। tasmātsandhyeti tāmāhuruṣāvyuṣṭyoryadantaram । uṣā rātriḥ smṛtā viprairvyuṣṭiścāpi tvahaḥ smṛtam ।।
sūryāgnigrasamānānāṃ saṃdhyākāle hi rakṣasām । prajāpatiniyogena śāpastveṣāṃ durātmanām ।। akṣayatvaṃ tu dehasya prāpitāmraṇaṃ tathā । tisraḥ koṭyastu vikhyātā mandehā nāma rākṣasāḥ ।।
prārthayanti sahasrāṃśubhudayantaṃ dinedine । tāpayantaṃ durātmānaḥ sūryamicchanti khāditum ।। atha sūryasya teṣāṃ ca yuddhamāsītsudāruṇam । tato brahmā ca devāśca brāhmamāścaiva sattamāḥ ।।
saṃdhyāṃ tu samupāsīnāḥ prakṣipanti jalaṃ sadā । oṅkārabrahmasaṃyuktaṃ gāyatryā cābhimantritam ।। sphūrjajjyotiśca caṇḍāṃśustathā dīpyati bhāskaraḥ । tataḥ punarmahātejā mahābalaparākramaḥ ।।
yojanānāṃ sahasrāṇi ūrddhvamuttiṣṭhate śatam । prayāti bhagavānāśu brāhmaṇairabhirakṣitaḥ । vālakhilyaiśca munibhirdhṛtārciḥ samarīcibhiḥ ।। kāṣṭhā nimeṣā daśa pañca caiva triṃśacca kāṣṭhā gaṇayetkalāṃ tu ।
triṃśatkalāścāpi bhavenmuhūrttastaistriṃśatā rātryahanī samete ।। hrāsavṛddhī tvaharbhāgairdivasānāṃ yathākramāt ।। saṃdhyā muhūrttamātrā tu hrāsavṛddhistu sā smṛtā । lekhāprabhṛtyathāditye trimuhūrttagate tu vai ।।
prātastataḥ smṛtaḥ kālo bhāgaścāhnaḥ sa pañcamaḥ । tasmātprātastanātkālātrrimuhūrttastu saṃgavaḥ ।। madhyāhnastrimuhūrttastu tasmātkālaśca saṃgavāt । tasmānmadhyandinātkālādaparāhṇa iti smṛtaḥ ।।
traya eva muhūrttāstu kālāgaḥ smṛto budhaiḥ । aparāhṇe vyatīte tu kālaḥ sāyāhna ucyate ।। daśapañca muhūrtāhno muhūrttāstraya eva ca । daśapañcamuhūrtta vai hyaharvaiṣuvataṃ smṛtam ।।
varddhante ca hrasaṃte ca hyayane dakṣiṇottare । ahastu grasate rātriṃ rātriśca grasate tvahaḥ ।। śaradvasaṃtayormadhyaṃ viṣuvatparibhāvyate । ahorātre kalāścaiva samaṃ somaḥ samaśnute ।।
tathā pañcadaśāhāni pakṣa ityabhidhīyate । dvauca pakṣaubhavenmāso dvaumāsāvarkajāvṛtuḥ ।। ṛtutritayamayane dve hi varṣaṃ tu saurakam । nimeṣā vidyutaścaiva kāṣṭāstā daśa pañca ca ।।
kalāstāstriśataḥ kāṣṭhā mātrā śītidvayātmikā । saptaikā dvyadhikā triśanmātrā ṣaṭatriṃśaduttarā ।। dviṣāṣṭinā trayoviṃśanmātrāyāśca kalā bhavet । catvāri śatsahasrāṇi śatānyaṣṭau ca vidyutaḥ ।।
saptatiścaiva tatrāpi navatiṃ viddhi niścaye । catvāryeva śatānyāhurvidyute dve ca saṃyute ।। varāṃśo hyeṣa vijñeyo nāḍikā cātra kāraṇam । saṃvatsarādayaḥ pañca caturmānavikalpitāḥ ।।
niścayaḥ sarvakālasya yugamityabhidhīyate । saṃvatsarastu prathamo dvitīyaḥ parivatsaraḥ ।। iḍāvatsarastṛtīyastu caturthaścānuvatsaraḥ । pañcamovatsarasteṣāṃ kālastu yugasaṃhitaḥ ।।
triṃśacchataṃ bhavetpūrṇaṃ parvaṇāṃ tu raveryuge । śatānyaṣṭādaśa triṃśadudayādbhāskarasya ca ।। ṛtavastriṃśataḥ saurādayanāni daśaiva tu । pañca ca triśataṃ cāpi ṣaṣṭivarṣaṃ ca bhāskaram ।।
triśadeva tvahorātrāstaistu māsastu bhāskaraḥ । ekaṣaṣṭi tvahorātramṛtureko vibhāvyate ।। ahnāṃ tu tryadhikāśītiḥ śataṃ cāpyadhikaṃ bhavet । mānaṃ taccitrabhānostu vijñeyamayanasya ha ।।
sauraṃ saumyaṃ tu vijñeyaṃ nākṣatraṃ sāvanaṃ tathā । mānānyetāni catvāri yaiḥpurāṇe hi niścayaḥ ।। yaḥ śvetasyottaraścaiva śṛṅgavānnāma parvvataḥ । trīṇitasya tu śṛṅgāṇi spṛśantīva nabhastalam ।।
taiścāpi śṛṅgaissanagaḥ śṛṅgavā niti kathyate । ekaśca mārgaviṣkaṃbhavistāraścāsya kīrtitaḥ ।। tasya vai pūrvataḥ śṛṅgaṃ madhyamaṃ taddhiraṇmayam । dakṣiṇaṃ rājataṃ caiva śṛṅgaṃ tu sphaṭikaprabham ।।
sarvaratnamayaṃ caiva śṛṅgamuttaramuttamam । evaṃ kūṭaistribhiḥ śailaḥ śṛṅgavāniti viśrutaḥ ।। yattadvai pūrvataḥ śṛṅgaṃ tadarkaḥ pratipadyate । śaradvasaṃtayormadhye madhyamāṃ gatimāsthitaḥ ।।
atastulyamahorātraṃ karoti timirā pahaḥ । haritāśca hayā divyāstasya yuktā mahārathe । anuliptā ivābhānti padmaraktairgabhastibhiḥ ।। meṣati ca tulānte ca bhāskarodayataḥ smṛtāḥ ।
muhūrttā daśa pañcaiva aho rātriśca tāvatī ।। kṛttikānāṃ yadā sūryaḥ prathamāṃ śagato bhavet । viśākhānāṃ tadā jñeyaścaturthāṃśa niśākaraḥ ।। viśākhānāṃ yadā sūryaścarateṃśaṃ tṛtīyakam ।
tadā candraṃ vijānīyātkṛttikāśirasi sthitam ।। viṣuvaṃ taṃ vijānīyādevamāhurmaharṣayaḥ ।। sūryeṇa viṣuvaṃ vidyā tkālaṃ somena lakṣayet । samā rātrirahaścaiva yadā tadviṣuvaṃ bhavet ।।
tadā dānāni deyāni pitṛbhyo viṣuveṣu ca । brāhmaṇebhyo viśeṣeṇa mukhametattu daivatam ।। ūnamāsādhimāsau ca kalā kāṣṭhā muhūrttakāḥ । paurṇamāsī tathā jñeyā amāvāsyā tathaiva ca ।
sinīvālī kuhūścaiva rākā cānumatistathā ।। tapastapasyau madumādhavau ca śukraḥśuciścāyanamuttaraṃ syāt । nabhonabhasyāviṣaūrjasaṃjñau sahaḥsahasyāviti dakṣiṇaṃ syāt ।। ārtavāśca tato jñeyā pañcābdā brahmaṇāḥ sutāḥ ।।
tasmācca ṛtavo jñeyā ṛtubhyo hyārttavāḥ smṛtāḥ । tasmādṛtumukhī jñeyā amāvāsyāsya parvaṇaḥ ।। tasmāttu viṣuvaṃ jñeyaṃ pitṛdevahitaṃ sadā । parva jñātvā na muhyeta pitrye daive ca mānavaḥ ।।
tasmātsmṛtaṃ pracānāṃ vai viṣuvatsarvagaṃ sadā । ālokāttu smṛto loko lokālokaḥ sa ucyate ।। lokapālāḥ sthitāstatra lokālokasya madhyataḥ । catvāraste mahātmānastiṣṭantyābhūtasaṃplavāt ।।
sudhāmā caiva vairājaḥ kardamaḥ śaṅkhapāstathā । hiraṇyaromā parjanyaḥ ketumānrājasaśca yaḥ ।। nirdvandvā nirabhīmānā niḥ sīmā niṣparigrahāḥ । lokapālāḥ sthitā hyete lokāloke caturdiśam ।।
uttaraṃ yadapastasya hyajavīthyāśca dakṣiṇām । pitṛyānaḥ sa vai panthā vaiśvānarapathādvahiḥ ।। tatrāsate prajāvanto munayo ye agnihotriṇaḥ । lokasya saṃtānakarāḥ pitṛyānapathe sthitāḥ ।।
bhūtāraṃbhakṛtaṃ karma āśiṣo ṛtvigudyatāḥ । prārabhante lokakāmāsteṣāṃ panthāḥ sa dakṣiṇāḥ ।। calitaṃ te punardharmaṃ sthāpayanti yugeyuge । saṃtaptāstapasā caiva maryādābhiḥ śrutena ca ।।
jāyamānāstu pūrve vai paścimānāṃ gṛhe ṣviha । paścimāścaiva pūrveṣāṃ jāyante nidhaneṣvapi ।। evamāvarttamānāste tiṣṭhantyābhūtasaṃplavāt । aṣṭāśītisahasrāṇi ṛṣīmāṅgṛhamedhinām ।।
saviturdakṣiṇaṃ mārgaśritā hyācandratārakam । kriyāvatāṃ prasaṃkhyaiṣā ye śmaśānāni bhejire ।। lokasaṃvyavahārāśca bhūtāraṃbhakṛtena ca । icchādveṣapravṛttyā ca maithunopagamena vai ।।
tathā kāmakṛteneha sevanādviṣayasya ca । etaistaiḥ kāraṇaiḥ siddhā ye śmaśānāni bhejire ।। pracaiṣiṇaste munayo dvāpareṣviha jajñire । nāgavīthyuttaro yaśca saptarṣigaṇadakṣiṇaḥ ।।
uttaraḥ savituḥ panthā devayānaśca sa smṛtaḥ । yatra te vāsinaḥ siddhā vimalā brahmacāriṇaḥ ।। saṃtatiṃ te jugupsaṃte tasmānmṛtyustu tairjitaḥ । aṣṭāśītisahasrāṇi ṛṣīṇāmūrddhvaretasām ।।
udakpanthānamatyarthaṃ śritā hyāśritasaṃplavāt । te saṃprayogāllokasya maithunasya ca varjanāt ।। icchādveṣanivṛttyā ca bhūtāraṃbhavivarjanāt । punaścākāmasaṃyogācchabdāderdeṣadar śanāt ।।
ityetaiḥ kāraṇaiḥ siddhāste amṛtatvaṃ hi bhejire । ābhūtasaṃplavasthānāmamṛtatvaṃ vibhāvyate ।। trailokyasthiti kālāya punardārābhigaminām । brūṇahatyāśvamedhābhyāṃ puṇyapāpakṛto apare ।।
ābhūtasaṃplavānte tu kṣīyaṃ te hyūrdhvaretasaḥ । urddhvottaramṛṣibhyastu dhruvo yatra sa vai smṛtaḥ ।। etadviṣṇupadaṃ divyaṃ tṛtīyaṃ vyomni bhāsvaram । yatra gatvā na śocanti tadviṣṇoḥ paramaṃ padam ।
dharmadhruvādyāstiṣṭhanti yatra te lokasādhakāḥ ।। svāyaṃbhūvanisarge tu vyākhyātānyantarāṇi ca । bhaviṣyāṇi ca sarvāṇi teṣāṃ vakṣyāmyanukramam ।। etacchrutavā tu munayaḥ papracchū romaharṣaṇam ।
sūryācandramasoścāraṃ grahāṇāṃ caiva sarvaśaḥ ।। ṛṣaya ṛcuḥ । bhramanti kathametāni jyotīṣi divamaṇḍalam । avyūhena ca sarvāṇi tathaivāsaṃkareṇa vā ।।
kaścidbhāmayate tāni bhramante yadi vā svayam । etadveditumicchāmastanno nigada sattama ।। bhūtasaṃmohanaṃ hyetadvadato me nibodhata । pratyakṣamapi dṛśyaṃ ca saṃmohayati yatprajāḥ ।।
yo ayaṃ caturddiśaṃ pucche śaiśumāre vyavasthitaḥ । uttānapādaputro asau meḍhībhūto dhruvo divi ।। sa vai bhrāmayate nityaṃ candrādityau grahaiḥ saha । bhramantamanugacchanti nakṣatrāṇi ca cakravat ।।
dhruvasya manasā cāsau sarvate jyotiṣāṃ gaṇaḥ । sūryācandramasau tārā nakṣatrāṇi grahaiḥ saha ।। vātānīkamayairbandhairdhruve baddhāni tāni vai । teṣāṃ yogaśca bhedaśca kālaścārastathaiva ca ।।
astodayau tathotpātā ayane dakṣaṇottare । viṣuvadgrahavarṇāśca druvātsarvaṃ pravarttate ।। varṣā gharmo himaṃ rātriḥ saṃdhyā caiva dinaṃ tathā । śubhāśubhaṃ prajānāṃ ca dhruvātsarvaṃ pravarttate ।।
dhruveṇādhiṣṭitaścaiva sūryo apo gṛhya varṣati । tadeṣa dīpta kiraṇaḥ sa kālagnirdivākaraḥ ।। parivarttakramādviprā bhābhirālokayan diśaḥ । sūryaḥ kiramajālena vāyuyuktena sarvaśaḥ ।।
jagato jalamādatte kṛtsnasya dvijasattamāḥ । ādityapītaṃ sakalaṃ somaḥ saṃkramate jalam ।। nāḍībhirvāyuyuktābhirlokadhārā pravarttate । yatsomātsravate hyaṃbu tadanneṣveva tiṣṭhati ।।
meghā vāyuvighātena visṛjanti jalaṃ bhūvi । evamutkṣipyate caiva patate cāsakṛjjalam ।। na nāśa udakasyāsti tadeva parivarttate । saṃdhāraṇārthaṃ lokānāṃ māyaiṣā viśvanirmitā ।।
anyā māyayā vyāptaṃ trailokyaṃ sacarācaram । viśveśo lokakṛddevaḥ sahasrākṣaḥ prajāpatiḥ ।। dhātā kṛtsnasya lokasya prabhaviṣṇurdivākaraḥ । sārvalokikamaṃbho yattatsomānnabhasaśvyutam ।।
somādhāraṃ jagatsarvametattathyaṃ prakīrtitam । sūryāduṣṇaṃ nisravate somācchītaṃ pravarttate ।। śītoṣṇavīryauṃ dvāvetau yuktyā dhārayato jagat । somādhārā nadī gaṅgā pavitrā vimalodakā ।।
bhadrasomapurogāśca mahānadyo dvijottamāḥ । sarvabhūtaśarīreṣu hyāpo hyanusṛtāśca yāḥ ।। teṣu saṃdahyamāneṣu jaṅgamasthāvareṣu ca । dhūmabhūtāstu tā hyāpo niṣkāmantīha sarvaśaḥ ।।
tena cābhrāṇi jāyante sthānamabhramayaṃ smṛtam । tejor'kaḥ sarvabhūtebhya ādatte raśmibhirjalam ।। samudrādvāyusaṃyogādvahantyāpo gabhastayaḥ । saṃjīvanaṃ ca sasyānāmaṃbhastadamṛtopamam ।।
tatastvṛtuvaśātkāle parivatya divākaraḥ । yacchatyāpo hi meghebhyaḥ ghuklāśuklairgabhastibhiḥ ।। abhrasthāḥ prapatantyāpo vāyunā samudīritāḥ । sarvabhūtahitārthāya vāyumiśrāḥ samantataḥ ।।
tato varṣati ṣaṇmāsānsarvabhūtavivṛddhaye । vāyavyaṃ stanitaṃ caiva vaidyutaṃ cāgnisaṃbhavam ।। mehanācca mihedhātomaghatvaṃ vyajayanti hi । na bhraśyanti yataścāpastadabhaṃ kavayo viduḥ ।।
meghānāṃ punarutpattiśtrividhā yonirucyate । āgneyā brahmajāścaiva pakṣajāśca pṛthagvidhāḥ ।। tridhā meghāḥ samākhyātāsteṣāṃ vakṣyāmi saṃbhavam । āgneyā stūṣṇajāḥ proktāsteṣāṃ dhūmapravarttanam ।।
śītadurdinavātā ye svaguṇāste vyavasthitāḥ । mahiṣāśca vārāhāśca mattamātaṅgarūpiṇaḥ ।। bhūtvā dharaṇimabhyetya ramante vicaranti ca । jīmūtā nāma te meghā hyetebhyo jīvasaṃbhavaḥ ।।
vidyudguṇavihīnāśca jaladhārā vilaṃbinaḥ । mūkameghā mahākāyā āvahasya vaśānugāḥ ।। krośamātrācca varṣanti krośārddhādapi vā punaḥ । parvatāgra nitaṃbeṣu varṣati ca rasaṃti ca ।।
balākāgarbhadāścaiva balākāgarbhadhāriṇaḥ । brahmajā nāma te meghā brahmaniśvāsasaṃbhavāḥ ।। te hi vidyudguṇopetāstanayitnupriyasvanāḥ । teṣāṃ śaśrvatpraṇādena bhūmiḥ svāṅgarūhodbhavā ।।
rājñī rājyābhiṣikteva punaryauṃvanamaśnute । teṣviyaṃ prāvṛḍāsaktā bhūtānāṃ jīvitodbhavā ।। dvitīyaṃ pravahaṃ vāyuṃ meghāste tu samāśritāḥ । etaṃ yojanamātrācca sādhyarddhā niṣkṛtādapi ।।
vṛṣṭirgarbhastridhā teṣāṃ dhārāsāraḥ prakīrttitaḥ । puṣkarāvarttakā nāma te meghāḥ pakṣasaṃbhavāḥ ।। śakreṇa pakṣacchinnā ye parvatānāṃ mahaujasām । kāmāgānāṃ pravṛddhānāṃ bhūtānāṃ śivamicchatā ।।
puṣkarā nāma te meghā bṛṃhantastoyamatsarāḥ । puṣkarāvarttakāstena kāraṇeneha śabditāḥ ।। nānārūpadharāścaiva mahāghorasvanāśca te । kalpāntavṛṣṭeḥ sraṣṭāraḥ saṃvartāgne rniyāmakāḥ ।।
varṣantyete yugānteṣu tṛtīyāste prakīrttitāḥ । anekarūpasaṃsthānāḥ pūrayanto mahītalam ।। vāyuṃ purā vahantaḥ syurāśritāḥ kalpasādhakāḥ । yānyaṇḍasya tu bhinnasya prākṛtasyābhavaṃstadā ।।
yasminbrahmā samutpannaścaturvaktraḥ svayaṃprabhuḥ । tānyevāṇḍakapālāni sarve meghāḥ prakīrttitāḥ ।। teṣāmāpyāyanaṃ dhūmaḥ sarveṣāmaviśeṣataḥ । teṣāṃ śreṣṭhastu parjanyaścatvāraścaiva diggajāḥ ।।
gajānāṃ parvatānāṃ ca meghānāṃ bhogibhiḥ saha । kulamekaṃ pṛthagbhūtaṃ yonirekā jalaṃ smṛtam ।। parjanyo diggajā ścaiva hemante śītasaṃbhavāḥ । tuṣāravṛṣṭiṃ varṣanti śiṣṭaḥ sasyapravṛddhaye ।।
ṣaṣṭhaḥ parivaho nāma teṣāṃ vāyurapāśrayaḥ । yo asau bibartti bhagavāngaṅgāmākāśagocarām ।। divyāmṛtajalā puṇyāṃ tridhāsvātipathe sthitām । tasyā niṣyandatoyāni diggajāḥ pṛthubhiḥ karaiḥ ।।
śīkaraṃ saṃpramuñcanti nīhāra iti sa smṛtaḥ । dakṣiṇena giriryo asau hemakūṭa iti smṛtaḥ ।। udagghimavataḥ śaila uttaraprāyadakṣiṇe । puṇḍraṃ nāma samākhyātaṃ nagaraṃ tatra vistṛtam ।।
tasminnipatitaṃ varṣaṃ tattuṣārasamudbhavam । tatastadā vaho vāyurhemavantaṃ samudvahan ।। ānayatyātmayogena siṃcamāno mahāgirim । himavantamatikramya vṛṣṭiśeṣaṃ tataḥ param ।।
ihābhyeti tataḥ paścādaparāntavivṛddhaye । varṣadvayaṃ samākhyātaṃ sasyadvayavivṛddhaye ।। meghāścāpyāyanaṃ caiva sarvametatprakīrttitam । sūrya eva tu vṛṣṭīnāṃ sraṣṭā samupadiśyate ।।
sūryamūlā ca vai vṛṣṭirjalaṃ sūryātpravartate । dhruveṇādhiṣṭhitaḥ sūryastasyāṃ vṛṣṭau pravarttate ।। dhruveṇādhiṣṭito vāyurvṛṣṭiṃ saṃharate punaḥ । graho niḥsṛtya sūryāttu kṛtsne nakṣatramaṇḍale ।।
caritvānte viśatyarkaṃ dhruveṇa samādhiṣṭhitam । tataḥ sūryarathasyātha sanniveśaṃ nibodhata ।। saṃsthitenaikacakreṇa pañcāreṇa trinābhinā । hiraṇmayena bhagavāṃstathaiva haridarvaṇā ।।
aṣṭāpadanibaddhena ṣaṭprakāraikaneminā । cakreṇa bhāsvatā sūryaḥ syandanena prasarpati ।। daśayojanasāhasro vistārāyāmataḥ smṛtaḥ । dviguṇo asya rathopasthādīṣādaṇḍaḥ pramāṇataḥ ।।
sa tasya brahmaṇā sṛṣṭo ratho hyarthavaśena tu । asaṃgaḥ kāñcano divyo yuktaḥ pavanagairhayaiḥ ।। chandobhirvājirūpaistu yataścakraṃ tataḥ sthitaiḥ । vāruṇasyandanasyeha lakṣaṇaiḥ sadṛśastu saḥ ।।
tenāsau sarvate vyomni bhāsvatā tu divākaraḥ । athaitāni tu sūryasya pratyaṅgāni rathasya ha ।। saṃvatsarasyāvayavaiḥ kalpi tasya yathākramam । ahastu nābhiḥ saurasya ekacakrasya vai smṛtaḥ ।।
arāḥ pañcārttavāṃstasya nemiḥ ṣaḍṛtavaḥ smṛtaḥ । rathanīḍaḥ smṛto hyeṣa cāyane kūbarāvubhau ।। muhūrttā bandhurāstasya ramyāścāsya kalāḥ smṛtāḥ । tasya kāṣṭhā smṛtā ghoṇā akṣadaṇḍaḥ kṣaṇastu vai ।।
nimeṣaścānukarṣo asya hīṣā cāsya lavāḥsmṛtāḥ । rātrirvarūtho dharmo asya dhvaja ūrddhva samucchritaḥ ।। yugākṣakoḍī te tasya arthakāmāvubhau smṛtau । saptāśvarūpāśchandāsi vahanto vāmato dhuram ।।
gāyatrī caiva triṣṭupya hyanuṣṭubjagatī tathā । paṅktiśca bṛhatī caiva hyuṣṇikcaiva tu saptamī ।। cakramakṣe nibaddhaṃ tu dhruve cākṣaḥ samarpitaḥ । sahacakro bhramatyakṣaḥ sahakṣo bhramate dhruvaḥ ।।
akṣeṇa saha cakreśo bhramate asau dhruveritaḥ । evamarthavaśāttasya sanniveśo rathasya tu ।। tathā saṃyogabhāvena saṃsiddho bhāsuro rathaḥ । tenāsau taraṇirdevo bhāsvatā sarpate divi ।।
yugākṣakoṭisannaddhau dvau raśmī syandanasya tu । dhruve tau bhrāmyate raśmī ca cakrayugayostu vai ।। bhramato maṇḍalānyasya khecarasya rathasya tu । yugākṣakoṭī te tasya dakṣiṇe syandanasya hi ।।
dhruveṇa pragṛhīte vai vicakrama turakṣavat । bhramantamanugacchetāṃ dhruvaṃ raśmī tu tāvubhau ।। yugākṣakoṭistattasya raśmibhiḥ syandanasya tu । kīlāsaktā yathā rajjurbhraṃmate sarvato diśam ।।
hrasatastasya raśmī tu maṇḍaleṣūttarāyaṇe । varddhate dakṣiṇe caiva bhramato maṇḍalāni tu ।। yugākṣakoṭisaṃbaddhau raśmī dvau syandanasya tu । dhruveṇa pragṛhītau vai tau raśmī nayato ravim ।।
ākṛṣyete yadā tau vai dhruveṇa sama dhiṣṭhitau । tadā so abhyantare sūryo bhramate maṇḍalāni tu ।। aśītirmaṇḍalaśataṃ kāṣṭhayorantaraṃ smṛtam । dhruveṇa mucyamānābhyāṃ raśmibhyāṃ punareva tu ।।
tathaiva bāhyataḥ sūryo bhramate maṇḍalāni tu । udveṣāṭayansa vegena maṇḍalāni tu gacchati ।। saratho adhiṣṭhito devairādityairmunibhistathā । gandharvairapsarobhiśca grāmaṇīsarparākṣasaiḥ ।।
ete vasaṃti vai sūrye dvau dvau māsau krameṇa tu । dhātār'yamā pulastyaśca pulahaśca prajāpatiḥ ।। erāvato vāsukiśca kaṃso bhīmaśca tāvubhau । rathakṛcca rathaujāśca yakṣāvetāvudā tdṛtau ।।
tuṃbururnāradaścaiva susthalā puñjikasthalā । rakṣo hetiḥ prahetiśca yātudhānāvudāhṛtau ।। ete vasaṃti vai sūryye madhumādhavayoḥ sadā । mitraśca varuṇaścaiva muniratrirudāhṛtaḥ ।।
tathā vasiṣṭho vikhyātaḥ sahajanyā ca menakā । rākṣasau ca samākhyātau pauruṣeyo vadhastathā ।। hāhā hūhūśca gandharvauṃ yajñaścāpi rathasvanaḥ । rathacitrastathaivānyo nāgasākṣakasaṃjñetaḥ ।।
raṃbhakaśca vasantyete māsayoḥ śuciśukrayoḥ । tataḥ sūrye punastvanyā nivasaṃtīha devatāḥ ।। idraścaiva vivasvāṃśca aṅgirā bhṛgureva ca । elāpatrastathā sarpaḥ śaṅkhapālāśca tāvubhau ।।
viśvāvasūgrasenau ca śvetaścaivāruṇastathā । pramlocā iti vikhyātānumloceti ca te ubhe ।। yātudhānastadā sarpo vyāghraścava tu tāvubhau । nabhonabhasyayoreṣa gāṇo vasati bhāskare ।।
parjanyaścaiva pūṣā ca bhāradvājaḥ sagautamaḥ ।। parāvasuśca gandharvastathaiva suruciśca yaḥ । viśvācī ca ghṛtācī ca ubhe te śubhalakṣaṇe ।। nāga erāvataścaiva viśrutaśca dhanañjayaḥ ।
ścenajicca suṣeṇaśca senīrgrāma ṇīśca tau ।। āpo vātaśca dvāvetau yātudhānāvudāhṛtau । vasaṃtyete tu vai sūrye sadaivāśvinakartike ।। haimantikau tu dvau māsau vasaṃti ca divākare ।
aṃśo bhagaśca dvāvaitau kaśyapaśya kratuśca ha ।। bhujaṅgaśca mahāpadmaḥ sarvaḥ karkeṭaka stathā । citrasenaśca gandharva ūrṇāyuścaiva tāvubhau ।। urvaśī pūrvacittiśca tathaivāpsarasā ubhe ।
tārkṣaścāriṣṭanemiśca senānīr grāmaṇīśca tau ।। vidyutsphūrjaḥ śatāyuśca yātudhānāvudātdṛtau । sahe caiva sahasye ca vasaṃtyete divākare ।। tataḥ śaiśira yoścāpi māsayornivasaṃti vai ।
tvaṣṭā viṣṇurjāmadagnyo viśvāmitrastathaiva ca ।। kādraveyau tathā nāgau kaṃbalāśvatarāvubhau । gandharvo dhṛtarāṣṭraśca sūryavarcāstathaiva ca ।। tilottamā tathā raṃbhā brahmāpetaśca rākṣasaḥ ।
yajñāpetamtathaivānyo viśyāto rākṣaso ttamaḥ ।। ṛtajitsatyajiccaiva gandharvauṃ samudāhṛtau । tapastapasyayoḥ sūrye vasaṃti munisattamāḥ ।। pitṛdevamanuṣyādīnsa sadāpyāyayanprabhuḥ ।
parivarttatyahorātrakāraṇaṃ savitā dvijāḥ ।। ete devā vasaṃtyarke dvau dvau māsau krameṇa tu । sthānābhimānino hyete gāṇā dvādaśasaptakāḥ ।। suryasyāpyāyayantyete tejasā teja uttamamā ।
grathitaiḥ svairvacobhiśca stuvanti hyṛṣayo ravim ।। gandharvāpsarasaścaiva gītanṛtyairupāsate । grāmaṇīyakṣabhūtāni kurvate abhīṣusaṃgraham ।। sarpā vahanti vai sūryaṃ yātudhānāstu yānti ca ।
vālakhilyā naṃyatyastaṃ parivāryodayādravim ।। eteṣāmeva devānāṃ yathāvīryaṃ yathātapaḥ । yathādharmaṃ yathāyogaṃ yathāsatyaṃ yathābalam ।। tapatyasau taśrā sūrya eṣāmindrastu tejasā ।
ityete nivasaṃtīha dvau dvau māsau divākare ।। ṛṣayo devagandharvāḥ pannagāpsarasāṃ gaṇāḥ । grāmaṇyaśca tathā yakṣā yātudhānāśca mukhyaśaḥ ।। ete tapanti varṣanti bhānti vānti sṛjanti ca ।
bhūtānāṃ caśubhaṃ karma vyapohanti prakīrttitāḥ ।। mānavānāṃ śubhaṃ hyete harante duritātmanām । duritaṃ supracārāṇāṃ vyapohanti kvaci tkvacit ।। ete sahaiva sūryeṇa bhramanti divāsānugāḥ ।
varṣantaśca tapantaśca hlādayantaśca vai prajāḥ ।। gopāyanti ca bhūtāni sarvāṇīhāmanukṣayāt । sthānābhimānināmetatsthānaṃ manvantareṣu vai ।। atītānāgatānāṃ ca varttante sāṃprataṃ ca ye ।
evaṃ vasaṃti vai sūrye saptakāste caturdaśa । caturdaśasu sarveṣu gaṇā manvantareṣviha ।। grīṣme ca varṣāsu ca muñcamāno gharmaṃ himaṃ varṣa dinaṃ niśāṃ ca । gacchatyasāvṛtuvaśātparivṛttaraśmirdevān pitṝṃśca manujāṃśca hi tarpayanvai ।।
prīṇāti devānamṛtena sūryaḥ somaṃ suṣumṇena ca varddhayitvā । śukle tu pūrṇaṃ divasakrameṇa taṃ kṛṣṇapakṣe vibudhāḥ pibanti ।। pītaṃ ca somaṃ hi kalāvaśiṣṭaṃ kṛṣṇakṣaye raśmibhirakṣarantam । sudhāmṛtaṃ tatpitaraḥ pibanti devāśca saumyāśca tathaiva kāvyāḥ ।।
sūryeṇa gobhiśca samujjhitābhiradbhiḥ punaścaiva samuddhṛtābhiḥ । vṛṣṭyābhivṛddhābhirathauṣadhībhirmartyāḥ kṣudhaṃ tvannapānairjayanti ।। tṛptiśca śukle sudhayā surāṇāṃ pakṣe ca kṛṣṇe sudhayā pitaṇām । annena śaśvacca dadhāti martyānsuryastapaṃstānsubibhartti gobhiḥ ।।
hriyanharistairharibhisturaṅgamairharatyathāpaḥ kiraṇairharidbhiḥ । visargakāle visṛjaṃśca tāḥ punarbibhartti śaśvatsavitā carācaram ।। harirharidbhirhri yate turaṅgamaiḥ pibatyathāpo haribhiḥ sahasradhā । tataḥ pramuñcatyapi tāstvasau hariḥ samūhyamāno haribhisturaṅgamaiḥ ।।
ityeṣa ekacakreṇa sūryastūrṇarathena tu । bhadraistairakramairaśvaiḥ spandane vaidikakṣayaḥ ।। ahorātrādrathenāsāvekacakreṇa vai bhraman । saptadvīpasamudrāntāṃ saptabhiḥ saptabhirhayaiḥ ।।
chandobhiraśvarūpaistairyataścakraṃ tataḥ sthitaiḥ । kāmarūpaiḥ sakṛdyuktairvāmatastairmanojavaiḥ ।। haritaikhyayaiḥ piṅgairīśvarairbrahmavādibhiḥ । tryaśītimaṇḍalaśataṃ bhramantyabdena te hayāḥ ।।
bāhyamābhyantaraṃ caiva maṇḍalaṃ divasakramāt । kalpādau saṃpra yuktāste vahantyābhūtasaṃplavāt ।। āvṛttā vālakhilyaiste bhramante rātryahāni tu । vacobhiragryairgrathitaiḥ stūyamāno maharṣibhiḥ ।।
sevyate gītanṛtyaiśca gandharvaiścāpsarogaṇaiḥ । pataṅgaiḥ patagairaśvairbhramamāṇo divaspatiḥ ।। rathāstracakraḥsomasya kudābhāstasya vājinaḥ । vāmadakṣiṇato yuktā daśa tena carantyasau ।।
vīthyāśrayāṇi ṛkṣāṇi dhruvādhāreṇa vegitāḥ । hrāsavṛddhī tathaivāsya raśmīnāṃ sūryavatsmṛte ।। tricakrobhayato aśvaśca vijñeyaḥ śaśino rathaḥ । apāṃ garṇātsamutpanno rathaḥ sāśvaḥ sasārathiḥ ।।
śatāraiśca tribhiścakrairyuktaḥ śuklairhayottamaiḥ । daśabhistu kṛśairdivyairasaṃgaistairmanojavaiḥ ।। sakṛdyukte rathe tāsminvahante cāyugakṣayāt । saṃgṛhītarathe tasmiñśvetaścakṣuḥśravāśca vai ।।
aśvāstamekavarṇaste vahante śaṅkhavarcasaḥ । yajuścaṇḍamanāścaiva vṛṣo vājī naro hayaḥ ।। aśvo gaviṣṇurvikhyāto haṃso vyomo mṛgastathā । ityete nāmabhiḥ sarve daśa candramaso hayāḥ ।।
ete candramasaṃ devaṃ vahanti saha dīkṣayā । devaiḥ parivṛtaḥ somaḥ pitṛbhiścaiva gacchati ।। somasya śuklapakṣādau bhāskare parataḥ sthire । āpūryate parasyānte satataṃ divasakramāt ।।
devaiḥ pītatanuṃ somamāpyāyayati nityadā । kṣīṇaṃ pañcadaśāhaṃ tu raśminaikena bhāskaraḥ ।। āpūrayansuṣumṇena bhāgaṃ bhāgamahaḥkramāt । suṣumṇāpyāyamānasya śuklā varddhanti vai kalāḥ ।।
tasmāddhrasaṃti vai kṛṣṇe śukle svāpyāyayanti tam । ityevaṃ sūryavīryeṇa candraścāpyāyitastataḥ ।। paurṇamāsyāṃ sa dṛśyeta śuklaḥ saṃpūrṇamaṇḍalaḥ । evamāpyāyitaḥ somaḥ śukla pakṣe dinakramāt ।।
tato dvitīyāprabhṛti bahulasya caturddaśīm । apāṃ sāramayasyendo rasamātrātmakasya tu ।। pibatyaṃbumayaṃ devā hṛṣṭāḥ saumyaṃ svadhāmṛtam । saṃbhṛtaṃ tvarddhamāsena hyamṛtaṃ sūryatejasā ।।
bhakṣārthamamṛtaṃ somaḥ paurṇamāsyāmupāsate । ekāṃ rātriṃ suraiḥ sarvaiḥ pitṛbhiḥ sarṣibhiḥ saha ।। somasya kṛṣṇapakṣādau bhāskarābhimukhasya tu । prakṣīyante pidṛdevaiḥ pīyamānāḥ kalāḥ kramāt ।।
trayaśca triṃśataścaiva trayastriṃśattathaiva ca । trayaśca trisahasrāśca devāḥ somaṃ pibanti vai ।। ityetaiḥ pīyamānasya kṛṣṇā varddhati vai kalāḥ । kṣīyanti tasmācchuklāśca kṛṣṇā āpyāyayanti ca ।।
evaṃ dinakramātpīte vibudhaistu niśākare । pītvārddha māsaṃ gacchanti cāmāvāsyāṃ surottamāḥ ।। pitaraścopatiṣṭhanti hyamāvāsyāṃ niśākaram । tataḥ pañcadaśekāle kiñcicchiṣṭe kalātmake ।।
aparāhṇe pitṛgaṇā jaghanyaṃ payupāsate । pibanti dvilavaṃ kālaṃ śiṣṭāstasya kalāstu yāḥ ।। niḥsṛtaṃ tadamāvāsyāṃ gabhastibhyaḥ svadhāmṛtam । tāṃ svadhāṃ māsatṛptyai ca pītvā gacchanti te amṛtam ।।
sūryastasminsuṣumṇe yastāpitastena candramāḥ । kṛṣṇapakṣe suraistadvatpīyate vai sudhāmayaḥ ।। saumyā barhiṣadaścaiva agniṣvāttāśca te tridhā । kāvyaścaiva tu ye proktāḥ pitaraḥ sarva eva te ।।
saṃvatsarāstu vai kāvyāḥ pañcābdā ye dvicaiḥ smṛtāḥ । saumyāstu ṛtuvo jñeyā māsā barhiṣadaḥ smṛtāḥ ।। agniṣvāttārttavāścaiva pitṛsargā hi vai dvijāḥ । pitṛbhiḥ pīyamānasya pañcadaśyāṃ kalā tu vai ।।
yāvatprakṣīyate tasya bhāgaḥ pañcadaśastu yaḥ । amāvāsyāṃ tadā tasya tata āpūryate paraḥ ।। vṛddhakṣayau vai pakṣādau ṣoḍaśyāṃ śaśinaḥ smṛtā । evaṃ sūryanimittaiṣa kṣayovṛddhirniśākare ।।
tārāgrahāṇāṃ vakṣyāmi svarbhānośca rathānpunaḥ । teyatejomayaḥ śubhraḥ somaputrasya vai rathaḥ ।। sopāsaṃgapa tākastu sadhvajo meghanisvanaḥ । bhārgavasya rathaḥ śrīmāṃstejasā sūryasannibhaḥ ।।
pṛthivīsaṃbhavairyukto nānāvarṇairhayottamaiḥ । śvetaḥ piśaṅgaḥ sāraṅgo nīlaḥ pīto vilohitaḥ ।। kṛṣṇaśca haritaścaiva pṛṣataḥ pṛśrireva ca । daśabhistairmahābhāgairakṛśairvātaraṃhasaiḥ ।।
aṣṭāśvaḥ kāñcanaḥ śrīmānbhaumasyāpi rathottamaḥ । asaṃgairlohitairaśvaiḥ sarvagairagnisaṃbhavaiḥ ।। prasarpati kumāro vai ṛjuvakrānuva kragaiḥ । tataścāṅgiraso vidvāndevācāryo bṛhaspatiḥ ।।
gaurairaśvaiḥ kāñcanena syandanena prasarpati । abjaistu vājibhirdivyairaṣṭabhirvātaraṃhasaiḥ ।। nakṣatre abdaṃ sa tiṣṭhanvai saṃvedhāstena gacchati । tataḥ śanaiścaro apyaśvaiḥ sabalairvyomasaṃbhavaiḥ ।।
kārṣṇāyasaṃ samāruhya syandanaṃ yāti vai śanaiḥ । svarbhānośca tathaivāśvāḥ kṛṣṇā hyaṣṭau manojavāḥ ।। rathaṃ tamomayaṃ tasya sakṛdyuktā vahaṃ tyuta । ādityānniḥsṛto rāhuḥ somaṃ gacchati parvasu ।।
ādityameti somaśca punaḥ saureṣu parvasu । atha keturathasyāśvā aṣṭau vai vātaraṃhasaḥ ।। palāladhūmavarṇābhā sabalā rāsabhāruṇāḥ । ete vāhā grahāṇāṃ ca hyupākhyātā rathaiḥ saha ।।
sarve dhruvaniba ddhāste pravṛddhā vātaraśmibhiḥ । tapante brāmyamāṇāstu yathāyogaṃ bhramanti vai ।। vāyavyābhiradṛśyābhiḥ pravṛddhā vātaraśmibhiḥ । paribhramanti tadbraddhāṃścandrasuryagrahā divi ।।
bhramantamanugachanti dhruvaṃ te jyotiṣāṃ gaṇāḥ । yathā nahyudake naustu salilena saho hyate ।। tathā devālayā hyete ūhyante vātaraśmibhiḥ । sarppamāṇā na dṛśyante vyomni devagaṇāstu te ।।
yāvatyaścaiva tārāśca tāvanto vātaraśmayaḥ । sarvā dhruve nibaddhāśca bhramantyo bhrāmayanti tāḥ ।। tailapīḍā yathā cakraṃ bhramanto bhrāmayanti ha । tathā bhramanti jyotīṃṣi vātabaddhāni sarvaśaḥ ।।
alātacakravadyānti vātacakreritāni tu । yato jyotīṃṣi vahate pravahastena sa smṛtaḥ ।। evaṃ dhruvanibaddho asau sarpate jyotiṣāṃ gaṇaḥ । saiṣa tārāmayo jñeyaḥ śiśumāro dhruvo divi ।।
yadahnā kurute pāpaṃ dṛṣṭvā tanniśimuñcate । yāvatyaścaiva tārāstāḥ śiśumārāśritā divi ।। tāvantyeva tu varṣāṇi jīvatābhyadhikāni tu । sākāraḥ śiśumāraśca vijñeyaḥ pravibhāgaśaḥ ।।
auttānapādastasyātha vijñeyo hyattaro hanuḥ । yajñaḥ parastu vijñeyo dharmo marddhānamāśritaḥ ।। hṛdi nārāyaṇaḥ sādhyo hyaśvinau pūrvapādayoḥ । varuṇaścāryamā caiva paścime tasya sakthinī ।।
śiśraṃ saṃvatsarastasya mitro apānaṃ samāśritaḥ । pucche agniśca mahendraśca mārīcaḥ kaśyapo dhruvaḥ ।। tārakāḥ śiśumārasya nāstaṃ yāti catuṣṭayam । nakṣatracandramūryāśca grahāstārāgaṇaiḥ saha ।।
unmukhā vimukhāḥ sarve vakrībhūtāḥ śritā divi । dhruveṇādhiṣṭhitāścaiva dhruvameva pradakṣiṇam ।। pariyāntīśvaraśreṣṭhaṃ meḍhībhūtaṃ druvaṃ divi । agnīndrakaśyapānāṃ tu caramo asau dhruvaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।
eka eva bhramatyeṣa meruparvatamūrddhani । jyotiṣāṃ cakrametaddhi gadā karṣannavāṅmukhaḥ । merumālokayatyeṣa paryante hi pradakṣiṇam ।। etacchrutvā tu sunayaḥ punaste saṃśayānvitāḥ ।
papracchuruttaraṃ bhūyastadā te romaharṣaṇam ।। yadetaduktaṃ bhavatāgṛhāṇītyeva vistṛtam । kathaṃ devagṛhāṇi syuḥ kathaṃ jyotīṃṣivarṇaya ।। etatsarvaṃ samācakṣva jyotiṣāṃ caiva nirṇayam ।
śrutvā tu vacanaṃ teṣāṃ tadā sūtaḥ samāhitaḥ ।। uvāca paramaṃ vākyaṃ teṣāṃ saṃśayanirṇayam । asminnarthe māhāprājñairyaduktaṃ jñānabuddhibhiḥ ।। etadvo ahaṃ pravakṣyāmi sūryācandramasorbhavam ।
yathā devagṛhāṇīha sūryacandragrahāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। tataḥ paraṃ ca trividhasyāgnervakṣye samudbhavam । divyasya bhautikasyāgnerabyoneḥ pārthi vasya tu ।। vyuṣṭāyāṃ tu rajanyāṃ vai brahmaṇo avyaktajanmanaḥ ।
avyākṛtamidaṃ tvāsīnnaiśena tamasāvṛtam ।। sarvabhūtāvaśiṣṭe asmiṃlloke naṣṭaviśeṣaṇe । svayaṃbhūrbhagavāṃstatra lokatantrārthasādhakaḥ ।। khadyotavatsa vyacaradāvirbhāvacikīrṣayā ।
so agniṃ dṛṣṭvātha lokādau pṛthivījalasaṃśritam ।। saṃvṛtya taṃ prakāśārthaṃ tridhā vyamajadīśvaraḥ । pavano yastu loke asminpārthivaḥ so agnirucyate ।। yaścāsau tapate sūrye śuciragnistu sa smṛtaḥ ।
vaidyuto abjastu vijñeyasteṣāṃ vakṣye atha lakṣamam ।। vaidyuto jāṭharaḥ sauro hyapāṃ garbhāstrayo agrayaḥ । tasmādapaḥ pibansūryo gobhirdīpyatyasau divi ।। vaidyutena samāviṣṭo vārṣyo nādbhiḥ praśāmyati ।
mānavā nāṃ ca kukṣistho nādbhiḥ śāsyati pāvakaḥ ।। tasmātsauro vaidyutaśca jāṭharaścapyanindhanaḥ । kiñcidapsu mataṃ tejaḥ kiñciddṛṣṭamabiṃ dhanam ।। kāṣṭhendhanastu nirmathyaḥ so adbhiḥ śāmyati pāvakaḥ ।
arciṣmānpavamāno agnirniṣprabho jāṭharaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। yaścāyaṃ maṇḍale śuklo nirūṣmā saṃprakāśakaḥ । prabhā saurī tu pādena hyastaṃ yāti devākare ।। agnimāviśate rātrau tasmāddūrātprakāśate ।
udyantaṃ ca punaḥ sūryamauṣṇamayamāgneyamāviśat ।। pādena pārthivasyāgnestasmādagnistapatyasau । prākāśyaṃ ca tathauṣṇyaṃ ca saurāgneye tu tejasī ।। parasparānupraveśādāpyāyete parasparam ।
uttare caiva bhūmyarddhe tathā hyagniśca dakṣiṇe ।। uttiṣṭhati punaḥ sūrye rātrirāviśate hyapaḥ । tasmāttaptā bhavantyāpo divāratripraveśanāt ।। astaṃ yāti puna sūrye aharvai praviśatyapaḥ ।
tasmānnaktaṃ punaḥ śuklā āpo adṛśyanta bhāsvarāḥ ।। etena kramayogena bhūmyarddhe dakṣiṇottare । udayāstamane nityamahorātraṃ viśatyapaḥ ।। yaścāsau tapate sūryaḥ pibannaṃbho gabhastibhiḥ ।
pārthivāgnivimiśro asau divyaḥ śuciriti smṛtaḥ ।। sahasrapādasau vahnirghṛtakuṃbhanibhaḥ śuciḥ । ādatte sa tu nāḍīnāṃ sahasreṇa samantataḥ ।। nādeyīścaiva sāmudrīḥ kaupyāścaiva samantataḥ ।
sthāvarā jaṅgamāścaiva yāśca kulyādikā apaḥ ।। tasya raśmisahasraṃ tu śītavarṣoṣṇaniḥstavam । tāsāṃ catuḥśatā nāḍyo varṣante citra mūrttayaḥ ।। candanāścaiva sādhyaśca kūtanākūtanāstathā ।
amṛtā nāmataḥ sarvā raśmayo vṛṣṭisarjanāḥ ।। himodgatāśca tābhyo anyā raśmayastriśatāḥ punaḥ । dṛśyā meghāśca yāmyaśca hradinyo himasarjanāḥ ।। candrāstā nāmataḥ proktā mitābhāstu gabhastayaḥ ।
śuklāśca kuhakāścaiva gāvo viśvabhṛtastathā ।। śuklāstā nāmataḥ sarvastriśatā dharmasarjanāḥ । samaṃ vibhajya nāḍīstu manuṣṭapitṛdevatāḥ ।। manuṣyānauṣadheneha svadhayā tu pitṝnapi ।
amṛtena surānsarvāṃstrīṃstribhistarpayatyasau ।। vasaṃte caiva grīṣme ca śataiḥ sa tapati tribhiḥ । varṣāsvatho śaradi vai caturbhiśca pravarṣati ।। hemante śiśire caiva hima mutsṛjate tribhiḥ ।
indro dhātā bhagaḥ pūṣā mitro atha varuṇor'yamā ।। aṃśurvivasvāstvaṣṭā ca savitā viṣṇureva ca । māghamāse tu varuṇaḥ pūṣā caiva tu phalālgune ।। caitre māsi tu detoṃśurdhātā vaiśākhatāpanaḥ ।
jyeṣṭhamāse bhavedindraścāṣāḍhe savitā raviḥ ।। vivasvāñchrāvaṇe māsi proṣṭhe māse bhāgaḥ smṛtaḥ । parjanyo aśvayuje māsi tvaṣṭā ca kārtike raviḥ ।। mārgaśīrṣe bhavenmitraḥ pauṣeviṣṇuḥ sanātanaḥ ।
pañcaraśmisahasrāṇi varuṇasyārkakarmaṇi ।। ṣaḍbhiḥ sahasraiḥ pūṣā tu devo aśusaptabhistathā । dhātāṣṭabhiḥ sahasraistu navabhistu śatakratuḥ ।। savitā daśabhiryāti yātyekādaśabhirbhagaḥ ।
saptabhistapate sitrastvaṣṭā caivāṣṭabhistapet ।। aryamā daśābhiryāti parjanyo navabhistapet । ṣaḍbhī raśmisahasraistu viṣaṇustapati medinīm ।। vasaṃte kapilaḥ sūryo grīṣmer'kaḥ kanakaprabhaḥ ।
śvetavarṇastu varṣāsu pāṇḍuḥ śaradi bhāskaraḥ ।। hemante tāmravarṇastu śaiśire lohito raviḥ । iti varṇāḥ samā khyātāḥ sūryasyartusamudbhavāḥ ।। auṣadhīṣu balaṃ dhatte svadhayā ca pidṛṣvapi ।
sūryo amareṣvapyamṛtaṃ trayaṃ triṣu na yacchati ।। evaṃ raśmisahasraṃ tu sauraṃ lokārthasādhakam । bhidyate ṛtumāsādya jalaśītoṣṇanisravam ।। ityetanmaṇḍalaṃ śuklaṃ bhāsvaraṃ sūrya saṃjñitam ।
nakṣatragrahasomānāṃ pratiṣṭhā yonireva ca ।। candraṛkṣagrahāḥ sarve vijñeyāḥ sūryasaṃbhavāḥ । nakṣatrādhipatiḥ somo graha rājo divākaraḥ ।। śeṣāḥ pañca grahā jñeyā īśvarāḥ kāmacāriṇaḥ ।
paṭhyate cāgnirāditya udakaṃ candramāḥ smṛtaḥ ।। śeṣāṇā prakṛtīḥ smayagvarṇyamānā nibodhata । surasenāpatiḥ skandaḥ paṭhyate aṅgārako grahaḥ ।। nārāyaṇaṃ budhaṃ prāhurvedajñānavido budhāḥ ।
rudro vaivasvataḥ sākṣādyamo lokaprabhuḥ svayam ।। mahāgraho dvijaśreṣṭho mandagāmī śanaiśvaraḥ । devāsuragurū dvau tu bhānumantau mahā grahau ।। prajāpatisutāvetāvubhau śukrabṛhaspatī ।
ādityamūlamakhilaṃ trailokyaṃ nātra saṃśayaḥ ।। bhavatyasmājjagatkṛtsnaṃ sadevāsuramānuṣam । rudropendrendracandrāṇāṃ viprendrāstridivaukasām ।। dyutirdyutimatāṃ kṛtsnaṃ yattejaḥ sārvalaukikam ।
sarvātmā sarvalokeśo mahādevaḥ prajāpatiḥ ।। sūrya eva trilokasya sūlaṃ paramadaivatam । tataḥ saṃjāyate sarvaṃ tatra caiva pralīyate ।। bhāvābhāvau hi lokānāmādityānniḥmṛtau purā ।
jagajjñeyo graho viprā dīptimānsuprabho raviḥ ।। atra gacchanti nidhanaṃ jāyante ca punaḥ punaḥ । kṣaṇā muhūrttā divasā niśāḥ pakṣāśca kṛtsnaśaḥ ।। māsāḥ saṃvatsarāścaiva ṛtavo atha yugāni ca ।
tadādityādṛte hyeṣā kālaṃsakhyā na vidyate ।। kālādṛte na nigamo na dīkṣā nāhnikakramaḥ । ṛtūnāmavibhāgācca puṣpamūlaphalaṃ kutaḥ ।। kutaḥ sasyaviniṣpattistṛṇauṣadhigaṇo api vā ।
abhāvo vyavahārāṇāṃ jantūnāṃ divi caiha ca ।। jagatpratāpanamṛte bhāskaraṃ vāritaskaram । sa eṣa kālaścāgniśca dvādaśātmā prajāpatiḥ ।। tapatyeṣa dvijaśreṣṭhāstrailokyaṃ sacarācaram ।
sa eṣa tecasāṃ rāśistamo ghransārvalaukikam ।। uttamaṃ mārgamāsthāya vāyorbhābhiridaṃ jagat । pārśvamūrdhvamadhaścaiva tāpayatyeṣa sarvaśaḥ ।। yathā prabhākaro dīpogṛhamadhye avalaṃbitaḥ ।
pārśvamūrdhvamadhaścaiva tamo nāśayate samam ।। tadvatsahasrakiraṇo graharājo jagatpatiḥ । sūryo gobhirjagatsarvamādīpayati sarvataḥ ।। rave raśmisahasraṃ yatprāṅmayā samudātdṛtam ।
teṣāṃ śreṣṭhāḥ punaḥ sapta raśmayo grahayo nayaḥ ।। suṣumṇo harikeśaśca viśvakarmā tathaiva ca । viśvaśravāḥ punaścānyaḥ saṃpadvasurataḥ paraḥ ।। arvāvasuḥ punaścānyaḥ svarāḍanyaḥ prakīrttitaḥ ।
suṣumṇaḥ sūryaraśmistu kṣīṇa śaśinamedhayet ।। tiryagūrdhvapracāro asau suṣumṇaḥ parikīrttitaḥ । hari keśaḥ purastādya ṛkṣayoniḥ sa kītyate ।। dakṣiṇe viśvakarmā tu raśminvarddhayate vudham ।
viśvaśravāstu yaḥ paścacchukrayoniḥ smṛto budhaiḥ ।। saṃpadvasustu yo raśmiḥ sa yonirlohitasya tu । ṣaṣṭhastvarvvāvasū raśmiryonistu sa bṛhaspateḥ ।। śanaiścaraṃpuna ścāpi raśmirāpyāyate svarāṭ ।
evaṃ sūryaprabhāveṇa grahanakṣatratārakāḥ ।। vartnte divi tāḥ sarvā viśvaṃ caidaṃ punarjagat । nakṣīyante yatastāni tasmānnakṣatrasaṃjñitāḥ ।। kṣetrāṇyetāni vai pūrvamāpatanti gabhastibhiḥ ।
teṣāṃ kṣetrāṇyathādatte sūryo nakṣatrakārakāḥ ।। tīrṇānāṃ sukṛteneha sukṛtānte grahāśrayāt । tāraṇāttārakā hyetāḥ śuklatvāccaiva tārakāḥ ।। divyānāṃ pārthivānāṃ ca naiśānāṃ caiva sarvaśaḥ ।
ādānānnityamādityastejasā tapasāmapi ।। svanaṃ syandanārthe cu dhātureṣu vibhāvyate । svanāttejaso apāṃ ca tenāsau savitā mataḥ ।। bahvarthaścadirityeṣa hlādane dhāturucyate ।
śuklatve cāmṛtatve ca śītatve ca vibhāvyate ।। sūryācandramaso rdivye maṇḍale bhāsvare khage । jalatecaumaye śukle vṛttakuṃbhanibhe śubhe ।। ghanatoyātmakaṃ tatra maṇḍalaṃ śaśinaḥ smṛtam ।
ghanatejomayaṃ śuklaṃ maṇḍalaṃ bhāskarasya tu ।। viśanti sarvadevāstu sthānānyetāni sarvaśaḥ । manvantareṣu sarveṣu ṛkṣasūryagrahāśrayāḥ ।। tāni devagṛhāṇyeva tadākhyāste bhavanti ca ।
sauraṃ sūryo viśetsthānaṃ saumyaṃ somastathaiva ca ।। śaukraṃ śukro viśetsthānaṃ ṣoḍa śārciḥ prabhāsvaram । jaivaṃ bṛhaspatiścaiva lauhitaṃ caiva lohitaḥ ।। śanaiścaro rviśetsthānaṃ devaḥ śānaiscaraṃ tathā ।
baudhaṃ budho atha svarbhānuḥ svarbhānusthānamāsthitaḥ ।। nakṣatrāṇi ca sarvāṇi nakṣatrāṇi viśantyuta । gṛhāṇyetāni sarvāṇi jyotīṃṣi sukṛtātma nām ।। kalpādau saṃpravṛttāni nirmitāni svayaṃbhuvā ।
sthānānyetāni tiṣṭhanti yāvadātrūtasaṃplavam ।। manvantareṣu sarveṣu devasthānāni tāni vai । abhimānino avatiṣṭhante devasthānāni vai punaḥ ।। atītaistu sahātītā bhāvyā bhāvyaiḥ suraiḥ saha ।
varttante varttamānaiśca sthānibhistaiḥ suraiḥ saha । asminmanvantare caiva grahā vaitānikāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। vivasvānaditeḥ putraḥ sūryo vaivasvate antare । tviṣināmā dharmasutaḥ somo devo vasuḥ smṛtaḥ ।।
śukro devastu vijñeyo bhārgavo asurayājakaḥ । bṛhattejāḥ smṛto devo devācāryo agi rassutaḥ ।। budho manoharaścaiva tviṣiputrastu sa smṛtaḥ । śanaiścaro virūpastu saṃjñāputro vivasvataḥ ।।
agnervikeśyāṃ jajñe tu yuvāsau lohitādhipaḥ । nakṣatrāṇyṛkṣanāmāno dākṣāyaṇyastu tāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। svarbhānuḥ siṃhikāputro bhūtasaṃtāpano asuraḥ । somarkṣagrahasūryeṣu kīrttitā hyabhimāninaḥ ।।
sthānānyetāni coktāni sthāninaścātha devatāḥ । śuklamagnimayaṃ sthānaṃ sahasrāṃśorvivasvataḥ ।। sahasrāṃśostviṣeḥ sthānamammayaṃ śuklameva ca । āpyaṃ śyāmaṃ manojñasya pañcaraśmergṛhaṃ smṛtam ।।
śukrasyāpyammayaṃ śuklaṃ padmaṃ ṣauḍaḥśaraśmiṣu । navaraśmestu bhaumasya lauhitaṃ sthānamammayam ।। haridāpyaṃ bṛhatsthānaṃ dvādaśāṃśairbṛhaspateḥ । aṣṛ raśmigṛhaṃ proktaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ mandasya cāmmayam ।।
svarbhānostāmasaṃ sthānaṃ bhūtasaṃtāpanālayam । vijñeyāstārakāḥ sarvā ammayāsttve karaśmayaḥ ।। āśrayāḥ puṇyakīrtīnāṃ suśuklāścāpi varṇataḥ । ghanatoyātmikā jñeyāḥ kalpādāveva nirmitāḥ ।।
ādityaraśmisaṃyogātsaṃprakāśātmikāḥ smṛtāḥ । navayojanasāhasro viṣkaṃbhaḥ savituḥ smṛtaḥ ।। triguṇāstasya vistāro maṇḍalasya pramāṇataḥ । dviguṇaḥ sūryavistārādvistāraḥ śaśinaḥ smṛtaḥ ।।
tulyastayostu svarbhānurbhūtvādhastātprasarpati । uddhṛtya pṛthivīchāyāṃ nirmito maṇḍalākṛtiḥ ।। svarbhānostu bṛhatsthānaṃ tṛtīyaṃ yattamomayam । ādityāttacca niṣkramya somaṃ gacchati parvasu ।।
ādityameti somācca punaḥ saureṣu parvasu । svarbhāsā nudate yasmāttasmātsvarbhānurucyate ।। candrasya ṣoḍaśo bhāgo bhārgavastu vidhīyate । viṣkaṃbhānmaṇḍalāccaiva yojanāgrātpramāṇataḥ ।।
bhārgavātpādahīnastu vijñeyo vai bṛhaspatiḥ । bṛhaspateḥ pāda hīnau bhaumasaurāvubhau smṛtau ।। vistārānmaṇḍalāccaiva pādahīnastayorbudhaḥ । tārānakṣatrarūpāṇi vapuṣmanti ca yāni vai ।।
budhena samarūpāṇi vistārānmaṇḍalācca vai । prāyaśaścandrayogīni vidyādṛkṣāṇi tattvavit ।। tārānakṣatrarūpāṇi hīnāni tu parasparāt । śatāni pañca catvāri trīṇi dve caiva yojane ।।
pūrvāparanikṛṣṭāni tārakāmaṇḍalāni ca । yojanādyarddhamātrāṇi tebhyo hrasvaṃ na vidyate ।। upariṣṭāttrayasteṣāṃ grahā ye dūrasarpiṇaḥ । sauroṅgirāśca vakraśca jñeyā mandavicāriṇaḥ ।।
tebhyo adha stāttu catvāraḥ punareva mahāgrahāḥ । sūryasomau budhaścaiva bhārgavaścaiva śīghragāḥ ।। tāvatyastārakākoṭyo yāvadṛkṣāṇi sarvaśaḥ । vidhinā niyamāccaiṣāmṛkṣacaryā vyavasthitā ।।
gatistāsu ca sūryasya nīcaucce tvayanakramāt । uttarāyaṇamārgastho yadā parvasu candramāḥ ।। uccatvāddṛśyate śīghraṃ nītivyaktairgabhastibhiḥ । tadā dakṣiṇamārgasyo nīyāṃ vithīmupāśritaḥ ।।
bhūmi lekhāvṛtaḥ sūryaḥ pūrṇāmāvāsyayoḥ sadā । na dṛśyate yathākālaṃ śīghramastamupaiti ca ।। tasmāduttaramārgastho hyamāvasyāṃ niśākaraḥ । dṛśyate dakṣiṇe mārge niyamāddṛśyate na ca ।।
jyotiṣāṃ gatiyogena sūryācandramasāvṛtaḥ । samānakālāstamayau viṣuvatsu samodayau ।। uttarāsu ca vīthīṣu vyantarāstamanodayau । pūrṇāmavāsyayorjñoyau jyotiścakrānuvartinau ।।
dakṣiṇāyanamārgastho yadā carati raśmivān । tadā sarvagrahāṇāṃ ca sūryo adhastātprasarpati ।। vistīrṇa maṇḍalaṃ kṛtvā tasyorddhva carate śaśī । nakṣatramaṇḍalaṃ kṛtsnaṃ somādūrddhva prasarpati ।।
nakṣatrebhyo budhaścorddhra budhādūrddhvaṃ tu bhārgavaḥ । vakrastu bhārgavādūrddhva vakrādūrddhvaṃ bṛhaspatiḥ ।। tasmācchanaiścaraścorddhvaṃ tasmātsaptarṣimaṇḍalam । ṛṣīṇāṃ cāpi saptānāṃ dhruva ūrddhvaṃ vyavasthitaḥ ।।
dviguṇeṣu sahasreṣu yojanānāṃ śateṣu ca । tārāgrahāntarāṇi syurupariṣṭādyathākramam ।। grahāśca candrasūryauṃ ca divi divyena teja sā । nityamṛkṣeṣu yujyante gacchanto niyatāḥ kramāt ।।
grahanakṣatrasūryāstu nīcoccamṛjavastathā । samāgame ca bhede ca paśyanti yugapatprajāḥ ।। parasparasthitā hyete yujyante ca parasparam । asaṃkareṇa vijñeyasteṣāṃ yogastu vai budhaiḥ ।।
ityevaṃ sanniveśo vai vṛthivyā jyautiṣasya ca । dvipānāmudadhīnāṃ ca parvatānāṃ tthaiva ca ।। varṣāṇāṃ ca nadīnāṃ ca ye ca teṣu vasaṃti vai । eteṣveva grahāḥ sarve nakṣatreṣu samutthitāḥ ।।
vivasvānaditeḥ putraḥ sūryo vai cākṣuṣeṃ'tare । viśākhāsu samutpanno grahāṇāṃ prathamo grahaḥ ।। tviṣimān dharmaputrastu somo devo vasossutaḥ । śītaraśmiḥ samutpannaḥ kṛttikāsu niśākaraḥ ।।
ṣoḍaśārcirbhṛgoḥ putraḥ śukraḥ sūryādanantaram । tārāgrahāṇāṃ pravarastiṣyaṛkṣe samutthitaḥ ।। grahaścāṅgirasaḥ putro dvādaśārcirbṛhaspatiḥ । phālgunīṣu samutpannaḥ pūrvāsu ca jagadguruḥ ।।
navārcirlohitāṅgaśca prajāpatisuto grahaḥ । āṣāḍhāsviha pūrvāsu samutpanna iti śrutiḥ ।। revatīṣveva saptārcistathā sauriḥ śanaiścaraḥ । saumyo budho dhaniṣṭhāsu pañcārcirudito grahaḥ ।।
tamomayo mṛtyusutaḥ prajākṣayakaraḥ śikhī । ārśleṣāsu samutpannaḥ sarvahārī mahāgrahaḥ ।। tathā svanāmadheyeṣu dākṣāyaṇyaḥ samuchritāḥ । tamovīryamayo rāhuḥ prakṛtyā kṛṣṇamaṇḍalaḥ ।।
bharaṇīṣu samutpanno grahaścandrārkamarddanaḥ । ete tārā grahāścāpi boddhavyā bhārgavādayaḥ ।। janmanakṣatrapīḍāsu yānti vaiguṇyatāṃ yataḥ । spṛśyante tena doṣeṇa tatastadgrahabhaktitaḥ ।।
sarvagrahāṇāmeteṣāmādirāditya ucyate । tārāgrahāṇāṃ śukrastu ketūnāmapi dhūmavān ।। dhruvaḥ kīlo grahāṇāṃ tu vibhaktānāṃ caturddiśam । nakṣatrāṇāṃ śraviṣṭhā syādayanānāṃ tathottaram ।।
varṣāṇāṃ cāpi pañcānāmādyaḥ saṃvatsaraḥ smṛtaḥ । ṛtūnāṃ śiśiraścāpi māsānāṃ māgha eva ca ।। pakṣāṇāṃ śuklapakṣaśca tithīnāṃ pratipattathā । ahorātravibhāgānāmahaścāpi prakīrtitam ।।
muhūrttānāṃ tathaivādirmuhūrtto rudradaivataḥ । kṣaṇaścāpi nimeṣādiḥ kālaḥ kālavidāṃ varāḥ ।। śravaṇāntaṃ dhaniṣṭhādi yugaṃ syātpañcavārṣikam । bhānorgativiśeṣeṇa cakravatparivarttate ।।
divākaraḥ smṛtastasmātkālastadvidbhirīśvaraḥ । caturvidhānāṃ bhūtānāṃ pravarttakanivarttakaḥ ।। tasyāpi bhagavānrudraḥ sākṣāddevaḥ pravarttakaḥ । ityeṣa jyotiṣāmeva saṃniveśor'thaniścayāt ।।
lokasaṃvyavahārārtha mīśvareṇa vinirmitaḥ । uttarāśravaṇenāsau saṃkṣiptaśca dhruve tathā ।। sarvatasteṣu vistīrṇo vṛttākāra iva sthitaḥ । buddhibūrvaṃ bhāgavatā kalpadau saṃpravarttitaḥ ।।
sāśrayaḥ so abhimānī ca sarvasya jyotiṣātmakaḥ । vaiśvarūpapradhānasya pariṇāmo ayamadbhutaḥ ।। naitacchakyaṃ prasaṃkhyātuṃ yāthātathyena kenacit । gatāgataṃ manuṣyeṇa jyotiṣāṃ sāṃsacakṣuṣā ।।
āgamādanumā nācca pratyakṣadupapattitaḥ । parikṣya nipuṇaṃ buddhyā śraddhātavyaṃ vipaścitā ।। cakṣuḥ śāstraṃ jalaṃ lekhyaṃ gaṇitaṃ buddhivittamāḥ । pañcaite hetavo viprā jyotirgaṇavivecane ।।
etadukvā mahābuddhirvāyurllokahite rataḥ । jjāpa japyaṃ bhagavānmadhyaṃ prāpte divākare ।। ṛṣayaścāpi te sarve ye tatrāsansamāgatāḥ । te sarve niyatātmānastasthuḥ prāñjalayastathā ।।
ya ijyo niyamasyānte prāṇināṃ jīvanaḥ prabhuḥ । nīlakaṇṭha namaste astu ityuvāca sadāgatiḥ ।। śrutvā tu bhāvitātmāno munayaḥ śaṃsitavratāḥ । vālakhilyeti vikhyātāḥ pataṅgasahacāriṇaḥ ।।
aṣṭāśītisahasrāmi ṛṣīṇāmūrdhvaretasām । te sma pṛcchanti vāyu ca vāyuparṇāṃbu bhojanāḥ ।। nīlakaṇṭheti yatproktaṃ tvayā pavanasattama । etadguhyaṃ pavitrāṇāṃ puṣṇaṃ puṇyavidāṃ varaḥ ।।
tadvayaṃ śrotumicchāma stanno nigada sattama । tatsarva śrotumicchāmastvatprasādātprabhañjana ।। nīlatā yena kaṇṭhasya kāraṇenāṃvikāpateḥ । śrotumicchāmahe deva tava vaktrādviśeṣataḥ ।।
yāvadvācaḥ pravarttante sarvāstāḥ preritastvayā । varṇasthānagate vāyo vāgvidhiḥ saṃpravarttate ।। jñāna pūrvamathotsāhastvatto vāyo pravarttate । tvayi niṣpūyamāne tu śeṣā varṇapravṛttayaḥ ।।
yatra vāco nivarttante dehavarṇāśca durlabhāḥ । tvatto hi varṇasadbhāvaḥ sarvagastvaṃ sadānila ।। nānyaḥ sarvagato devastvadṛte asti samīraṇa । eṣa vai jīvalokaste pratyakṣaḥ sarvato anila ।।
vettha vācaspatiṃ devaṃ manonāyakamīśvaram । brūhi tatkaṇṭhadeśe tu kiṃ kṛtvā rūpavikriyā ।। vacaḥ śrutvā tatasteṣāṃ munīnāṃ bhāvitātmanāma । pratyuvāca mahātejā vāyurllokanamaskṛtaḥ ।।
purā kṛtayuge vipro vedanirṇayatatparaḥ । vasiṣṭho nāma dharmātmā mānaso vai prajāpatiḥ ।। papraccha kārttikeyaṃ vai mayūravaravāhanam । mahiṣāsuranārīṇāṃ nayanāñjanataskaram ।।
mahāsenaṃ mahātmanaṃ meghastanitanisvanam । umāmanaḥ praharṣāṇāṃ bārakacchadmarūpiṇam ।। kraiñcajīvitahartāraṃ gaurīhṛdayanandanam । yadetaddṛśyate varya śubhraṃ śubhrāñjanopamam ।।
tatkimarthaṃ samutpannaṃ kaṇṭhe kaṇṭhekundendusaprabhe । etaddīptāṃya dāntāya bhaktāya brūhi pṛcchate ।। kathāṃ maṅgalasaṃyuktāṃ pavitrāṃ pāpanāśinīm । matpriyārthaṃmahābhāga vaktumarhasyaśeṣataḥ ।।
śrutvā vākyaṃ tatastasya vasiṣṭhasya mahātmanaḥ । pratyuvāca mahātejā devāribalasūdanaḥ ।। śṛṇuṣva vadatāṃ śreṣṭakathyamānaṃ vaco mama । umotsaṃgopaviṣṭena yathāpūrvaṃ mayā śrutam ।।
pārvatyā saha saṃvādaḥ śarvasya ca mahātmanaḥ । tamahaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi tvatpriyārthaṃ mahāmune ।। kailāsaśikhare ramye nānādhātuvicitrite । taruṇādityasaṃkāśe taptacāmīkaraprabhe ।।
vajrasphaṭikasopāne citrapādaśilātale । jāṃbūnadamaye divye nānādhātu vicitrite ।। nānādrumalatākīrṇe nānāpuṣpaphalopage । haṃsakāraṇḍavākīrṇe cakravākopaśobhite ।।
ṣaṭpadodgītabahule dhārāsaṃpātanādite । mattakraiñcamayūrāṇāṃ nādairvikruṣṭakandare ।। apsarogaṇasaṃkīrṇe kinnarairupaśobhite । jīvaṃ jīvakajātīnāṃ virāvairupakūjite ।।
kokilārāvabahule siddhacāraṇasevite । saurabheyaninādāḍhyaṃ meghastanitanisvane ।। vināyakabhayodvignakuṃ jarairmuktakandaraiḥ । vīṇāvāditranirgheṣaiḥ śrotrendriyamanoramaiḥ ।।
dolālaṃbitasaṃghāte vanitāsaṃghasevite । dhvajālaṃbitadolānāṃ ghaṇṭānāṃ ninadākule ।। vallakīveṇubahule triṃśadbarhiṇasaṃkule । mukhamarddalavāditrairvalitāsphoṭitaistathā ।।
krīḍāvegavivādānāṃ nirghoṣaiḥ pūrṇakandare । haṃsaiḥ parāvataiścaiva bakarājaiḥ sukhasthite ।। dehabandhairvicitraiścaprakrīḍitagaṇeśvare । siṃhavyāghramukhairghoravāśitaiścaṇḍavegitaiḥ ।।
mṛgamaṣamukhaiścānyairgajavājimukhaistathā । biḍālavadanaiścograiḥ kroṣṭukākārasūrttibhiḥ ।। hrasvairdīrghaiśca sukṛśairlaṃbodaramahīdaraiḥ । hrasvajaṅghaiḥ praleboṣṭhaistālajaṅghaistathāparaiḥ ।।
gokarṇairekakarṇaiśca mahākarṇairakarṇakaiḥ । bahupādairmahāpādairekapādairapādakaiḥ ।। bahunetrairmahānetrairekanetrairanetrakaiḥ । ekadaṃṣṭrairmahādaṃṣṭrairbahudaṃṣṭrairadaṃṣṭrakaiḥ ।।
ekaśīrṣairmahāśīrṣabahuśīrṣairaśīrṣakaiḥ । ekajihvairmahājihvairbahujihvairajihvakaiḥ । evaṃrūpairmahāyogaibhūtarbhūtapatirvṛtaḥ ।। viśuddhamuktāmaṇiratnabhūṣite śilātale svarṇamaye suramyake ।
sukhopaviṣṭaṃ madanāganāśanaṃ provāca vākyaṃ girirājaputrī ।। bhagavanbhūtabhavyeśa govṛṣāṅkitaśāsana । tava kaṇṭhe mahādeva bhrājateṃbudasannibham ।। nātyulbaṇaṃ śubhaṃśubhre nīlābujacayopamam ।
kimidaṃ dīpyate deva kaṇṭhe kāmāṅganāśana ।। ko hetuḥ kāraṇaṃ kiṃ vā kaṇṭhe nīlasttvamīśvara । etatsarvaṃ yathānyāyaṃ būhi kautūhalaṃ hi me ।। śrutvā vākyaṃ tatastasyāḥ pārvatyāḥ pāvatīpriyaḥ ।
kathāṃ maṅgalasaṃyuktāṃ kathayāmāsa śaṅkaraḥ ।। mathyamāne amṛte pūrvaṃ kṣīrode suradānavaiḥ । agre samutthitaṃ ghoraṃ viṣaṅkālānalaprabham ।। taṃ dṛṣṭvā surasaṃghasca daityāścaiva varānane ।
viṣaṇṇavadanāḥ sarve gatāste brahmaṇo antakam ।। dṛṣṭvā suragaṇānbhītānbrahmovāca mahādyutiḥ । kimarthaṃ vai mahābhāgā bhītā udvignacetanāḥ ।। mayā triguṇamaiśvaryaṃ bhavatāṃ saṃprakalpitam ।
tena vyāvarttitaiśvaryā yūyaṃ bho surasattamāḥ ।। tralokyasyeśvarā yūyaṃ sarve vai vigatajvarāḥ । prajāsarge na so astīha yaścājñāṃ me ativartayet ।। vimānacāriṇa sarve sarve svacchandagāminaḥ ।
ādhyātmike cādhibhūte adhidaive ca nityaśaḥ ।। prajāḥ karmavipākena śaktā yūyaṃ pravarttitum । tatkimarthaṃ bhayodvignā mṛgāḥ siṃhārditā iva ।। kiṃ duḥśaṃ ko anusaṃtāpaḥ kuto vā bhayamāgatam ।
etatsarvaṃ yathānyāyaṃ śīghramākhyā tumarhatha ।। śrutvā vākyaṃ tatastasya brahmaṇaḥ paramātmanaḥ । ūcuste ṛṣibhiḥ sārddhaṃ suradaityendradānavāḥ ।। surāsurairmathyamāne pajorāśau pitamāha ।
bhujaṅgabhṛṅgasaṃkāśaṃ nīlajīmūtasannibham ।। prādurbhūtaṃ viṣaṃ ghoraṃ saṃvartāgnisamaprabham । kālamṛtyurivodbhūtaṃ yugāntādityavarcasam ।। trailokyotsādasūryābhaṃ visphurattat samantataḥ ।
viṣeṇottiṣṭhamānena kālānalasamatviṣā ।। nirdagdho raktagaurāṅgo kṛtaḥ kṛṣṇo janārddanaḥ । taṃ dṛṣṭvā raktagaurāṅgaṃ kṛtaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ janārddanam ।। tataḥ sarve vayaṃ bhītāstvā meva śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ ।
surāṇāmasurāṇāṃ ca śrutvā vākyaṃ bhayāvaham ।। pratyuvāca mahātejā brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ । śṛṇvantu devatāḥ sarve ṛṣayaśca tapodhanāḥ ।। yattadagre samutpannaṃ mathyamāne mahodadhau ।
viṣaṃ kālānalaprakhyaṃ kālakūṭamiti śrutam ।। yena prodbhūtamātreṇa na vyarājanta devatāḥ । tasya viṣṇurahaṃ vāpi sarve vā surapuṅgavāḥ ।। na śaknuvanti vai soḍhuṃ vegamanyatra śaṅkarāt ।
ityuktvā padmagarbhābhaḥ padmāyonirayonijaḥ ।। oṅkāraṃ samanusmṛtya dhyāyañjayotiḥ samantataḥ । tataḥ stotuṃ samārabdho brahmā veda vidāṃ varaḥ ।। namastubhyaṃ virūpākṣa namaste divyacakṣuṣe ।
namaḥ pinākahastāya vajrahastāya vai namaḥ ।। namastrailokya nāthāya bhūtānāṃ pataye namaḥ । namaḥ surārihantre ca somasūryāgnicakṣuṣe ।। brahmaṇe caiva rudrāya viṣṇave caiva te namaḥ ।
sāṃkhyāya caiva yogāya bhūtagrāmāya vai namaḥ ।। manmathāṅgavināśāya kālapṛṣṭhāya vai namaḥ । suretase atha rudrāya devadevāya raṃhase ।। kapardine karālāya śaṅkarāya harāya ca ।
kapāline virūpāya śivāya varadāya ca ।। tripuraghnamakhaghnāya mātṝṇāṃ pataye namaḥ । vṛddhāya caiva śuddhāya muktāyaiva balāya ca ।। lokatrayaikavīrāya candrāya varuṇāya ca ।
agrāya caiva cogrāya viprāyānekacakṣuṣe ।। rajase caiva sattvāya namaste avyaktayonaye । nityāya caivānityāya nityānityāya vai namaḥ ।। vyaktāya caivāvyaktāya vyaktāvyaktāya vai namaḥ ।
cintyāya caivācintyāya cintyācintyāya vai namaḥ ।। jagatāmārttināśāya priyanārāyaṇāya ca । umāpriyāya śarvāya nandivaktrāṅkitāya ca ।। pakṣamāsāhddhamāsāya ṛtusaṃvatsarāya ca ।
bahurūpāya muṇḍāya daṇḍine ca varūthine ।। namaḥ kapālahastāya digvāsāya śikhaṇḍine । dhanvine rathine caiva yamine brahmacāriṇe ।। ṛgyajuḥ sāmavedāya puruṣāyeśvarāya ca ।
ityeva mādicaritaiḥ stotraiḥ stutya namī'stu te । evaṃ stutvā tato brahmā praṇipatya varānane ।। jñātvā tu bhaktiṃ mama devatānāṃ gaṅgājalā sphālitamuktakeśaḥ । sūkṣmo asi yogātiśayādacintyo na hi prabho vyaktimuphaiṣi rudraḥ ।।
evaṃ bhagavatā pūrvaṃ brahmaṇā lokakartṛṇā । stuto ahaṃ vividhaiḥ stotrairvedavedāṅgasaṃbhavaiḥ ।। tato ahaṃ mukhyayā vācā pitāmahamathābravam । bhūtabhavyabhavannātha lokanātha jagatpate ।।
kiṃ kāryaṃ te mayā brahmankarttavyaṃ vada suvrata । śrutvā vākyaṃ tato brahmā pratyuvācāṃbujekṣaṇaḥ ।। bhūtabhavyabhavannātha śrūyatāṃ kāraṇeśvara । surāsurairmathyamāne payodhau paṅkajekṣaṇa ।।
bhagavanmeghasaṃkāśaṃ nīlajīmūtasannibham । prādurbhūtaṃ viṣaṃ ghoraṃ saṃvarttāgnisamaprabham ।। taṃ dṛṣṭvā ca vayaṃ sarve bhītāḥ saṃbhrāntacetasaḥ । tatpibasva mahādeva lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā ।।
bhavāñchaktaśca bhoktā vai bhavāndevavaraḥ prabho । tvadṛte anyo mahādeva vegaṃ soḍhuṃ na vidyate ।। evaṃ tasya vacaḥ śrutvā brahmaṇaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ । bāḍha mityeva tadvākyaṃ pratigṛhya varānane ।।
tato ahaṃ pātumārabdho viṣamantakasannibham । pibato me mahāghoraṃ viṣaṃ surabhayapradam ।। kaṇṭhaḥ samabhavattūrṇaṃ kṛṣṇo vai varavarṇini । taṃ dṛṣṭvotpalapatrābhaṃ kaṇṭhasaktamivoragam ।।
takṣakaṃ nāgarājānaṃ lelihānamivotthitam । athovāca mahātejā brahmā lokapitāmahaḥ ।। śobhase tvaṃ mahādeva kaṇṭhenānena suvrata । tatastasya vacaḥśrutvā mayā girivarātmaje ।।
kaṇṭhe dhṛtaṃ viṣaṃ ghoraṃ nīlakaṇṭhastato asmyaham । paśyatāṃ surasaṃghānāṃ daityānāṃ ca varānane । yakṣagandharvabhūtānāṃ piśācoragarakṣasām ।। tatkālakūṭaṃ viṣamugravegaṃ kaṇṭhe dhṛtaṃ parvatarājaputri ।
niveśyamānaṃ suradaityasaṃgho dṛṣṭvā paraṃ vismayamājagāma ।। tataḥ muragaṇāḥ sarve sadaityoragarākṣasāḥ । ūcuḥ prāñjalayo bhūtvā mattamātaṅgagāmini ।। ahobalaṃ vīryaparākramaste tvaho vapuryogabalaṃ taveśa ।।
aho prabhutvaṃ tava devadeva mahādbhutaṃ manmathadehanāśana । tvameva viṣṇuścaturānanastvaṃ tvameva mṛtyurvaradastvameva ।। tvameva sūryo rajanīkaraśca vyaktistvamevāsya carācarasya । tvameva vahniḥ pavanastvameva tvameva bhūmiḥ salilaṃ tvameva ।।
tvameva sarvasya carācarasya dhātā vidhātā pralayastvameva । ityeva muktvā vacanaṃ suredrāḥ pragṛhya somaṃ praṇipatya mūrdhrā । gatā vimānairanilopavegairmahānagaṃ merumupetya sarve ।। ityetatparamaṃ guhyaṃ puṇyātpuṇyatamaṃ mahat ।।
nīlakaṇṭha iti proktaṃ triṣu lokeṣu viśrutam । svayaṃbhuvā svayaṃ proktā kathā pāpapraṇāśinī ।। yastu dhārayate nityaṃ brahmodgītāmimāṃ śubhām । tasyāhaṃ saṃpravakṣyāmi phalaṃ suvipulaṃ mahat ।।
viṣaṃ tasya varārohe sthāvaraṃ jaṅgamaṃ tathā । gātraṃ prāpya tu suśroṇi kṣapraṃ tatpratihanyate ।। śamāyatyaśubhaṃ ghoraṃ duḥkhapnaṃ cāpakarṣati । strīṣu vallabhatāṃ yāti sabhāyāṃ pārthivasya ca ।।
vivāde jayamāpnoti yuddhe vijayameva ca । gacchati kṣemamadhvānaṃ gṛhebhyo nityasaṃpadā ।। śarīrasyeha vakṣyāmi gatiṃ tasya varānane । hariśmaśrurnīlakaṇṭhaḥ śaśāṅkāṅkitamūrddhajaḥ ।।
tryakṣastriśūlapāṇiśca vṛṣa cānaḥ pinākadhṛk । nanditulyabalaḥ śrīmānnanditulyaparākramaḥ ।। vicaratyakhilāṃllokāmsaptalokānmamājñayā । na hanyate gati stasya anilasya yathāṃbare ।।
mama tulyabalo bhūtvā tiṣṭhatyābhūtasaṃplavāt । mama bhaktayā varārohe ye ca śṛmvanti mānavāḥ ।। teṣāṃ gatiṃ pravakṣyāmi tviha loke paratra ca । brāhmaṇo vedamāpnoti kṣatriyo vindate mahīm ।।
vaiśyastu labhate lābhaṃ śūdraḥ sukhamavāpnuyāt । vyādhito mucyate rogādbaddho mucyeta bandhanāt ।। gurviṇī labhate putraṃ kanyā vidati satpatim । naṣṭaṃ ca labhate dravyamiha loke paratra ca ।।
gavāṃ śatasahasrasya samyagdattasya yatphalam । tatphalaṃ labhate martyaḥ śrutvā divyā mimāṃ kathām ।। pādaṃ vāthārddhapādaṃ vār ślokarṃ ślokārddhameva vā । yastu dhārayate nityaṃ rudralokaṃ sa gacchati ।।
athavā sarvamevedaṃ devabrāhmaṇasannidhau । yaḥ paṭhenmānavo nityaṃ madgatenāntarātmanā ।। śraddhadhānaḥ sadā bhakto rūdralokaṃ sa gacchati । paṭhecca devi bhaktyā ca pāṭhayecca naraḥ sadā ।।
ataḥ parataraṃ stotraṃ na bhūtaṃ na bhaviṣyati । nāpi yakṣāḥ piśācā vā na bhūtā na vināyakāḥ । kuryurvighnaṃ gṛhe tasya yatrāyaṃ tiṣṭhati stavaḥ ।। mayā nu tuṣṭena tavāṃbujekṣaṇe stavasya māhātmyama ghaughanāśanam ।
niveditaṃ puṇyaphalādiyuktaṃ svayaṃ ca kītaṃ caturānanena ।। kathāmimāṃ puṇyaphalādiyuktāṃ nivedya devyai śaśibaddhamūrddhajaḥ । vṛṣasya pṛṣṭhena sahomayā prabhujagāma kailāsaguhāṃ guhapriyaḥ ।। śrutaṃ mayā pāpaharaṃ tadantike niveditaṃ te atha mayā prajāpateḥ ।
adhītya sarvaṃ tvakhilaṃ salakṣaṇaṃ prayāti cādityapadaṃ dvijottamaḥ ।। mahādevasya mahātmyaṃ prabhutvaṃ ca mahātmanaḥ । śrotumicchāmahe samyagaiśvaryaguṇavistaram ।। pūrvaṃ trailokyavijaye viṣṇunā samudātdṛ tam ।
baliṃ baddhvā mahāvīryaṃ trailokyādhipatiṃ purā ।। pranaṣṭeṣu tu daityeṣu prahṛṣṭe tu śacīpatau । athājagmuḥ prabhuṃ draṣṭuṃ sarve devāḥ sanātanam ।। yatrāste viśvarūpātmā kṣīrodasya masīpataḥ ।
siddhā brahmarṣayo yakṣā gandharvāpsarasāṃ gaṇāḥ ।। nāgā devarṣayaścaiva nadyaḥ sarve ca parvatāḥ । abhigamya mahātmānaṃ stuvanti puruṣaṃ harim ।। tvaṃ dhātā tvaṃ ca kartāsi tvaṃ lokānsṛjasi prabho ।
tvatprasādācca kalyāṇaṃ prāptaṃ trailokyamavyayam ।। asurāśca jitāḥ sarve balirbaddhaśca vai tvayā । evamuktaḥ surairviṣṇaḥ siddhaiśca paramarṣibhiḥ ।। pratyuvāca tadā devān sarvāṃstānpuruṣottamaḥ ।
śrūyatāmabhidhāsyāmi kāraṇaṃ surasattamāḥ ।। yaḥ sraṣṭā sarvabhūtānāṃ kālaḥ kālakaraḥ prabhuḥ । yenāhaṃ brahmaṇā sārddhaṃ sṛṣṭā lokāśca māyayā ।। tasyaiva ca prasādena ādau siddhatvamāgataḥ ।
purā tamasi cāvyakte trailokye grasite mayā ।। udarastheṣu bhūteṣu tveko ahaṃ śayita stadā । sahasraśīrṣā bhūtvā ca sahasrākṣaḥ sahasrapāt ।। śaṅkhacakragadāpāṇiḥ śayito vimaleṃ'bhasi ।
etasminnantare dūrātpaśyāmi hyamitaprabham ।। śatasūryapratīkāśaṃ jvalantaṃ svena tejasā । caturvaktraṃ mahāyogaṃ puruṣaṃ kāñcanaprabham ।। kṛṣṇājinadharaṃ devaṃ kamaṇḍaluvibhūṣitam ।
nimeṣāntaramātreṇa prāpto asau puruṣottamaḥ ।। tato māmabravīdbrahmā sarvalokanamaskṛtaḥ । kastvaṃ kuto vā ki ceha tiṣṭhase vada me vibho ।। ahaṃ kartāsmi lokānāṃ svayaṃbhūrviśvatomukhaḥ ।
evamuktastadā tena brahmaṇāhamuvāca tam ।। ahaṃ karttā hi lokānāṃ saṃhartā ca punaḥ punaḥ । evaṃ saṃbhāṣamāṇau tu parasparajayaiṣiṇau ।। uttarāṃ diśamāsthāya jvālāmadrākṣva viṣṭhitām ।
jvālāṃ tatastāmālokya vismitau ca tadānaghāḥ ।। tejasā ca balenātha śārvaṃ jyotiḥ kṛtāñjalī । varddhamānāṃ tadā jvālāmatyantaparamādbhutām ।। abhidudrāva tāṃ jvālāṃ brahmā cāhaṃ ca satvarau ।
divaṃ bhūmiṃ ca nirbhidya tiṣṭhantaṃ javālamaṇḍalam ।। tasyā jvālasya madhye tu paśyāvo vipulaprabham । prādeśamātramavyaktaṃ liṅgaṃ paramadīptimat ।। na ca tatkāñcanaṃ madhye naśailaṃ na ca rājatam ।
anirdeśyamacintyaṃ ca lakṣyālakṣyaṃ punaḥ punaḥ ।। jvālāmālāsahasrāḍhyaṃ vismayaṃ paramadbhutam । mahatā tejasāyuktaṃ vardabhamānaṃbhṛśantathā ।। jvālāmālātataṃ nyastaṃ sarvabhūtabhayaṅkaram ।
ghorarūpiṇamatyarthaṃ bhindaṃ tamiva rodasī ।। tato māmabravīdbrahmā adho gaccha tvamāśu vai । antamasya vijānīvo liṅgasya tu mahātmanaḥ ।। ahamūrdhvaṃ gamiṣyāmi yāvadanto asya dṛśyate ।
tadā tu samayaṃ kṛtvā gata urddhvamadhaśca hi ।। tato varṣasahasraṃ tu hyahaṃ punaradho gataḥ । na paśyāmi ca tasyāntaṃ bhītaścāhaṃ tato abhavam ।। tathaiva brahmā hyūdhva ca na cāntaṃ tasya labdhavān ।
samāgato mayā sārddha tatraiva ca mahābhasi ।। tato vismayamāpannau bhītau tasya mahātmanaḥ । māyayā mohitau tena naṣṭasaṃjñai vyavasthitau ।। tato dhyānaratau tatra ceśvaraṃ sarvatomukham ।
prabhavaṃ nidhanaṃ caiva laukānāṃ prabhumavyayam ।। prahvāñjalipuṭau bhūtvā tasmai śarvāya śūline । mahābhairavanādāya bhīmarūpāya daṃṣṭriṇe । avyaktāyātha mahate namaskāraṃ prakurvahe ।।
namo astu te lokasureśa deva namo astu te bhūtapate mahātman । namo astu te śāśvatasiddhayogine namostu te sarvajagatpratiṣṭhita ।। parameṣṭhī paraṃ brahma tvakṣaraṃ paramaṃ padam । jyeṣṭhastvaṃ vāmadevaśca rudraḥ skandaḥ śivaḥ prabhuḥ ।।
tvaṃ yatvaṃ vaṣaṭkārastvamoṅkāraḥ parantapaḥ । svāhākāro namaskāraḥ saṃskāraḥ sarvakarmaṇām ।। svadhākāraśca yajñaśca vratāni niyamāstathā । vedā lokāśca devāśca bhagavāneva sarvaśaḥ ।।
ākāśasya ca śabdastvaṃbhūtānāṃ prabhavāpyayaḥ । bhūmau gandho rasaścāpsu tejorūpaṃ maheśvaraḥ ।। vāyoḥ sparśaśca deveśa vapuścandramasastathā ।। buddhau jñānaṃ ca deveśa prakṛterbījameva ca ।।
saṃharttā sarvalokānāṃ kālo mṛtyumayoṃ'takaḥ । tvaṃ dhārayasi lokāṃstrīṃstvameva sṛjasi prabho ।। pūrveṇa vadanena tvamindratvaṃ prakaroṣi vai । dakṣiṇena tu vaktreṇa lokānsaṃkṣipase punaḥ ।।
paścimena tu vaktreṇa varuṇastho na saṃśayaḥ । uttareṇa tu vaktreṇa somastvaṃ devasattamaḥ ।। ekadhā bahudhā deva lokānāṃ prabhavāpyayaḥ । ādityā vasavo rudrā marutaśca sahāśvinaḥ ।।
sādhyā vidyādharā nāgāścāraṇāśca tapodhanāḥ । vālakhilyā mahātmānastapaḥ siddhāśca suvratāḥ ।। tvattaḥ prasūtā deveśa ye cānye niyatavratāḥ । umā sītā sinīvālī kuhūrgāyatrya eva ca ।।
lakṣmīḥ kīrttirdhṛtirmedhā lajjā kāntirvapuḥ svadhā । tuṣṭiḥ puṣṭiḥ kriyā caiva vācāṃ devī sarasvatī । tvattaḥ prasūtā deveśa saṃdhyā rātristathaiva ca ।। sūryāyutānāmayutaprabhāva namo astu te candrasahasragaura ।
namo astu te vajrapinākadhāriṇe namostu te deva hiraṇyavāsase ।। namostu te bhasmavibhūṣitāṅga namo astu te kāmaśarīranāśana । namo astu te deva hiraṇyaretase namo astu te deva hiraṇyavāsase ।। namo astu te deva hiraṇyayone namo astu te deva hiraṇyanābha ।
namo astu te deva hiraṇyaretase namo astu te netrasahasracitra ।। namo astu te deva hiraṇyavarṇa namo astu te deva hiraṇyakeśa । namo astu te deva hiraṇyavīra namo astu te deva hiraṇyadāyine ।। namo astu te deva hiraṇyanātha namo aśtute deva hiraṇyanāda ।
namo astu te deva pinākapāṇe namo aśtute te śaṅkara nīlakaṇṭha ।। evaṃ saṃstūyamānastu vyakto bhūtvā mahāmatiḥ । devadevo jagadyoniḥ sūrya koṭisamaprabhaḥ ।। ābabhāṣe kṛpāviṣṭo mahādevo mahādyutiḥ ।
vaktrakoṭisahasreṇa grasamāna ivāṃbaram ।। kaṃbugrīvaḥ suja ṭharo nānābhūṣaṇabhūṣitaḥ । nānāratnavicitrāṅgo nānāmālyānulepanaḥ ।। pinākapāṇirbhagavānsurapūjyastriśūladhṛk ।
vyālaya jñopavītī ca surāṇāmabhayaṅkaraḥ ।। dundubhisvaranirghoṣaḥ parjanyaninadopamaḥ । mukto hāsastadā tena sarvamāpūrayañjagat ।। tena śabdena mahatā cāvāṃ bhītau mahātmanaḥ ।
athovāca mahādevaḥ prīto ahaṃ surasattamau ।। paśyatāṃ ca mahāyogaṃ bhayaṃ sarva pramucyatām । yuvāṃ prasūtau gātrebhyo mama pūrvaṃ sanātanau ।। yaṃ me dakṣiṇo bāhurbrahmā lokapitāmahaḥ ।
vāmo bāhuśca me viṣṇurnityaṃ yuddheṣvanirjitaḥ ।। prīto ahaṃ yuvayoḥ samyagvaraṃ dadyāṃ yathaipsitam । tataḥ prahṛṣṭamanasau praṇatau pādayoḥ prabhoḥ ।। abrūtāṃ ca mahādevaṃ prasādābhimukhaṃ sthitam ।
yadi prītiḥ samutpannā yadi deyo varaśca te । bhaktirbhavatu nau nityaṃ tvayi deva sureśvara ।। evamastu mahābhāgau sṛjatāṃ vipulāḥ prajāḥ । evamuktvā sa bhagavāṃstatraivātaradhādvibhuḥ ।।
eṣa eva mayokto vaḥ prabhāvastasya dhīmataḥ । etaddhi paramaṃ jñānamavyaktaṃ śivasaṃjñitam ।। etatsūkṣmamacintyaṃ ca paśyanti jñaacakṣuṣaḥ । tasmai devādhidevāya namaskāraṃ prakurmahe ।
mahādeva namaste astu maheśvara namo astu te ।। etacchrutvā gatāḥ sarve surāḥ svaṃ svaṃ niveśanam । namaskāraṃ prakurvāṇāḥ śaṅkarāya mahātmane ।। imaṃ stavaṃ paṭhidyastu ceśvarasya mahātmanaḥ ।
