kāmāṃśca labhate sarvān pāpebhyaśca pramucyate ।। etatsarvaṃ tadā tena na viṣṇunā prabhaviṣṇunā । mahādevaprasādena hyuktaṃ brahma sanātanam । etadvaḥ sarvamākhyātaṃ mayā māheśvaraṃ balam ।।
bhūya ṣuta mahābuddhe kathayasva mahātmanaḥ । mahādevasya māhātmyaṃ śrotuṃ kautūhalaṃ ca naḥ ।। kathaṃ dāruvaṇe deva-ṛṣisaṃghaniṣevite । cakāra veṣaṃ vikṛtaṃ yena buddhā maharṣayaḥ ।।
jñātvā ca te mahādevaṃ tato bhrāntā hyacetasaḥ । ārādhayanprasādārthaṃ naiṣāṃ tuṣṭaḥ punarbhavaḥ ।। etatsarvaṃ yathāvṛttaṃ devadevena ceṣṭitam । tatsarvaṃ kathayasveha tvaṃ no buddhimatāṃ varaḥ ।।
śrūyatāmabhidhāsyāmi dharmametamatandritāḥ । nirmmitaṃ devadevena bhaktānāmanukaṃpayā ।। purā kṛtayuge viprāḥ śṛṅge himavataḥ śubhe । devadāruvanaṃ ramyaṃ nānādrumalatākulam ।।
bahavo munayastatra tapasyanto munivratāḥ । śaivāla bhojanāḥ kecitkecidantarjaleśayāḥ ।। kecidabhrāvakāśāstu pādāṅguṣṭhāgradhiṣṭhitāḥ । dantolūkhalinaścānye tvaśmakuṭṭāstathā pare ।।
sthānavīrāsanāścānye mṛgayaryāratāstathā । kālaṃ nayanti tapasā tīvreṇa ca mahādhiyaḥ ।। tatasteṣāṃ prasādārtha devastadvanamāgataḥ । bhasmapāṇḍuradigdhāṅgo nagno vikṛtalakṣaṇaḥ ।।
vikṛtasrastakeśaśca karāladaśanastathā । ulmukavyagrahastaśca raktapiṅgalalocanaḥ ।। śiśnaṃ savṛṣaṇaṃ tasya raktagairikasannibham । mukhamaṅgāravarṇena śuklena ca vibhūṣitam ।।
kvacitsa hasate raudraṃ kvacidgāyati vismi taḥ । kvacinnṛtyati śṛṅgārī kvacidrauti muhurmuhuḥ ।। nṛtyanta rurudhustūrṇaṃ patnyasteṣāṃ vimohitāḥ । āśrame abhyāgato abhīkṣṇaṃ yā cate ca punaḥ punaḥ ।।
bhāryā kṛtā tathārūpā tṛṇābharaṇabhūṣitā । vṛṣanādaṃ pragarjanvai kharanādaṃ nanāda ca ।। tathā vañcitumā rabdho hāsayansarvadehinaḥ । tataste munayaḥ kruddhāḥ krodhena kaluṣīkṛtāḥ ।।
mohitā māyayā sarve śapituṃ samupasthitāḥ । karavadgāyase yasmātkharastasmādbhaviṣyasi ।। rākṣaso vā piśāco vā dānavo vātha vā tathā । yathā vaicchaṃstathā sarve kruddhāste munayaḥ samam ।।
śepuḥ śāsaistu vividhaistaṃ devaṃ bhuvaneśvaram । tapāṃsi teṣāṃ sarveṣāṃ pratyāhanyanta śaṅkare ।। yathādityaprakāśena tārakā nabhasi sthitāḥ । na dyotante prakāśena tadvattejāṃsi śaṅkare ।।
śrūyate ṛṣiśāpena brahmaṇaḥ sumahātmanaḥ । samṛddhaḥ śreyasāṃ yauniryajño vai nāśamāptavān ।। bhṛgorapi ca śāpena viṣṇuḥ paramaviyavān । prādurbhāvāndaśa prāpto duḥkhitaśca sadā kṛtaḥ ।।
indrasyāpi hi dharmajñaḥ śiśnaṃ savṛṣaṇaṃ purā । ṛṣiṇā gautamenorvyāṃ kruddhena vinipātitam ।। garbhavāso vasūnāṃ ca śāpena vihita stathā । ṛṣīṇāṃ caiva śāpena nahuṣaḥ sarpatāṃ gataḥ ।।
kṣīrodaśca samudraśca hyapeyo brāhmaṇaiḥ kṛtaḥ । dharmaścātra praśapto vai māṇḍavyena mahātmanā ।। ete cānye ca bahavo yātanāṃ ca samāgatāḥ । varjayitvā virūpākṣaṃ devadevaṃ maheśvaram ।।
evaṃ hi mohitāstena na cābuddhyanta śaṅkaram । tataste ṛṣayaḥ sarve parasparamathābruvan ।। na cāyaṃ vidhirasmākaṃ gṛhasthānāṃ vidhīyate । brahmacarya ratānāṃ ca vane vā vanavāsinām ।।
yatīnāṃ vā tathā dharmo nāyaṃ dṛṣṭaḥ kathañcana । anayastu mahāneṣa yenāyaṃ mohito dvijāḥ ।। liṅgaṃ prapātayasvaitannāyaṃ dharmastapasvinām । vadasva vācā madhuraṃ vastramekaṃ samāśraya ।।
tyājite ca tvayā liṅge tataḥ pūjāmavāpsyasi । ṛṣīṇāṃ tadvacaḥ śrutvā bhagavānbhaganetrahā ।। uvāca ślakṣṇayā vācā prahasanniva śaṅkaraḥ । na śakyamidamasmā kaṃ liṅgaṃ pātayituṃ balāt ।।
brahmādidaivataiḥ sarvaiḥ kimutānyaistapodhanaiḥ । pātayeyamahaṃ caitalliṅgaṃ bho dvijasattamāḥ ।। āśrame tiṣṭha vā gaccha vākyamityeva te abruvan । evamukto mahādevaḥ pratdṛṣṭendriyaceṣṭitaḥ ।।
sarveṣāṃ paśyatāmeva tatraivāntardadhe prabhuḥ । antarhite bhagavati tathā liṅge kṛte bhave ।। trailokye sarvabhūtānāṃ prādurbhāvo na jāyate । vyākulaṃ ca tadā sarvaṃ na prakāśeta kiñcana ।।
tapate caiva nādityo niṣprabhaḥ pāvakastathā । nakṣatrāṇi grahāścaiva viparītā vijajñire ।। saṃtānārtha pravṛttānāmṛṣīṇāṃ vibhavātmanām । kratavo na vyavarttanta ṛtukālābhigāminām ।।
te carati punarddharmmaṃ nirmamā nirahaṅkṛtāḥ । naṣṭaprabhāvavīryāśca naṣṭatejasa eva ca ।। dharme caiva matisteṣāṃ tadā na vyavatiṣṭhate । te tusarve samāgamya brahmalokamupāgatāḥ ।।
brahmaṇo bhavanaṃ gatvā dṛṣṭvā puṣpakasaṃbhavam । pādayoḥ patitāḥ sarve śivavṛttāntamūcire ।। vikaṭaḥ stabdhakeśaśca karāladaśanastathā । ulūkavyagrahastaśca raktapiṅgalalocanaḥ ।।
śiśnaṃ savṛṣaṇaṃ tasya raktaṃ gairikamaṇḍitam । snuṣāṇāṃ ca duhitṝṇāṃ putrīṇāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ ।। vartamānastataḥ pārśve viparītābhilāṣataḥ । unmatta iti vijñāya so asmābhiravamānitaḥ ।।
ākruṣṭastāḍitaścāpi liṅgaṃ cāpyasya coddhṛtam । tasya krodhaprasādārthaṃ vayaṃ te śaraṇaṃ gatāḥ ।। etatkāryaṃ na jānīmastanno brūhi pitāmaha । ṛṣīṇāṃ tadvacaḥ śrutvā dhyānādvijñāya ceśvaram ।।
pratyuvāca tato brahmā vākyaṃ ca susamā hitaḥ । eṣa devo mahādevo vijñeyastu maheśvaraḥ ।। na tasya paramaṃ kiñcitpadaṃ samadhigamyate । devānāṃ ca ṛṣīṇāṃ ca pitṛṇāṃ caiva sa prabhuḥ ।।
sahasrayugaparyante pralaye sarvadehinām । saṃharatyeṣa bhagavān kālo bhūtvā maheśvaraḥ ।। eṣa caiva prajāḥ sarvāḥ sṛjatyekaḥ svatejasā । eṣa cikrī ca vakṣojaśrīvatsakṛtalakṣaṇaḥ ।।
yegī kṛtayuge caiva tretāyāṃ kraturucyate । dvāpare caiva kālāgnirdharmaketuḥ kalau smṛtaḥ ।। rudrasya mūrttayastisro vijñeyāścāpi paṇḍitaiḥ । tamo hyagnī rajo brahmā sattvaṃ viṣṇuḥ prakāśakaḥ ।।
mūrttirekā smṛtā yasya digvāsāśca śivāhvayā । yatra tiṣṭhanti tadbrahmayogena tu samanvitam ।। tasmāddevaṃ devadevamī śānaṃ prabhumavyayam । ārādhayata viprendrā jitakrodhā jitendriyāḥ ।।
dṛṣṭaṃ vai yādṛśaṃ tasya liṅgamāsīnmahātmanaḥ । tādṛkpratikṛtiṃ kṛtvā śūlapāṇiṃ prapadyata ।। tato drakṣyatha deveśaṃ durdarśamakṛtātmabhiḥ । yaṃ dṛṣṭvā sarvamajñānamadharmaśca pramaśyati ।।
tataḥ pradakṣiṇaṃ kṛtvā brahmāṇamamitaujasam । āsthitā vītaśokāste devadāruvane tataḥ ।। ārādhayitumārabdhā brahmaṇā kathitaṃ yathā । sthaṇḍileṣu vicitreṣu parvateṣu guhāsu ca ।।
nadīnāṃ ca vicitreṣu pulineṣu śubheṣu ca । evaṃ saṃvatsare pūrṇe vasaṃte samupasthite । tadeva rūpamāsthāya devastadvanamāgataḥ ।। kusumitabahupādapālatākaṃ bhramaragaṇai rupagīyamānakhaṇḍam ।
parabhṛtaparipūrṇacāruśabdaṃ praviśati tadvanamāśramaṃ maheśaḥ ।। tatastaṃ munayaḥ sarve tuṣṭuvuḥ susamāhitāḥ ।। adbhirvivadhamālyaiśca dhūpamandhaistathaiva ca । sapatnīkā mahābhāgāḥ saputrāḥ saparicchadāḥ ।।
mṛdu bhaste tadā vāgbhirgirīśamidamabruvan । ajñānāddevadevasya yadasmābhignuṣṭhitam ।। karmaṇā manasā vācā tatsarvaṃ kṣantumarhasi । caritāni vicitrāṇi guhyāni gahanāni ca ।।
brahmādīnāṃ ca devānāṃ durvijñeyāni śaṅkara । svāgataṃ te na jānīmo gatiṃ naiva ca naiva ca ।। viśveśvara mahādeva yo asi so asi namo astu te । stuvanti tvāṃ mahātmāno devadevaṃ maheśvaram ।।
namo bhavāya bhavyāya bhāvanāyodbhavāya ca । anantabalavīryāya bhūtānāṃ pataye namaḥ ।। saṃhartre kapiśāṅgāya avyayāya vyayāya ca । gaṅgā saliladhārāya cādhārāya guṇātmane ।।
tryaṃbakāya trinetrāya triśūlavaradhāriṇe । kandarpāya namastubhyaṃ namo astu paramātmane ।। śakarāya vṛṣāṅkāya gaṇānāṃ pataye namaḥ । daṇḍahastāya kālāya pāśahastāya vai namaḥ ।।
vedamantrapradhānāya śatajihvāya te namaḥ । bhūtaṃ bhavyaṃ bhaviṣyacca sthāvaraṃ caṅgamaṃ ca yat ।। tava dehātsamutpannaṃ deva sarvamidaṃ jagat । śebho pāhi ca bhadraṃ te prasīda bhagavaṃstataḥ ।।
ajñānādyadi vā jñānādyatkiñcitkurute naraḥ । tatsarvaṃ bhagavāneva kurute yogamāyayā ।। evaṃ stutvā tu munayaḥ prahṛṣṭenāntarātmanā । yācante tapasā yuktāḥ paśyāmasttvāṃ yathā purā ।।
prakṛtisthaṃ ca te liṅgaṃ tathaivāstu yathā purā । namo digvāsase nityaṃ kiṅkiṇījālamāline ।। vikaṭāya karālāya karālavadanāya ca । arūpāya surūpāya viśvarūpāya te namaḥ ।।
kaṭaṅkaṭāya rūdrāya svāhākārāya vai namaḥ । sarvaprāṇātmane tubhyaṃ guṇadehāya vai namaḥ ।। durggandhāya sugandhāya śūlahastāya vai namaḥ । svayaṃ nīlaśikhaṇḍāya śrīkaṇṭhāya namo namaḥ ।
nīlakaṇṭhāya devāya citābhasmāṅgarāgiṇe ।। guṇatrayātmane tubhyaṃ namo viśvāya vedhase । śmaśānavāsine nityaṃ pretarūpāya vai namaḥ ।। tvaṃ brahmā sarvadevānāṃ rudrāṇāṃ nīlalohitaḥ ।
ātmā ca sarvabhūtānāṃ sāṃkhyaiḥ puruṣa ucyate ।। parvatānāṃ mahāmerurnakṣatrāṇāṃ ca candramāḥ । ṛṣīṇāṃ ca vasiṣṭhastvaṃ devānāṃ vāsavastathā ।। oṅkaraḥ sarvavedānāṃ jyeṣṭhasāma ca sāmasu ।
āraṇyānāṃ ca sarveṣāṃ siṃhastvaṃ parameśvaraḥ ।। grāmyāṇāmṛṣabhaścāpi bhagavāṃllokapūjitaḥ । sarvathā varttamāno api yoyo bhāvo bhaviṣyati ।। tvāmeva tatra paśyāmo brahmaṇā kathitaṃ yathā ।
kāmaḥ krodhaśca lobhaśca viṣādo mada eva ca ।। etadicchāma vai roddhuṃ prasīda parameśvara । mahāsaṃharaṇe prāpte tvayā deva kṛtātmanā ।। karaṃ lalāṭe saṃpīḍya vahnirutpāditastvayā ।
tenāgninā tadā lokā arcirbhiḥ sarvato vṛtāḥ ।। tasmādagnisamā hyete bahavo vikṛtāgnayaḥ । yāni cānyānibhūtāni sthāvarāṇi carāṇi ca ।। dahyante prāṇinaste tu tvatsamutthena vāhninā ।
asmākaṃ dahyamānānāṃ trātā bhava sureśvara ।। tvaṃ ca lokahitārthāya bhūtāni pariṣiñcasi । maheśvara mahābhāga prabho śubhanirīkṣaka ।। ājñāpaya vayaṃ nātha karttāro vacanaṃ tava ।
rūpakoṭisahasreṣu rūpakoṭiśateṣu ca ।। antaṃ gantuṃ na śaktāḥ sma tava deva namo astu te । tatastu bhagavānīśa idaṃ vacanamabravīt ।। ye hi me bhasmaniratā bhasmanā dagdhakilbiṣāḥ ।
yathoktakāriṇo dāntā viprā dhyānaparāyaṇāḥ ।। na tānparivadedvidvān na ca tānatilaṅghayet । na cemānapriyaṃ brūyādamutreha hitārthavān ।। yastānnindati mūḍhātmā mahādevaṃsa nindati ।
yastvetānpūjayennityaṃ sa pūjayati śaṅkaram । evaṃ caratha bhadraṃ vo mattaḥ siddhimavāpsyatha ।। atulamiha mahātamaḥ praṇāśaṃśivakathitaṃ paramaṃ vidhiṃ viditvā । apagatabhayalobhamohacintāḥ saha patitāḥ mahasā śirobhirūhuḥ ।।
tataste muditā viprāḥ prakṛtisthe maheśvare । gandhodakaiḥ suśuddhaiśca kuśapuṣpavimiśritaiḥ ।। snāpayanti mahākumbhairadbhirdevaṃ maheśvaram । gāyanti vividhairguhyair huṃkāraiścāpi susvaraiḥ ।।
namo digvāsase deva kiṅkiṇīdhrāya vai namaḥ । arddha nārīśarīrāya sāṃkhyayogapravarttine ।। ghanavāhanakṛṣṇāya gajacarmanivāsine । kṛṣṇājinottarīyāya vyālayajñopavītine ।।
suracitacitravicitrakuṇḍalāya suracitamālyavibhūṣaṇāya tubhyam । mṛgapativaracarmavāsase te pṛthuparaśo ca namostu śaṅkarāya ।। bhūyaśca sthāpite liṅge lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā । varṇadharmaparāścaiva ceruste munisattamāḥ ।।
tatastānsa munīnprītaḥ pratyuvāca maheśvaraḥ । prītosmi yuṣmattapasā varaṃ vṛṇuta muvratāḥ ।। tataste munayassarve praṇipatya maheśvaram । bhṛgvaṅgirā vasiṣṭhaśca viśvāmitrastathaiva ca ।।
gautamo atriḥ sukeśaśca pulastyaḥ pulahaḥ kratuḥ । marīciḥ kaśyapaścāpi saṃvartaśca mahātapāḥ ।। te praṇamya mahādevamidaṃ vacanamabruvan । bhasmasnānaṃ ca nagnatvaṃ vāmatvaṃ pratilomatā ।
sevyāsevyatvaṃ tu vibho etadicchāma veditum ।। etadvaḥ saṃpravakṣyāmi kathāsarvasvamadya vai । agnirhyahaṃ somayutaḥ somaścāgnimupaśritaḥ ।। kṛtākṛtaṃ vadantyagniṃ bhūyo lokāḥ samāśritāḥ ।
asakṛccāgninā dagdhaṃ jagatsthāvarajaṅgamam ।। bhasmasādhyaṃ hi tatsarvaṃ pavitramida muttamam । bhasmanā vīryamāsthāya bhūtāni pariṣiñcati ।। agnikāryaṃ ca yatkṛtvā kariṣyati ca tryāyuṣam ।
bhasmanā mama vīryeṇa mucyate sarvakilbiṣaiḥ ।। bhāsayatyeva yadbhasma śubhaṃ vāsayate ca yat । tatkṣaṇātsarvapāpānāṃ bhasmeti parikīrtyate ।। ūṣmapāḥ pitaro jñeyā devā vai somasaṃbhavāḥ ।
agnīṣomātmakaṃ sarvaṃ jagatsthāvarajaṃ gamam ।। ahamagnirmahātejāḥ somaścaiṣā mamāṃbikā । ahamagniśca somaśca prakṛtyā puruṣaḥ svayam ।। tasmādbhasma mahābhāgā madvīryamiti cocyate ।
svavīryaṃ vapuṣā caiva dhārayāmīti vai sthitiḥ ।। tadā prabhṛti lokeṣu rakṣārthamaśubheṣu ca । bhasmanā kriyate rakṣā sūtikānāṃ gṛheṣu ca ।। bhasmasnānaviśuddhātmā jitakrodho jitendriyaḥ ।
matsamīpasupāgamya na bhūyo vinivartate ।। vrataṃ pāśupataṃ yogaṃ kāpālaṃ yoganirmitam । pūrvaṃ pāśupataṃ hyetannirmitaṃ tadanuttamam ।। śeṣāścāśramiṇaḥ sarve paścātsṛṣṭāḥ svayaṃbhuvā ।
sṛṣṭireṣā mayā sṛṣṭā lajjāmohabhayātmikā ।। nagnā eva hi jāyante devatā munayastathā । ye cānyemānavā loke sarve jāyantyavāsasaḥ ।। indriyairajitairnagnā dukūlenāpi saṃvṛtāḥ ।
taireva saṃvṛto guptona vastraṃ kāraṇaṃ smṛtam ।। kṣamā dhṛtirahiṃsā ca vairāgyaṃ caiva sarvaśaḥ । tulyau mānāpamānau ca tatprāvaraṇamuttamam ।। bhasmapāṇḍuradigdhāṅgo dhyāyate manasā bhavam ।
yadyakāryasahasrāṇi kṛtvā snāyati bhasmanā ।। tatsarvaṃ dahate bhasma yathāgnistejasā vanam । tasmā dyatnaparo bhūtvā trikālamapi yaḥ sadā ।। bhasmanā kurute snānaṃ gāṇapatyaṃ sa gacchati ।
saṃhṛtya ca kratūnsarvāngṛhītvāmṛtamutta mam ।। dhyāyanti ye mahādevaṃ līnāstadbhāvabhāvitāḥ । uttareṇātha panthānaṃ te amṛtatvamavāpnuyuḥ ।। dakṣiṇenātha panthānaṃ ye śmaśānāni bhejire ।
aṇimā mahimā caiva laghimā prāptireva ca ।। garimā pañcamī caiva ṣaṣṭhaṃ prākāmyameva ca । īśitvaṃ ca vaśitvaṃ ca hyamaratvaṃ ca te gatāḥ ।। indrādayastathā devāḥ kāmikaṃ vratamāsthitāḥ ।
aiśvaryaṃ paramaṃ prāpya sarve prathitatejasaḥ ।। vyapagatamadamohamuktarāgāstamerahajadoṣavivarjitasvabhāvāḥ । paribhavamidamuttamaṃ viditvā paśupatidayitamidaṃ vrataṃ caradhvam ।। yaḥ paṭhedvai śucirbhūtvā śraddadhāno jitendriyaḥ ।
sarvapāpaviśuddhātmā rudralokaṃ sa gacchati ।। agātkathamamāvasyāṃ māsi māsi divaṃ nṛpaḥ । ailaḥ purūravāḥ sūta kathaṃ vātarpayatpitṝn ।। tasya te ahaṃ pravakṣyāmi prabhāvaṃ śāṃśapāyane ।
ailasyādityasaṃyogaṃ somasya ca mahātmanaḥ ।। antaḥsāramayasyendoḥ pakṣayoḥ śuklakṛṣṇayoḥ । hrāsavṛddhī pidṛmataḥ pitryasya ca vinirṇayam ।। somāccaivāmṛtaprāptiṃ pitṝṇāṃ tarvaṇaṃ tathā ।
kāvyāgniṣvāttamaumyānāṃ pitṝṇāñcaiva darśanam ।। yathā purūravāścaiva tarpayāmāsa vai pitṝn । etatsarvaṃ pravakṣyāmi parvāṇi ca yathākramam ।। yadā tu candrasūryauṃ vai nakṣatreṇa samāgatau ।
amāvasyāṃ nivasata ekarātraikamaṇḍalau ।। sa gacchati tadā draṣṭuṃ divākaraniśākarau । amāvasyāmamāvāsyāṃ mātāmahapitāmahau ।। abhivādya sa tau tatra kālāpekṣaḥ pratīkṣate ।
prasyandamānātsomāttu pitrarthaṃ tu pariśravān ।। ailaḥ purūravā vidvānmāsaśrāddhacikīrṣayā । upāste pitṛmantaṃ taṃ somaṃ divi samāsthitaḥ ।। dvilavāṃ kuhūmātrāṃ ca te ubhe tu vicārya saḥ ।
sinīvālīpramāṇebhyaḥ sinīvālīmupāsya saḥ ।। kuhūmātraḥ kalāṃ caiva jñātvopāste kuhūṃ tathā । sa tadā tāmupāsīnaḥ kālāpekṣaḥ prapaśyati ।। sudhāmṛtaṃ tu tatsomātsravadvai māsatṛptaye ।
daśabhiḥ pañcabhiścaiva sudhāmṛtaparisravaiḥ ।। kṛṣṇapakṣe bhujāṃ prītyā dahyamānāṃ tathāṃśubhiḥ । sadyaḥ prakṣaratā tena saumyena madhunā tu saḥ ।। nirvāteṣtratha pakṣeṣu pitryeṇa vidhinā divi ।
sudhāmṛtena rājaindrastarpa yāmāsa vai pitṝn ।। saumyānbarhiṣadaḥ kāvyānagniṣvāttāṃstathaiva ca । ṛtamagnistu yaḥ proktaḥ sa tu saṃvatsaro mataḥ ।। jajñire hyṛtavastasmāddhyṛtubhyaścārttavāstathā ।
ārtavā hyarddhamāsākhyāḥ pitaro hyṛtusūnavaḥ ।। ṛtavaḥ pitāmahā māsā ayanāhyabdasūnavaḥ । prapitāmahāstu vai devāḥ pañcābdā brahmaṇaḥ sutāḥ ।। saumyāstu somajā jñeyāḥ kāvyā jñeyāḥ kaveḥ sutāḥ ।
upahūtāḥ smṛtā devāḥ somajāḥ somapāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। ājyapāstu smṛtāḥ kāvyāstisrastāḥ pitṛjātayaḥ । kāvyā barhiṣada ścaiva agniṣvāttāśca tāstridhā ।। gṛhasthā ye ca yajvāna ṛturbarhiṣado dhruvam ।
gṛhasthāścāpyayajvāna agniṣvāttāstathārttavāḥ ।। aṣṭakāpatayaḥ kāvyāḥ pañcābdāstānnibodhata । teṣāṃ saṃvatsaro hyagniḥ sūyastu parivatsaraḥ ।। soma iḍvatsaraḥ prokto vāyuścaivānuvatsaraḥ ।
rudrastu vatsarasteṣāṃ pañcābdāste yugātmakāḥ ।। kāvyāścaivoṣmapāścaiva divākīrtyāśca te smṛtāḥ । ye te pibantyamāvasyāṃ māsimāsi sudhāṃ divi ।। tāṃstena tarpayāmāsa yāvadāsītpurūravāḥ ।
yasmātprasravate somānmāsi māsi dhinoti ca ।। tasmātsudhāmṛtaṃ tadvai pitṝṇāṃ somapāyinām । evaṃ tadamṛtaṃ saumyaṃ sudhā ca madu caiva ha ।। kṛṣṇapakṣe yathā vendoḥ kalāḥ pañcadaśa kramāt ।
pibantyaṃbumayaṃ devāstrayastriṃśattu chandanāḥ ।। pītvārddhamāsaṃ gacchanti caturdaśyāṃ sudhāmṛtam । ityevaṃ pīyamānaistu devaiḥ sarvairniśākaraḥ ।। samāgacchatyamāvasyāṃ bhāge pañcadaśe sthitaḥ ।
suṣumṇāpyāyitaṃ caiva hyamāvasyāṃ yathā kramam ।। pibanti dvilavaṃ kālaṃ pitaraste sudhāmṛtam । pītakṣayaṃ tataḥ somaṃ sūryo asāvekaraśminā ।। āpyāyayatsuṣumṇātaḥ punastānsomapāyinaḥ ।
niḥ śeṣāyāṃ kalāyāṃ tu somamāpyāyayatpunaḥ ।। suṣumṇāpyāyamānasya bhāgaṃ bhāgamahaḥ kramāt । kalāḥ kṣīyanti tāḥ kṛṣṇāḥ śuklā cāpyāyayanti tam ।। evaṃ sūryasya vīryeṇa candrasyāpyāyitā tanuḥ ।
dṛśyate paurṇamāsyāṃ vai śuklaḥ saṃpūrṇamaṇḍalaḥ ।। saṃsiddhirevaṃ somasya pakṣayoḥ śuklakṛṣṇayoḥ । ityevaṃ pitṛmānsomaḥ smṛta iḍvatsarātmakaḥ ।। krāntaḥ pañcadaśaiḥ sārddhaṃ sudhāmṛtaparisravaiḥ ।
ataḥ parvāṇi vakṣyāmi varvaṇāṃ saṃdhayaśca ye ।। granthimanti yathā parvāṇīkṣuve ṇvorbhavantyuta । tathārddhamāsi parvāṇi śuklakṛṣṇāni caiva hi ।। pūrṇāmāvasyayorbhedau granthayaḥ saṃdhayaśca vai ।
arddhamāsaṃ tu parvāṇi dvitīyāprabhṛtīni tu ।। anvādhānakriyā yasmātkriyate parvasaṃdhiṣu । tasmāttu parvaṇāmādau pratipatsarvasaṃdhiṣu ।। sāyāhne ahyanumatyādau kālo dvilava ucyate ।
lavau dvāveva rākāyāṃ kālo jñeyo aparāhṇakaḥ ।। pratipatkṛṣṇapakṣasya kāle atīte aparāhṇake । sāyāhne pratipanne ca sa kālaḥ paurṇamāsikaḥ ।। vyatīpāte sthite sūrye lekhārddhe tu yugāntare ।
yugāntarodite caiva leśārddhe śaśinaḥ kramāt ।। paurṇamāsī vyatīpāte yadīkṣetāṃ parasparam । yasminkāle samau syātāṃ tau vyatīpāta eva saḥ ।। taṃ kālaṃ sūryanirddeśyaṃ dṛṣṭvā saṃkhyāṃ tu sarpati ।
sa vai vaṣaṭākriyākālaḥ sadyaḥ kālaṃ vidhīyate ।। pūrṇandoḥ pūrṇapakṣe tu rātrisaṃdhiśca pūrṇimā । tato virajyate naktaṃ paurṇamāsyāṃ niśākaraḥ ।। yadīkṣete vyatīpāte divā pūrṇe parasparam ।
candrārkāvaparāhṇe tu pūrṇātmānau tu pūrṇimā ।। yasmāttāmanumanyante pitaro daivataiḥ saha । tasmādanumatirnāma pūrṇimā prathamā smṛtā ।। atyarthaṃ bhrājate yasmādvyomnyasyāṃ vai niśākaraḥ ।
rañjanāccaiva candrasya rāketi kavayo abruvan ।। amāvasetāmṛkṣe tu yadā candradivākarau । rākā pañcadaśī rātriramāvāsyā tataḥ smṛtā ।। vyucchidya tamamāvasyāṃ paśyatastau samāgatau ।
anyonyaṃ candrasūryauṃ tau yadā tadvarśa ucyate ।। dvau dvau lavāvamāvāsyā sa kālaḥ parvasaṃdhiṣu । dvyakṣara kuhumātraśca parvakālāstrayaḥ smṛtāḥ ।। naṣṭacandrā tvamāvasyā yā madhyāṅnātpravarttate ।
divasārddhena rātryā ca sūryaṃ prāpya tu candramāḥ ।। sūryeṇa saha sāmudraṃ gatvā prātastanātsa vai । dvau kālau saṃgamaṃ caiva madhyāhne niyataṃ raviḥ ।। pratipacchuklapakṣasya candramāḥ sūrya maṇḍalāt ।
vimucyamānayormadhye tayormaṇḍalayostu vai ।। sa tadā hyāhuteḥ kālo darśasya tu vaṣaṭkriyā । etadṛtumukhaṃ jñeyamamā vāsyāsya parvaṇaḥ ।। divāparva hyamāvāsyā kṣīṇendau bahule tu vai ।
tasmāddivā hyamāvāsyāṃ gṛhyate asau divākaraḥ ।। gṛhyate tu divā tasmādamāvāsyāṃ divi kṣayām । kalānāmapi caitāsāṃ vṛddhihānyā jalātmanaḥ ।। tithīnāṃ nāmadheyāni vidvadbhiḥ saṃjñitāni vai ।
darśayetāmathātmānaṃ sūryācandramasāvubhau ।। niṣkrāmatyatha tenaiva kramaśaḥ sūryamaṇḍalāt । dvilavonamahorātraṃ bhāskaraṃ spṛśate śaśī ।। sa tadā hyāhuteḥ kālodarśasya tu vaṣaṭkriyā ।
kuheti kokilenokto yaḥ sa kālaḥ samāpyate ।। tatkālasaṃmitā yasmādamāvāsyā kuhūḥ smṛtā । sinīvālīpramāṇastu kṣīṇaśeṣo niśākaraḥ ।। āmāvasyāṃ viśatyarkassinī vālītataḥ smṛtā ।
anumatyāścarākāyāḥ sinīvālyāḥ kuhūṃvinā ।। etāsāṃ dvilavaḥ kālaḥ kuhūmātraṅkuhūḥsmṛtāḥ । candrasūryavyatīpāte saṃgate pūrṇimāntare ।। pratipatpratipadyeta parvakālo dvimātrakaḥ ।
kālaḥ kahūsinīvālyoḥ sāmudrasya tu madhyataḥ ।। arkāgni maṇḍale some parvakālaḥ kalāsamaḥ । evaṃ sa śuklapakṣe vai rajanyāṃ parvasaṃdhiṣu ।। saṃpūrmamaṇḍalaḥ śrīmāṃścandramā uparajyate ।
yasmādā dāpyāyate somaḥ pañcadaśyāṃ tu pūrṇimā ।। daśabhiḥ pañcabhiścaiva kalābhirdivasakramāt । tasmātkalāḥ pañcadaśa somenāsya tu ṣoḍaśī ।। tasmātsomasya bhavati pañcadaśyāprapāṃ kṣayaḥ ।
ityete pitaro devāḥ somapāḥ somavarddhanāḥ ।। ārtavā ṛtavo hyṛddhā devāstānbhāvayanti vai । ataḥ pitṝnpravakṣyāmi māsaśrāddhabhujastu ye ।। teṣāṃ gatiṃ satattvāṃ ca prāptiṃ śrāddhasya caiva hi ।
na mṛtānāṃ gatiḥ śakyā jñātuṃ na punarāgatiḥ ।। tapasāpi prasiddhena kiṃpunarmāsacakṣuṣā । anudevapitṝnete pitaro laukikāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। devāḥ saumyāśca kāvyāśca ayajvāno hyaconijāḥ ।
devāste pitaraḥ sarve devāstānvādayantyuta ।। manuṣyapitaraścaiva tebhyo anye laukikāḥ smṛtāḥ । pitā pitāmahaścāpi tathā yaḥ prapitāmahaḥ ।। yajvāno ye tu sāmena somavantastu te smṛtāḥ ।
ye yajvāno haviryajñe te vai barhiṣadaḥ smṛtāḥ ।। agniṣvāttāḥ smṛtāsteṣāṃ homino ayājyayājinaḥ । teṣāṃ tu dharmasādharmyātsmṛtāḥ sāyujyagā dvijaiḥ ।। ye cāpyāśramadharmāṇāṃ prasthāneṣu vyavasthitāḥ ।
ante tu nāvasīdanti śraddhāyuktāstu karmasu ।। tapasā brahmacaryeṇa yajñena prajayā ca vai । śrāddhena vidyayā caiva pradānena ca saptadhā ।। karmasveteṣu ye yuktā bhavantyādehapātanāt ।
daivaistaiḥ pitṛbhiḥ sārddhaṃ sūkṣmajaiḥ somayājanaiḥ ।। svargatā divi modante pitṛvatta upāsate । teṣāṃ nivāpe datte tu tatkulīnaiśca bandhubhiḥ ।। māsaśrāddhabhujastṛptiṃ labhante somalaukikāḥ ।
ete manuṣyapitaro māsaśrāddhabhujastu ye ।। tebhyo apare tu ye apyanye saṃkīrṇāḥ karmayoniṣu । bhraṣṭāścāśramadharmebhyaḥ svadhāsvāhāvivarjitāḥ ।। bhinnadehā durātmānaḥ pretabhūtā yamakṣaye ।
svakarmāṇya nuśocanto yātanāsthānamāgatāḥ ।। dīrghāyuṣo atiśuṣkāśca śmaśrulāśca vivāsasaḥ । kṣutpipāsāparītāśca vidravantastatastataḥ ।। saritsarastaḍāgāni vāpīścāpyupalipsavaḥ ।
parānnāni ca lipsaṃtaḥ kālyamānāstatastataḥ ।। sthāneṣu pātyamānāśca yātanāśca punaḥ punaḥ । śālmale vaitaraṇyāṃ ca kuṃbhīpāke tathaiva ca ।। karaṃbhavālukāyāṃ ca asipatravane tathā ।
śilā saṃpeṣaṇe caiva pātyamānāḥ svakarmabhiḥ ।। tatrasthānāṃ hi teṣāṃ vai duḥ khitānāmanāśinām । teṣāṃ lokāntarasthānāṃ bāndhavairnāma gotrataḥ ।। bhūmāvasavyaṃ darbheṣu dattāḥ piṇḍāstrayastu vai ।
yānti tāstarpayante ca pretasthāneṣvadhiṣṭhitān ।। aprāptā yātanāsthānaṃ prabhraṣṭā ya ca pañcadhā । paścādye sthāvarānte vai jātā nīcaiḥ svakarmabhiḥ ।। nānārūpāsu jāyante tiryagyoniṣvayoniṣu ।
yadāhārā bhavantyete tāsu tāsviha yoniṣu ।। tasmiṃstasmiṃstadāhāre śrāddhaṃ dattaṃ pratiṣṭhate । kāle nyāyāgataṃ pātre vidhinā pratipāditam ।। prāpnotyannaṃ yathādattaṃ janturyatrāvatiṣṭhate ।
yathā goṣu pranaṣṭāmu vatso vindati mātaram ।। tathā śrāddheṣu dattānnaṃ mantraḥ prāpayate pitṝn । evaṃ hyaviphalaṃ śrāddhaṃ śraddhādattaṃ tu mantrataḥ ।। tattatkumāraḥ provāca paśyandivyena cakṣuṣā ।
gatāgatajñaḥ pretānāṃ prāptiṃ śrāddhasya taiḥ saha ।। bāhlīkāścoṣmapāścaiva divākīrtyāśca te smṛtāḥ । kṛṣṇapakṣastvahasteṣāṃ śuklaḥ svapnāya śarvarī ।। ityete pitaro devā devāśca pitaraśca vai ।
ṛtvartavārddhamāsāstu anyonyaṃ pitaraḥ smṛtāḥ ।। ityeta pitaro devā manuṣyapitaraśca ye । prīteṣu teṣu prīyante śrāddhayukteṣu karmasu ।। ityeṣa vicayaḥ proktaḥ pitṝṇāṃ somapāyinām ।
evaṃ pitṛsatattvaṃ hi purāṇe niścayaṃ gatam ।। ityarkapitṛsomānāmailasya ca samāgamaḥ । sudhāmṛtasya ca prāptiḥ pitṝṇāṃ caiva tarppaṇam ।। pūrṇā māvāsyayoḥ kālo yātanāsthānameva ca ।
samāsātkīrtitastubhyameṣa sargaḥ manātanaḥ ।। vaiśvarūpyaṃ tu sargasya kathitaṃ hyekadaiśikam । na śakyaṃ parisaṃkhyātuṃ śraddheyaṃ bhūtimicchatā ।। svāyaṃbhuvasya hi hyeṣa sargaḥ krānto mayā tu vai ।
vistareṇānupūrvyā ca bhūyaḥ kiṃ varṇayāmyaham ।। caturyugāni yānyāsanpūrvaṃ svāyaṃbhuve antare । teṣāṃ nisargaṃ tattvaṃ ca śrotumicchāmi vistarāt ।। pṛthivyādiprasaṃgena yanmayā prāgudīritam ।
teṣāṃ caturyugaṃ hyetattadvakṣyāmi nibodhata ।। saṃkhyayeha prasaṃkhyāya vistarāccaiva sarvaśaḥ । yugaṃ ca yugabhedaśca yugadharmastathaiva ca ।। yugasaṃdhyāṃśakaścaiva yugasaṃdhānameva ca ।
ṣaṭprakāśayugākhyaiṣā tā pravakṣyāmi tattvataḥ ।। laukikena pramāṇena niṣpādyābdaṃ tu mānuṣam । tenābdena prasaṃkhyāyai vakṣyāmīha vaturyugam । nimeṣakāla tulyaṃ hi vidyāllaghvakṣaraṃ ca yat ।।
kāṣṭhā nimeṣā daśa pañca caiva triśacca kāṣṭhā gaṇayetkalāṃ tu । triṃśatkalāścāpi bhavenmuhūrttastai striṃśatā rātryahanī same te ।। ahorātrau vibhajate sūryo mānuṣalaukikau ।। tatrāhaḥ karmaceṣṭāyāṃ rātriḥ svapnāya kalpate ।
pitrye rātryahanī māsaḥ pravibhāgastayoḥ punaḥ ।। kṛṣṇapakṣastvahasteṣāṃ śuklaḥ svapnāya śarvarī । triṃśadye mānuṣā māsāḥ pitryo māsastu saḥ smṛtaḥ ।। śatāni trīṇi māsānāṃ ṣaṣṭyā cāpyadhikāni vai ।
pitryaḥ saṃvatsaro hyeṣa mānuṣeṇa vibhāvyate ।। mānuṣe ṇaiva mānena varṣāṇāṃ yacchataṃ bhavet । pitṝṇāṃ trīṇi varṣāṇi saṃkhyātānīha tāni vai ।। daśa caivādhikā māsāḥ pitṛsaṃkhyeha saṃjñitāḥ ।
laukikenaiva mānena hṛbdo yo mānuṣaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। etaddivyamahorātraṃ śāstre syānniścayo gataḥ । divye rātryahanī varṣa pravibhāgastayoḥ punaḥ ।। ahastatrodagayanaṃ rātriḥ syāddakṣiṇāyanam ।
ye te rātryahanī divye prasaṃkhyānaṃ tayoḥ punaḥ ।। triṃśadyāni tu varṣāṇi dipyo māsastu sa smṛtaḥ । yanmānuṣaṃ śataṃ viddhi divyā māsāstrayastu te ।। daśa caiva tathāhāni divyo hyeṣa vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ ।
trīṇi varṣaśatānyeva ṣaṣṭivarṣāṇi yāni tu । divyaḥ saṃvatsaro hyeṣa mānuṣeṇa prakīrttitaḥ ।। trīṇi varṣa sahasrāṇi mānuṣāṇi pramāṇataḥ । triṃśadanyāni varṣāṇi mataḥ saptarṣivatsaraḥ ।।
nava yāni sahasrāṇi varṣāṇāṃ mānuṣāṇi tu । anyāni navatiścaiva dhruvaḥ saṃvatsaraḥ smṛtaḥ ।। ṣaḍviṃśatisahasrāṇi varṣāṇi mānuṣāṇi tu । varṣāṇāṃ tu śataṃ jñeyaṃ divyo hyeṣa vidhiḥ smṛtaḥ ।।
trīṇyeva niyutānyāhurvarṣāṇāṃ mānuṣāṇi tu ।। ṣaṣṭiścaiva sahasrāṇi saṃkhyātāni tu saṃkhyāyā । divyavarṣasahasra tu prāhuḥ saṃkhyāvido janāḥ ।। ityevamṛṣibhirgītaṃ divyayā saṃkhyāyā tviha ।
divyenaiva pramāṇena yugasaṃkhyāprakalpanam ।। catvāri bhārate varṣe yugāni kavayo abuvan । kṛtaṃ tretā dvāparaṃ ca kaliśceti catuṣṭayam ।। pūrva kṛtayukaṃ nāma tatastretī vidhīyate ।
dvāparaṃ ca kaliścaiva yugānyetāni kalpayet ।। catvāryāhuḥ sahasrāṇi varṣāṇāṃ ca kṛta yugam । tasya tāvacchatī saṃdhyā saṃdhyāṃśaḥ saṃdhyāyā samaḥ ।। itareṣu sasaṃdhyeṣu sasaṃdhyāṃśeṣu ca triṣu ।
ekanyāyena vartante sahasrāṇi śatāni ca ।। trīṇi dve ca sahasrāṇi tretādvāparayoḥ kramāt । triśatī dviśatī saṃdhye saṃdhyāṃśau cāpi tatsamau ।। kaliṃ varṣasarasraṃ tu yugamāhurdvijottamāḥ ।
tasyaikaśatikā saṃdhyā saṃdhyāṃśaḥ saṃdhyayā samaḥ ।। teṣāṃ dvādaśasāhasrī yugasaṃkhyā prakīrttitā । kṛtaṃ tretā dvāparaṃ ca kaliścaiva catuṣṭayam ।। atra saṃvatsarā dṛṣṭā mānuṣeṇa pramāṇataḥ ।
kṛtasya tāvadvakṣyāmi varṣāṇi ca nibodhata ।। sahasrāṇāṃ śatānyāhuścaturdaśa hi saṃkhyāyā । catvāriṃśatsahasrāṇi tathānyāni kṛtaṃ yugam ।। tathā śatasahasrāṇi varṣāṇi daśasaṃkhyāyā ।
aśītiśca sahasrāṇi kālastretāyugasya saḥ ।। saptaiva niyutānyāhurvarṣāṇāṃ mānuṣeṇa tu । viṃśatiśca sahasrāmi kālaḥ sa dvāparasya ca ।। tathā śatasahasrāṇi varṣāṇāṃ trīṇi saṃkhyayā ।
ṣaṣṭiścaiva sahasrāṇi kālaḥ kaliyugasya tu ।। evaṃ caturyuge kāla ṛtaiḥ saṃdhyāṃśakaiḥ smṛtaḥ । niyutānyeva ṣaḍiṃśānnirasāni yugāni vai ।। catvāriṃśattathā trīṇi niyutā nīha saṃkhyayā ।
viṃśatiśca sahasrāṇi sa saṃdhyāṃśaścaturyugaḥ ।। evaṃ caturyugākhyānāṃ sādhikā hyekasaptatiḥ । kṛtatretādiyuktānāṃ manorantaramucyate ।। manvantarasya saṃkhyāṃ tu varṣāgreṇa nibodhata ।
triṃśatkoṭyastu varṣāṇāṃ mānuṣeṇa prakīrttitāḥ ।। sapta ṣaṣṭistathānyāni niyutānyadhikāni tu । viśatiśca sahasrāṇi kālo ayaṃ sādhikaṃ vinā ।। manvantarasya saṃkhyaiṣā saṃkhyā vidbhirdvijaiḥ smṛtā ।
manvantarasya kālo ayaṃ yugaiḥ sārddhaṃ ca kīrttitaḥ ।। catuḥ sāhasrayuktaṃ vai prākṛtaṃ tatkṛtaṃ yugam । tretāśiṣṭaṃ pravakṣyāmi dvāparaṃ kalimeva ca ।। yugapatsamayenārtho dvidhā vaktuṃ na śakyate ।
kramāgataṃ mayā hyetattubhyaṃ nokta yuga dvayam ।। ṛṣivaṃśaprasaṃgena vyākulatvāttathaiva ca । atra tretāyugasyādau manuḥ saptarṣayaśca ye ।। śrauta smārtta ca te dharma brahmaṇānupracauditam ।
dārāgnihotrasaṃbandhamṛgyajuḥ sāmasaṃhitam ।। ityādilakṣaṇaṃ śrautaṃ dharma saptarṣayo abruvan । paraṃparāgataṃ dharma smārttaṃ cācāralakṣaṇam ।। varṇāśramācārayutaṃ manuḥ svāyaṃbhuvo abravīt ।
satyena brahmacaryeṇa śrutena tapasā ca vai ।। teṣāṃ tu taptatapasā ārṣeṇopakrameṇa tu । saptarṣīṇāṃ manoścaiva hyādye tretāyuge tathā ।। abuddhipūrvakaṃ teṣāmakriyāpūrvameva ca ।
abhivyaktāstu te mantrāstārakādyairnidarśanaiḥ ।। ādikalpe tu devānāṃ prādurbhūtāstu yāḥ svayam । prāṇāśeṣvatha siddhīnāmanyāsāṃ ca pravarttanam ।। āsanmantrā vyatīteṣu ye kalpeṣu sahasraśaḥ ।
te mantrā vai punasteṣāṃ pratibhāyāmupasthitāḥ ।। ṛco yajūṃṣi sāmāni mantraścātharvaṇāni tu । saptarṣibhistu te proktāḥ smārttaṃ dharmaṃ manurjagau ।। tretādau saṃhitā vedāḥ kevalā dharmasetavaḥ ।
saṃrodhādāyuṣaścaiva vartsyante dvāpareṣu vai ।। ṛṣayastapasā vedāndvāparādiṣvadhīyate । anādinidhinā divyāḥ pūrvaṃ sṛṣṭāḥ svayaṃbhuvā ।। sadharmāḥ savratāḥ sāṃgā yathādharmaṃ yugeyuge ।
vikriyante samānārthā vedavādā yathāyugam ।। āraṃbhayajñāḥ kṣatrāśca haviryajñā viśastathā । paricārayajñāḥ śūdrāstu japayajñā dvijottamāḥ ।। tadā pramuditā varṇāstretāyāṃ dharmapālitāḥ ।
kriyāvantaḥ prajāvantaḥ samṛddhāḥ sukhinastathā ।। brāhmaṇānanurttante kṣatriyāḥ kṣatriyānviśaḥ । vaiśyānuvarttinaḥ śudrāḥ parasparamanuvratāḥ ।। śubhāḥ pravṛttayasteṣāṃ dharmā varṇāśramāstathā ।
saṃkalpitena manasā vācoktena svakarmaṇā ।। tretāyuge ca viphalaḥ karmāraṃbhaḥ prasiddhyati । āyurmedhā balaṃ rūpamārogyaṃ dharmaśīlatā ।। sarvasādhāraṇā hyete tretāyāṃ vai bhavaṃ tyuta ।
varṇāśramavyavasthānaṃ teṣāṃ brahmā tadākarot ।। punaḥ prajāstu tā mohāddharmā stānapyapālayan । parasparavirodhena manuṃ tāḥ punarabhyayuḥ ।। punaḥ svāyaṃbhuvo dṛṣṭvā yāthātathyaṃ prajāpatiḥ ।
dhyātvā tu śatarūpāyāṃ putrau sa udapādayat ।। priyavrato ttānapādau prathamau tau mohīkṣitau । tataḥ prabhṛti rājāna utpannā daṇḍadhāriṇaḥ ।। prajānāṃ rañjanāccaiva rājānaste abhavannṛpāḥ ।
pracchanna pāpāstairye ca na śakyāstu narādhipaiḥ ।। dharmarājaḥ smṛtasteṣāṃ śāstā vaivasvato yamaḥ । varṇānāṃ pravibhāgāśca tretāyāṃ saṃprakīrttitāḥ ।। saṃbhṛtācca tadā mantrā ṛṣibhirbrahmaṇaḥ sutaiḥ ।
yajñāḥ pravarttitāścaiva tadā hyeva tu daivataiḥ ।। yāmaśukrārjitaiścaiva sarvasādhana saṃbhṛtaiḥ । sārddhaṃ viśvabhujā caiva devendreṇa mahaujasā ।। svāyaṃbhuveṃ'tare devairyajñastaiḥ prākpravarttitaḥ ।
satyaṃ japastapo dānaṃ tretāyā dharma ucyate ।। tadā dharmmasahasrānte ahiṃsādharmaḥ pravarttate । jāyante ca tadā śūrā āyuṣmanto mahābalāḥ ।। vyastadaṇḍā mahābhāgā dharmiṣṭhā brahmavādinaḥ ।
padmapatrāyatākṣāśca pṛthūraskāḥ susaṃhatāḥ ।। siṃhātaṅkā mahāsattvā mattamātaṅgagaminaḥ । mahādhanurddharāścaiva tretāyāṃ cakravarttinaḥ ।। sarvalakṣaṇasampūrmā nyagrodhaparimaṇḍalāḥ ।
nyagrodhau tu smṛtau bāhū vyāmo nyagrodha ucyate ।। vyāme naivochrayo yasya sama ūrddhaṃ tu dehinaḥ । samochrayaparīṇāho jñeyo nyagrodhamaṇḍalaḥ ।। cakraṃ ratho maṇirbhāryā nidhiraśvo gajastathā ।
saptaitāni ca ratnāni sarveṣāṃ cakravartināma ।। cakraṃ ratho maṇiḥ khaḍgaścarmaratnaṃ ca pañcamam । keturnidhiśca saptaiva prāṇahīnāni cakṣate ।। bhāryā purohitaścaiva senānī rathakṛcca yaḥ ।
mantryaśvaḥ kalabhaścaiva prāṇinaḥ sapta kīrttitāḥ ।। ratnānyetāni divyāni saṃsiddhāni mahātmanām । caturdaśa vidheyāni sarveṣāṃ cakravarttinām ।। viṣṇoraṃśena jāyante pṛthivyāṃ cakravarttinaḥ ।
manvantareṣu sarveṣu atītānāgateṣviha ।। bhūtabhavyāni yānīha varttamānāni yāni ca । tretāyuge ca tānyatra jāyante cakravarttinaḥ ।। bhadrāṇīmāni teṣāṃ vai bhavantīha mahīkṣitām ।
atyadbhutāni catvāri balaṃ dharmaḥ sukhaṃ dhanam ।। anyonyasyāvirodhena prāpyante tu nṛpaiḥ samam । artho dharmaśca kāmaśca yaśo vijaya eva ca ।। aiśvaryeṇāṇimādyena prabhuśaktyā tathaiva ca ।
śrutena tapasā caiva munīnabhibhavanti vai ।। balena tapasā caiva devadānavamānavān । lakṣaṇaiścaiva jāyante śarīrasthairamānuṣaiḥ ।। keśāḥsnigdhā lalāṭoccā jihvā cāsya pramārjinī ।
tāmraprabhoṣṭanetrāśca śrīvatsāścaiddhvaromaśāḥ ।। ājānubāhavaschaiva tadāmrahastāḥ kaṭau kṛśāḥ । nyagrodhapariṇāhāśca siṃhaskandhāstu mehanāḥ ।। gajedragatayaścaiva mahāhanava eva ca ।
pādayoścakramatsyontu śaṅkhapadmau tuhastayoḥ ।। pañcāśītisahasrāṇi te rājantyajarā nṛpāḥ । asaṃgagatayasteṣāṃ catasraścakravarttinām ।। antarikṣe samudri ca pātāle parvateṣu ca ।
ijyā dānaṃ tapaḥ satyaṃ tretāyāṃ dharma ucyate ।। tadā pravarttate dharmo varṇāśramavibhāgaśaḥ । maryādāsthāpanārthaṃ ca daṇḍanītiḥ pravarttate ।। tdṛṣṭapuṣṭāḥ prajāḥ sarvā arogāḥ pūrṇamānasāḥ ।
eko vedaścatuṣpādastretāyugavidhausmṛtaḥ ।। trīṇi varṣasahasrāṇi tadā jīvanti mānavāḥ । putrapautrasamākīrṇā mriyante ca krameṇa tu ।। eṣa tretāyuge dharmastretāsaṃdhyāṃ nibodhata ।
tretāyugasvabhāvānāṃ saṃdhyā pādena varttate । saṃdhyāpādaḥ svabhāvastu soṃ'śapadena tiṣṭhati ।। kathaṃ tretāyugamukhe yajñasya syātpravarttanam । pūrvaṃ svāyaṃbhuve sarge yathāvattacca brūhi me ।।
antarhitāyāṃ saṃdhyāyāṃ sārddhaṃ kṛtayugena vai । kālākhyāyāṃ pravṛttāyāṃ prāpte tretāyuge tadā ।। auṣadhīṣu ca jātāsu pravṛtte vṛṣṭisarjane । pratiṣṭhitāyāṃ vārttāyāṃ gṛhāśramapare punaḥ ।।
varṇāśramavyavasthānaṃ kṛtavantaśca saṃkhyayā । saṃbhārāṃstāṃstu maṃbhṛtya kathaṃ yajñaḥ pravarttitaḥ ।। etacchutvābravītsūtaḥ śrūyatāṃ śāṃśapāyane । yathā tretāyugamukhe yajñasya syātpravartanam ।।
pūrvaṃ svāyaṃbhuve sarge tadvakṣyāmyānupūrvyataḥ । antarhitāyāṃ saṃdhyāyāṃ sārddhaṃ kṛtayugena tu ।। kālākhyāyāṃ pravṛttāyāṃ prapte tretāyuge tadā । auṣadhīṣu ca jātāsu pravṛtte vṛṣṭisarjane ।।
pratiṣṭhitāyāṃ vārttāyāṃ gṛhaśramapareṣu ca । varṇāśramavyavasthānaṃ kṛtvā mantrāṃstu saṃhatān ।। mantrāṃstānyojayitvātha ihāmutra ca karmasu । tadā viśvabhugindraśca yajñaṃ prāvarttayatprabhuḥ ।।
daivataiḥ sahitaiḥ sarvaiḥ sarvasaṃbhārasaṃbhṛtaiḥ । tasyāśvamedhe vitate samājagmurmaharṣayaḥ ।। yajantaṃ paśubhirme dhyairūcuḥ sarve samāgatāḥ । karmavyagreṣu ṛtvikṣu saṃtate yajñakarmaṇi ।।
saṃpragītheṣu sarveṣu sāmageṣvatha susvagm । parikrānteṣu laghuṣu hyadhvaryuvṛṣabheṣu ca ।। ālabdheṣu ca medhyeṣu tathā paśugaṇeṣu ca । haviṣyagnau hūyamāne brāhmaṇaiścāgnihotribhiḥ ।।
āhūteṣu ca sarveṣu yajñabhākṣu kramāttadā । ya indriyātmakā devāstadā te yajñabhāginaḥ ।। tadyacante tadā devānkalpādiṣu bhavanti ye । adhvaryavaḥ praiṣakāle vyatthitā vai maharṣayaḥ ।।
maharṣayastu tāndṛṣṭvā dīnānpaśugaṇāṃstadā । prapacchuridraṃ saṃbhūya ko ayaṃ yajña vidhistava ।। adharmo balavāneṣa hiṃsādharmepsayā tataḥ । tataḥ paśuvadhaścaiṣa tava yajñe surottama ।।
adharmo dharmaghātāya prārabdhaḥ paśuhisayā । nāyaṃ dharmo hyadharmo ayaṃ na hiṃsā dharma ucyate ।। āgamena bhavānyajñaṃ karotu yadihecchati । vidhidṛṣṭena yajñena dharmeṇāvyapasetunā ।।
yajñabīcaiḥ sureśraṣṭha yeṣu hiṃsā na vidyate । trivarṣaṃ paramaṃ kālamuṣitairaprarohibhiḥ ।। eṣa dharmo mahāprājña virañcivihitaḥ purā । evaṃ viśvabhugindrastu ṛṣibhistattvadarśibhiḥ ।।
tadā vivādaḥ sumahānindrasyāsīnmaharṣibhiḥ । jaṅgamasthāvaraiḥ kairhi yaṣṭavyamiti cocyate ।। te tu khinnā vivādena tattvamuttvā maharṣayaḥ । sandhāya vākyamindreṇa papracchuḥ khecaraṃ vasum ।।
sahāprājña kathaṃ dṛṣṭastvayā yajñavidhirnṛpa । auttānapāde prabrūhi saṃśayaṃ no nuda prabho ।। śrutvā vākyaṃ vasusteṣāma vicārya balābalam । vedaśāstramanusmṛtya yajñatattvamuvāca ha ।।
yathopanīrtairyaṣṭavyamiti hovāca pārthivaḥ । yaṣṭavyaṃ paśubhirme dhyairatha bījaiḥ phalairapi ।। hiṃsāsvabhāvo yajñasya iti me darśanāgamau । yatheha devatā mantrā hiṃsāliṅgā maharṣibhiḥ ।।
dīrgheṇa tapasā yuktairdarśanaistārakādibhiḥ । tatprāmāṇyānmayā coktaṃ tasmātsa prāptumarhatha ।। yadi pramāṇaṃ tānyeva mantravākyāni vai dvijāḥ । tathā pravatatāṃ yajño hyanyathā vo anṛtaṃ vacaḥ ।।
evaṃ kṛtottarāste vai yuktātmānastapodhanāḥ । avaśyabhāvitaṃ dṛṣṭvā tamatho vāgyatābhavan ।। ityuktamātre nṛpatiḥ praviveśa rasātalam । ūrdhvacārī vasurbhūtvā rasātalacaro abhavat ।।
vasudhā talavāsī tu tena vākyena so abhavat । dharmāṇāṃ saṃśayacchettā rājā vasuradhogataḥ ।। tasmānna vācyamekena bahujñenāpi saṃśaye । bahudvārasya dharmasya sūkṣmā dūratarā gatiḥ ।।
tasmānna niścayādvaktuṃ dharmaḥ śakyastu kenacit । devānṛṣīnupādāya svāyaṃbhuvamṛte manum ।। tasmādahiṃsā dharmasya dvāramuktaṃ maharṣibhiḥ । ṛṣikoṭisahasrāṇi svatapobhirdivaṃ yayuḥ ।।
tasmānna dānaṃ yajñaṃ vā praśaṃsaṃti maharṣayaḥ । uñchamūlaphalaṃ śākamudapātraṃ tapodhanāḥ ।। etaddatvā vibhavataḥ svarge loke pratiṣṭhitāḥ । adrohaścāpya lobhaśca tapo bhutadayā damaḥ ।।
brahmacaryaṃ tathā satyamanukrośaḥ kṣamā dhṛtiḥ । sanātanasya dharmasya mūlametaddurāsadam ।। śrūyante hi tapaḥsiddhā brahmakṣatrādayo anaghāḥ । priyavratottānapādau dhruvo medhātithirvasuḥ ।।
sudhāmā virajāścaiva śaṅkhaḥ pāṇḍyaja eva ca । prājīnabarhiḥ parjanyo havirdhānādayo nṛpaḥ ।। ete cānye ca bahavaḥ svaistapobhirdivaṃ gatāḥ । rājarṣayo mahāsattvā yeṣāṃ kīrttiḥ pratiṣṭhitā ।।
tasmādviśiṣyate yajñāttapaḥ sarvaistu kāraṇaḥ । brahmaṇā tapasā sṛṣṭaṃ jagadviśvamidaṃ purā ।। tasmānnānveti tadyajñastapomūlamidaṃ smṛtam । dravyamantrātmako yajñastapastvanaśanātmakam ।।
yajñena devānāpnoti vairājaṃ tapasā punaḥ । brāhmaṃ tu karma saṃnyāsādvairāgyātprakṛterjayam ।। jñānātprāpnoti kaivalyaṃ pañcaitāgatayaḥ smṛtāḥ । evaṃ vivādaḥ sumahānya jñasyāsītpravarttane ।।
devatānāmṛṣīṇāṃ ca pūrva svāyaṃbhuve antare । tatastamṛṣayo dṛṣṭvā hataṃ dharmabalena tu ।। vasorvākyamanā dṛtya jagamuḥ sarve yathāgatam । gateṣu munisaṃgheṣu devā yajñaṃ samāpnuvan ।।
yajñapravarttanaṃ hyevamāsītsvāyaṃbhuve antare । tataḥ prabhṛti yajño ayaṃ yugaiḥ saha vivarttitaḥ ।। ata ūrddhaṃ pravakṣyāmi dvāparasya vidhiṃ punaḥ । tatra tretāyuge kṣīṇe dvāparaṃ pratipadyate ।।
dvāparādau prajānāṃ tu siddhistretāyuge tu yā । parivṛtte yuge tasmiṃstatastābhiḥ praṇaśyati ।। tataḥ pravarttate tāsāṃ prajānāṃ dvāpare punaḥ । saṃbhedaścaiva varṇānāṃ kāryāṇāṃ ca viparyayaḥ ।।
yajñāvadhāraṇaṃ daṇḍo mado daṃbhaḥ kṣamā balam । eṣā rajastamoyuktā pravṛttirdvāpare smṛtā ।। ādye kṛte yo dharmo asti sa tretāyāṃ pravarttate । dvāpare vyākulībhūtvā praṇaśyati kalau yuge ।।
varṇānāṃ viparidhvaṃsaḥ saṃkīyata tathāśramāḥ । dvaividhyaṃ pratipadyeteyuge tasmiñchruti smṛtī ।। dvaidhāttathā śrutismṛtyorniścayo nādhigamyate । aniścayādhigamanāddharmatattvaṃ na vidyate ।।
dharmāsattvena mitrāṇāṃ matibhedo bhavennṛṇām । parasparavibhinnaistaidṛṣṭīnāṃ vibhrameṇa ca ।। ayaṃ dharmo hyayaṃ neti niścayo nādhigamyate । kāraṇānāṃ ca vaikalpyātkāryāṇāṃ cāpyaniścayāt ।।
matibhedena teṣāṃ vai dṛṣṭīnāṃ vibhramo bhavet । tato dṛṣṭivibhannaistu kṛtaṃ śāstrākulaṃ tvidam ।। eko vedaścatuṣpāddhi tretāsviha vidhīyate । saṃkṣayādāyupaścaiva vyasyate dvāpareṣu ca ।।
ṛṣimantrātpunarbhedādbhidyate dṛṣṭivibhramaiḥ । mantrabrāhmaṇavinyāsaiḥ svaravarṇaviparyayaiḥ ।। saṃhitā ṛgyajuḥsāmnāṃ saṃpaṭhyante maharṣibhiḥ । sāmānyā vaikṛtāścaiva dṛṣṭibhinne kvacitkvacit ।।
brāhmaṇaṃ kalpasūtrāṇi mantrapravacanāni ca । anye api prasthitāstānvai kecittānpratyavasthitāḥ ।। dvāpareṣu pravarttante nivarttante kalau yuge । ekamādhvaryavaṃ tvāsītpunardvaidhamajāyata ।।
sāmānyaviparītārthaiḥ kṛtaśāstrākulaṃ tvidam । ādhvaryavasya prasthānairbahudhā vyākulīkṛtaiḥ ।। tathaivātharvaṛksāmnāṃ vikalpaiścāpi saṃjñayā । vyākuledvāpare nityaṃ kriyate bhinna darśanaiḥ ।।
teṣāṃ bhedāḥ pratībhedā vikalpāścāpi saṃkhyāyā । dvāpare saṃpravarttate vinaśyanti tataḥ kalau ।। teṣāṃ viparyayotpannā bhavanti dvāpare punaḥ । avṛṣṭirmaraṇaṃ caiva tathaiva vyādhyupadravāḥ ।।
vāṅmanaḥ karmarjeduḥkhairnirvedo jāyate punaḥ । nirvedājjāyate teṣāṃ duḥkhamokṣavicāraṇā ।। vicāraṇācca vairāgyaṃ vairāgyāddoṣadarśanam । doṣadarśanatascaiva dvāpare ajñānasaṃbhavaḥ ।।
teṣāma jñānināṃ pūrvamādye svāyaṃbhuve antare । utpadyante hi śāstrāṇāṃ dvāpare paripanthinaḥ ।। āyurvedavikalpaśca hyagānāṃ jyotiṣasya ca । arthaśāstravikalpāśca hetuśāstravikalpanam ।।
prakriyākalpasūtrāṇāṃ bhāṣyavidyāvikalpanam । smṛtiśāstraprabhedaśca prasthānāni pṛthakpṛthak ।। dvāpareṣvabhivarttante matibhedāśrayānnṛṇām । manasā karmaṇā vācā kṛcchrādvārtā prasiddhyati ।।
dvāpare sarvabhūtānāṃ kāyakleśapuraskṛtā । lobho vṛttirvaṇikpūrvā tattvānāmaviniścayaḥ ।। vedaśāstrapraṇayanaṃ dharmāṇāṃ saṃkarastathā । varṇāśramaparidhvaṃsaḥ kāmakrodhau tathaiva ca ।।
dvāpareṣu pravarttante rāgo lobho vadhastathā । vedaṃ vyāsaścaturddhā tu vyasyate dvāparādiṣu ।। niḥśeṣe dvāpare tasmiṃstasya saṃdhyā tu yādṛśī । pratiṣṭhate guṇairhīno dharmo asau dvāparasya tu ।।
tathaiva saṃdhyā pādena hyaṅgaḥ saṃdhyā itīṣyate । dvāparasyāvaśeṣeṇa tiṣyasya tu nibodhata ।। dvāparasyāśaseṣaṇa pratipattiḥ kalerapi । hiṃsāsūyānṛtaṃ māyā vadhaścaiva tapasvinām ।।
ete svabhāvāstiṣyasya sādhayanti ca vai prajāḥ । eṣa dharmaḥ kṛtaḥ kṛtsno dharmaśca parihīyate ।। manasā karmaṇā stutyā vārtā sidhyati vā na vā । kalau pramārakī rogaḥ satataṃ kṣudbhayāni ca ।।
anāvṛṣṭibhayaṃ ghoraṃ deśānāṃ ca viparyayaḥ । na pramāṇaṃ smṛterasti tiṣye lokeṣu vai yuge ।। garbhastho mriyate kaścidyauva nasthastathāparaḥ । sthavirāḥ ke api kaumāre mriyante vai kalau prajāḥ ।।
duriṣṭairduradhītaiśca duṣkṛtaiśca durāgamaiḥ । viprāṇāṃ karmadoṣaistaiḥ prajānāṃ jāyate bhayam ।। hiṃsā māyā tatherṣyā ca krodho asūyā kṣamā nṛṣu । tiṣye bhavanti jantūnāṃ rāgo lobhaśca sarvaśaḥ ।।
saṃkṣobho jāyate atyathai karimāsādya vai yugam । pūrṇe varṣasahasre vai paramāyustadā nṛṇām ।। nādhīyate tadā vedānna yajaṃ te dvijātayaḥ । utsīdanti narāścaiva kṣatriyāśca viśaḥ kramāt ।।
śūdrāṇāmantyayonestu saṃbandhā brāhmaṇaiḥ saha । bhavantīha kalau tasmiñchayanāsanabhojanaiḥ ।। rājānaḥ śūdrabhūyiṣṭhāḥ pākhaṇḍānāṃ pravarttakāḥ । guṇahīnāḥ prajāścaiva tadā vai saṃpravarttate ।।
āyurmedhā balaṃ rūpaṃ kulaṃ caiva praṇaśyati । śūdrāśca brāhmaṇācārāḥ śūdrācārāśca brāhmaṇāḥ ।। rājavṛttāḥ sthitāścorā ścorācārāśca pārthivāḥ । bhṛtyā ete hyasubhṛto yugānte samavasthite ।।
aśīlinyo anṛtāścaiva striyo madyāmiṣapriyāḥ । māyāvinyo bhaviṣyanti yugānte munisattama ।। ekapatnyo na śiṣyanti yugānte munisattama । śvāpadaprabalatvaṃ ca gavāṃ caiva hyupakṣayaḥ ।।
sādhūnāṃ vinivṛttiṃ ca vidyāstasminyugakṣaye । tadā dharmo mahodarke durlabho dānamūlavān ।। cāturāśramaśaithilyo dharmaḥ pravicariṣyati । tadā hyalpaphalā bhūmiḥ kvaciccāpi mahāphalā ।।
na rakṣitāro boktāro balibhāgasya pārthivāḥ । yugānte ca bhaviṣyanti svarakṣaṇaparāyaṇāḥ ।। arakṣitāro rājāno viprāḥ śūdropajīvinaḥ । śūdrābhivādinaḥ sarve yugānte dvijasattamāḥ ।।
adṛśūlā janapadāḥ śivaśūlā dvijāstathā । pramadāḥ keśaśūlāśca yugānte samupasthite ।। tapoyajñaphalānāṃ ca vikretāro dvijottamāḥ । yatayaśca bhaviṣyanti bahavo asminkalau yuge ।।
citravarṣī yadā devastadā prāhuryugakṣayam । sarve vāṇijakāścā pi bhaviṣyantyadhame yuge ।। bhūyiṣṭhaṃ kūṭamānaiśca paṇyaṃ vikrīṇate janāḥ । kuśīlacaryāpākhaṇḍairvyādharūpaiḥ samāvṛtam ।।
puruṣālpaṃ bahustrīkaṃ yugānte samupasthite । bāhuyācanako loko bhaviṣyati parasparam ।। avyākartā krūravākyā nārjavo nānasūyakaḥ । na kṛte pratikarttā ca yuge kṣīṇe bhaviṣyati ।।
aśaṅkā caiva patite yugānte tasya lakṣaṇam । tataḥ śūnya vasumatī bhaviṣyati vasundharā ।। goptāraścāpyagoptāraḥ prabhaviṣyanti śāsakāḥ । harttāraḥ pararatnānāṃ paradāravimarśakāḥ ।।
kāmātmāno durātmāno hyadhamāḥ sāhasapriyāḥ । pranaṣṭaceṣṭanā dhūrttā muktakeśāsttvaśūlinaḥ ।। ūnaṣoḍaśavarṣāśca prajā yante yugakṣaye । śukladantā jitākṣāśca muṇḍāḥ kāṣāyavāsasaḥ ।।
śūdrā dharmaṃ cariṣyati yugānte samupasthite । sasyacorā bhaviṣyanti tathā cailāpahāriṇaḥ ।। corāccorāśca harttāro harturharttā tathāparaḥ । jñānakarmamyuparate loke niṣkriyatāṃ gate ।।
kīṭamūṣakasarpāśca dharṣayiṣyanti mānavān । abhīkṣṇaṃ kṣemamārogyaṃ sāmarthyaṃ durlabhaṃ tathā ।। kauśikānprativatsyanti deśāḥ kṣudbhayapīḍitāḥ । duḥkhenābhiplutānāṃ ca paramāyuḥ śataṃ tadā ।।
dṛśyante ca na dṛśyante vedā kaliyuge akhilāḥ । tatsīdante tathā yajñāḥ kevalādharmapīḍitāḥ ।। kāṣāyiṇo atha nirgranthā tathā kāpālikāśca ha । vedavikrayimaścanye tīrthavikrayiṇo apare ।।
varṇāśramāṇāṃ ye cānye pākhaṇḍāḥ paripanthinaḥ । utpadyante tadā te vai saṃprāpte tu kalau yuge ।। adhīyate tadā vedāñchūdrā dharmārtha kovidāḥ । yajante cāśvamedhena rājānaḥ śūdrayonayaḥ ।।
strībālagovadhaṃ kṛtvā hatvānye ca parasparam । apahatya tathānyonyaṃ sādhayanti tadā prajāḥ ।। duḥkhapravacanālpāyurdehālpāyuśca rogataḥ । adharmābhiniveśitvāttamovṛttaṃ kalau smṛtam ।।
prajāsu bhrūṇahatyā ca tadā vairātpravarttate । tasmādāyurbalaṃ rūpaṃ kaliṃ prāpya prahīyate ।। tadā cālpena kālena siddhiṃ gacchanti mānavāḥ । dhanyā dharmaṃ cariṣyanti yugānte dvijasattamāḥ ।।
śrutismṛtyuditaṃ dharmaṃ ye carantyanasūyakāḥ । tretāyāmābdiko dharmo dvāpare māsikaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। yathāśakti caranprājñastadahnā prāpnuyātkalau । eṣā kaliyugāvasthā saṃdhyāṃśaṃ tu nibodhata ।।
yugeyuge tu hīyante tritripādāstu siddhayaḥ । yugasvabhāvātsaṃdhyāsu tiṣṭhantīha tu yādṛśaḥ ।। saṃdhyāsvabhāvāḥ svāṃśeṣu pādaśeṣāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ । evaṃ saṃdhyāṃśake kāle saṃprāpte tu yugāntike ।।
teṣāṃ śāstā hyasādhūnāṃ bhṛgūṇāṃ nidhanotthitaḥ । gotreṇa vai candra maso nāmnā pramatirucyate ।। mādhavasya tu soṃ'śena pūrvaṃ svāyaṃbhuve antare । samāḥ saviṃśatiḥ pūrṇāḥ paryaṭanvai vasuṃdharām ।।
anukarṣansa vai senāṃ savājirathakuñjarām । pragṛhītāyudhairvipraiḥ śataśo atha sahasraśaḥ ।। sa tadā taiḥ parivṛto mlecchānhanti smasarvaśaḥ । saha vā sarvaśaścaiva rājñastāñchūdrayonijān ।।
pāravaṇḍāstu tataḥ sarvān niḥ śeṣaṃ kṛtavānvibhuḥ । nātyartha dhārmikā ye ca tānsarvānhanti sarvaśaḥ ।। varṇavyatyāsajātāśca ye ca tānanujīvinaḥ । udīcyānmadhyadeśyāṃśca pavatīyāṃstathaiva ca ।।
prācyānpratīcyāṃśca tathā vindhyapṛṣṭhacarānapi । tathaiva dākṣiṇātyāṃśca draviḍānsiṃhalaiḥ saha ।। gāndhārānpāradāṃścaiva pahlavānyava nāñśakān । tuṣārānbarbarāṃścīnāñchūlikāndaradān khaśān ।।
laṃpākārānsakatakānkirātānāṃ ca jātayaḥ । pravṛttacakro balavānmlecchānāmantakṛtprabhuḥ ।। adṛṣṭaḥ sarvabhūtānāṃ cacārātha vasundharām । mādhavasya tu soṃ'śena devasyeha vijajñivān ।।
pūrvajanmani vikhyātaḥ pramatirnnāma vīryavān । gotrato vai candramasaḥ pūrve kaliyuge prabhuḥ ।। dvātriṃśe abhyudite varṣe prakrānto viṃśatīḥ samāḥ । vinighnansarvabhūtāni mānavāneva sarvaśaḥ ।।
kṛtvā bījāvaśeṣaṃ tu pṛthvyāṃ kūreṇa karmaṇā । paraspara nimittena kopenākasmikena tu ।। susādhayitvā vṛṣalānprāyaśastānadharmikān । gaṅgāyamunayormadhye niṣṭhāṃ prāptaḥ sahānugaḥ ।।
tato vyatīte kalpe tu sāmānye sahasainikaḥ । utsādya pārthivānsarvānmalecchāṃścaiva sahasraśaḥ ।। tatra saṃdhyāṃśake kāle saṃprāpte tu yugāntake । sthitāsvalpāvaśiṣṭāsu prajāsviha kvacitkvacit ।।
apagrahāstatastā vai lobhāviṣṭāstu vṛndaśaḥ । upahisaṃti cānyonyaṃ pothayantaḥ parasparam ।। arājake yugavaśātsaṃkṣaye samupasthite । prajāstā vai tataḥ sarvāḥ parasparabhayārdditāḥ ।।
vyākulāśca paribhrāntāstyaktvā dārāngṛhāṇi ca । svānpraṇānanapekṣanto niṣkāraṇasuduḥkhitāḥ ।। naṣṭe śraute smṛtau dharme parasparahatāstadā । nirmaryādā nirākrandā niḥsnehā nirapatrapāḥ ।।
naṣṭe dharme pratihatā hrasvakāḥ pañcaviṃśatim । hitvā putrāṃśca dārāṃśca viṣādavyākuledriyāḥ ।। anāvṛṣṭihatāścaiva vārttāmutsṛjya duḥkhitāḥ । pratyantāṃstā niṣevante hitvā janapadānsvakān ।।
saritaḥ sāgarānūpānsevante parvatāṃstathā । māṃsairmūlaphalaiścaiva vartayantaḥ suduḥkhitāḥ ।। cīrapatrācinadharā niṣkriyā niṣparigrahāḥ । varṇāśramaparibhraṣṭāḥ saṃkaraṃ ghoramāsthitāḥ ।
etāṃ kāṣṭhāmanuprāptā alpaśeṣāḥ prajāstataḥ ।। jarāvyādhikṣudhā viṣṭā duḥkhānnirvedamāgaman । vicāraṇā tu nirvedātsāmyāvasthā vicāraṇāt ।। sāmyāvasthātmako bodhaḥ saṃbodhāddharmaśīlatā ।
tāsūpaśamayuktāsu kaliśiṣṭāsu vai svayam ।। ahorātraṃ tadā tāsāṃ yugānte parivarttini । cittasaṃmohanaṃ kṛtvā tāsāṃ vai suptamattavat ।। bhāvinor'thasya ca balāttataḥ kṛtamavarttata ।
pravṛtte tu tatastasminpūte kṛtayuge tu vai ।। utpannāḥ kaliśiṣṭāsu prajāḥ kārtayugāstadā । tiṣṭhanti ceha ye siddhā adṛṣṭā vicaranti ca ।। saha saptarṣibhiścaiva tatra te ca vyavasthitāḥ ।
brahmakṣatraviśaḥ śūdrā bījārthaṃ ye smṛtā iha ।। kalijaiḥ saha te saṃti nirviśeṣāstadābhavan । teṣāṃ saptarṣayo dharmaṃ kathayantītareṣu ca ।। varṇāśramācārayuktaḥ śrautaḥ smārtto dvidhā tu saḥ ।
tatasteṣu kriyāvatsu vartante vai prajāḥ kṛte ।। śrautasmārtte kṛtānāṃ ca dharme saptarṣidarśite । keciddharmavyavasthārthaṃ tiṣṭhantīhāyugakṣayāt ।। manvantarādhikāreṣu tiṣṭhanti munayastu vai ।
yathā dāvapradagdheṣu tṛṇeṣviha tapena tu ।। vanānāṃ prathamaṃ vṛṣṭyā teṣāṃ mūleṣu saṃbhavaḥ । tathā kārtayugānāṃ tu kalijaṣviha saṃbhavaḥ ।। evaṃ yugo yugasyeha saṃtānastu parasparam ।
varttate hyavyavacchedādyāvanmanvantarakṣayaḥ ।। sukhamāyurbalaṃ rūpandharmor'thaḥ kāma eva ca । yugeṣvetāni hīyante tritripādāḥ krameṇa ca ।। sasaṃdhyāśeṣu hīyante yugānāndharmasiddhayaḥ ।
ityeṣa pratisaṃdhiryaḥ kīrttitastu mayā dvijāḥ ।। caturyugānāṃ sarveṣāmetenaiva prasādhanam । eṣā caturyugāvṛttirāsahasradguṇīkṛtā ।। brahmaṇastadahaḥ proktaṃ rātriścaitāvatī smṛtā ।
atrārjavaṃ jaḍībhāvo bhūtānāmāyugakṣayāt ।। etadeva tu sarveṣāṃ yugānāṃ lakṣaṇaṃ smṛtam । eṣā caturyugānāṃ ca guṇitā hyekasaptatiḥ ।। krameṇa parivṛttā tumanorantaramucyate ।
caturyuge yathaikasminbhavatīha yathā tu yat ।। tathā cānyeṣu bhavati punastadvadyathākramam । sarge sarge tathā bhedā utpadyante tathaiva tu ।। pañcatriṃśatparimitā na nyūnā nādhikāḥ smṛtāḥ ।
tathā kalpā yugaiḥ mārddhaṃ bhavanti saha lakṣaṇaiḥ । manvantarāṇāṃ sarveṣāmetadeva tu lakṣaṇam ।। yathā yugānāṃ parivarttanāni cirapravṛttāni yugasvabhāvāt । tathā na saṃtiṣṭhati jīvalokaḥ kṣayodayābhyāṃ parivarttamānaḥ ।।
ityeta llakṣaṇaṃ proktaṃ yugānāṃ vai samāsataḥ ।। atītānāgatānāṃ hi sarvamanvantaroṣviha । manvantareṇa caikena sarvāṇyevāntarāṇi vai ।। khyātānīha vijānīdhvaṃ kalpaṃ kalpena caiva ha ।
anāgateṣu tadvacca tarkaḥ kāryo vijānatā ।। manvantareṣu sarveṣu atītānāgateṣviha । tulyābhimāninaḥ sarve nāmarūpairbhavantyuta ।। devā hyaṣṭavidhā ye vā iha manvantareśvarāḥ ।
ṛṣayo manavaścaiva sarve tulyāḥ prayojanaiḥ ।। evaṃ varṇāśramāṇāṃ tu pravibhāgaṃ purā yuge । yugasvabhāvāṃśca tathā vidhatte vai sadā prabhuḥ ।। varṇāśramavibhāgāśca yugāni yugasiddhayaḥ ।
anuṣaṅgātsamākhyātāḥ sṛṣṭisargaṃ nibodhata । vistareṇānupūrvyā ca sthitiṃ vakṣye yugeṣviha ।। yugeṣu yāstu jāyante prajāstā me nibodhata । āsurī sarpagāndharvā paiśācī yakṣarākṣasī ।।
yasminyuge ca saṃbhūti stāsāṃ yāvacca jīvitam । piśācāsuragandharvāṃ yakṣarākṣasapannagāḥ ।। pariṇāhocchrayaistulyā jāyante ha kṛte yuge । ṣaṇṇavatyaṅgulo tsedho hyaṣṭānāṃ devajanmanām ।।
svenāṅgulapramāṇena niṣpannena ca pauṣṭikāt । etatsvābhāvikaṃ teṣāṃ pramāṇamiti kurvate ।। manuṣyā vartamānāstu yugaṃ saṃdhyāśakeṣviha । devāsurapramāṇaṃ tu saptasaptaṅgulādasat ।।
aṅgulānāṃ śataṃ pūrṇamaṣṭapañcāśaduttaram । devāsurapramāṇaṃ tu ucchrayātkalijaiḥ smṛtam ।। catvāraścāpyaśītiśca kalijairaṅgulaiḥ smṛtaḥ । svenāṅgulipramāṇena ūrddhvamāpādamastakāt ।।
ityeṣa mānuṣotsedho hrasatīha yugāṃśake । sarveṣu yugakāleṣu atītānāgateṣviha ।। svenāṅgulipramāṇena aṣṭatālaḥ smṛto naraḥ । āpādatalamastiṣko navatālo bhavettu yaḥ ।।
saṃhatā jānubāhustu sa surairapi pūjyate । gavāśvahastināṃ caiva mahiṣa syāvarātmanām ।। karmaṇaitena vijñeye hrāsavṛddhī yuge yuge । ṣaṭsaptatyaṅgulotsedhaḥ paśūnāṃ kakudastu vai ।।
aṅgulāṣṭaśataṃ pūrṇamutsedhaḥ kariṇāṃ smṛtaḥ । aṅgulānāṃ sahasraṃ tu catvāriṃśāṅgulairvinā ।। pañcāśatā yavānāṃ ca utsedhaḥ śākhināṃ smṛtaḥ । mānuṣasya śarīrasya sanniveśastu yādṛśaḥ ।।
tallakṣaṇastu devānāṃ dṛśyeta tattvadarśanāt । buddhyātiśayayuktaśca devānāṃ kāya ucyate ।। tathā sātiśayaschaiva mānuṣaḥ kāya ucyate । ityete vai parikrāntā bhāvā ye divyamānuṣāḥ ।।
paśūnāṃ pakṣiṇāṃ caiva sthāvarāṇāṃ ca sarvaśaḥ । gāvo hyajāvayo aśvāśca hastinaḥ pakṣiṇo nagāḥ ।। upayuktāḥ kriyāsvete yajñiyāsviha sarvaśaḥ । devasthāneṣu jāyante tadrūpā eva te punaḥ ।।
yathāśayopabhogāstu devānāṃ śubhamūrttayaḥ । teṣāṃ rūpānurūpaistu pramāṇaiḥ sthāṇujaṅgamaiḥ ।। manojñaistatra bhāvaiste sukhino hyupapedire । ataḥ śiṣṭānpravakṣyāmi sataḥ sādhūṃstathaiva ca ।।
saditi brahmaṇaḥ śabdastadvanto ye bhavantyuta । sājātyādbrahmaṇastvete tena santaḥ pracakṣate ।। daśātmake ye viṣaye kāraṇe cāṣṭalakṣaṇe । na krudhyanti na tdṛṣyanti jitātmānastu te smṛtāḥ ।।
sāmānyeṣu tu dharmeṣu tathā vaiśeṣikeṣu ca । brahmakṣatraviśo yasmādyuktāstasmā ddvijātayaḥ ।। varṇāśrameṣu yuktasya svargatau sukhacārimaḥ । śrautasmārtasya dharmasya jñānāddharmajña ucyate ।।
vidyāyāḥ sādhanātsādhurbrahmacārī gurorhitaḥ । gṛhāṇāṃ sādhanāccaiva gṛhasthaḥ sādhurucyate ।। sādhanāttapaso araṇye sādhurvaikhānasaḥ smṛtaḥ । yatamāno yatiḥ sādhuḥ smṛto yogasya sādhanāt ।।
evamāśramadharmāṇāṃ sādhanātsādhavaḥ smṛtāḥ । gṛhastho brahmacārī ca vānaprastho yatistathā ।। atha devā na pitaro munayo na ca mānuṣāḥ । ayaṃ dharmo hyayaṃ neti vindate bhinnadarśanāḥ ।।
dharmādharmāvihaproktau śabdāvetau kriyātmakau । kuśalākuśalaṃ karma dharmādharmāviha smṛtām ।। dhāraṇartho dhṛtiścaiva dhātuḥ śabde prakīrttitaḥ । adhāraṇāmahattve ca adharma iti cocyate ।।
atheṣṭaprāpako dharma ācāryairupadiśyate । adharmaścāniṣṭaphalohyācāryairupadiśyate ।। vṛddhāścālolupāścaiva tvātmavanto hyadāṃbhikāḥ । samyagvinītā ṛjavastānācāryānprajakṣate ।।
svayamācarate yasmādācāraṃ sthāpayatyapi । ācinoti ca śāstrāṇi ācāryastena cocyate ।। dharmajñairvihito dharmaḥ śrautaḥ smārtto dvidhā dvijaiḥ । dārāgnihotrasambandhāddvidhā śrautasya lakṣaṇam ।।
smārtto varṇāśramācārairyamaiḥ saniyamaiḥ smṛtaḥ । pūrvebhyo vedayitveha śrautaṃ saptarṣa yo abruvan ।। ṛco yajūṃsāmāni brahmaṇo aṅgāni ca śrutiḥ । manvantarasyātītasya smṛtvācārānmanurjagau ।।
tasmā tsmārttaḥ dharmo varṇāśramavibhājakaḥ । sa eṣa vividho dharmaḥ śiṣṭācāra ihocyate ।। śeṣaśabdaḥ śiṣṭa iti śeṣaṃ śiṣṭaṃ pracakṣate । manvantareṣu ye śiṣṭā iha tiṣṭhanti dhārmikāḥ ।।
manuḥ saptarṣayaścaiva lokasaṃtānakāramāt । dharmārthaṃ ye ca tiṣṭhanti tāñchiṣṭānvai pracakṣate ।। manvādayaśca ye aśiṣṭā ye mayā prāgudīritāḥ । taiḥ śiṣṭaiścarito dharmaḥ samyageva yuge yuge ।।
trayī vārttā daṇḍanītirijyā varṇāśramāstathā । śiṣṭairācaryate yasmānmanunā ca punaḥ punaḥ ।। pūrvaiḥ pūrvagatatvācca śiṣṭācāraḥ sa sātvataḥ । dānaṃ satyaṃ tapo jñānaṃ vidyejyā vrajanaṃ dayā ।।
aṣṭau tāni caritrāṇi śiṣṭācārasya lakṣaṇam । śiṣṭā yasmāccarantyenaṃ manuḥ saptarṣayastu vai ।। manvantareṣu sarveṣu śiṣṭācārastataḥ smṛtaḥ । vijñeyaḥ śravaṇācchrautaḥ smaraṇātsmārtta ucyate ।।
ijyāvedātmakaḥ śrautaḥ smārtto varṇāśramātmakaḥ । pratyaṅgāni ca vakṣyāmi dharmasyeha tu lakṣaṇam ।। dṛṣṭvā tu bhūtamarthaṃ yaḥ pṛṣṭo vai na nigū hati । yathā bhūtapravādastu ityetatsatyalakṣaṇam ।।
brahmacaryaṃ japo maunaṃ nirāhāratvameva ca । ityetattapaso rūpaṃ sughoraṃ sudurā sadam ।। paśūnāṃ dravyahaviṣāmṛksāmayajuṣāṃ tathā । ṛtvijāṃ dakṣiṇānāṃ ca saṃyogo yajña ucyate ।।
ātmavatsarvabhūteṣu yā hitāyāhitāya ca । pravarttante samā dṛṣṭiḥ kṛtsnāpyeṣā dayā smṛtā ।। ākruṣṭo nihato vāpi nākrośedyo na hanti ca । vāṅmanaḥkarmabhirvetti titikṣaiṣā kṣamā smṛtā ।।
svāminā rakṣyamāṇānāmutsṛṣṭānāṃ ca saṃbhrame । parasvānāmanādānamalobha iti kīrtyate ।। maithunasyāsamācāro na cintā nānujalpanam । nivṛttirbrahmacaryaṃ tadacchidraṃ tapa ucyate ।।
ātmārthaṃ vā parārthaṃ vā cendriyāṇīha yasya vai । mithyā na saṃpravarttante śāmasyaitattu lakṣamam ।। daśātmake yo viṣaye kāraṇe cāṣṭalakṣaṇe । na kruddhyeta pratihataḥ sa jitātmā vibhāvyate ।।
yadyadiṣṭatamaṃ dravyaṃ nyāyenaivāgataṃ ca yat । tattadguṇavate deyamityetaddānalakṣaṇam ।। dānaṃ trividhamityetatkaniṣṭhajyeṣṭhamadhyamam । tatra naiśreyasaṃ jyeṣṭhaṃ kaniṣṭhaṃ svārthasiddhaye ।।
kāruṇyātsarvabhūteṣu saṃvibhāgastu madhyamaḥ । śrutismṛtibhyāṃ vihito dharmo varmāśramātmakaḥ ।। śiṣṭācārāviruddhaśca dharmaḥ satsādhusaṃmataḥ । apradveṣohyani ṣṭeṣu tatheṣṭasyābhinandanam ।।
prītitāpaviṣādebhyo vinivṛttirviraktatā । saṃnyāsaḥ karmaṇāṃ nyāsaḥ kṛtānāmakṛtaiḥ saha ।। kuśalākuśalānāṃ tu prahāṇaṃ nyāsa ucyate । vyaktā ye viśeṣāste vikāre asminnacetane ।।
cetanācetanānyatvavijñānaṃ jñānamucyate । pratyaṅgānāṃ tu dharmasya tvityetallakṣaṇaṃ smṛtam ।। ṛṣibhirdharmatattvajñaiḥ pūrvaṃ svāyaṃbhuve antare । atra vo varṇayiṣyāmi vidhiṃ manvantarasya yaḥ ।।
tathaiva cāturhetrasya cāturvidyasya caiva hi । pratimanvantare caiva śrutiranyā vidhīyate ।। ṛco yajūṃṣi samāni yathā ca pratidaivatam । ābhūtasaṃplavasyāpi varjyaikaṃ śatarudriyam ।।
vidhirhaitrastathā stotraṃ pūrvavatsaṃpravartate । dravyastotraṃ guṇastotraṃ phalastotraṃ tathaiva ca ।। caturthamābhijanakaṃ stotrametaccaturvidham । manvantareṣu sarveṣu yathā devā bhavanti ye ।।
pravartayati teṣāṃ vai brahmā stotraṃ caturvidham । evaṃ mantragaṇānāṃ tu samutpattiścaturvidhā ।। atharvagaryajuṣāṃ sāmnāṃ vedeṣviha pṛthakpṛthak । ṛṣīṇāṃ tapyatāmugraṃ tapaḥ paramaduṣkaram ।।
mantrāḥ prādurbabhūvurhi pūrvamanvantareṣviha । asaṃtoṣādbhayā dduḥkhātsukhācchokācca pañcadhā ।। ṛṣīṇāṃ tārakākhyena darśanena yadṛcchayā । ṛṣīṇāṃ yadṛṣitvaṃ hi tadvakṣyāmīha lakṣaṇaiḥ ।।
atītānāgatānāṃ ca pañcadhā tvṛṣirucyate । atastvṛṣīṇāṃ vakṣyāmi tatra hyārṣasamudbhavam ।। guṇasāmye varttamāne sarvasaṃpralaye tadā । avibhāge tu vedānāmanirdeśye tamomaye ।।
abuddhibūrvakaṃ tadvai cetanārthe pravarttate । cetanābuddhipūrvaṃ tu cetanena pravarttate ।। pravarttate tathā dvau tu yathā matsyodake ubhe । cetanādhiṣṭhitaṃ sattvaṃ pravarttati guṇātmakam ।।
kāraṇatvāttathā kāryaṃ tadā tasya pravarttate । viṣayo viṣayitvācca arther'thatvāttathaiva ca ।। kālena prāpaṇīyena bhedāstu karaṇātmakāḥ । saṃsidhyanti tadā vyaktāḥ krameṇa mahadādayaḥ ।।
mahataścāpyahaṅkārastasmādbhūtedriyāṇi ca । bhūtabhedāśca bhūtebhyo jajñire sma parasparam ।। saṃsiddhakāryakaraṇaḥ sadya eva vyavarttata । yatholmukāttu truṭayaḥ ekakālādbhavanti hi ।।
tathā vivṛttāḥ kṣetrajñāḥ kālenaikena kāraṇāt । yathāndhakāre khadyotaḥ sahasā saṃpradṛśyate ।। tathā vivṛtto hyavyaktātkhadyota iva sañjvalan । sa māhansaśarīrastu yatraivāyamavarttata ।।
tatraiva saṃsthito vidvāndvāraśālāmukhe vibhuḥ । mahāṃstu tamasaḥ pāre vailakṣaṇyādvibhāvyate ।। tatraiva saṃsthite vidvāṃstamasoṃ'ta iti śrutiḥ । buddhirvivarttamānasya prādurbhūtā caturvidhā ।।
jñānaṃ vairāgyamaiśvaryaṃ dharmaśceti catuṣṭayam । sāṃsiddhikānyathaitāni vijñeyāni narasya vai ।। sa mahātmā śarīrasya vaivarttātsiddhirucyate । anuśete yataḥ sarvānkṣetrajñānamathāpi vā ।।
puriṣatvācca puruṣaḥ kṣatrejñānātsa ucyate । yasmādvuddhyānuśete ca tasmādvodhātmakaḥ sa vai ।। saṃsiddhaye parigataṃ vyaktāvyaktamacetanam । evaṃ vivṛttaḥ kṣetrajñaḥ kṣetrajñānābhisaṃhitaḥ ।।
vivṛttisamakālaṃ tu buddhyāvyaktamṛṣiḥ svayam । paraṃ hyarṣayate yasmātparamarṣitvamasya tat ।। gatyarthādṛṣaterdhātornāma nirvṛtirāditaḥ । yasmādeva svayaṃ bhūtastasmāccāpyṛṣitā smṛtā ।।
īśvarātsvayamudbhūtā mānasā brahmaṇaḥ sutāḥ । yasmādutpadyamānaistairmahānparigataḥ paraḥ ।। yasmāda-ṣanti te dhīrā mahāntaṃ sarvato guṇaiḥ । tasmānmaharṣayaḥ proktā buddheḥ parama darśinā ।।
īśvarāṇāṃ sutāsteṣāṃ mānasā aurasāśca vai । ahaṅkāraṃ tapaścaiva ṛṣanti ṛṣitāṃ gatāḥ ।। tasmātsaptarṣayaste vai bhūtādau tattvadarśanāt । ṛṣiputrā ṛṣīkāstu maithunādgarbhasaṃbhavāḥ ।।
tanmātrāṇi ca satyaṃ ca ṛṣante te mahaujasaḥ । saptaṣaryasta taste ca parasatyasya darśanāḥ ।। ṛṣīkāṇāṃ sutāste syurvijñeyā ṛṣiputrakāḥ । ṛṣanti te ṛtaṃ yasmādviśeṣāṃścaiva tattvataḥ ।।
tasmātsaptarṣayastepi śruteḥ paramadarśanāt । avyaktātmā mahānātmāhaṅkārātmā tathaiva ca ।। bhūtātmā cendriyātmā ca teṣāṃ tajjñānamucyate । ityetā ṛṣijātīstā nāmabhiḥ pañca vai śṛṇu ।।
bhṛgurmarīciratriśca hyaṅgirāḥ pulahaḥ kratuḥ । manurdakṣo vasiṣṭaśca pulastyaśceti te daśa ।। brahmaṇo mānasā hyete udbhūtāḥ svayamīśvarāḥ । paratvenarṣayo yasmātsmṛtāstasmānmaharṣayaḥ ।।
īśvarāṇāṃ sutā hyete ṛṣayastānnibodhata । kāvyo bṛhaspatiścaiva kaśyapaśvyavanastathā ।। utathyo vāmadevaśca apā syaścośijastathā । kardamo viśravāḥ śaktirvālakhilyāstathārvataḥ ।।
ityete ṛṣayaḥ proktāstapasā carṣitāṃ gatāḥ । ṛṣiputrānṛ ṣīkāṃstu garbhotpannānnibodhata ।। vatsaro nagṛhūścaiva bharadvājastathaiva ca । ṛṣidīrghatamāścaiva bṛhadukthaḥ śaradvataḥ ।।
vājaśravāḥ śuciścaiva vaśyāśvaśca parāśaraḥ । dadhīcaḥ śaṃśapāścaiva rājā vaiśravaṇastathā ।। ityete ṛṣikāḥ proktāste satyādṛṣitāṃ gatāḥ । īśvarā ṛṣayaścaiva ṛṣikāścaiva te smṛtāḥ ।।
ete mantrakṛtaḥ sarve kṛtsnaśastānnibodhata । bhṛguḥ kāvyaḥ pracetāśca ṛcīko hyātmavānapi ।। aurvātha jamadagniśca vidaḥ sārasvatastathā । ārṣṭiṣeṇo yudhājicca vītahavyasuvarcasau ।।
vainyaḥ pṛthurdivodāso bādhyaśvo gṛtsaśaunakau । ekonaviśatirhyetebhṛgavo mantravāditaḥ ।। aṅgirā vaidyagaścaiva bharadvājo atha bāṣkaliḥ । ṛtavākastathā gargaḥ śiniḥ saṃkṛtireva ca ।।
purukutsaśca māndhātā hyaṃbarīṣastathaiva ca । yuvanāśvaḥ paurakutsastrasaddasyuśca dasyumān ।। āhāryo hyajamīḍhaśca tukṣayaḥ kapireva ca । vṛṣādarbho virūpāśvaḥ kaṇvaścaivātha mudgalaḥ ।।
utathyaśca sanadvājastathā vājaśravā api । ayāsyaścakravarttī cavāmadevastathaiva ca ।। asijo bṛhadukthaśca ṛṣirdīrghatamāstathā । kakṣīvāṃśca trayastriṃśatsmṛtā hyāṅgirasā varāḥ ।।
ete mantrakṛtaḥ sarve kāśyapāṃstu nibodhata । kāśyapaścaiva vatsāro naidhruvo raibhya eva ca ।। asito deva laścaiva ṣaḍete brahmavādinaḥ । atrirarvasanaścaiva śyāvāśvaśca gaviṣṭhiraḥ ।।
āvihotra ṛṣirddhīmāṃstathā pūrvātithiśca saḥ । ityete cā trayaḥ proktā mantrakārā maharṣayaḥ ।। vasiṣṭhaścaiva śaktiśca tathaiva ca parāśaraḥ । caturtha indrapramatiḥ pañcamaśca bharadvasuḥ ।।
ṣaṣṭhaśca maitrāvaruṇiḥ kuṇḍinaḥ saptamastathā । iti sapta vaśiṣṭhāśca vijñeyā brahmavādinaḥ ।। viśvāmitrastu gādheyo devarātastathodgalaḥ । tathā vidvānmadhucchandā ṛṣiścānyo aghamarṣaṇaḥ ।।
aṣṭako lohitaścaiva kataḥ kolaśca tāvubhau । devaśravāstathā reṇuḥ pūraṇo atha dhanañjayaḥ ।। trayodaśaite dharmiṣṭhā vijñeyāḥ kuśikāvarāḥ । agastyo ayo dṛḍhāyuśca vidhmavāhastathaiva ca ।।
brahmiṣṭhāgastapā hyete trayaḥ paramakīrttayaḥ । manurvaivasvataścaiva elo rājā purūkhāḥ ।। kṣatrriyāṇāṃ carāvetau vijñeyau mantravādinau । bhalandanaśca vatsaśca saṃkīlaścaiva te trayaḥ ।।
ete mantrakṛtaścaiva vaiśyānāṃ pravarāḥ smṛtāḥ । ityeṣā navatiḥ proktā mantrā yairṛṣibhiḥ kṛtāḥ । brāhyaṇāḥ kṣatriyā vaiśyā ṛṣiputrānnibodhata ।। ṛṣikāṇāṃ sutāścāpi vijñeyā ṛṣiputrakāḥ ।
brāhyaṇānāṃ pravaktāro nāmataśca nibodhata ।। sapradhānāḥ pravakṣyante samāsācca śrutarṣayaḥ । bahvṛco bhārgavaḥ pailaḥ sāṃkṛtyo jājalistathā ।। saṃdhyāstirmāṭharaścaiva yājñavalkyaḥ parāśaraḥ ।
upamanyurindrapramatirmāḍūkiḥ śākaliśca saḥ ।। bāṣkaliḥ śokapāṇiśca nailaḥ pailo alakastathā । pannagāḥ pakṣagantāśca ṣaḍaśītiḥ śrutarṣayaḥ ।। ete dvijātayo mukhyā bahvṛcānāṃ śrutarṣayaḥ ।
vaiśaṃpāyanalauhityau kaṇṭhakālāvaśāvadhaḥ ।। śyāmāpatiḥ palāḍuśca ālaṃbiḥ kamalāpatiḥ । teṣāṃ śiṣyāḥ praśiṣyāśca ṣaḍaśīti śrutarṣayaḥ ।। ete dvijarṣayaḥ proktāścarakādhvaryavo dvijāḥ ।
caiminiḥ sabharadvājaḥ kāvyaḥ pauṣyañjireva ca ।। hiraṇyanābhaḥ kauśilyo laugākṣiḥ kusumistathā । laṅgalī śālihotraśca śaktirājaśca bhārgavaḥ ।। sāmagānāmathācārya ailo rājā purūravāḥ ।
ṣaṭcatvāriṃśadanye vai teṣāṃ śiṣyāḥ śrutarṣayaḥ ।। kauśītiḥ kaṅkamudgaśca kuṇḍakaḥ saparāśaraḥ । lobhālobhaśca dharmātmā tathā brahma balaśca saḥ ।। kranthalo atho madagalo mārkaṇḍeyo atha dharmavit ।
ityete navatirjñeyā hotravadbrahmacāriṇaḥ ।। carakādhvaryavaścāpi hyanumaṃntraṃ tu brāhmaṇam । calūbhiḥ sumatiścaiva tathā devavaraśca yaḥ ।। anukṛṣṇastathāyuśca anubhūmistathaiva ca ।
tathāprītaḥ kṛśāśvaśva sumūlirbāṣkalistathā ।। carakādhvaryakādhvaryunamasyurbrahmacāriṇaḥ । vaiyāsakiḥ śuko vidvāṃllaukirbhūriśravāstathā ।। somāviratunāntakyastathā dhaumyaśca kāśyapaḥ ।
āraṇyā ilakaścaiva upamanyurvidastathā ।। bhārgavo madhukaḥ piṅgaḥ śveta ketustathaiva ca । prajādarpaḥ kahoḍaśca yājñavalkyo atha śaunakaḥ ।। anaṅgo niratālaśca madhyamādhvaryavastute ।
aditirdevamātā ca jalāpā caiva mānavī ।। urvaśī viśvayoṣā ca hyapsaraḥpravare śubhe । mudgalā cātujīvaiva tārā caiva yaśasvinī ।। prātimedhī ca mārgā ca sujātā ca mahātapā ।
lopāmudrā ca dharmajñā yā ca kośītikā smṛtā ।। etāśca brahmavādinya apsaro rūpaṃsamatāḥ । ityetā mukhyaśaḥ proktā mayā ca ṛṣiputrakāḥ ।। vaidaśākhāpraṇayanāstataste ṛṣayaḥ smṛtāḥ ।
īśvarā mantravaktāra ṛṣayo hyṛṣikāstathā ।। ṛṣiputrāḥ pravaktaraḥ kalpānāṃ brāhmaṇasya tu । īśvarāṇāmṛṣīṇāṃ ca ṛṣikāṇāṃ sahātmajaiḥ ।। tathā vākyāni janīṣva yathaiṣāṃ mantradṛṣṭayaḥ ।
tatrājñāyuktamadvaitaṃ dīptaṃ gaṃbhīraśabdavat ।। atyantamaparokṣaṃ ca liṅgaṃ nāma tathaiva ca । sarvabhūtānyabhūtaṃ ca paridānaṃ ca yadbhavet ।। kvacinniruktaproktārthaṃ vākyaṃ svāyaṃbhuvaṃ viduḥ ।
yatkiñcinmantrasaṃyuktaṃ tatra nāmavibhaktibhiḥ ।। pratyakṣābhihitaṃ caivamṛṣīṇāṃ vacanaṃ matam । naigamairvividhaiḥ śabdairnipātairbahulaṃ ca yat ।। yaccāpyasti mahadvākyamṛṣīkāṇāṃ vacaḥ smṛtam ।
avispaṣṭapadaṃ yacca yacca syādbahusaṃśayam ।। ṛṣiputravacastadvai sarvāśca paridevatāḥ । hetudṛṣṭānta bahulaṃ citraśabdamapārthakam ।। sarvāstu tamaśaktaṃ ca vākyametattu mānuṣam ।
miśrā iti samākhyātāḥ prabhāvādṛṣitāṃ gātāḥ ।। samutkarṣāya karṣābhyāṃ jātivyatyāsasaṃbhavāḥ । bhūtabhavyabhavajjñāna janmaduḥkhacikitsanam ।। miśrāṇāṃ tadbhavedvākyaṃ gurorbalapravarttanam ।
dharmaśāstrapraṇetāro mahimnā sarvagāśca vai ।। tapaḥprakarṣaḥ sumahānyeṣāṃ te ṛṣayaḥ smṛtāḥ । bṛhaspatiśca śukraśca vyāsaḥ sārasvatastathā ।। vyāsāḥ śāstrapraṇayanā vedavyāsa iti smṛtāḥ ।
yasmādavārajāḥ saṃtaḥ pūrvebhyo medhayādhikāḥ ।। aiśvaryeṇa ca saṃpannāstataste ṛṣayaḥ smṛtāḥ । yasminkālo na caṃ vayaḥ pramāṇamṛṣibhāvane ।। dṛśyate hi pumānkaścitkaścijjyeṣṭhatamo dhiyā ।
yasmādbuddhyā ca varṣīyānbalo api śrutavānṛṣiḥ ।। yaḥ kaścitpādavānmadhye prayukto akṣara saṃpadā । viniyuktāvasānāṃ tu tāmṛcaṃ paricakṣate ।। yaḥ kaścitkaraṇairmantro na ca pādakṣarairmitaḥ ।
atiyuktāvasānaṃ ca tadyajurvai pracakṣate ।। hrīṅkāraḥ praṇavo gītaḥ prastāvaśca caturthakam । pañcamaḥ pratihotraśca ṣaṣṭhamāhurupadravam ।। nidhanaṃ saptamaṃ sāmnaḥ saptavindhya midaṃ smṛtam ।
pañcavindhya iti proktaṃ hrīṅkāraḥ praṇavādṛte ।। brahmaṇe dharmamatyuktau yattadā jñāpyater'thataḥ । āśāstistu prasaṃkhyātā vilāpaḥ paridevanā ।। krodhādvā dveṣaṇāccaiva praśrākhyānaṃ tathaiva ca ।
etattu sarvavidyānāṃ vihitaṃ mantralakṣaṇam ।। mantrā navavidhāḥ proktā ṛgyajuḥ sāmalakṣaṇāḥ । mūrtirnindā praśaṃsā cākrośastoṣastathaiva ca ।। praśrānujñāstathākhyānamāśāsmatividhayo matāḥ ।
mantrabhedāṃśca vakṣyāmi caturviśatilakṣaṇān ।। praśaṃsā stutirākrośo nindā ca paridevanā । abhiśāpo viśāpaśca praśnaḥ prativacastathā ।। āśīryajñastathākṣepa arthākhyānaṃ ca saṃkathā ।
viyogā hyabhiyogāśca kathā saṃsthā varaśca vai ।। pratiṣedhopa deśau ca namaskāraḥ spṛhā tathā । vilāpaśceti mantrāṇāṃ caturviṃśatiruddhṛtāḥ ।। ṛṣibhiryajñatattvajñairvihitaṃ brahmaṇaṃ purā ।
hetu rnirvacanaṃ nindā praśastiḥ saṃśayo nidhiḥ ।। purākṛtipurākalpau vyavadhāraṇakalpanā । upamā ca daśaite vai vidhayo brāhmaṇasya tu ।। lakṣaṇaṃ brāhmaṇasyainadvihitaṃ sarvaśākhināma ।
heturhanteḥ smṛto dhātoryannihantyuditaṃ paraiḥ ।। athavārthe pariprāpte hino tergatikarmaṇā । tathā nirvacanaṃ brūyādvākyārthasyāvadhāraṇam ।। nindāṃ tāmāhurāyāryā yaddoṣe nindanaṃ vacaḥ ।
prapūrvācchaṃsaterdhātoḥ praśaṃsāguṇavattayā ।। idaṃ tvidamidaṃ naidamityaniścitya saṃśayam । idamevaṃ vidhātavyamityayaṃ vidhirucyate ।। anyasyānyasya cauktiryā budhaiḥ soktā purākṛtiḥ ।
yo hyatyantaparokṣārthaḥ sa purākalpa ucyate ।। purātikrāntavācitvātpurākalpasya kalpa nām । mantrabrāhmaṇakalpaiśca nigamaiḥ śuddhavistaraiḥ ।। aniścitya kṛtāmāhurvyavadhāraṇakalpanām ।
yathā hīdaṃ tathā tadvai idaṃ caiva tathaiva tat ।। ityevameṣā hyupamā daśamo brāhmaṇasya tu । ityetadbrahmaṇasyādau vihitaṃ rakṣaṇaṃ budhaiḥ ।। tasya tadvidbhiruddiṣṭā vyākhyāmyanupadaṃ dvijaiḥ ।
mantrāṇāṃ kalpanā caiva vidhidṛṣṭiṣu karmasu ।। mantro mantrayaterddhātorbrāhmaṇo brāhmaṇena tu । alpākṣaramasaṃdigdhaṃ sāravadviśvatomukham । astobhamanavadyaṃ ca sūtraṃ sūtravido viduḥ ।।
ṛṣayastadvacaḥ śrutvā sūtamāhustaduttaram । kathaṃ vedāḥ punarvyastāstanno brūhi mahāmate ।। dvāpare tu purāvṛtte manoḥ svāyaṃbhuvāntare । brahmā manumuvācedaṃ rakṣavedaṃ mahāmate ।।
parivṛttaṃ yugaṃ tāta svalpavīryā dvijātayaḥ । saṃvṛtā yugadoṣeṇa sarve caiva yathākramam ।। tasya mānaṃ yugavaśādalpaṃ caiva hi dṛśyate । daśasāhasrabhāgena hyavaśiṣṭaṃ kṛtoditam ।।
vāya tejo balaṃ cālpaṃ sarvaṃ caiva praṇaśyati । vedakriyā hi kāryāḥ syurmābhūdvedavināśanam ।। vede nāśamanuprāpte yajño nāśaṃ gamiṣyati । yajñe naṣṭe vedanāśastataḥ sarvaṃ praṇaśyati ।।
ādyo vedaśca tuṣpādaḥ śatasāhasrasaṃmitaḥ । punardaśaguṇaḥ kṛṣṇo yajño vai sarvakāmadhuk ।। evamuktastathetyuktvā manurlaukahite rataḥ । vedamekaṃ catuṣpādaṃ caturddhā vyabhajatprabhuḥ ।।
brahmaṇo vacanāttāta lokānāṃ hitakāmyayā । tadahaṃ varttamānena yuṣmākaṃ vedakalpanam ।। manvantareṇa vakṣyami vyatītānāṃ prakalpanam । pratyakṣeṇa varokṣaṃvai tannibodhata sattamāḥ ।।
asminyuge tadā vyāsaḥ pārāśaryaḥ parantapaḥ । dvaipāyana iti khyāto viṣṇoraṃśaḥ sanātanaḥ ।। brahmaṇā coditaḥ so asmin vedaṃ vaktuṃ pracakrame । atha śiṣyānsajagrāha caturo vedakāraṇāt ।।
jaiminiṃ ca sumantuṃ ca vaiśaṃpāyanameva ca । caturthaṃ pailameteṣāṃ pañcamaṃ lomaharṣaṇam ।। ṛgvedaśrāvakaṃ pailamagrahīdvidhivaddvijāḥ । yajurvedapravaktāraṃ vaiśaṃpāyanameva ca ।।
jaiminiṃ sāmavedārthaśrāvakaṃ so anvapadyata । tathaivāthar vavedasya sumantumṛṣisattamam ।। itihāsapurāṇasya kalapavākyasya caiva hi । māṃ caiva pratijagrāha bhagavānīśvaraḥ prabhuḥ ।।
eka āsīdyajurvedastaṃ caturddhā vyakalpayat । cāturhetramabhūttasmiṃstena yajñamakalpayat ।। ādhvaryavaṃ yajurbhistu ṛgbhirhetraṃ tathaiva ca । audgātraṃ sāmabhiścakre brahmatvaṃ cāpyatharvabhiḥ ।।
tataḥ sa ṛca uddhṛtya ṛgvedaṃ samakalpayat । hotṛkaṃ kalpayattena yajurvedaṃ jagatpatiḥ ।। sāmabhiḥ sāmavedaṃ ca tenaudgātramakalpayat । rātvatharvavedena sarvakarmāṇyakārayat ।।
ākhyānaiścāpyupākhyānairgāthābhiḥ kalpajoktibhiḥ । purāmasaṃhitāṃ cakre purāṇārthaviśāradaḥ ।। yacchiṣṭaṃ tu yajurvede tena yaayuñjata । yajanātsa yajurveda iti śāstraviniścayaḥ ।।
pādānāmuddhatatvācca yajūṃṣi viṣamāṇi ca । śatenoddhatavīryastu ṛtvigbhirvedapāragaiḥ ।। prayujyate hyaśvamedhastena vā puṣyate tu saḥ । ṛco gṛhītvā pailastu vyabhajattu dvidhā punaḥ ।।
dve kṛtvā saṃhite caiva śiṣyābhyā madadādvibuḥ । indrapramattaye caikāṃ dvitīyāṃ bāṣkalāya ca ।। catasraḥ saṃhitāḥ kṛtvā bāṣkalo dvijasattamaḥ । śiṣyānadhyāpayā māsa śuśruṣābhiratānhitān ।।
bodhyāṃ tu prathamāṃ śākhāṃ dvitīyāmagnimātaram । pārāśarīṃ tṛtīyāṃ tu yāalkyāmathāparām ।। indrapramatirekāṃ tu saṃhitāmṛṣisattamaḥ । adhyāpayanmahābhāgaṃ māṇḍūkeyaṃ yaśasvinam ।।
styasravasamagryaṃ tu putraṃ sa tu mahāyaśāḥ । satyasravāḥ satyahitaṃ putramadhyāpayadvibhuḥ ।। so api satyahitaḥ putraṃ punaradhyāpayaddvijāḥ । satyaśriyaṃ mahātmānaṃ satya dharmaparāyaṇam ।।
abhavaṃstasya śiṣyā vai trayastu sumahaujasaḥ । satyaśriyāśca vidvāṃsaḥ śāstragrahaṇatatparāḥ ।। śākalyaḥ prathamasteṣāṃ tasmādanyo rathītaraḥ । bāṣkaliśca bharadvāja iti śākhāpravarttakāḥ ।।
devamitrastu śākalyo jñānāhaṅkāragarvitaḥ । janakasya sa yajñe vai vināśāmagamaddvijāḥ ।। kathaṃ vināśamagamatsa munirjñānagarvitaḥ । janakasyāśvamedhe tu katha vādābhyajāyata ।।
kimarthaṃ vābhavadvādaḥ kena sārddhamathāpi vā । etatsarvaṃ yathā vṛttamācakṣtra viditaṃ tava ।। janakasyāśvamedhe tu mahānāsītsamāgamaḥ । ṛṣīṇāṃ hi sahasrāṇi tatrājagmuranekaśaḥ ।।
rājarṣerjanakasyātha taṃ yajñaṃ hi didṛkṣavaḥ । āgatānbrāhmaṇāndṛṣṭvā jijñāsāsyābhavattataḥ ।। ko nveṣāṃ brāhmaṇaśreṣṭhaḥ kathaṃ me niścayo bhavet । iti niścitya manasā buddhiṃ cakre janādhipaḥ ।।
gavāṃ sahasramādāya suvarṇamadhikaṃ tataḥ । grāmānratnāni dāsīscha munīnprāha narādhipaḥ ।। sarvānahaṃ prapanno vaḥ śirasā śreṣṭhabhāginaḥ । yadetadāhṛtaṃ vittaṃ yo vā śreṣṭhatamo bhavet ।।
tasmai tadupanītaṃ me vitta vittaṃ dvijottamāḥ । janakasya vacaḥ śrutvā ṛṣayaste śrutikṣamāḥ ।। dṛṣṭvā dhanaṃ mahāsāraṃ dhanagṛdhnā jighṛkṣavaḥ । āhvayāñcakrire anyonyaṃ vedajñānamadolbaṇān ।।
manasā gatavittāste mamaitaddhanamityuta । mamaitanna tavetyanyo brūhi vā kiṃ vikatthase ।। ityevaṃ dhanadoṣeṇa vādāṃścakuranekaśaḥ । athānyastatravai vidvānbrahmaṇastu sutaḥ kaviḥ ।।
yājñavalkyo mahātejāstapasvī brahmavittamaḥ । brahmaṇoṃ'śasamutpanno vākyaṃ provāca susvaram ।। śiṣyaṃ brahmavidāṃ śreṣṭhaṃ dhanametadgṛhāṇa vai । nayasva ca gṛhaṃvatsa mamaitannātra saṃśayaḥ ।।
sarvavādeṣvahaṃ vaktā nānyaḥ kaścittu matsamaḥ । yo vā na prīyate vidvānsamāhvayatu māciram ।। tato brahmārṇavaḥ kṣubdaḥ samudra iva saṃplave । tānuvāca tataḥ svastho yājñavalkyo hasanniva ।।
krodhaṃ mā kārṣṭa vidvāṃso bhavantaḥ satyavādinaḥ । vadāmahe yathāśakti jijñāsaṃtaḥ parasparam ।। tato abhyupagatāsteṣāṃ vādāḥ śabdairanekaśaḥ । sahasradhā śubhairarthaiḥ sukṣmadarśanasaṃbhavaiḥ ।।
loke vede tathādhyātmavidyāsthānairalaṅkṛtaiḥ । saṃtyuttamaguṇairyuktā nṛpasyāpi parīkṣakāḥ ।। vādāḥ samabhavaṃstatra dhanahetormahātmanām । ṛṣayastvekataḥ sarve yājñavalkyastathaikataḥ ।।
sarve te munayastena yājñavalkyena dhīmatā । ekaikaśastataḥ pṛṣṭā naivottaramathābruvan ।। sa vijitya munīnsarvān brahmarāśirmahāmatiḥ । śākalyamiti hovāca vādakarttāramañjasā ।।
śākalya vada vaktavyaṃ kiṃ dhyāyannavatiṣṭhase । paṇastu yajamānena baddho nīto yathā dhṛtaḥ ।। evaṃ sa dharṣitastena roṣāttāmrāsyalocanaḥ । provāca yājñavalkyaṃ sapuruṣaṃ munisannidhau ।।
tvamasmāstṛṇavatkṛtvā tathaivānyāndvijottamān । vidyādhanaṃ mahāsāraṃ svayaṅgrāhaṃ jighṛkṣasi ।। śākalyenaivamuktastu yājñavalkyastamabravīt । brahmiṣṭhānāṃ balaṃ viddhi vidyātattvārthadarśanam ।।
kāmasyārthena saṃbandhastenārthaṃ kāmayāmahe । kāmaprarśnadhanā viprāḥ kāmapraśnaṃ vadāmahe ।। paṇaścaivāsya rājarṣestasmānnītaṃ dhanaṃ mayā । etacchrutvā vacastasya śākalyaḥ krodhamūrcchitaḥ ।।
yāalkyamathovāca kāmapraśnārthakṛdvacaḥ । brūhīdānīṃ mayoddiṣṭānkāmapraśnānyathārthataḥ ।। tataḥ samabhavadvādastayorbrahmavidormahān । sāgraṃ praśnasahasraṃ tu śākalyaḥ so akarottadā ।।
yājñavalkyo abravītsarvamṛṣīṇāṃ śṛṇvatāṃ tadā । śākalyastvāsa nirvādo yājñavalkyastamabravīt ।। praśnamekaṃ mamāpi tvaṃ śākalya vada kāmikam । paṇaprāpyasya vādasya bruvatormṛtyuratra vai ।।
susūkṣmajñānasaṃyuktaṃ sāṃkhyaṃyogamathāpi vā । adhyātmasya gatiṃ mukhyāṃ dhyānamārgamathāpi vā ।। atha saṃcoditaḥ praśno yājñavalkyena dhīmatā । śākalyastamavijñāya tathā mṛtyumavāptavān ।।
evaṃ smṛtaḥ sa śākalyaḥ praśnavyākhyānapīḍitaḥ । evaṃ vivādaḥ sumahānāsītteṣāṃ dhanārthinām ।। ṛṣīṇāmṛṣibhiḥ sārddhaṃ yājñavalkyasya caiva hi । yājñavalkyo dhanaṃ gṛhya yaśo vikhyāya cātmanaḥ ।
jagāma vai gṛhaṃ svacchaṃ śiṣyaiḥ parivṛto vaśī ।। devamitraśca śākalyo mahātmā dvijapuṅgavaḥ । cakāra saṃhitāḥ pañca buddhimānvedavittamaḥ ।। pañca tasyābhavañchiṣyā mudgalo gokhalastathā ।
khalīyānsutapā vatsaḥ śaiśireyaśca pañcamaḥ ।। provāca saṃhitāstisraḥ śāko vaiṇo rathītaraḥ । niruktaṃ ca punaścakre caturthaṃ dvijasattamaḥ ।। tasya śiṣyāstu catvāraḥ pailaścekṣalakastathā ।
dhīmāñcha tabalākaśca gajaścaiva dvijottamāḥ ।। bāṣkalistu bharadvājastisraḥ provāca saṃhitāḥ । trayastasyābhavañcchiṣyā mahātmāno guṇānvitāḥ ।। dhīmāṃśca tvāpanāpaśca pānnagāriśca buddhimān ।
tṛtīyaścārjavaste ca tapasā śaṃsitavratāḥ ।। vītarāgā mahātejāḥ saṃhitājñānapāragāḥ । ityete bahūvṛcāḥ proktāḥ saṃhitā yaiḥ pravartitāḥ ।। vaiśaṃpāyanaśiṣyo asau yajurvedamakalpayat ।
ṣaḍaśītistu tenoktāḥ saṃhitā yajuṣāṃ śubhāḥ ।। śiṣyebhyaḥ pradadau tāśca jagūhuste vidhānataḥ । ekastatra parityakto yāalkyo mahātapāḥ ।। ṣaḍaśītistathā śiṣyāḥ saṃhitānāṃ vikalpakāḥ ।
sarveṣāmeva teṣāṃ vai tridhā bhedāḥ prakīrttitāḥ ।। tridhā bhedāstu te vedabhede asminnavame śubhe । udīcyā madhyadeśyāśca prācyaścaiva pṛthagvidhāḥ ।। śyāmāyanirudīcyānāṃ pradhānaḥ saṃbabhūva ha ।
madhyadeśapratiṣṭhātā cāsuriḥ prathamaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। ālaṃbirādiḥ prācyānāṃ trayodeśyādayastu te । ityete carakāḥ proktāḥ saṃhitā vādino dvijāḥ ।। carakādhvaryavaḥ kena kāraṇaṃ brūhi tattvataḥ ।
kiṃ cīrṇaṃ kasya vā hetoścarakatvaṃ hi bhejire ।। kāryamāsīdṛṣīṇāṃ ca kiñcidbrāhmaṇasattamāḥ । merupṛṣṭhaṃ samāsādya taistadā tviti mantritam ।। yo vātra saptarātreṇa nāgaccheddvijasattamaḥ ।
sa kuryādbrahmahatyāṃ vai samayo naḥ prakīrtitaḥ ।। tataste sagaṇāḥ sarve vaiśaṃpāyanavarjitāḥ । prayayuḥ saptarātreṇa yatra saṃdhiḥ kṛto abhavat ।। brahmaṇānāṃ tu vacanādbrahmahatyāṃ cakāra saḥ ।
śiṣyānatha samānīya sa vaiśaṃpāyano abravīt ।। brahmahatyāṃ caradhvaṃ vai matkṛte dvijasattamāḥ । sarve yūyaṃ samāgamya brūta kāmaṃ hitaṃ vacaḥ ।। ahamekaścariṣyāmi tiṣṭhantu munayastvime ।
balenotthāpayiṣyāmi tapasā svena bhāvitaḥ ।। eva muktastataḥ kruddho yāalkyama thātyajat । uvāca yattvayādhītaṃ sarvaṃ pratyarpayasva me ।। evamuktaḥ sarūpāṇi yajūṃṣi gurave dadau ।
rudhireṇa tathāktāni ccharditvā brahmavittamāḥ ।। tataḥ sa dhyānamāsthāya saryamārādhayaddvijaḥ । sūrye brahma yadutpannaṃ taṃ gatvā pratitiṣṭhati ।। tato yāni gatānyūrdhvaṃ yajūṣyādityamaḍalam ।
tāni tasmai dadau tuṣṭaḥ sūryo vai brahmarātaye ।। aśvarūpāya mārttaṇḍo yājñavaklyāya dhīmate । yajūṃṣyadhīyate tāni brāhmaṇā yena kenacit ।। aśvarūpāya dattāni tataste vājino amavan ।
brahmahatyā tu yaiścīrṇā caraṇāccarakāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। vaiśaṃpāyanaśiṣyāste carakāḥ samudāhṛtāḥ । ityete carakāḥ proktā vājinastu nibodhata ।। yāalkyasya śiṣyāste kaṇvo baudheya eva ca ।
madhyandinastu sāpatyo vaidheyaścāddhabauddhakau ।। tāpanīyaśca vatsāśca tathā jābālakevalau । āvaṭī ca tathā puṇḍro vaiṇoyaḥ saparāśaraḥ ।। ityete vājinaḥ proktā daśapañca ca sattamāḥ ।
śatamekādhikaṃ jñeyaṃ yajuṣāṃ ye vikalpakāḥ ।। putramadhyāpayāmāsa sumantumatha jaiminiḥ । sumantuścāpi sutvānaṃ putramadhyāpayatpunaḥ ।। sukarmāṇaṃ tataḥ sunvānputramadhyāpayatpunaḥ ।
sa sahasramadhītyāśu sukarmāpyatha saṃhitāḥ ।। provācātha sahasrasya sukarmā sūryavarcasaḥ । anadhyāyeṣvadhīyānāṃstañjaghāna śatakratuḥ ।। prāyopaveśamakarottato asau śiṣyakāramāt ।
kruddhaṃ dṛṣṭvā tataḥ śakrovaraṃ so atha punardadau ।। bhaviṣyato mahāvīryauṃ śiṣyau te atulavarcasau । adhīyātāṃ mahāprājñau sahasraṃ saṃhitā ubhau ।। ete surā mahābhāgāḥ saṃkruddhā dvijasattama ।
ityuktvā vāsavaḥ śrīmānsukarmāṇaṃ yaśasvinam ।। śāntakrodhaṃ dvijaṃ dṛṣṭvā kṣipramantara dhātprabhuḥ । tasya śiṣyo abhavaddhīmān pauṣyañjirdvijasattamāḥ ।। hiraṇyanābhaḥ kauśalyo dvitīyo abhūnnarādhipaḥ ।
adhyāpayata pauṣyāñjiḥ sahasrārddhaṃ tusaṃhitāḥ ।। te nāmnodīcyasāmānaḥ śiṣyāḥ pauṣyañjinaḥ śubhāḥ । sattvāni pañca kauśilyaḥ saṃhitānā madhītavān ।। śiṣyā hiraṇyanābhasya smṛtāstu prācyasāmagāḥ ।
laugākṣiḥ kuśumiścaiva kuśīdirlāṅgalistathā । pauṣyañji śiṣyāścatvārasteṣāṃ bhedānnibodhata ।। nāḍāyanīyaḥ sahataṇḍiputrastasmādanovainanāmā suvidvān । sakotiputraḥ susahāḥ sunāmā caitānbhedānvittalaugākṣiṇastu ।।
trayastu kuśumeḥ śiṣyā aurasaḥ sa parāśaraḥ ।। nābhirvittastu tejasvī trividhā kauśumāḥ smṛtāḥ । śauriṣuḥ śṛṅgiputraśca dvāvetau tu ciravratau ।। rāṇāyanīyiḥ saumitriḥ sāmavedaviśāradau ।
provāca saṃhitāsti sraḥ śṛṅgiputrau mahātpāḥ ।। vainaḥ prājīnayogaśca surālaśca dvijauttamaḥ । provāca saṃhitāḥ ṣaṭtu pārāśaryastu kauthumaḥ ।। āsurāyaṇavaiśākhyau vedavṛddhaparāyaṇau ।
prācīnayogaputraśca buddhimāṃśca patañjaliḥ ।। kauthumasya tu bhedāśca pārāśaryasya paṭ samṛtāḥ । lāṅgalaḥ śālihotraśca ṣaḍuvācātha saṃhitāḥ ।। hālinirjyāmahāniśca jaiminirlomagāyaniḥ ।
kaṇḍuśca kohalaścaiva ṣaḍe te lāṅgalāḥ smṛtāḥ ।। ete lāṅgalinaḥ śiṣyāḥ saṃhitā yaiḥ pravarttitāḥ । eko hiraṇyanābhasya kṛtaḥ śiṣyo nṛpātmajaḥ ।। so akarottu caturviśasaṃhitā dvipadāṃ varaḥ ।
provāca caiva śiṣyebhyo yebhyastāśca nibodhata ।। rāḍiśca rāḍavīyaśca pañjamau vāhanastathā । talako māṇḍukaścaiva kāliko rājikaṃstathā ।। gautamaścājabastaśca somarājāyanastataḥ ।
puṣṭiśca parikṛṣṭaśca ulūkhalaka eva ca ।। yavīyasastu vai śālīraṅgulīyaśca kauśikaḥ । śālimañjaripākaśca śadhīyaḥ kāniniśca yaḥ ।। pārāśaryastu dharmātmā iti krāntāstu sāmagāḥ ।
sāmagānāṃ tu sarveṣāṃ śreṣṭhau dvau parikīrttitau ।। pauṣyañjiśca kṛtaścaiva saṃhitānāṃ vikalpakau । atharvāṇaṃ dvidhā kṛtvā sumanturadadāddvijāḥ ।। kabandhāya punaḥ kṛṣṇaṃ sa ca vidvānyathāśrutam ।
kabandhastu dvidhā kṛtvā pathyāyaikaṃ punardadau ।। dvitīyaṃ devadarśāyasa caturdhākarotprabhuḥ । modo brahmabalaścaiva pippalādastathaiva ca ।। śaulkāyaniśca dharmajñaścaturthastapasi sthitaḥ ।
devadarśasya catvāraḥ śiṣyā hyete dṛḍhavratāḥ ।। punaśca trividhaṃ viddhi pathyānāṃ bhedamuttamam । jājaliḥ kumudādiśca tṛtīyaḥ śaunakaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। śaunakastu dvidhā kṛtvā dadāvekāntu babhrave ।
ddvitīyāṃ saṃhitāṃ dhīmānsaindhavāyanasaṃjñi te ।। saindhavo muñjakeśyaśca bhinnāmādhāddvidhā punaḥ । nakṣatrakalpo vaitānastṛtīyaḥ saṃhitāvidhiḥ ।। caturthoṃ'girasaḥ kalpaḥ śāntikalpaśca pañcamaḥ ।
śreṣṭhāstvatharvaṇāmete saṃhitānāṃ vikalpakāḥ ।। khaḍgaḥ kṛtvā mayā yuktaṃ purāṇamṛṣisattamāḥ । ātreyaḥ sumatirdhīmānkāśyapo hyakṛtavraṇaḥ ।। bhāradvājo agnivarcāśca vāsiṣṭhā mitrayuśca yaḥ ।
sāvarṇiḥ somadattiśca suśarmā śāṃśapāyanaḥ ।। ete śiṣyā mama proktāḥ purāṇeṣu dhṛtavratāḥ । tribhistatra kṛtāstisraḥ saṃhitāḥ punareva hi ।। kāśyapaḥ saṃhitā karttā sāvarṇiḥ śāṃśapāyanaḥ ।
māmikā tu caturthī syāccatasro mūlasaṃhitāḥ ।। sarvāstā hi catuṣpādāḥ sarvāścaikārthavācikāḥ । pāṭhāntare vṛthābhūtā vedaśākhā yathā tathā ।। catuḥ sāhasrikāḥ sarvāḥ śāṃśapāyanikāmṛte ।
laumaharṣaṇikā mūlā tataḥ kāśyapikā parā ।। sāvarṇikā tṛtīyāsāvṛjuvākyārthamaṇḍitā । śāṃśapāyanikā cānyā nodanārthavibhūṣitā ।। sahasrāṇi ṛcāṃ cāṣṭau ṣaṭśatāni tathaiva ca ।
etāḥ pañcadaśānyāśca daśānyā daśabhistathā ।। savālakhilyāḥ saptaitāḥ sasuparṇāḥ prakīrttitāḥ । aṣṭau sāmasahasrāṇi sāmāni ca caturddaśa ।। sāraṇyakaṃ sahohaṃ ca etadgāyanti sāmagāḥ ।
dvādaśaiva sahasrāṇi cchanda ādhvaryavaṃ smṛtam ।। yajuṣāṃ brāhmaṇānāṃ ca tathā vyāso vyakalpayat । sagrāmyāraṇyakaṃ tasmātsamantrakaraṇaṃ tathā ।। ataḥ paraṃ kathānaṃ tu pūrvā iti viśeṣaṇam ।
grāmyāraṇyaṃ samantraṃ tadṛgbrāhmaṇayajuḥ smṛtam ।। tathā hāridravīryāṇāṃ khilānyupakhilānitu । tathaiva taittirīyāṇāṃ parakṣudrā iti smṛtam ।। dve sahasre śatanyūne vede vājasaneyake ।
ṛggamaḥ parisaṃkhyāto brāhmaṇaṃ tu caturguṇam ।। aṣṭau sahasrāṇi śatāni vāṣṭāvaśītiranyānyadhikāni vā ca । etatpramāṇaṃ yajuṣāmṛcāṃ ca saśukriyaṃ sakhilaṃ yājñavalkyam ।। tathā cāraṇavidyānāṃ pramāṇasahitaṃ śṛṇu ।
ṣaṭsahasramṛcāmuktamṛcaḥ ṣaḍviṃśatiṃ punaḥ ।। etāvadadhikaṃ teṣāṃ yajuḥ ki mapi vakṣyate । ekādaśasahasrāṇi ṛcaścānyā daśottarāḥ ।। ṛcāṃ daśasahasrāṇi hyaśītistriṃśadeva tu ।
sahasramekaṃ mantrāṇāmṛcāmuktaṃ pramāṇataḥ ।। etāvānṛci vistāro hyanyaccātharvikaṃ bahu । ṛcāmatharvaṇāṃ pañcasahasrāṇīti niścayaḥ ।। sahasramanyadvijñeyamṛṣi bhirviśatiṃ vinā ।
etadaṅgirasāṃ proktaṃ teṣāmāraṇyakaṃ punaḥ ।। iti saṃkhyā prasaṃkhyātā śākhābhedāstathaiva tu । kartāraśacaiva śākhānāṃ bhedahetūṃstathaiva ca ।। sarvamanvantareṣvevaṃ śākhābhedāḥ samāśritāḥ ।
prājāpatyā śrutirnityā tadvikalpāstvime smṛtāḥ ।। anityabhāvāddevānāṃ mantrotpattiḥ punaḥ punaḥ । dvāpareṣu punarbhedāḥ śrutīnāṃ parikīrttitāḥ ।। evaṃ vedaṃ tadāpyasya bhagavānṛṣisattamaḥ ।
śiṣcebyaśca pradattvā tu tapastaptu vana gataḥ ।। tasya śiṣyapraśiṣyaistu śākhābhedāstvime kṛtāḥ । aṅgāni vedāścatvāro mīmāṃsā nyāyavistaraḥ ।। dharmaśāstraṃ purāṇaṃ ca vidyāścemāścaturdaśa ।
āyurvedo dhanurvedo gāndharvaśceti te trayaḥ ।। arthaśāstraṃ caturthaṃ tu vidyā hyaṣṭādaśaiva hi । jñeyā brahmarṣayaḥ pūrvaṃ tebhyo devarṣayaḥ punaḥ ।। rājarṣayaḥ punastebhya ṛṣiprakṛtayastridhā ।
kāśyapeṣu vasiṣṭheṣu tathā bhṛgvaṅgiro atriṣu ।। pañcasveteṣu jāyante gotreṣu brahmavādinaḥ । yasmādṛṣanti brahmāṇaṃ tato brahmarṣayaḥ smṛtāḥ ।। dharmasyātha pulastyasya kratośca pulahasya ca ।
