pratyūṣasya ca devasya kaśyapasya tathā punaḥ ।। devarṣayaḥ sutāsteṣāṃ nāmatastānnibodhata । devārṣī dharmaputrau tu naranārāyaṇavubhau ।। vālakhilyāḥ kratoḥ putrāḥ kardamaḥ pulahasya tu ।
kuberaścaiva paulastyaḥ pratyūṣasya dalaḥ suta ।। nāradaḥ parvataścaiva kaśyapasyātmajāvubhau । ṛṣanti vedānyasmātte tasmāddevarṣayaḥ smṛtāḥ ।। mānave caiva ye vaṃśe ailavaṃśe ca ye nṛpāḥ ।
ye ca aikṣvākanābhāgā jñeyā rājarṣayastu te ।। ṛṣanti rañjanādyasmātprajā rājarṣayastataḥ । brahmalokapratiṣṭhāstu samṛtā brahmarṣayo amalāḥ ।। devalokapratiṣṭhāstu jñeyā devarṣayaḥ śubhāḥ ।
indralokapratiṣṭhāstu sarve rājarṣayo matāḥ ।। abhijātyātha tapasā mantravyāharaṇaistathā । ye ca brahmarṣayaḥ proktā divyā devarṣayaśca ye ।। rājarṣayastathā caiva teṣāṃ vakṣyāmi lakṣaṇam ।
bhūtaṃ bhavyaṃ bhavajjñānaṃ satyābhi vyātdṛtaṃ tathā ।। saṃtuṣṭāśca svayaṃ ye tu saṃbuddhā ye ca vai svayam । tapaseha prasiddhā ye garbhe yaiśca praveditam ।। mantravyāhāriṇo ye ca aiśvaryātsarvagāśca ye ।
ete rājarṣayo yuktā devādvijanṛpāśca ye ।। etānbhāvānadhigatā ye vai ta ṛṣayo matāḥ । saptaite saptabhiścaiva guṇaiḥ saptarṣayaḥ smṛtāḥ ।। dīrghāyuṣo mantrakṛta īśvarāddivyacakṣuṣaḥ ।
buddhāḥ pratyakṣa dharmāṇo gotraprāvarttakāśca te ।। ṣaṭkarmaniratā nityaṃ śālīnā gṛhamedhinaḥ । tulyairvyavaharanti sma hyaduṣṭaiḥ karmahetubhiḥ ।। agrāmyairvarttayanti sma rasaiścaiva svayaṅkṛtaiḥ ।
kuṭuṃbino buddhimanto vanāntaranivāsinaḥ ।। kṛtādiṣu yugākhyāsu sarvaireva punaḥ punaḥ । varṇāśramavyavasthānaṃ kriyate prathamaṃ tu vai ।। prāpte tretāyugamukhe punaḥ saptarṣayastviha ।
pravarttayanti ye varṇānāśramāṃścaiva sarvaśaḥ ।। teṣāmevānvaye vīrā utpadyante punaḥ punaḥ । jāyamāne pitāputre putraḥ pitari caiva hi ।। evaṃ saṃtatya vicchedādvartayantyāyugakṣayāt ।
aṣṭāśītisahasrāṇi proktāni gṛhamedhinām ।। aryamṇo dakṣiṇaṃ ye tu pitṛyānaṃ samāśritāḥ । dārāgnihotriṇaste vai yai prajāhetavaḥ smṛtāḥ ।। gṛhamedhinastvasaṃkhyeyāḥ śmaśānānyāśrayanti te ।
aṣṭāśītisahasrāṇi nihitā uttarāpathe ।। ye śrūyante divaṃ prāptā ṛṣayo hyūrdhvaretasaḥ । mantrabrāhmaṇakarttāro jāyante ca yugakṣayāt ।। evamāvarttamānāstedvāpareṣu punaḥ punaḥ ।
kalpānāmārṣavidyānāṃ nānāśāstrakṛtaśca ye ।। kriyate yairvyavatdṛtirvaidikānāṃ ca karmaṇām । vaivasvate antare tasmindvāpareṣu punaḥ punaḥ ।। aṣṭāviṃśatikṛtvo vai vedā vyastā maharṣibhiḥ ।
saptame dvāpare vyamatāḥ svayaṃ vedāḥ svayaṃbhuvā ।। dvitīye dvāpare caiva vedavyāsaḥ prajāpatiḥ । tṛtīye cośanā vyāsaścaturthe ca bṛhaspatiḥ ।। savitā pañcame vyāso mṛtyuḥ ṣaṣṭhe smṛtaḥ prabhuḥ ।
saptame ca tathaivendro vasiṣṭhaścāṣṭame smṛtaḥ ।। sārasvatastu navame tridhāmā daśame smṛtaḥ । ekādaśe tu trivarṣā sanadvājastataḥ param ।। trayodaśe cāntarikṣo dharmaścāpi caturdaśe ।
traiyyāruṇiḥ pañcadaśe ṣoḍaśe tu dhanañjayaḥ ।। kṛtañjayaḥ saptadaśe ṛjīṣo aṣṭādaśe smṛtaḥ । ṛjīṣāttu bharadvājo bharadvājāttu gautamaḥ ।। gautamāduttamaścaiva tato haryavanaḥ smṛtaḥ ।
haryavanātparo venaḥ smṛto vājaśravāstataḥ ।। arvākca vājaśravasaḥ somamukhyāyanastataḥ । tṛṇabindustatastasmāttatajastṛṇabindutaḥ ।। tatajācca smṛtaḥ śaktiḥ śakteścāpi parāśaraḥ ।
jātūkarṇo bhavattasmātta smāddvaipāyanaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। aṣṭāviṃśatirityete vedavyāsāḥ purātanāḥ । bhaviṣye dvāpare caiva dvoṇirdvaipāyane api ca ।। vedavyāse hyatīte asminbhavitā sumahātapāḥ ।
bhaviṣyanti bhaviṣyeṣu śākhāpramayanāni tu ।। tasyaiva brahmaṇo brahma tapasaḥ prāptamavyayam । tapasā karma ca prāptaṃ karmaṇā cāpi te yaśaḥ ।। punaśca tejasā satyaṃ satyenānandamavyayam ।
vyāptaṃ brahmāmṛtaṃ śukraṃ brahmaivāmṛtamucyate ।। dhruvamekākṣaramidamomityeva vyavasthitam । bṛhatvādbṛṃhaṇāccaiva tadbrahmetyabhidhīyate ।। pramavā vasthitaṃ bhūyo bhūrbhuvaḥ svariti smṛtam ।
atharvaṛgyajuḥ sāmni yattasmai brahmaṇe namaḥ ।। jagataḥ pralayotpattau yattatkāraṇasaṃjñitam । mahataḥ paramaṃ guhyaṃ tasmai subrahmaṇe namaḥ ।। agādhāpāramakṣayyaṃ jagatsaṃbohasaṃbhavam ।
saṃprakāśapravṛttibhyāṃ puruṣārthaprayojanam ।। sāṃkhyajñānavatāṃ niṣṭhā gatiḥ śamadamātmanām । yattadavyaktamataṃ prakṛtirbrahma śāśvatam ।। pradhānamātmayoniśca gṛhyaṃ sattvaṃ ca śasyate ।
avibhāgastathā śukramakṣaraṃ bahudhātmakam ।। paramabrahmaṇe tasmai nityameva namonamaḥ । kṛte punaḥ kriyā nāsti kuta evākṛtakriyāḥ ।। sakṛdeva kṛtaṃ sarvaṃ yadvai loke kṛtākṛtam ।
śrotavyaṃ vā śrutaṃ vāpi tathaivāsādhu sādhu vā ।। jñātavyaṃ vāpyamantavyaṃ sapraṣṭavyaṃ bhojyameva ca । draṣṭavyaṃ vātha śrotavyaṃ ghrātavyaṃ vā kathañcana ।। darśitaṃ yadanenaiva jñātaṃ tadvai surarṣibhiḥ ।
yanna darśitavāneṣa kastadanveṣṭumarhati ।। sarvāṇi sarvaṃ sarvāṃśca bhagavāneva so abravīt । yadā yatkriyate yena tadā tasmo abhimanyate ।। yatredaṃ kriyate pūrvaṃ na tadanyena bhāṣitam ।
yadā ca kriyate kiñcitkenacidvā kathaṃ kvacit ।। tanaiva tatkṛtaṃ kṛtyaṃ karttṝṇāṃ pratibhāti vai । viriktaṃ cātiriktaṃ ca jñānājñānepriyāpriye ।। dharmādharmauṃ suśaṃ duḥkhaṃ mṛtyuścāmṛtameva ca ।
ūrddhvaṃ tiryyagadhobhāvastasyaivādṛṣṭakāriṇaḥ ।। svayaṃbhuvo atha jyeṣṭhasya brahmaṇaḥ parameṣṭhinaḥ । pratyekavedyaṃbhavati tretāsviha punaḥ punaḥ ।। vyasyate hyekavedyaṃ tu dvāpareṣu punaḥ punaḥ ।
brahmā caitānuvācādau tasminvaivasvate antare ।। āvarttamānā ṛṣayo yugākhyāsu punaḥ punaḥ । kurvanti saṃhitā hyete jāyamānāḥ parasparam ।। aṣṭāśītisahasrāṇi śrutarṣīṇāṃ samṛtāni vai ।
atīteṣu vyatītāni varttante punaḥ punaḥ ।। śritā dakṣiṇapanthānaṃ ye śmaśānāni bhejire । yuge yuge tu tāḥ śākhā vyasyante tai punaḥ punaḥ ।। dvāpareṣviha sarveṣu saṃhitāstu śrutarṣibhiḥ ।
teṣāṃ gotreṣvimāḥ śākhā bhavanti hi punaḥ punaḥ ।। tāḥ śākhāste ca karttāro bhavaṃ tīhāyugakṣayāt । evameva tu vijñeyā atītānāgateṣvapi ।। manvantareṣu sarveṣu śākhāpraṇayanāni vai ।
atīteṣu vyatītāni varttante sāṃprate antare ।। bhaviṣyanti ca yāni syurvartsyante anāgateṣvapi । pūrveṇa paścimaṃ jñeyaṃ vartamānena cobhayam ।। etena kramayogena manvantaraviniścayaḥ ।
evaṃ devāḥ sapitara ṛṣayo manavaśca vai ।। mantraiḥ sahordhvaṃ gacchanti hyāvarttante ca taiḥ saha । janalokātsurāḥ sarve daśakalpānpunaḥ punaḥ ।। paryāyakāle saṃprāpte saṃbhūtā nidhanasya te ।
avaśyabhāvinār'thena saṃbhadhyante tadā tu te ।। tataste doṣavajjanma paśyanto rogapūrvakam । nivarttate tadā vṛttiḥ sā teṣāṃ doṣadarśanāt ।। evaṃ devayugānīha daśakṛtvo vivartya vai ।
janalokāttapolokaṃ gacchantīhānivarttakam ।। evaṃ devayugānīha vyatī tāni sahasraśaḥ । nidhanaṃ brahmaloke vai gatāni ṛṣibhiḥ saha ।। na śakya ānupūrvyeṇa teṣāṃ vaktuṃ suvistaraḥ ।
anāditvācca kālasya saṃkhyānāṃ caiva sarvaśaḥ ।। manvantarāṇyatītāni yāni kalpaiḥ purā saha । pitṛbhirmunibhirdevaiḥ sārddhaṃ ca ṛṣibhiḥ saha ।। kālena pratisṛṣṭāni yugānāṃ ca vivarttanam ।
etena kramayogena kalpamanvantarāṇi ca ।। saprajāni vyatītāni śataśo atha sahasraśaḥ । manvantarānte saṃhāraḥ saṃhārānte ca saṃbhavaḥ ।। devatānāmṛṣīṇāṃ ca manoḥ pitṛgaṇasya ca ।
na śakya ānupūrvyeṇa vaktuṃ varṣaśatairapi ।। vistarastu nisargasya saṃhārasya ca sarvaśaḥ । manvantarasya saṃkhyā tu mānuṣeṇa nibodhata ।। manvantarāstu saṃkhyātāḥ saṃkhyānārthaviśāradaiḥ ।
triṃśatkoṭyastu saṃpūrṇā saṃkhyātāḥ saṃkhyāyā dvijaiḥ ।। saptaṣaṣṭistanthānyāni niyutāni ca saṃkhyāyā । viṃśatiśca sahasrāmi kālo ayaṃ sādhikaṃ vinā ।। manvantarasya saṃkhyeyaṃ mānuṣeṇa prakīrttitā ।
varṣāgreṇāpi divyena pravakṣyāmyuttaraṃ manoḥ ।। aṣṭau śatasahasrāṇi divyayā saṃkhyayā smṛtam । dvipañcāśattathānyāni sahasrāṇyadhikāni tu ।। caturdaśaguṇo hyeṣa kālo hyābhūtasaṃplavam ।
pūrṇaṃ yugasahasraṃ syāttadaharbrahmaṇaḥ smṛtam ।। tataḥ sarvāṇi bhūtāni dagdhānyādityaraśmibhiḥ । brahmāṇāmagrataḥ kṛtvā saha devarṣidānavaiḥ ।। praviśanti suraśreṣṭhaṃ devaṃ nārāyaṇaṃ prabhum ।
sa sraṣṭā sarva bhūtānāṃ kalpādiṣu punaḥ punaḥ ।। ityeṣa sthitikālo vai mato devarṣibhiḥ saha । sarvamanvantarāṇāṃ hi pratisaṃdhiṃ nibodhata ।। yugakhyā yā samuddiṣṭā prāgetasminmayānaghāḥ ।
kṛtatretādisaṃyuktaṃ caturyugamiti smṛtam ।। taccaikasaptatiguṇaṃ parivṛttaṃ tu sādhikam । manoretamadhīkāraṃ provāca bhagavānprabhuḥ ।। evaṃ manvantarāṇāṃ ca sarveṣāmeva lakṣaṇam ।
atītānāgatānāṃ vai varttimānena kīrttitam ।। ityeṣa kīttitaḥ sargo manoḥ svāyaṃbhuvasya te । pratisaṃdhiṃ tu vakṣyāmi tasya caivāparasya ca ।। manvantaraṃ yathā pūrvamṛṣibhirdaivataiḥ saha ।
avaśyabhāvinārthena yathāvadvinivarttate ।। etasminnantare pūrvaṃ trailākyasye śvarāstu ye । saptarṣayaśca devāśca pitaro manavastathā ।। manvantarasya kāle tu saṃpūrṇe sādhike tadā ।
kṣīṇe adhikāre saṃvignā buddhvā paryayamātmanaḥ ।। maharlokāya te sarve unmukhā dadhire matim । tato manvantare tasminprakṣīṇe devatāstu tāḥ ।। saṃpūrṇesthitikāle tu tiṣṭhedekaṃ kṛtaṃ yugam ।
utpadyante bhaviṣyanto ye vai manvantareśvarāḥ ।। devatāḥ pitaraścaiva ṛṣayo manureva ca । manvantare tu saṃpūrṇe tadvadante kalau yuge ।। saṃpadyate kṛtaṃ teṣu kaliśiṣṭeṣu vai tadā ।
yathā kṛtasya saṃtānaḥ kalipūrvaḥ smṛto budhaiḥ ।। tathā manvantarānteṣu ādirmanvantarasya ca । kṣīṇe manvantare pūrve pravṛtte cāpare punaḥ ।। mukhe kṛtayugasyātha teṣāṃ śiṣṭāstu ye tadā ।
saptarṣayo manuścaiva kālāpekṣāstu ye sthitāḥ ।। manvantarapratīkṣāste kṣīyamāṇāstapasvinaḥ । manvantarotsavasyārthe saṃtatyarthe ca sarvadā ।। pūrvavatsaṃpravarttante pravṛtte vṛṣṭisarjane ।
dvandveṣu saṃpravṛtteṣu utpannāsvauṣadhīṣu ca ।। prajāsu cāniketāsu saṃsthitāsu kvacitkvacit । vārttāyāṃ saṃpravṛttāyāṃ dharme caivopasaṃsthite ।। nirānande cāpi loke naṣṭe sthāvarajaṅgame ।
agrāmanagare caiva varṇāśramavivarjite ।। pūrvamanvantare śiṣṭā ye bhavantīha dhārmikāḥ । saptarṣayo manuścaiva saṃtānārthaṃ vyavasthitāḥ ।। prajārthaṃ tapatāṃ teṣāṃ tapaḥ paramaduścaram ।
utpadyante hi pūrveṣāṃ nidhaneṣviha pūrvavat ।। devāsurāḥ pitṛgaṇā ṛṣayo mānuṣāstathā । sarpā bhūtapiśācāśca gandharvā yakṣarākṣasāḥ ।। tatasteṣāṃ tu ye śiṣṭāḥ śiṣṭācārānprajakṣate ।
saptarṣayo manuścava hyādau manvantarasya hi ।। prārabhante ca karmāṇi manuṣyo daivataiḥ saha । ṛṣīṇāṃ brahmacaryeṇa gatvānṛṇyaṃ tu va tadā ।। pitṝṇāṃ prajāyā caiva devānāmijyayā tathā ।
śataṃvarṣasahasrāṇāṃ dharme varṇātmake sthitāḥ ।। trayī vārttā daṇḍanītirdharmānvarṇāśramāṃstathā । sthāpayitvāśramāṃścaiva svargāya dedhire manaḥ ।। pūrvadeveṣu teṣvevaṃ svargāyā bhimukheṣu vai ।
pūrvadevāstataste vai sthitā dharmeṇa kṛtsnaśaḥ ।। manvantare purāvṛtte sthānānyutsṛjya sarvaśaḥ । mantraiḥ sahordhvaṃ gacchanti maharlokamanāmayam ।। vinivṛttādhikārāste mānasīṃ siddhimāsthitāḥ ।
avekṣamāṇā vaśinastiṣṭhantyā bhūtasaṃplavāt ।। tatasteṣu vyatīteṣu pūrvadeveṣu vai tadā । śūnyeṣu devasthāneṣu trailokye teṣu sarvaśaḥ ।। upasthitā ihānye vai ye devāḥ svargavāsinaḥ ।
tataste tapasā yuktāḥ sthānānyāpūrayanti ca ।। satyena brahmacaryeṇa śrutena ca samanvitāḥ । saptarṣīṇāṃ manoścaiva devānāṃ pitṛbhiḥ saha ।। nidhanānīha pūrveṣāmāditāṃ ca bhaviṣyatām ।
teṣāṃ saṃtatyaviccheda ihāmanvantarakṣayāt ।। evaṃ pūrvānupūrvyeṇa sthitisteṣāmavasthitā । manvantareṣu sarveṣu yāvadābhūtasaṃplavam ।। pūrvamanvantarāṇāṃ tu pratisaṃdhānalakṣaṇam ।
atītānāgatānāṃ vai proktaṃ svāyaṃbhuvena tu ।। manvantareṣvatīteṣu bhaviṣyāṇāṃ tu sādhanam । evaṃ saṃtatyavicchedo bhavatyābhūtasaṃplavāt ।। manvantarāṇāṃ parivarttanāni hyekāntatastāni mahargatāni ।
mahājanaṃ caiva janāntapaśca caikāntagāni prabhavanti satye ।। tadbhāvināṃ tatra tu darśanena nānātvadṛṣṭena ca pratyayena । stye sthitā nityatayā tu nityaṃ prāpte vikāre pratisarga kāle ।। manvantarāṇāṃ parivarttanāni muñcanti satyaṃ tu tato aparānta ।
tato abhiyogā viṣayaprahāṇādviśanti nārāyaṇameva devam ।। manvantarāṇāṃ parivarttaneṣu cirapravṛtteṣu vidhisvabhāvāt । kṣaṇaṃ na vai tiṣṭhati jīvalokaḥ kṣayodayābhyāṃ parivartamānaḥ ।। ityantarāṇyevamṛṣistutānāṃ dharmātmanāṃ divyadṛśāṃ manūnām ।
vāyupraṇītānyupalabhya dṛśyād divyaujasāṃ vyāsasamāsayogaiḥ ।। sarvāṇi rājarṣisurarthimanti brahmarṣidevoragavanti caiva । sureśasaptarṣipitṛprajeśairyuktāni samyak parivarttanāni ।। udāravaṃśābhijana śrutīnāṃ prakṛṣṭamedhābhisamedhitānām ।
kīrtidyutikhyātibhirarcitānāṃ puṇyaṃ hi viśyāpanamīśvarāṇām ।। svargīyametatparamaṃ pavitraṃ putrīyametacca paraṃ rahasyam । japyaṃ mahāparvasu caitadagryaṃ duḥkhāpaśāntipradamāyuṣīyam ।। prajaśadavarṣimanupradhānāṃ puṇyāṃ prasūtiṃ prathitāmajasya ।
mamāpi vikhyāpayataḥ samāsātsiddhiṃ prajeśāḥ pradiśantu yuktāḥ ।। ityetadantaraṃ proktaṃ manoḥ svāyaṃbhuvasya ca । vistareṇānupūrvyā ca bhūyaḥ kiṃ varṇayāmyaham ।। manvantarāṇi śeṣāṇi śrotumicchāmyanukramāt ।
manvantarādhipāṃścaiva śakradevapurogamān ।। manvantarāṇi yāni syuratītānāgatāni ha । samāsā dvistarāccaiva bruvato me nibodhata ।। svāyaṃbhuvo manuḥ pūrvaṃ manuḥ svārociṣastathā ।
uttamastāmasaścaiva raivataścākṣuṣastathā ।। ṣaḍete manavo atītā vakṣyāmyaṣṭāvanāgatān । sāvarṇiścaiva raucyaśca bhautyo vaivasvatastathā ।। vakṣyāmyetānpurastāttu manorvevasvatasya ca ।
manavaḥ pañca ye atītā mānasāṃstānnibodhata ।। manvantaraṃ mayā vo adhya krāntaṃ svāyaṃbhuvasya ha । ata ūrdhvaṃ pravakṣyāmi manāḥ svārociṣasya ha ।। prajāsargaṃ samāsena dvitīyasya mahātmanaḥ ।
āsanvai tuṣitā devā manoḥ svārociṣe antare ।। pārāvatāśca vidvāṃso dvāveva tu gaṇau smṛtau । tuṣitāyāṃ samutpannāḥ kratoḥ putrāḥ svarociṣaḥ ।। pārāvatāśca vāsiṣṭhā dvādaśa dvau gaṇau smṛtau ।
chandajāśca caturviṃśaddevāste vai tadā smṛtāḥ ।। divasparśo atha jāmitro gopado bhāsurastathā । ajaśca bhagavāścaiva draviṇaśya mahā balaḥ ।। āyaścāpi mahābāhurmahaujāścāpi vīryavān ।
cikitvānviśruto yastu cāṃśo yaścaiva paṭhyate ।। ṛtaścadvādaśasteṣāṃ tuṣitāḥ parikīrttitāḥ । ityete kratuputrāstu tadāsansomapāyinaḥ ।। pracetāścaiva yo devo viśvadevastathaiva ca ।
samañjo viśruto yastu hyajihmaścārimarddanaḥ ।। āyurdāno mahāmāno divyamānastathaiva ca । ajeyaśca mahābhāgo yavīyāṃśca mahābalaḥ ।। hotā yajvā tathā hyete parikrāntāḥ parāvatāḥ ।
ityetā devatā hyāsanmanoḥ svārociṣāntare ।। somapāstu tadā hyetāścaturviśati devatāḥ । teṣāmindrastadā hyāsīdvipaścillokaviśrutaḥ ।। ūrjā vasiṣṭhaputraśca staṃbaḥ kāśyapa eva ca ।
bhārgavaśca tadhā prāma ṛṣabhoṃ'ṅgirasastathā ।। paulastyaścaiva datto atrirātreyo niścalastathā । paulaho athārvarīvāṃśca ete saptarṣayastathā ।। caitraḥ kiṃpuruṣa ścaiva kṛtānto vibhṛto raviḥ ।
bṛhaduktho navaḥ setuḥ śrutaśceti nava smṛtāḥ ।। manoḥ svārociṣasyaite putrā vaṃśakarāḥ prabho । purāṇe parisaṃkhyātā dvitīyaṃ vai tadantaram ।। saptarṣayo manurdevāḥ pitaraśca catuṣṭayam ।
mūlaṃ manvantarasyaite teṣāṃ caivānvayāḥ prajāḥ ।। ṛṣīṇāṃ devatāḥ putrāḥ pitaro devasūnavaḥ । ṛṣayo devaputrāśca iti śāstre viniścayaḥ ।। manoḥ kṣatraṃ viśaścaiva saptarṣibhyo dvijā tayaḥ ।
etanmanvantaraṃ proktaṃ samāsācca na vistarāt ।। svāyaṃbhuve na vistāro jñeyaḥ svārociṣasya ca । na śakyo vistarastasya vaktuṃ varṣaśatairapi ।। punaruktabahutvāttu prajānāṃ vai kulekule ।
tṛtīye tvatha paryāye uttamasyāntare manoḥ ।। pañca devagaṇā proktāstānvakṣyāmi nibodhata । sudhāmānaśca ye devā ye cānye vaśavarttinaḥ ।। pratardanāḥ śivāḥ satyāgaṇā dvādaśakāḥ smṛtāḥ ।
satyo dhṛtirdamo dāntaḥ kṣamaḥ kṣāmo dhvaniḥ śuciḥ ।। iṣorjjaśca tathā śreṣṭhaḥ suparṇo dvādaśastathā । ityete dvādaśa proktāḥ sudhāmānastu nāmabhiḥ ।। sahasradhāro viśvāyuḥ samitāro vṛhadvasuḥ ।
viśvadhā viśvakarmā ca mānasastu virājasaḥ ।। jyotiścaiva vibhāsaśca kīrttitā vaṃśavartinaḥ । avadhyo avaratirdevo vasurdhiṣṇyo vibhāvasuḥ ।। vittaḥ kratuḥ sudharmā ca dhṛtadharmā yaśasvijaḥ ।
rathormiḥ ketumāñchcaiva kīrttitāstu pratardanāḥ ।। haṃsasvārau vadānyau ca pratardanayaśaskarau । sudāno vasudānaśca sumañjasaviṣāvubhau ।। yamo vahnir yatiścaiva sucitraḥ sutapāstathā ।
śivā hyete tu vijñeyā yajñiyā dvādaśāparāḥ ।। satyānāmapi nāmāni nibodhata yathātatham । dikpatirvākpatiścaiva viśvaḥ śaṃbhustathaiva ca ।। svamṛḍīko diviścaiva varcodhāmā bṛhadvapuḥ ।
aśvaścaiva sadaśvaśca kṣemānandau tathaiva ca ।। satyā hyete parikrāntā yajñiyā dvādaśāparāḥ । ityetā devatā hyāsannauttamasyāntare manoḥ ।। teṣāmindrastu devānāṃ suśāntirnāma viśrutaḥ ।
putrāsttavaṅgirasaste vai uttamasya prajāpateḥ ।। vaśiṣṭhaputrāḥ saptāsanvāśiṣṭhā iti viśrutāḥ । saptarṣayastu te sarva uttamasyāntare manoḥ ।। ācaśca paraśuścaiva divyo divyauṣadhirnayaḥ ।
devāmvujaścāpratimau mahotsāho gajastathā ।। vinītaśca suketuśca sumitraḥ sumatiḥ śrutiḥ । uttamasya manoḥ putrāstrayodaśa mahātmanaḥ ।। ete kṣatrapraṇetārastṛtīyaṃ caitadantaram ।
auttamaḥ parisaṃkhyātaḥ sargaḥ svārociṣeṇa tu ।। vistareṇānupūrvyā ca tāmasasya nibodhata । caturthe tvatha paryāye tāmasasyātare manoḥ ।। satyāḥ surūpāḥ sudhiyo harayaśca gaṇāḥ smṛtāḥ ।
pulastyaputrāste devāstāmasasyāntare manoḥ ।। gaṇastu teṣāṃ devānāmekaikaḥ pañcaviṃśakaḥ । indriyāṇāṃ pratīyeta ṛṣayaḥ pratijānate ।। sapramāṇāstu śīrṣaṇyaṃ manaścaivāṣṭamaṃ tathā ।
indriyāṇi tathā devā manostasyāntare smṛtāḥ ।। teṣāṃ babhūva devānāṃ śibirindraḥ pratāpavān । saptarṣayoṃ'tare ye ca tānnibodhata sattamāḥ ।। kāvya āṅgirasaścaiva kāśyapaḥ pṛthureva ca ।
atreyastvagnirityeva jyotirdhāmā ca bhārgavaḥ ।। paulahaścarakaścātra vāśiṣṭhaḥ pīvarastathā । caitrastathaiva paulastya ṛṣayastāmaseṃ'tare ।। jānujaṅghastathā śāntirnaraḥ khyātiḥ śubhastathā ।
priyabhṛtyo parīkṣicca prasthalo atha dṛḍheṣudhiḥ ।। kṛśāśvaḥ kṛtabandhuśca tāmasasya manoḥ sutāḥ । pañcametvatha paryāye manoḥ svārociṣeṃ'tare ।। guṇāstu ye samākhyātā devānāṃ tānnibodhata ।
amitābhā bhūtarayo vaikuṇṭhāḥ sasumedhasaḥ ।। variṣṭhāśca śubhāḥ putrā vasiṣṭhasya prajāpateḥ । caturdaśa tu catvāro gaṇāsteṣāṃ subhāsvarāḥ ।। ugraḥ prajño agnibhāvaśca prajyotiścāmṛtastathā ।
sumatirvā virāvaśca dhāmā nādaḥ śravāstathā ।। vṛttirāśī ca vādaśca śabaraśca caturdaśa । amitābhāḥ smṛtā hyete devāḥ svārociṣeṃ'tare ।। matiśca sumatiścaiva ṛtasatyau tathaidhanaḥ ।
adhṛtirvidhṛtiścaiva damo niyama eva ca ।। vrato viṣṇuḥ sahaścaiva dyutimānsuśravāstathā । ityetānīha nāmāni ābhūtayasāṃ viduḥ ।। vṛṣo bhettā jayo bhīmaḥ śucirdānto yaśo damaḥ ।
nātho vidvānajeyaśca kṛśo gauro dhruvastathā ।। kīrttitāstu vikuṇṭhā vai sumedhāṃstu nibodhata । medhā medhā tithiścaiva satyamedhāstathaiva ca ।। pṛśnimedhālpamedhāśca bhūyomedhāśca yaḥ prabhuḥ ।
dīptimedhā yaśomedhā sthiramedhāstathaiva ca ।। sarvamedhā sumedhāśca pratimedhāśca yaḥ smṛtaḥ । medhajā medhahantā ca kīrttitāste sumedhasaḥ ।। vibhurindrastathā teṣāmāsīdvi krāntapauruṣaḥ ।
paulastyo davabāhuśca sudhāmā nāma kāśyapaḥ ।। hiraṇyaromāṅgiraso vedaśrīścaiva bhārgavaḥ । ūrdhvabāhuśca vāśiṣṭhaḥ parjanyaḥ paulahastathā ।। satyanetrastathātreya ṛṣayo raivateṃ'tare ।
mahāvīryaḥ susaṃbhāvyaḥ satyako harahā śuciḥ ।। balabandhurnirāmitraḥ kaṃbuḥ śṛgo dhṛtavrataḥ । raivatasya ca putrāste pañcamaṃ vai tadantaram ।। svārociṣaścottamo api tāmaso raivatastathā ।
priyavratānvayā hyete catvāro manavaḥ smṛtāḥ ।। ṣaṣṭhe khalvapi paryāye devā ye cākṣuṣeṃ'tare । ādyāḥ prasūtā bhāvyaśca pṛthukāśca divaukasaḥ ।। mahānubhāvā lekhāscha pañca devagaṇāḥ smṛtāḥ ।
divaukasaḥ sarva eva procyante mātṛnāmabhiḥ ।। atreḥ putrasya naptāro hyāraṇyasya prajāpateḥ । gaṇastu teṣāṃ devānāmekaiko hyaṣṭakaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। antarikṣo vasurhavyo hyatithiśca priyavrataḥ ।
śrotā mantānumantā ca tvādyā hyete prakīrttitāḥ ।। śyenabhadrastathā caiva śvetacakṣurmahāyaśāḥ । sumanāśca pracetāśca vanenaḥ supracetsau ।। muniścaiva mahāsattvaḥ prasūtāḥ parikīrttitāḥ ।
vijayaḥ sujayaścaiva manasyodau tathaiva ca ।। matiḥ parimatiścaiva vicetāḥ priyaniścayaḥ । bhavyā hyete smṛtā devāḥ pṛthukāṃśca nibodhata ।। ojiṣṭhaḥ śakuno devo vānatdṛṣṭastathaiva ca ।
satkṛtaḥ satyadṛṣṭiśca jigīṣurvijayastathā ।। ajitaśca mahābhāgaḥ pṛthukāste divaukasaḥ । leśāstathā pravakṣyāmi nāmatastānnibodhata ।। manojavaḥ praghāsaśca pracetāśca mahāyaśāḥ ।
dhruvo dhruvakṣitiścaiva atyutaścaiva vīryavān ।। yuvanā bṛhaspatiścaiva lekhāḥ saṃparikīrttitāḥ । manojavo mahāvīryasteṣāmindrastadābhavat ।। uttamo bhārgavaścaiva haviṣmānaṅgiraḥsutaḥ ।
sudhāmā kāśyapaścaiva vaśiṣṭho virajāstathā ।। atināmā ca paulastyaḥ sahiṣṇuḥ paulahastathā । madhurātreya ityete sapta vai cākṣuṣeṃ'tare ।। ūruḥ puruḥ śatadyumnastapasvī satyavākkṛtiḥ ।
agniṣṭudatirātraśca sudyumnaśaceti te nava ।। abhimanyuśca daśamo nāḍvaleyā manoḥ sutāḥ । cākṣuṣasya sutāḥ hyete ṣaṣṭhaṃ caiva tadantaram ।। vaivasvatena saṃkhyātastatsargaḥ sāṃpratena tu ।
vistareṇānupūrvyā ca cākṣuṣasyāntare manoḥ ।। cākṣuṣaḥ kasya dāyādaḥ saṃbhūtaḥ sakya vānvaye । tasyānvavāye ye apyanyetānno brūhi yathātatham ।। cākṣuṣasya visargaṃ tu samāsācchṛṇuta dvijāḥ ।
yasyānvavāye saṃbhūtaḥ pṛthurvainyaḥ pratāpavān ।। prajānāṃ patayaścānye dakṣaḥ prācetasastathā । uttānapādaṃ jagrāha putramatriprajāpatiḥ ।। dattakaḥ sa tu putro asya rājā hyāsītprajāpatiḥ ।
svāyaṃbhuvena manunā datto atreḥ kāraṇaṃ prati ।। manvantaramathāsādya bhaviṣyaccākṣuṣasya ha । ṣaṣṭhaṃ tadanu vakṣyāmi upoddhātena vai dvijāḥ ।। uttānapādāccaturaḥ sūnṛtāsūta bhāminī ।
dharmasya kanyā suśroṇī sūnṛtā nāma viśrutā ।। utpannā jāpi dharmema dhruvasya jananī śubhā । dharmasya patnyāṃ lakṣmayāṃ vai utpannā sā śucismitā ।। dhruvaṃ ca kīrttimantaṃ ca tvāyuṣmantaṃ vasuṃ tathā ।
uttānapādo ajanayatkanye dve ca śucismite ।। svarāmanasvinī caiva tayoḥ putrāḥ prakīrttitāḥ । dhruvo varṣasahasrāṇi daśa divyāni vīryavān ।। tapastepe nirāhāraḥ prārthayanvipulaṃ yaśaḥ ।
tretāyuge tu prathame pautraḥ svāyaṃbhuvasya tu ।। ātmānaṃ dhārayanyogānprārthayansumahadyaśaḥ । tasmai brahmā dadau prīto jyotiṣāṃ sthānamuttamam ।। ābhūtasaṃplavāddivyamastodayavivārjitam ।
tasyātimātrāmṛddhiṃ ca mahimānaṃ nirīkṣya tu ।। daityā surāṇāmācāryaḥ ślokamapyuśānā jagau । aho asya tapaso vīryamaho śrutamaho vratam ।। kṛtvā yadenamupari dhruvaṃ saptarṣayaḥ sthitāḥ ।
druve tridivamāsaktamīśvaraḥ sa divaspatiḥ ।। dhruvātsṛṣṭiṃ ca bhavyaṃ ca bhūmistau suṣuve nṛpau । svāṃ chāyāmāha vai sṛṣṭirbhavanārīti tāṃ prabhuḥ ।। satyābhivyahṛtestasya sadyaḥ strī sābhavattadā ।
divyasaṃhananā chāyā divyābharaṇabhūṣitā ।। chāyāyāṃ sṛṣṭirādhatta pañca putrānakalmaṣān । prājīnagarbhaṃ vṛṣabhaṃ vṛkañca vṛkalaṃ dhṛtim ।। patnī prācīnagarbhasya suvarcā suṣuve nupam ।
nāmnodāradhiyaṃ putramindro yaḥ pūrvajanmani ।। saṃvatsarasahasrānte sakṛdāhāramāharan । evaṃ manvantaraṃ yukta indratvaṃ prāptavānprabhuḥ ।। udāradheḥ sutaṃ bhadrājanayatsā divañjayam ।
ripuṃ ripuñjayājjajñe varāṅgī tu divañjayāt ।। riporādhatta bṛhatī vakṣuṣaṃ sarvatejasam । tasya putro manurvidvān brahmakṣattrapravattakaḥ । vyajījanatpuṣkariṇī vāruṇī cākṣuṣaṃ manum ।।
prajāpateḥ sutā kasmādvāruṇī procyate anagha । etadācakṣva tatvena kuśalo hyasi vistare ।। araṇyasyodakaḥ putro varuṇatvamupāgataḥ । tena sā vāruṇī jñeyā bhrātrā khyātimupāgatā ।।
manorajāyanta daśa naḍvalāyāṃ sutāḥ śubhāḥ । kanyāyāṃ sumahāvīryā virajasya prajāpateḥ ।। ūruḥ puruḥ śatadyumnastapasvī satyavākkṛtiḥ । agniṣṭudatirātraśca sudyumnaśceti vai nava ।।
abhimanyuśca daśamo naḍvalāyāṃ manoḥ sutāḥ । ūrorajanayatputrānṣaḍāgneyī mahāprabhān ।। aṅgaṃ sumanasaṃ khyātiṅgayaṃ śukraṃ vrajājinau । aṅgātsunīthāpatyaṃvai venamekaṃ vyajāyata ।।
tasyāparādhādvenasya prakopastu mahānabhūt । prajārthamṛṣayo yasyamamanthurdakṣiṇāṃ karam ।। janitastasya pāṇau tu mathite rūpavānpṛthuḥ । janayitvā sutaṃ tasya pṛthuṃ prathitapauruṣam ।।
abru vaṃstveṣa vo rājā ṛṣayo muditāḥ prajāḥ । sa dhanvī kavacī jajñe tejasā nirdahanniva ।। vṛttīnāmeṣa vo dātā bhaviṣyati narādhipaḥ । pṛthurvainyastadā lokānrarakṣa kṣatrapūrvajaḥ ।।
rājasūyābhiṣiktānāmādyassa vasudhādhipaḥ । tasya stavārthamutpannau nipuṇau sūtamāgadhau ।। teneyaṃ gaurmahārājñā dugdhā sasyāni dhīmatā । prajānāṃ vṛttikāmānāṃ devaiścarṣigaṇaiḥ saha ।।
pitṛbhir dānavaiścaiva gandharvaiścāpsarogaṇaiḥ । sarpaiḥ puṇyajanaiścaiva parvatairvṛkṣavīrudhaiḥ ।। teṣu teṣu tu pātreṣu duhyamānā vasuṃdharā । prādādyathepsi taṃ kṣīraṃ tena prāṇānadhārayan ।।
vistareṇa pṛthorjanma kīrttayasva mahāvrata । yathā mahātmanā tena pūrvaṃ dugdhā vasuṃdharā ।। yathā devaiśca nāgaiśca yathā brahmarṣibhiḥ saha । yakṣai rākṣasagandharvairapsarobhiryathā purā ।।
yathā yathā ca vai sūta vidhinā yena yena ca । teṣāṃ pātraviśeṣāṃśca dogdhāraṃ kṣīrameva ca ।। tathā vatsaviśeṣāṃśca tvaṃnaḥ prabrūhi pṛcchatām । yathā kṣīraviśeṣāṃśca sarvānevānupūrvaśaḥ ।।
yasmiṃśca kāraṇe pāṇirvanasya mathitaḥ purā । kuddhairmaharṣibhiḥ pūrvaiḥ kāraṇaṃ brūhi taddhi naḥ ।। kathayiṣyāmi vo viprāḥ pṛthorvainyasya saṃbhavam । ekāgrāḥ prayatāścaiva śuśrūṣadhvaṃ dvijottamāḥ ।।
nāśuddhāya na pāpāya nāśiṣyāyāhitāya ca । varttanīyamidaṃ brahma nāvratāya kathañcana ।। dhanyaṃ yaśasyamāyuṣyaṃ puṇyaṃ vedaiśca saṃmitam । rahasyamṛṣibhiḥ proktaṃ śṛṇuyādyo anasūyakaḥ ।।
yaścaivaṃ śrāvayenmartyaḥ pṛthorvainyasya saṃbhavam । brāhmaṇebhyo namaskṛtya na sa śocetkṛtākṛtam ।। goptā dharmasya rājāsau babhūvātrisamaḥ prabhuḥ । atrivaṃśasamutpanno hyaṅgo nāma prajāpatiḥ ।।
tasya putro abhavadveno nātyarthaṃ dhārmikastathā । jāto mṛtyusutāyāṃ vai sunīthāyāṃ prajāpatiḥ ।। sa mātāmahadoṣeṇa venaḥ kālātma jātmajaḥ । sa dharmaṃ vṛṣṭhataḥ kṛtvā kāmāllokeṣvartata ।।
sthāpanāṃ sthāpayāmāsa dharmāyetāṃ sa pārthivaḥ । vedaśāstrāṇyatikramya so adharme nirato abhavat ।। niḥsvādhyāyavaṣṭkāre tasminrājyaṃ praśāsati । na pibanti tadā somaṃ mahāyajñeṣu devatāḥ ।।
na yaṣṭavyaṃ na dātavyamiti tasya prajāpateḥ । āsītpratijñā krūreyaṃ vināśe pratyupasthite ।। ahamījyaśca pūjyaśca yajñe devadvijātibhiḥ । mayi yajñā vidhātavyā mayi hotavyamityapi ।।
tamatikrāntamaryādamavadānasusaṃvṛtam । ūcurmaharṣayaḥ sarve marīcipramukhāstadā ।। vayaṃ dīkṣāṃ pravekṣyāmaḥ saṃvatsaraśataṃ nṛpa । tvaṃ mā kārṣīradharmaṃ vai naiṣa dharmaḥ sanātanaḥ ।।
nidhane saṃprasūtastvaṃ prajāpatirasaṃśayaḥ । pālayiṣye prajāśceti pūrvaṃ te samayaḥ kṛtaḥ ।। tāṃ stathā vādinaḥ sarvānbrahmarṣīnabravīttadā । venaḥ prahasya durbuddhirviditena ca kovidaḥ ।।
sraṣṭā dharmasya kaścānyaḥ śrotavyaṃ kasya vā mayā । vīryaṇa tapasā satyairmayā vā kaḥ samo bhuvi ।। mandātmāno na nūnaṃ māṃ yūyaṃ jānīta tattvataḥ । prabhavaṃ sarvalokānāṃ dharmāṇāṃ ca viśeṣataḥ ।।
icchandaheyaṃ pṛthivīṃ plāvayeyaṃ jalena vā । sṛjeyaṃ vā graseyaṃ vā nātra kāryā vicāraṇā ।। yadā na śakyate staṃbhādānāryyabhṛśasaṃhitaḥ । anunetuṃ tadā venastataḥ kruddhā maharṣayaḥ ।।
nigṛhya taṃ ca bāhubhyāṃ visphurantaṃ mahā balam । tato asya vāmahastaṃ te mamanthurbhṛśakopitāḥ ।। tasmātpramathyamānādvai jajña pūrvamiti śrutiḥ । hrasvo atimātraṃ puruṣaḥ kṛṣṇaścāpi babhūva ha ।।
sa bhītaḥ prāñjaliścaiva tasthivānākulendriyaḥ । tamārttaṃ vihvalaṃ dṛṣṭvā niṣīdetyabruvankila ।। niṣādavaṃśakartāsau babhūvānantavikramaḥ । dhīvarānasṛjaccāpi venakalmaṣasaṃbhavān ।।
ye cānye vindhyanilayāstaṃburāstuburāḥ khaśāḥ । adharmarucayaścāpi viddhi tānvenakalmaṣān ।। punarmaharṣayastasya pāṇiṃ venasya dakṣiṇam । araṇīmiva saṃrabdhā mamanthurjātamanyavaḥ ।।
pṛthustasmātsamutpannaḥ karājjalajasannibhāt । pṛthoḥ karatalādvāpi yasmājjātaḥ pṛṣustataḥ ।। dīpyamānaśca vapuṣā sākṣādagniriva jvalan । ādyamājagavaṃ nāma dhanurgṛhya mahāravam ।।
śārāṃśca bibhradrakṣārtha kavacaṃ ca mahāprabham । tasmiñjā te atha bhūtāni saṃprahṛṣṭāni sarvaśaḥ ।। samāpeturmahārājaṃ venaśca tridivaṃ gataḥ । samutpannena rājarṣiḥ satputreṇa mahātmanā ।।
trātaḥ sa puruṣavyāghraḥ punnāmno narakāttadā । taṃ nadyaśca samudrāśca ratnānyādāya sarvaśaḥ ।। abhiṣekāya toyaṃ ca sarva evopata sthire । pitāmahaśca bhagavānaṅgirobhiḥ sahāmaraiḥ ।।
sthāvarāṇi ca bhūtāni jaṅgamāni ca sarvaśaḥ । samāgamya tadā vainyamabhya ṣiñcannarādhipam ।। mahatā rājarājena prajāpālaṃ mahādyutim । so abhiṣikto mahārājo devairaṅgirasaḥ sutaiḥ ।।
ādi rājo mahābhāgaḥ pṛthurvainyaḥ pratāpavān । pitrāparañjitāstasya prajāstenānurañjitāḥ ।। tato rājeti nāmāsya hyanurāgādajāyata । āpastastaṃbhire tasya samudramabhiyāsyataḥ ।।
parvatāścāvadīryanta dhvajabhaṅgaśca nābhavat । akṛṣṭapacyā pṛthivī siddhyantyannāni cintayā ।। sarvakāmadughā gāvaḥ pṛṭake puṭake madhu । etasminneva kāle tu yajatastasya vai makhe ।।
some sute samu tpannaḥ sūtaḥ sautye tadāhani । tasminnevaṃ samutpanne punarjajñe atha māgadhaḥ ।। sāmageṣu ca gāyatsu śubhāṇḍe vaiśvadevike । samāgate samutpannastasmānmāgadha ucyate ।।
aindreṇa haviṣā cāpi haviḥ pṛktaṃ bṛhaspateḥ । juhāvendrāya daivena tataḥ sūto vyajāyata ।। pramādastatra saṃjajña prāyaścittaṃ ca karmasu । śiṣyahavyena yatpṛktamabhibhūtaṃ gurorhaviḥ ।।
adharottaracāreṇa jajñe tadvarṇavaikṛtam । yacca kṣatrātsamabhavadbrāhmaṇyāṃ hīnayonitaḥ ।। sūtaḥ pūrveṇa sādharmyāttulyadharmaḥ prakīrttitaḥ । madhyamo hyeṣa sūtasya dharmaḥ kṣetropajīvanam ।।
rathanāgāśvacaritaṃ jaghanyaṃ ca cikitsitam । pṛthustavārthaṃ tau tatra samāhūtau maharṣibhiḥ ।। tāvūcurmunayaḥ sarve stūyatāmeṣa pārthivaḥ । karmaitadanurūpaṃ ca pātraṃ cāyaṃ narādhipaḥ ।।
tāvūcatustataḥ sarvāṃstānṛṣīnsūtamāgadhau । āvāṃ devānṛṣīṃścaiva prīṇayāvaḥ svakarmataḥ ।। na cāsya vidvo vai karma na tathā lakṣaṇaṃ yaśaḥ । stotraṃ yenāsya kuryāva procustejasvino dvijāḥ ।।
eṣa karmarato nityaṃ satyavāksaṃyatendriyaḥ । jñānaśīlo vadānyaśca saṃgrāmeṣvaparajitaḥ ।। ṛṣibhistau niyuktau tu bhaviṣyaiḥ stūyatāmiti । yāni karmāṇi kṛtavān pṛthuḥ paścānmahābalaḥ ।।
tāni gītanibaddhāni hyastutāṃ sūtamāgadhau । tatastavānte suprītaḥ pṛthuḥ prādātprajeśvaraḥ ।। anūpadeśaṃ sūtāya magadhaṃ māgadhāya ca । tadādi pṛthivīpālāḥ stūyante sūtamāgadhaiḥ ।।
āśīrvādaiḥ prabodhyante sūtamāgadhabandibhiḥ । taṃ dṛṣṭvā paramaprītāḥ prajā ūcurmaharṣayaḥ ।। eṣa vṛttiprado vainyo bhaviṣyati narādhipaḥ । tato vainyaṃ mahābhāgaṃ prajāḥ samabhidudruvuḥ ।।
tvaṃ no vṛttiṃ vidhatsveti mahārṣivaca nāttadā । so abhidrutaḥ prajābhistu prajāhitacikīrṣayā ।। dhanurgṛhītvā bāṇāṃśca vasudhāmādravadbalī । tato vainyabhayatrastā gaurbhūtvā prādravanmahī ।।
tāṃ pṛthurdhanurādāya dravantīmanvadhāvata । sā lokānbrahmalokādīngatvā vainyabhayāttadā ।। saṃdadarśāgrato vainyaṃ kārmukodyatapāṇikam । jvaladbhirniśitairbāṇairdīptatejasamacyutam ।।
mahāyogaṃ mahātmānaṃ durddharṣamamarairapi । alabantī tu sā trāṇaṃ vainyamevānvapadyata ।। kṛtāñjalipuṭā devī pūjyā lokaistribhiḥ sādā । uvāca vainaṃ nādharmaḥ strīvadhe paripaśyati ।।
kathaṃ dhārayitā cāsi prajā yā varddhitā mayā । mayi lokāḥ sthitā rājanmayedaṃ dhāryate jagat ।। matkṛte na vinaśyeyuḥ prajāḥ pārthiva varddhitāḥ । sa māṃ narhasi vai hantuṃ śreyastvaṃ ca cikīrṣasi ।।
prajānāṃ pṛthivīpāla śṛṇu cedaṃ vaco mama । upāyataḥ samārabdhā sarve siddhyantyupakramāḥ ।। hatvāpi māṃ na śaktastvaṃ prajānāṃ pālane nṛpa । antarbhūtā bhaviṣyāmi jahi kopaṃ mahādyute ।।
avadhyaśca striyaḥ prāhustiryagyonigateṣvapi । sattvaṣu pṛthivīpāla dhama na tyaktumarhasi ।। evaṃ bahuvidhaṃ vākyaṃ śrutvā tasyā mahāmanāḥ । krodhaṃ nigṛhya dharmātmā vasudhāmidamabravīt ।।
ekasyārthāya yo hanyādātmano vā parasya ca । ekaṃ prāṇī bahūnvāpi karma tasyāsti pātakam ।। yasmiṃstu nihate bhadre jīvante bahavaḥ sukham । tasminhate nāsti śubhe pātakaṃ copapātakam ।।
so ahaṃ prajānimittaṃ tvāṃ haniṣyāmi vasundhare । yadi me vacanaṃ nādya kariṣyasi jagaddhitam ।। tvāṃ nihatyāśu bāṇena macchāsanaparāṅmukhīm । ātmānaṃ prathayitveha prajā dhārayitā svayam ।।
sā tvaṃ vacanamāsthāya mama dharmabhṛtāṃ vare । saṃjīvaya prajā nityaṃ śaktā hyasi na saṃśayaḥ ।। duhitṛtvaṃ ca me gaccha caivametamahaṃ śaram । niyaccheyaṃ tvadvadhārthamudyantaṃ ghoradarśanam ।।
pratyuvāca tato vainyamevamuktā satī mahī । sarvametadahaṃ rājanvidhāsyāmi na saṃśayaḥ ।। vatsaṃ tu mama taṃ paśya kṣareyaṃ yena vatsalā । samāṃ ca kuru sarvatra māṃ tvaṃ dharmmabhṛtāṃ vara ।
yathā vispandamānaṃ me kṣīraṃ sarvatra bhāvayet ।। tata utsārayāmāsa śilājālani sarvaśaḥ । dhanuṣkoṭyā tathā vainyastena śailā vivarddhitāḥ ।। manvantareṣvatīteṣu viṣamāsīdvasundharā ।
svabhāvenā bhavattasyāḥ samāni viṣamāṇi ca ।। na hi pūrvanisarge vai viṣame pṛthivītale । pravibhāgaḥ purāṇāṃ vā grāmāṇāṃ vāpi vidyate ।। na sasyāni na gorakṣaṃ na kṛṣirna vaṇikpathaḥ ।
cākṣuṣasyāntare pūrvamāsīdetatpurā kila ।। vaivasvateṃ'tare tasminsarva syaitasya saṃbhavaḥ । samatvaṃ yatra yatrāsīdbhūmeḥ kasmiṃścideva hi ।। tatra tatra prajāstā vai nivasaṃti ca sarvaśaḥ ।
āhāraḥ phala mūle tu prajānāmabhavatkila ।। kṛcchreṇaiva tadā tāsāmityevamanuśuśruma । vainyātprabhṛti loke asminsarvasyaitasya saṃbhavaḥ ।। sa kalpayitvā vatsaṃ tu cākṣuṣaṃ manumīśvaraḥ ।
pṛthurdudoha sasyāni sve tale pṛthivīṃ tataḥ ।। tenānnena tatastā vai varttayanti śubhāḥ prajāḥ । ṛṣibhiḥ śrūyate cāpi punardugdhā vasuṃdharā ।। vatsaḥ somastvabhūtteṣāṃ dogdhā cāpi bṛhaspatiḥ ।
chandāsipātramāsīttu gāyatryādīni sarvaśaḥ ।। kṣīramāsīttadā teṣāṃ tapo brahma ca śāśvatam । punastato devagaṇaiḥ purandarapurogamaiḥ ।। sauvarṇaṃ pātramādāya dugdhā saṃśrūyate mahī ।
vatsastu maghavānāsīddogdhā ca savitā vibhuḥ ।। kṣīramūrjaṃ ca madhu ca varttante tena devatāḥ । pitṛbhiḥ śrūyate cāpi punardugdhā vasundharā ।। rājataṃ pātramādāya svadhāmāśu vitṛptaye ।
vaivasvato yamastvāsītteṣāṃ vatsaḥ pratāpavān ।। antakaścābhavaddogdhā pitṝṇāṃ balavānprabhuḥ । asuraiḥ śrūyate cāpi punardugdhā vasundharā ।। āyasaṃ pātramādāya kila māyaśca sarvaśaḥ ।
virocanastu prāhrādirvatsasteṣāṃ mahāyaśāḥ ।। tratvigdvimūrddhā daityānāṃ dogdhābhūdditinandanaḥ । pāyasā te ca māyābhiḥ sarve māyāvino asurāḥ ।। varttayanti mahāvīryāstadeṣāṃ paramaṃ balam ।
nāgaistu śrūyate dugdhā vatsaṃ kṛtvā tu takṣakam ।। alābaātramādāya viṣaṃ kṣīraṃ tadā mahī । teṣāṃ vai vāsukirdegdhā kādraveyaḥ pratāpavān ।। nāgānāṃ vai dvijaśreṣṭha sarpāṇāṃ caiva sarvaśaḥ ।
tenaiva varttayantyugrā mahākāyā viṣolbaṇāḥ ।। tadāhārāstadācārāsta dvīryāstadupāśrayāḥ । āmapātre punardugdhā tvantardhānapriyaṃ mahī ।। vatsaṃ vaiśravaṇaṃ kṛtvā yakṣaiḥ puṇyajanaistathā ।
dogdhā rajatanābhastu pitā maṇidharasya yaḥ ।। yajñātmajo mahātejā vaśī ca sumahāyaśāḥ । tena te varttayantīti paramarthatayā ca ha ।। rākṣasaiśca piśācaiśca punardugdhā vasundharā ।
brahmā brāhyāstu vai dogadhā teṣāmāsītkuberakaḥ ।। vatsaḥ sumālī balavānkṣīraṃ rudhirameva ca । kapālapātre nirdugdhā hyantarddhanaṃ ca rākṣasaiḥ ।। tena kṣīreṇa rakṣāṃsi varttayantīha sarvaśaḥ ।
padmapātre punardugdhā gandharvaiścāpsa rogaṇaiḥ ।। vatsaṃ citrarathaṃ kṛtvā śucīngandhāmahī tadā । teṣāṃ vasurucistvāsīddogdhā putro muneḥ śubhaḥ ।। gandharvarājo atibalo mahātmā sūryasannibhaḥ ।
śailaiśca śrūyate dugdhā punardevī vasundharā ।। tadauṣadhīrmūrtimatī ratnāni vividhāni ca । vatsastu himavānāsīddogdhā merurmahāgiriḥ ।। pātraṃ tu śailamevāsīttena śailāḥ pratiṣṭhitāḥ ।
śrūyate vṛkṣavīrudbhiḥ punardugdhā vasundharā ।। pālāśaṃ pātramādāya chinnadagdhaprarohaṇam । kāmadhuk puṣpitaḥ śālaḥ plakṣo vatso yaśasvinām ।। sarvakāmadughā dogdhrī pṛthivī bhūtabhāvinī ।
saiva dhātrī vidhātrī ca dhāraṇī ca vasundharā ।। dugdhā hitārthaṃ lokānāṃ pṛthuneti hi naḥ śrutam । carācarasya lokasya pratiṣṭhā yonireva ca ।। āsīdiha samudrāntā vasudheti yathā śrutam ।
vasu dhatte yatastasmādvasudhā seti gīyate ।। madhukaiṭabhayoḥ pūrvaṃ medasā saṃpariplutā । teneyaṃ medinītyuktā niruktyā brahmavādibhiḥ ।। tato abhyupagamādrājñaḥ pṛthorvainyasya dhīmataḥ ।
duhitṛtvamanuprāptā pṛthivī paṭhyate tataḥ ।। pṛthunā pravibhāgaścadharāyāḥ sādhitaḥ purā । tasyākaravatī rājñaḥ pattanākaramālinī ।। cāturvarṇamayasamākīrṇā rakṣitā tena dhīmatā ।
evaṃprabhāvorājāsīdvainyaḥ sadvijasattamāḥ ।। namasyaścaiva pūcyaśca bhūtagrāmeṇa sarvaśaḥ । brāhmaṇaiśca mahābhāgairvedavedāṅgapāragaiḥ ।। pṛthureva namaskāryo brahmayoniḥ sanātanaḥ ।
pārthivaiśca mahābhāgaiḥ prārthayadbhirmahadyaśaḥ ।। ādirājo namaskāryaḥ pṛthurvainyaḥ pratāpavān । yodhairapi ca saṃgrāme prāptukāmairjayaṃ yudhi ।। ādikarttāraṇānāṃ vai namasyaḥ pṛthureva hi ।
yo hi yoddhā raṇaṃ yāti kīrttayitvā pṛthuṃ nṛpam ।। sa ghorarūpātsaṃgrāmātkṣemī tarati kīrttimān । vaiśyairapi ca rājarṣirveśyavṛttimihāsthitaiḥ ।। pṛthureva namaskāryo vṛttidānānmahāyaśāḥ ।
ete vatsaviśeṣāśca dogdhāraḥ kṣīrameva ca ।। pātrāṇi ca mayoktāni sarvāṇyeva yathākramam । brahmaṇā prathamaṃ dugdhā purā pṛthvī mahātmanā ।। vāyuṃ kṛtvā tathā vatsaṃ bījāni vasudhātale ।
tataḥ svāyaṃbhuve pūrvaṃ tadā manvantare punaḥ ।। vatsaṃ svāyaṃbhuvaṃ kṛtvā sarvasasyāni caiva hi । tataḥ svārociṣe vāpi prāpte manvantare adhunā ।। vatsaṃ svārociṣaṃ kṛtvā dugdhā sasyāni medinī ।
uttamena tu tenāpi dugdhā devānu jena tu ।। manuṃ kṛtvottamaṃ vatsaṃ sarvasasyāni dhīmatā । punaśca pañcame pṛthvī tāmasasyāntare manoḥ ।। dugdheyaṃ tāmasaṃ vatsaṃ kṛtvā vai balabandhunā ।
cāriṣṭavasya vai ṣaṣṭhe saṃprāpte cāntare manoḥ ।। dugdhā mahī purāṇena vatsaṃ cāriṣṭavaṃ prati । cākṣuṣe cāpi saṃprāpte tadā manvantare punaḥ ।। dugdhā mahī purāṇena vatsaṃ kṛtvā tu cākṣuṣam ।
cākṣuṣasyāntare atīte prāpte vaivasvate punaḥ ।। vainyeneyaṃ purā dugdhā yathā te kathitaṃ mayā । etairdugdhā purā pṛthvī vyatīteṣvantareṣu vai ।। devādibhirmanuṣyaiśca tato bhūtādibhiśca ha ।
evaṃ sarveṣu vijñeyā atītānāgateṣviha ।। devā manvantare svasthāḥ pṛthostu śṛṇuta prajāḥ । pṛthostu putrau vikrāntau jajñāte antarddhipāṣanau ।। śikhaṇḍinī havirdhānamantarddhānāvdyajāyata ।
havirdhānātṣaḍāgneyī dhiṣaṇājanayatsutān ।। prācīnabarhiṣaṃ śuklaṃ gayaṃ kṛṣṇaṃ prajācinau । prācīnabarhirbhagavānmahānāsītprajāpatiḥ ।। balaśrutatapovīryaiḥ pṛthivyāmekarāḍasau ।
prācīnāgrāḥ kuśāstasya tasmātprācīnabarhyasau ।। samudratanayāyāṃ tu kṛtadāraḥ sa vai prabhuḥ । mahatastapasaḥ pāre savarṇāyāṃ prajāpatiḥ ।। savarṇādhatta sāmudrī daśa prācīnabarhiṣaḥ ।
sarvānpracetaso nāma dhanurvedasya pāragān ।। apṛthagdharmacaraṇāste atapyanta mahāttapaḥ । daśavarṣa sahasrāṇi samudrasalileśayāḥ ।। tapaścateṣu pṛthivīṃ tapyatsvatha mahīruhāḥ ।
arakṣyamāṇāmāvabrurbabhūvātha prajākṣayaḥ ।। pratyāhṛte tadā tasmiñcākṣuṣasyāntare manoḥ । nāśakanmāruto vātuṃ vṛttaṃ khamabhavaddrumaiḥ ।। daśavarṣasahasrāṇi na śekuśceṣṭituṃ prajāḥ ।
tadupaśrutya tapasā sarve yuktāḥ pracetasaḥ ।। mukhebhyo vāyumagniṃ ca sasṛjurjātamanyavaḥ । unmūlānatha vṛkṣāṃstānkṛtvā vāyuraśoṣayat ।। tānagniradahaddhora evamāsīddumakṣayaḥ ।
drumakṣayamatho buddhvā kiñcicchiṣṭeṣu śākhiṣu ।। upagamyābravī detānrājā somaḥ pracetasaḥ । dṛṣṭvā prayojanaṃ satyaṃ lokasaṃtānakāraṇāt ।। kopaṃ tyajata rājānaḥ sarve prācīnabarhiṣaḥ ।
vṛkṣāḥ kṣityāṃ janiṣyanti śāmyatāmagnimārutau ।। ratnabhūtā ca kanyeyaṃ vṛkṣāṇāṃ varavarṇinīḥ । bhaviṣyajjanatā hyeṣā dhṛtā garbheṇa vai mayā ।। māriṣā nāma nāmnaiṣā vṛkṣaireva vinirmitā ।
bhāryā bhavatu vo hyeṣā somagarbhā vivarddhitā ।। yuṣmākaṃ tejasārddhena mama cārdhena tejasā । asyāmutpatsyate vidvāndakṣo nāma prajāpatiḥ ।। sa imāṃ dagdhabhūyiṣṭhāṃ yuṣmattejomayena vai ।
agnināgnisamo bhūyaḥ prajāḥ saṃvarddhayiṣyati ।। tataḥ somasya vacanājjagṛhuste pracetasaḥ । saṃtdṛtya kopaṃ vṛkṣebhyaḥ patnīṃ dharmeṇa māriṣām ।। māriṣāyāṃ tataste vai manasā garbhamādadhuḥ ।
daśabhyastu pracetobhyo māriṣāyāṃ prajāpatiḥ ।। dakṣo jajñe mahātejāḥ somasyāṃśena vīryavān । asṛjanmanasā tvādau prajā dakṣo atha maithunāt ।। acarāṃśca carāṃścaiva dvipado atha catuṣpadaḥ ।
visṛjya manasā dakṣaḥ paścādasṛjata striyaḥ ।। dadau sa daśa dharmāya kaśyapāya trayāṃ daśa । kālasya nayane yuktāḥ saptaviṃśatimindave ।। ebhyo dattvā tato anyā vai catasro ariṣṭanemine ।
dve caiva bahuputrāya dve caivāṅgirase tathā ।। kanyāmekāṃ kṛśāśvāya tebhyo apatyaṃ babhūva ha । antaraṃ cākṣuṣasyātha manoḥ ṣaṣṭhaṃ tu gīyate ।। manorvaivasvatasyāpi saptamasya prajāpateḥ ।
vasudevāḥ khagā gāvo nāgā ditijadānavāḥ ।। gandharvāpsarasaścaiva jajñire anyāśca jātayaḥ । tataḥ prabhṛti loke asminprajā maithunasaṃbhavāḥ । saṃkalpāddarśanātsparśātpūrvāsāṃ sṛṣṭirucyate ।।
devānāṃ dānavānāṃ ca devarṣiṇāṃ ca te śubhaḥ । saṃbhavaḥ kathitaḥ pūrvaṃ dakṣasya ca mahātmanaḥ ।। prāṇātprajāpaterjanma dakṣasya kathitaṃ tvayā । kathaṃ prāce tastvaṃ ca punarlebhe mahātapāḥ ।।
etaṃ naḥ saṃśayaṃ sūta vyākhyātuṃ tvamihārhasi । dauhitraścaiva somasya kathaṃ śrvaśuratāṃ gataḥ ।। utpattiśca nirodhaśca nityaṃ bhūteṣu sattamāḥ । ṛṣayo atra na suhyanti vidyāvantaśca ye janāḥ ।।
yuge yuge bhavantyete sarve dakṣādayo dvijāḥ । punaścaiva nirudhyante vidvāṃstatra na muhyati ।। jyaiṣṭhyakāniṣṭhyamapyeṣāṃ pūrvamāsīddvijottamāḥ । tapa eva garīyo abhūtprabhāvaścaiva kāraṇam ।।
imāṃ visṛṣṭiṃ yo veda cākṣuṣasya carācaram । prajāvānāyuṣastīrṇaḥ svargaloke mahīyate ।। evaṃ sargaḥ samākhyātaścākṣuṣasya samāsataḥ । ityete ṣaṭ nisargāśca krāntā manvantarātmakāḥ ।।
svāyaṃbhuvādyāḥ saṃkṣepāccāśuṣāntā yathākramam । ete sargā yathā prājñaiḥ proktā ye dvijasattamāḥ ।। vaivasvatanisargeṇa teṣāṃ jñeyastu vistaraḥ । anyūnānatiriktāste sarve sargā vivasvataḥ ।।
ārogyāyuḥ pramāṇebhyo dharmataḥ kāmator'thataḥ । etāneva guṇāneti yaḥ paṭhannanasūyakaḥ ।। vaivasvatasya vakṣyāmi sāṃpratasya mahātmanaḥ । samāsavyāsataḥ sargaṃ bruvato me nibodhata ।।
saptama tvatha paryāye manorvaivasvatasya ha । mārīcātkaśyapāddevā jajñire paramarṣayaḥ ।। ādityā vasavī rudrāḥ sādhyā viśve marudgaṇāḥ । bhṛgavoṃ'girasaścaiva te aṣṭhau devagaṇāḥ smṛtāḥ ।।
ādityā maruto rudrā vijñeyāḥ kaśyapātmajāḥ । sādhyāśya vasavo viśve dharmaputrāstrayo gaṇāḥ ।। bhṛgostu bhṛgavo devā hyaṅgirasoṃ'giraḥ sutāḥ । vaivasvateṃ'tare hyasminnitye te chandajā matāḥ ।।
ete api ca gamiṣyanti mahāntaṃ kālaparyayāt । evaṃ sargastu mārīco vijñeyaḥ sāṃprataḥ śubhaḥ ।। tejasvī sāṃpratasteṣāmindro nāmnā mahābalaḥ । atītānāgatā ye ca varttante sāṃprataṃ ca ye ।।
sarve manvantaredrāste vijñeyāstulyalakṣaṇāḥ । bhūtabhavyabhavannāthāḥ sahasrākṣāḥ purandarāḥ ।। saghavantaścate sarve śṛṅgiṇo vajrapāṇayaḥ । sarvaiḥ kratuśateneṣṭaṃ pṛthakchataguṇena tu ।।
trailokye yāni sattvāni gatimanti dhruvāṇi ca । abhibhūyāvatiṣṭhanti dharmādyaiḥ kāraṇairapi ।। tejasā tapasā buddhyā balaśrutaparākramaiḥ । bhūtabhavyabhavannāthā yathā te prabhaviṣṇavaḥ ।।
etatsarvaṃ pravakṣyāmi bruvato me nibodhata । bhūtabhavyabhavaddhyeta tsamṛtaṃ lokatrayaṃ dvijaiḥ ।। bhūrloko ayaṃ smṛto bhūtamantarikṣaṃ bhavatsmṛtam । bhavyaṃ smṛtaṃ divaṃ hyetatteṣāṃ vakṣyāmi sādhanam ।।
dhyāyatā lokanāmāni brahmaṇāgre vibhāṣitam । bhūriti vyāhṛtaṃ pūrvaṃ bhūrloko ayamabhūttadā ।। bhū sattāyāṃ smṛto dhātustathāsau lokadarśane । bhūtatvāddarśanāccaiva bhūrloko ayamabhūttataḥ ।।
ato ayaṃ prathamo loko bhūtatvādbhūrdvajaiḥ smṛtaḥ । bhūte asminbhavadityuktaṃ dvitīyaṃ brahmaṇā punaḥ ।। bhavadityatpadyamāne kāle śabdo ayamucyate । bhavanāttu bhuvalloko niruttayā hi nirucyate ।।
antarikṣaṃ bhavattasmāddvitīyo loka ucyate । utpanne tu tathā loke dvitīye brahmaṇā punaḥ ।। bhavyeti vyāhṛtaṃ paścādbhavyo lokastato abhavat । anāgate bhavya ita śabda eṣa vibhāvyate ।।
tasmādbhavyo hyasau loko nāmatastridivaṃ smṛtam । bhūritīyaṃ smṛtā bhūmirantarikṣaṃ bhuvaḥ smṛtam ।। divaṃ smṛtaṃ tathā bhavyaṃ tralokyasyaiṣa nirṇayaḥ । trailokyayuktairvyāhāraistisro vyāhṛtayo abhavan ।।
nātha ityeṣa dhāturvai dhātujñaiḥ pālane smṛtaḥ । yasmādbhūtasya lokasya bhavyasya bhavatastathā ।। lokatrayasya nāthāste tasmādindrādvijaiḥ smṛtāḥ । pradhānabhūtā devendrā guṇabhūtāstathaiva ca ।।
manvantareṣu ye devā yajñabhājo bhavanti hi । yajñagandharvarakṣāṃsi piśāco ragamānuṣāḥ ।। mahimānaḥ smṛtā hyete devendrāṇāṃ tu sarvaśaḥ । devendrā guravo nāthā rājānaḥ pitaro hi te ।।
rakṣantīmāḥ prajā hyete dharmeṇeha surottamāḥ । ityetallakṣaṇaṃ proktaṃ devendrāṇāṃ samāsataḥ ।। saptarṣīnsaṃpravakṣyāmi sāṃprataṃ ye divaṃ śritāḥ । gādhijaḥ kauśiko dhīmānviśvāmitro mahātapāḥ ।।
bhārgavo jamadagniśca hyaurvaputraḥ pratāpavān । bṛhaspatisutaścāpi bharadvājo mahā yaśāḥ ।। autathyo gautamo vidvāñśaradvānnāma dhārmikaḥ । svāyaṃbhuvo atrirbhagavānbrahmakośaḥ sapañcamaḥ ।।
ṣaṣṭho vasiṣṭhaputrastu vasumāṃllokaviśrutaḥ । vatsaraḥ kāśyapaśyaiva saptaite sādhusaṃmatāḥ ।। ete saptarṣayaśyoktā varttante sāṃprateṃ'tare । ikṣvākuśca nṛgaścaiva dhṛṣṭaḥ śaryātireba ca ।।
nariṣyantaścavikhyāto nābhāgo diṣṭa eva ca । karūṣaśca pṛṣadhraśca pāṃśuścanavamaḥ smṛtaḥ ।। manorvaivasvatasyaite nava putrāḥ sudhārmikāḥ । kīrtitā vai tathā hyete saptamaṃ caitadantaram ।।
ityeṣa ha mayā pādo dvitīyaḥ kathitodvijāḥ । vistareṇānupūrvyā ca bhūyaḥ kiṃ kathayāmyaham ।।
